[1,i]	ārya mañju śriye kumāra bhūtāya namaḥ yaḥ anta dvaya āvāsa vidhūta vāsaḥ saṃbuddha dhī sāgara labdha janmā saddharma toyasya gabhīra bhāvam yathā anubuddham kṛpayā jagāda yasya darśana tejāṃsi paravādi mata indhanam dahanti adya api lokasya mānasāni tamāṃsi ca yasya asamajñāna vacaḥ śara oghāḥ nighnanti niḥśeṣa bhava ari senām tri dhātu rājya śriyam ādadhānā vineya lokasya sa devakasya nāgārjunāya praṇipatya tasmai tad kārikāṇām vivṛtim kariṣye uttāna sat prakriya vākya naddhām tarka anila avyākulitām prasannām 
[1,ii^1]	tatra na svatas na api paratas na dvābhyām ityādi vakṣyamāṇam śāstram tasya kāni saṃbandha abhidhāna prayojanāni iti praśne madhyamaka avatāra vihita vidhinā advaya jñāna alaṃkṛtam mahā karuṇa upāya puraḥsaram prathama citta utpādam tathāgata jñāna utpatti hetum ādim kṛtvā yāvat ācārya nāgārjunasya vidita aviparīta prajñāpāramitā ānīteḥ karuṇayā para avabodha artham śāstra praṇayanam iti eṣa tāvat śāstrasya saṃbandhaḥ yat śāsti vaḥ kleśa ripūn aśeṣān saṃtrāyate durgatitaḥ bhavāt ca tad śāsanāt trāṇa guṇāt ca śāstram etat vayam ca anya mateṣu na asti 
[1,ii^2_2,i]	 iti svayam eva ca ācāryaḥ vakṣyamāṇa sakala śāstra abhidheya artha sa prayojanam upadarśayan tad aviparīta saṃprakāśa tvena māhātmyam udbhāvya tad svabhāva avyatireka vartine parama gurave tathāgatāya śāstra praṇayana nimittakam praṇāmam kartu kāmaḥ āha anirodham anutpādam anucchedam aśāśvatam aneka artha manāna artham anāgamam anirgamam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam ityādi tad atra anirodhādi aṣṭa viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ śāstra abhidheya arthaḥ sarva prapañca upaśama śiva lakṣaṇam nirvāṇam śāstrasya prayojanam nirdiṣṭam tam vande vadatām varam iti anena praṇāmaḥ iti eṣa tāvat śoka dvayasya samudāya arthaḥ 
[2,ii]	avayava arthaḥ tu vibhajyate tatra niruddhiḥ nirodhaḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ nirodhaḥ iti ucyate utpādanam utpādaḥ ātma bhāva unmajjanam iti arthaḥ ucchittiḥ ucchedaḥ prabandha vid chittiḥ iti arthaḥ śāśvataḥ nityaḥ sarva kāle sthāṇuḥ iti arthaḥ ekaḥ ca asau arthaḥ ca iti eka arthaḥ abhinna arthaḥ na pṛthak iti arthaḥ nānā arthaḥ bhinna arthaḥ pṛthak iti arthaḥ āgatiḥ āgamaḥ viprakṛṣṭa deśa avasthitānām saṃnikṛṣṭa deśa āgamanam nirgatiḥ nirgamaḥ saṃnikṛṣṭa deśa avasthitānām viprakṛṣṭa deśa gamanam etiḥ gati arthaḥ pratiḥ prāpti arthaḥ upasarga vaśena dhātu artha vipariṇāmāt upasargeṇa dhātu arthaḥ balāt anyatra nīyate gaṅgā salila mādhuryam sāgareṇa yathā ambhasā pratītya śabdaḥ atra lyabantaḥ prāptau apekṣāyām vartate samutpūrvaḥ padiḥ prādurbhāva arthaḥ iti samutpāda śabdaḥ prādurbhāve vartate tatas ca hetu pratyaya apekṣaḥ bhāvānām utpādaḥ pratītyasamutpāda arthaḥ 
[2,iii^1]	apare tu bruvate itiḥ gamanam vināśaḥ itau sādhavaḥ ityāḥ pratirvīpsā arthaḥ iti evam tat hita antam iti aśabdam vyutpādya prati prati ityānām vināśinām samutpādaḥ iti varṇayanti teṣām pratītyasamutpādam vaḥ bhikṣavaḥ deśayiṣyāmi yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam paśyati sa dharma paśyati iti evamādau viṣaye vīpsā arthasya saṃbhavāt samāsasadbhāvāt ca syāt jyāyasī vyutpattiḥ iha tu cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpāṇi ca utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam iti evamādau viṣaye sākṣāt aṅgīkṛta artha viśeṣe cakṣuḥ pratītyā iti pratītya śabdaḥ eka cakṣuḥ indriya hetukāyām api eka vijñāna utpattau abhīṣṭāyām kutas vīpsā artha tā 
[2,iii^2]	prāpti arthaḥ tu anaṅgīkṛtārtha viśeṣe api pratītya śabde saṃbhavati prāpya saṃbhavaḥ pratītya samutpādaḥ iti aṅgīkṛta artha viśeṣe api saṃbhavati cakṣuḥ pratītya cakṣuḥ prāpya cakṣuḥ rūpam ca apekṣya iti vyākhyānāt tad hita ante ca iti aśabde cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpāṇi ca utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam iti atra pratītya śabdasya avyaya tva abhāvāt samāsa asadbhāvāt ca vibhakti śrutau satyām cakṣuḥ pratītya vijñānam rūpāṇi ca iti nipātaḥ syāt na ca etat evam iti avyayasya eva lyabantasya vyutpattiḥ abhyupeyā 
[3,i]	yaḥ tu vīpsā artha tvāt pratyupasargasya eteḥ prāpti artha tvāt samutpāda śabdasya ca saṃbhava artha tvāt tān tān pratyayān pratītya samutpādaḥ prāpya saṃbhavaḥ iti eke prati prati vināśinām utpādaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ iti anye iti para vyākhyānam anūdya dūṣaṇam abhidhatte tasya para pakṣa anuvādā kauśala tvam eva tāvat saṃbhāvyate kim kāraṇam yaḥ hi prāpti artham pratītya śabdam vyācaṣṭe na asau pratim vīpsā artham vyācaṣṭe na api etim prāpti artham kim tarhi pratim prāpti artham samuditam ca pratītya śabdam prāptau eva varṇayati 
[3,ii]	tena idānīm prāpya saṃbhavaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ iti evam vyutpāditena pratītyasamutpāda śabdena yadi niravaśeṣa saṃbhavi padārtha parāmarśaḥ vivakṣitaḥ tadā tām tām hetu pratyaya sāmagrīm prāpya saṃbhava pratītya samutpādaḥ iti vīpsā saṃbandhaḥ kriyate atha viśeṣa parāmarśaḥ tadā cakṣuḥ prāpya rūpāṇi ca iti na vīpsāyāḥ saṃbandhaḥ iti evam tāvat anuvāda akauśalam ācāryasya 
[3,iii]	etat vā ayuktam kim ca ayuktam etat cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpāṇi ca utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam iti atra artha dvaya asaṃbhavāt iti yat uktam dūṣaṇam tat api na upapadyate kim kāraṇam katham anena eva tad prāpteḥ saṃbhavaḥ iti yukti anupādānena pratijñā mātra tvāt atha ayam abhiprāyaḥ syāt arūpi tvā dvijñānasya cakṣuṣā prāptiḥ na asti rūpiṇām eva tad prāpti darśanāt iti etat api na yuktam prāpta phalaḥ ayam bhikṣuḥ iti atra api prāpti abhyupagamāt prāpya śabdasya ca apekṣya śabda paryāya tvāt prāpti arthasya eva ācārya ārya nāgārjunena pratītya śabdasya tat tat prāpya yat utpannam na utpannam tad svabhāvataḥ iti abhyupagamāt tatas dūṣaṇam api na upapadyate iti apare 
[3,iv_3,v]	yat ca api sva matam vyavasthāpitam kim tarhi asmin sati idam bhavati asya utpādāt idam utpadyate iti idaṃpratyaya tā arthaḥ pratītyasamutpāda arthaḥ iti tat api na upapadyate pratītyasamutpāda śabdayoḥ pratyekam artha viśeṣān abhidhānāt tad vyutpādasya ca vivakṣita tvāt atha api rūḍhi śabdam pratītyasamutpāda śabdam abhyupetya araṇyetilaka ādi vadevam ucyate tat api na upapannam avayava artha anugatasya eva pratītyasamutpādasya ācāryeṇa tat tat prāpya yat utpannam na utpannam tad svabhāvataḥ iti abhyupagamāt atha asmin sati idam bhavati hrasve dīrgham yathā sati iti vyākhyāyamānena nanu tat eva abhyupagatam bhavati hrasvam pratītya hrasvam prāpya hrasvam apekṣya dīrgham bhavati iti tatas ca yat eva dūṣyate tat eva abhyupagamyate iti na yujyate iti alam prasaṅgena 
[4,i]	tat evam hetu pratyaya apekṣam bhāvānām utpādam paridīpayatā bhagavatā ahetu eka hetu viṣama hetu saṃbhūta tvam sva para ubhaya kṛta tvam ca bhāvānām niṣiddham bhavati tat niṣedhāt ca sāṃvṛtānām padārthānām yathā avasthitam sāṃvṛtam sva rūpam udbhāvitam bhavati saḥ eva idānīm sāṃvṛtaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ svabhāvena anutpanna tvāt ārya jñāna apekṣayā na asmin nirodhaḥ vidyate yāvat na asmin nirgamaḥ vidyate iti anirodha ādibhiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ viśe ṣaṇaiḥ viśiṣyate yathā ca nirodha ādayaḥ na santi pratītyasamutpādasya tathā sakala śāstreṇa pratipādayiṣyati 
[4,ii]	ananta viśeṣaṇa saṃbhave api pratītyasamutpādasya aṣṭānām eva upādānam eṣām prādhānyena vivāda aṅga bhūta tvāt yathā avasthita pratītya samutpāda darśane sati āryāṇām abhidheya ādi lakṣaṇasya prapañcasya sarvathā uparamāt prapañcānām upaśamaḥ asmin iti saḥ eva pratītyasamutpādaḥ prapañca upaśamaḥ iti ucyate citta caittānām ca tasmin apravṛttau jñāna jñeya vyavahāra nivṛttau jāti jarā maraṇa ādi niravaśeṣa upadrava rahita tvāt śivaḥ yathā abhihita viśeṣaṇasya pratītyasamutpādasya deśanā kriyayā īpsitatama tvāt karmaṇā nirdeśaḥ 
[4,iii_4,v]	anirodham anutpādam anucchedam aśāśvatam aneka artha manāna artham anāgamam anirgamam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam prapañca upaśamam śivam deśayāmāsa saṃbuddhaḥ tam vande vadatām varam yathā upavarṇita pratītyasamutpāda a agamāt ca tathāgatasya eva ekasya aviparīta artha vādi tvam paśyan sarva para pravādān ca bāla pralāpān ivāvetya atīva prasāda anugataḥ ācāryaḥ bhūyas bhagavantam viśeṣayati vadatām varam iti atra ca nirodhasya pūrvam prativedhaḥ utpāda nirodhayoḥ paurvāparya avasthāyāḥ siddhaya bhāvam dyotayitum vakṣyati hi pūrvam jātiḥ yadi bhavet jarā maraṇam uttaram nirjara amaraṇā jātiḥ bhavet jāyeta ca amṛtaḥ iti tasmāt na ayam niyamaḥ yat pūrvam utpādena bhavitavyam paścāt nirodhena iti 
[4,vi]	idānīm anirodha ādi viśiṣṭa pratītya samutpāda pratipipāt ayiṣayā utpāda pratiṣedhena nirodha ādi pratiṣedha saukarya manyamānaḥ ācāryaḥ prathamam eva utpāda prativedham ārabhate utpādaḥ hi paraiḥ parikalpyamānaḥ svatas vā parikalpyeta paratas ubhayatas ahetutaḥ vā parikalpyeta sarvathā ca na upapadyate iti niścitya āha na svatas na api paratas na dvābhyām na api ahetutaḥ utpannāḥ jātu vidyante bhāvāḥ kvacana kecana 
[5,i_5,ii]	tatra jātu iti kadācid iti arthaḥ kvacana śabdaḥ ādhāra vacanaḥ kvacid śabda paryāyaḥ kecana śabdaḥ ādheya vacanaḥ kecid śabda paryāyaḥ tatas ca evam saṃbandhaḥ na eva svatas utpannāḥ jātu vidyante bhāvāḥ kvacana kecana evam pratijñā trayam api yojyam nanu ca na eva svatas utpannāḥ iti avadhāryamāṇe paratas utpannāḥ iti aniṣṭam prāpnoti na prāpnoti prasajya pratiṣedhasya vivakṣita tvāt paratas api utpādasya pratiṣetsyamāna tvāt yayā ca upapattyā svatas utpādaḥ na saṃbhavati sā tasmāt hi tasya bhavane na guṇaḥ asti kaścid jātasya janma punar eva ca na eva yuktam ityādinā madhyamaka avatāra ādi dvāreṇa avaseyā 
[5,iii_5,iv]	ācārya buddha pālitaḥ tu āha na svatas utpadyante bhāvāḥ tad utpāda vaiyarthyāt atiprasaṅga doṣāt ca na hi sva ātmanā vidyamānānām padārthānām punar utpāde prayojanam asti atha san api jāyeta na kadācid na jāyeta iti atra eke dūṣaṇam āhuḥ tat ayuktam hetu dṛṣṭānta anabhidhānāt para ukta doṣa aparihārāt ca prasaṅga vākya tvāt ca prakṛta artha viparyayeṇa viparīta artha sādhya tad dharma vyaktau parasmāt utpanna abhāva ajanma sāphalyāt janma nibodhāt ca iti kṛtānta virodhaḥ syāt 
[5,v^1]	sarvam etat dūṣaṇa m ayujyamānam vayam paśyāmaḥ katham kṛtvā tatra yat tāvat uktam hetu dṛṣṭāntān abhidhānāt iti tat ayuktam kim kāraṇam yasmāt paraḥ svatas utpattim abhyupagacchan pṛcchayate svatas iti hetu tvena tat eva ca utpadyate iti na ca vidyamānasya punar utpattau prayojanam paśyāmaḥ anavasthām ca paśyāmaḥ na ca tvayā utpannasya punar utpādaḥ iṣyate anavasthā ca api aniṣṭā iti tasmāt nirupapattikaḥ eva tvad vādaḥ sva abhyupagama virodhaḥ ca iti kim iti codite parona abhyupaiti yatas hetu dṛṣṭānta upāda āna sāphalyam syāt atha sva abhyupagama virodha codanayā api paraḥ na nivartate tadā nirlajja tayā hetu dṛṣṭāntābhyām api na eva nivarteta na ca unmattakena saha asmākam vivādaḥ iti tasmāt sarvathā priya anumāna tām eva ātmanaḥ ācāryaḥ prakaṭayati asthāne api anumānam praveśayan na ca mādhyamikasya sataḥ svatantram anumānam kartum yuktam pakṣa antara abhyupagama abhāvāt tathā uktam ārya devena sat asat sat asat ca iti yasya pakṣaḥ na vidyate 
[5,v^2]	upālambhaḥ cireṇa api tasya vaktum na śakyate vigraha vyāvartanyām ca uktam yadi kācana pratijñā syāt me tatas eva me bhavet doṣaḥ na asti ca mama pratijñā tasmāt na eva asti me doṣaḥ yadi kiṃcid upala meyam pravartayeyam nivartayeyam vā pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ arthaiḥ tad abhāvāt me anupālambhaḥ iti yadā ca evam svatantra anumāna anabhidhāyi tvam mādhyamikasya tadā kutas na ādhyātmikāni āyatanāni svatas utpannāni iti svatantrā pratijñāḥ yasyām sāṃkhyāḥ pratyavasthāpyante kaḥ arya pratijñā arthaḥ kim kārya ātmaka tvāt svatas uta kāraṇa ātmaka tvāt iti kim ca atas kārya ātmakāt ced siddha sādhanam kāraṇa ātmakāt ced viruddha artha tā kāraṇa ātmanā vidyamānasya eva sarvasya utpattimataḥ utpādāt iti kutas asmākam vidyamāna tvāt iti hetuḥ yasya siddha sādhanam viruddha artha tā vā syāt yasya siddha sādhanasya yasyāḥ ca viruddha artha tāyāḥ parihāra artham yatnam kariṣyāmaḥ tasmāt para ukta doṣa aprasaṅgāt eva tad parihāraḥ ācārya buddha pālitena na varṇanīyaḥ 
[6,i^1]	atha api syāt mādhyamikānām pakṣa hetu dṛṣṭāntānām asiddheḥ svatantra anumāna anabhidhāyi tvāt svatas utpatti pratiṣedha pratijñāta artha sādhanam mā bhūt ubhaya siddhena vā anumānena para pratijñā nirākaraṇam para pratijñāya astu svatas eva anumāna virodha codanayā svatas eva pakṣa hetu dṛṣṭānta doṣa rahitaiḥ pakṣa ādibhiḥ bhavitavyam tatas ca tad anabhidhānāt tad doṣa aparihārāt ca saḥ eva doṣaḥ iti ucyate na etat evam kim kāraṇam yasmāt yaḥ hi yam artham pratijānīte tena sva niścaya vat anyeṣām niścaya utpādana icchayā yayā upapattyā asau arthaḥ adhigataḥ sā eva upapattiḥ parasmai upadeṣṭavyā 
[6,i^2]	tasmāt eṣa tāvat nyāyaḥ yat pareṇa eva sva abhyupagata pratijñāta artha sādhanam upādeyam na ca anena param prati hetu dṛṣṭānta asaṃbhavāt pratijñā anusāra tayā eva kevalam sva pratijñāta artha sādhanam upādatte iti nirupapattika pakṣa abhyupagamāt sva ātmānam eva ayam kevalam visaṃvādayan na śaknoti pareṣām niścayam ādhātum iti idam eva asya spaṣṭataram dūṣaṇam yat uta sva pratijñāta artha sādhana āsāmarthyam iti kim atra anumāna bādha udbhāvanayā prayojanam atha api avaśyam svatas anumāna virodha doṣaḥ udbhāvanīyaḥ saḥ api udbhāvitaḥ eva ācārya buddha pālitena 
[6,i^3]	katham iti ced na svatas utpadyante bhāvāḥ tad utpāda vaiyarthyāt iti vacanāt atra hi tat iti anena sva ātmanā vidyamānasya parāmarśaḥ kasmāt iti ced tathā hi tasya saṃgraheṇa ukta vākyasya etat vivaraṇa vākyam na hi sva ātmanā vidyamānānām punar utpāde prayojanam iti anena ca vākyena sādhya sādhana dharma anugatasya para prasiddhasya sādharmya dṛṣṭāntasya upādānam tatra sva ātmanā vidyamānasya iti anena hetu parāmarśaḥ utpāda vayarthyāt ityanena sādhya dharma parāmarśaḥ tatra yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt kṛtaka tvam anityam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭaḥ tathā ca kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ 
[6,i^4]	tasmāt kṛtaka tvāt anityaḥ iti kṛtaka tvam atra upanaya abhivyaktaḥ hetuḥ evam iha api na svatas utpadyante bhāvāḥ sva ātmanā vidyamānānām punar utpāda vaiyarthyāt iha hi sva ātmanā vidyamānam puras avasthitam ghaṭa ādikam punar utpāda anapekṣam dṛṣṭam tathā ca mṛd piṇḍa ādi avasthāyām api yadi sva ātmanā vidyamānam ghaṭa ādikam iti manyase tadā api tasya sva ātmanā vidyamānasya na asti utpādaḥ iti evam sva ātmanā vidyamāna tvena upanaya abhivyaktena punar utpāda pratiṣedha avyabhicāriṇā hetunā svatas eva sāṃkhyasya anumāna virodha udbhāvanam anuṣṭhitam eva iti tat kim ucyate tat ayuktam hetu dṛṣṭāntān abhidhānāt iti 
[7,i]	na ca kevalam hetu dṛṣṭāntān abhidhānam na saṃbhavati para ukta doṣa aparihāra doṣaḥ na saṃbhavati katham kṛtvā sāṃkhyāḥ hi na eva abhivyakta rūpasya puras avasthitasya ghaṭasya punar abhivyaktim icchanti tasya eva ca iha dṛṣṭānta tvena upādānam siddha rūpa tvāt anabhivyakta rūpasya ca śakti rūpa āpannasya utpatti pratiṣedha viśiṣṭa sādhya tvāt kutas siddha sādhana pakṣa doṣa āśaṅkā kutas vā hetoḥ viruddhārtha tā śaṅkā iti tasmāt svataḥ anumāna virodha codanāyām api yathā upavarṇita doṣa abhāvāt para ukta doṣa aparihāra asaṃbhavaḥ eva iti asaṃbaddham eva etat dūṣaṇam iti vijñeyam 
[7,ii_7,iii]	ghaṭa ādikam iti ādi śabdena niravaśeṣa utpitsu padārtha saṃgrahasya vivakṣita tvāt anaikāntika tā api paiṭādibhiḥ na eva saṃbhavati athavā ayam anyaḥ prayoga mārgaḥ puruṣa vyatiriktāḥ padārthāḥ svatas utpatti vādinaḥ tatas eva na svatas utpadyante sva ātmanā vidyamāna tvāt puruṣa vat iti idam udāharaṇam udāhāryam 
[7,iv_7,v]	yadi api ca abhivyakti vādinaḥ utpāda pratiṣedhaḥ na bādhakaḥ tathā api abhivyaktau utpāda śabdam nipātya pūrvam paścāt ca anupalabdhi upalabdhi sādharmyeṇa utpāda śabdena abhivyakteḥ eva abhidhānāt ayam pratiṣedhaḥ na abādhakaḥ katham punar ayam yathā ukta artha abhidhānam vinā vyasta vicāraḥ labhyate iti ced tat ucyate atha vākyāni kṛtāni tāni mahārtha tvāt yathā uditam artham saṃgṛhya pravṛttāni tāni ca vyākhyāyamānāni yathoktam artha ātmānam prasūyante iti na atra kiṃcid anupāttam saṃbhāvyate 
[7,vi^1]	prasaṅga viparītena ca arthena parasya eva saṃbandhaḥ na asmākam sva pratijñāyāḥ abhāvāt tatas ca siddhānta virodha asaṃbhavaḥ parasya ca yāvat bahavaḥ doṣāḥ prasaṅga viparīta āpattyāḥ āpadyante tāvat asmābhiḥ abhīṣyate eva iti kutas nu khalu aviparīta ācārya nāgārjuna mata anusāriṇaḥ ācārya buddha pālitasya sa avakāśa vacana abhidhāyi tvam yatas asya paraḥ avakāśam labheta niḥsvabhāva bhāva vādinā sa svabhāva bhāva vādinaḥ prasaṅge pādyamāne kutas prasaṅga viparīta artha prasaṅgi tā na hi śabdāḥ dāṇḍa pāśikāḥ iva vaktāram asvatantrayanti kim tarhi satyām śaktau vaktuḥ vivakṣām anuvidhīyante 
[7,vi^2]	tatas ca para pratijñā pratiṣedha mātra phala tvāt prasaṅga āpādanasya na asti prasaṅga viparīta arthāpattiḥ tathā ca ācāryaḥ bhūyasā prasaṅga āpatti mukhena eva para pakṣam nirākaroti sma tat yathā na ākāśam vidyate kiṃcid pūrvam ākāśa lakṣaṇāt alakṣaṇam prasajyeta syāt pūrvam yadi lakṣaṇāt rūpa kāraṇa nirmukte rūpe rūpam prasajyate āhetukam na ca asti arthaḥ kaścid āhetukaḥ kvacid bhāvaḥ tāvat na nirvāṇam jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇam prasajyeta asti bhāvaḥ hi na jarā maraṇam vinā ityādinā atha artha vākya tvāt ācārya vākyānām mahārtha tve sati aneka prayoniṣpatti hetu tvam parikalpyate ācārya buddha pālita vyākhyānāni api kim iti na tathā eva parikalpyante 
[8,i_8,ii]	atha syāt vṛtti kārāṇām eṣa nyāyaḥ yad prayoga vākya vistara abhidhānam kartavyam iti etat api na asti vigraha vyāvartanyā vṛttim kurvatā api ācāryeṇa prayoga vākya anabhidhānāt api ca ātmanaḥ tarka śāstra ati kauśala mātram āviścikīrṣayā aṅgīkṛta madhyamaka darśanasya api yat svatantra prayoga vākya abhidhānam tat atitarām aneka doṣa samudāya āspadam asya tārkikasya upalakṣyate katham kṛtvā tatra yat tāvat evam uktam atra prayoga vākyam bhavati na paramārthataḥ ādhyātmikāni āyatanāni svatas utpannāni vidyamāna tvāt caitanya vat iti kim artha punar atra paramārthataḥ iti viśeṣaṇam upādīyate loka saṃvṛtya abhyupagatasya utpādasya apratiṣidhyamāna tvāt pratiṣedhe ca abhyupeta bādha aprasaṅgāt iti ced na etat yuktam saṃvṛtya api svatas utpatti anabhyupagamāt yathā uktam sūtre 
[8,iii_8,v]	sa ca ayam bīja hetukaḥ aṅkuraḥ utpadyamānaḥ na svayaṃkṛtaḥ na para kṛtaḥ na ubhaya kṛtaḥ na api ahetu samutpannaḥ niśvara kāla aṇu prakṛti svabhāva saṃbhūtaḥ iti tathā bījasya sataḥ yathā aṅkuraḥ na ca yaḥ bīju sa ca eva aṅkuraḥ na ca anyu tatas na ca eva tat evam anuccheda aśāśvata dharma tā iha api vakṣyati pratītya yat yat bhavati na hi tāvat tat eva tat na ca anyat api tat tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam iti 
[9,i_9,ii]	parama tāpekṣam viśeṣaṇam iti ced tat ayuktam saṃvṛtya api tadīya vyavasthā anabhyupagamāt satya dvaya aviparīta darśana paribhraṣṭāḥ eva hi tīrthikāḥ yāvat ubhayathā api niṣidhyante tāvat guṇaḥ eva saṃbhāvyate iti evam parama tāpekṣam api viśeṣaṇa abhidhānam na yujyate na ca api lokaḥ svatautpattim pratipannaḥ yatas tad apekṣayā api viśeṣaṇa sāphalyam syāt lokaḥ hi svatas paratas iti evam ādikam vicāram anavatārya kāraṇāt kāryam utpadyate iti etāvat mātram pratipannaḥ evam ācāryaḥ api vyavasthāpayāmāsa iti sarvathā viśeṣaṇa vaiphalyam eva niścīyate 
[9,iii]	api ca yadi saṃvṛtyā utpatti pratiṣedha nirāci kīrṣuṇā viśeṣaṇam etat upādīyate tadā svatas asiddha ādhāre pakṣa doṣaḥ āśraya asiddhau vā hetu doṣaḥ syāt paramārthataḥ svatas cakṣuḥ ādi āyatanānām anabhyupagamāt saṃvṛtyā cakṣuḥ ādi sadbhāvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced paramārthataḥ iti etat tarhi kasya viśeṣaṇam sāṃvṛtānām cakṣuḥ ādīnām paramārthataḥ utpatti pratiṣedhāt utpatti pratiṣedha viśeṣaṇe parama artha grahaṇam iti ced evam tarhi evam eva vaktavyam syāt sāṃvṛtānām cakṣuḥ ādīnām paramārthataḥ na asti utpattiḥ iti na ca evam ucyate ucyamāne api paraiḥ vastu satām eva cakṣuḥ ādīnām abhyupagamāt prajñapti satām anabhyupagamāt paratas asiddha ādhāraḥ pakṣa doṣaḥ syāt iti na yuktam etat 
[9,iv^1]	atha syāt yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti dharma dharmi sāmānyam eva gṛhyate na viśeṣaḥ viśeṣa grahaṇe hi sati anumāna anumeya vyavahāra abhāvaḥ syāt tathā hi yadi cāturmahābhautikaḥ śabdaḥ gṛhyate sa parasya asiddhaḥ atha ākāśa guṇaḥ gṛhyate sa bauddhasya svatas asiddhaḥ tathā vaiśeṣikasya śabda anitya tām pratijānānasya yadi kāryaḥ śabdaḥ gṛhyate sa paratas asiddhaḥ atha vyaṅgayaḥ sa svatas asiddhaḥ evam yathāsaṃbhavam vināśaḥ api yadi sa hetukaḥ sa bauddhasya svatas asiddhaḥ atha nirhetukaḥ sa parasya asiddhaḥ iti tasmāt yathā atra dharma dharmi sāmānya mātram eva gṛhyate evam iha api dharmi mātram utsṛṣṭa viśeṣaṇam grahīṣyate iti ced na etat evam yasmāt yadā eva utpāda pratiṣedhaḥ atra sādhya dharmaḥ abhipretaḥ tadā eva dharmiṇaḥ tad ādhārasya viparyāsa mātra āsādita ātma bhāvasya pracyutiḥ svayam eva anena aṅgīkṛtā 
[9,iv^2]	bhinnau hi viparyāsa aviparyāsau tat yadā viparyāsena asat sattvena gṛhyate taimirikeṇa iva keśa ādi tadā kutas sat bhūta padārtha leśasya api upalabdhiḥ yadā ca aviparyāsāt abhūtam na adhyāropitam vitaimirikeṇa iva keśa ādi tadā kutas asat bhūta padārtha leśasya api upalabdhiḥ yena tadānīm saṃvṛtiḥ syāt atas eva uktam ācārya pādaiḥ yadi kiṃcid upala meyam pravartayeyam nivartayeyam vā pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ arthaiḥ tad abhāvāt me anupālambhaḥ iti yatas ca evam bhinnau viparyāsa aviparyāsau atas viduṣām aviparīta avasthāyām viparītasya asaṃbhavāt kutas sāṃvṛtam cakṣuḥ yasya dharmi tvam syāt iti na vyāvartate asiddha ādhāre pakṣa doṣaḥ āśraya asiddhaḥ vā hetu doṣaḥ iti aparihāraḥ eva ayam 
[10,i_10,iii]	nidarśanasya api na asti sāmyam tatra hi śabda sāmānyam anitya tā sāmānyam ca avivakṣita viśeṣam dvayoḥ api saṃvidyate na tu evam cakṣuḥ sāmānyam śūnyatā śūnyatāvādibhyām saṃvṛtyāḥ aṅgīkṛtam na api paramārthataḥ iti na asti nidarśanasya sāmyam yaḥ ca ayam asiddha ādhāra pakṣa doṣa udbhāvane vidhiḥ eṣaḥ eva sattva ādityasya hetoḥ asiddhārtha tā udbhāvane api yojyaḥ ittham ca etat evam yat svayam aṣyanena ayam yathā uktaḥ arthaḥ abhyupagataḥ tārkikeṇa santi eva ādhyātmika āyatana utpādakāḥ hetu ādayaḥ tathā tathāgatena nirdeśāt yat hi yathā tathāgatena asti nirdiṣṭam tat tathā tat yathā śāntam nirvāṇam iti 
[10,iv]	asya para upakṣiptasya sādhanasya idam dūṣaṇam abhihitam anena kaḥ hi bhavatām abhipretaḥ atra hetu arthaḥ saṃvṛtyā tathā tathāgatena nirdeśāt uta paramārthataḥ iti saṃvṛtyā ced svatas hetoḥ asiddhārtha tā paramārthataḥ ced na san āsan na sat asat dharmaḥ nirvartate yadā sat asat ubhaya ātmaka kārya pratyaya tva nirākaraṇāt tadā katham nirvartakaḥ hetuḥ evam sati hi yujyate na eva asau nirvartakaḥ hetuḥ iti vākya arthaḥ tatas ca paramārthataḥ nirvartya nirvartaka tva asiddheḥ asiddhārtha tā viruddha artha tā vā hetoḥ iti 
[10,v]	yatas ca evam svayam eva amunā nyāyena hetoḥ asiddhiḥ aṅgīkṛta anena tasmāt sarveṣu eva anumāneṣu vastu dharma upanyasta hetukeṣu svatas evam hetu ādīnām asiddha tvāt sarvāṇi eva sādhanāni vyāhanyante tat yathā na paramārthataḥ parebhyaḥ tad pratyayebhyaḥ ādhyātmika āyatana janma paratvāt tat yathā paṭasya athavā na pare parama arthena vivakṣitāḥ cakṣuḥ ādi ādhyātmika āyatana nirvartakāḥ pratyayāḥ iti pratīyante paratvāt tat yathā tantu ādayaḥ iti paratva ādikam atra svatas eva asiddham 
[10,vi]	yathā ca anena utpannāḥ eva ādhyātmikāḥ bhāvāḥ tad viṣayi viśiṣṭa vyavahāra karaṇāt iti asya para abhihitasya hetoḥ asiddhārtha tām udbhāvayiṣuṇā idam uktam atha samāhitasya yoginaḥ prajñācakṣuṣā bhāva yāthātmyam paśyataḥ utpāda gati ādayaḥ santi paramārthataḥ iti sādhyate tadā tad viṣayi viśiṣṭa vyavahāra karaṇāt iti hetoḥ asiddhārtha tā gateḥ api utpāda niṣedhāt eva niṣedhāt iti evam sva kṛta sādhane api paramārthataḥ agatam na eva gamyate adhva tvāt gatādhva vat iti adhva tva hetoḥ svatas eva asiddhārtha tā yojyā 
[10,vii_11,i]	na paramārthataḥ sa bhāgam cakṣuḥ rūpam paśyati cakṣuḥ indriya tvāt tat yathā tad sa bhāgam tathā na cakṣuḥ prekṣate rūpam bhautika tvāt rūpavat khara svabhāvā na mahī bhūta tvāt tat yathā nirlaḥ ityādiṣu hetu ādi asiddhiḥ svatas eva yojyā sattvāt iti ca ayam hetuḥ paratas anaikāntikaḥ kim sattvāt caitanya vat na ādhyātmikāni āyatanāni svatas utpadyantām uta aho ghaṭa ādi vat svatas utpadyantām iti ghaṭa ādīnām sādhya sama tvāt na anā ekāntika tā iti ced na etat evam tathā anabhidhānāt 
[11,ii]	nanu ca yathā parakīyeṣu anumāneṣu dūṣaṇam uktam evam sva anumāneṣu api yathā ukta dūṣaṇa prasaṅge sati saḥ eva asiddha ādhārā siddha hetu ādi doṣaḥ prāpnoti tatas ca yaḥ ubhayoḥ doṣaḥ na tena ekaḥ codyaḥ bhavati iti sarvam etat dūṣaṇam ayuktam jāyate iti ucyate svatantram anumānam bruvatāmayam doṣaḥ jāyate na vayam svatantram anumānam prayuñjma mahe para pratijñā niṣedha phala tvāt asmad anumānānām tathā hi paraḥ cakṣuḥ paśyati iti pratipannaḥ sa tad prasiddhena eva anumānena nirākriyate cakṣuṣaḥ sva ātma adarśana dharmam icchasi para darśana dharma avinābhāvi tvam ca aṅgīkṛtam tasmāt yatra yatra sva ātma adarśanam tatra tatra para darśanam api na asti tat yathā ghaṭe asti ca cakṣuṣaḥ sva ātma adarśanam tasmāt para darśanam api asya na eva asti tatas ca sva ātma adarśana viruddham nīla ādi para darśanam sva prasiddhena eva anumānena virudhyate iti etāvat mātram asmadanūmānaiḥ udbhāvyate iti kutas asmad pakṣe yathā ukta doṣa avatāraḥ yatas samāna doṣa tā syāt 
[11,iii]	kim punar anyatara prasiddhena api anumānena asti anumāna bādhā asti sā ca sva prasiddhena eva hetunā na para prasiddhena lokataḥ evam dṛṣṭa tvāt kadācid hi loke arthi pratyarthibhyām pramāṇīkṛtasya sākṣiṇaḥ vacanena jayaḥ bhavati parājayaḥ vā kadācid sva vacanena para vacanena tu na jayaḥ na api parājayaḥ yathā ca loke tathā nyāye api laukikasya eva vyavahārasya nyāya śāstre prastuta tvāt atas eva kaiścid uktam na paratas prasiddhi balāt anumāna bādhā para prasiddheḥ eva nirācikīrṣita tvāt iti yaḥ tu manyate yaḥ eva ubhaya niścita vādī sa pramāṇam dūṣaṇam vā na anyatara prasiddha saṃdigdha vācī iti tena api laukikīm vyavasthām anurudhyamānena anumāne yathā uktaḥ eva nyāyaḥ abhyupeyaḥ 
[11,iv_11,vi]	tathā hi na ubhaya prasiddhena vā āgamena bādhā kim tarhi sva prasiddhena api sva artha anumāne tu sarvatra sva prasiddhiḥ eva garīyasī na ubhaya prasiddhiḥ atas eva tarka lakṣaṇa abhidhānam niṣprayojanam yathāsva prasiddhayā upapattyā buddhaiḥ tad anabhijña vineya jana anugrahāt iti alam prasaṅgena prakṛtam eva vyākhyāsyāmaḥ paratas api na utpadyante bhāvāḥ parābhāvāt eva etat ca na hi svabhāvaḥ bhāvānām pratyaya ādiṣu vidyate 
[11,vii]	iti atra pratipādayiṣyati tatas ca parābhāvāt eva na api paratas utpadyante api ca anyat pratītya yadi nāma paraḥ abhaviṣya jjāyeta tarhi bahulaḥ śikhinaḥ andhakāraḥ sarvasya janma ca bhavet khalu sarvatas ca tulyam paratvam akhile ajanake api yasmāt ityādinā madhyamaka avatārāt paratas utpatti pratiṣedhaḥ avaseyaḥ 
[12,i]	ācārya buddha pālitaḥ tu vyācaṣṭe na paratas utpadyante bhāvāḥ sarvatas sarva saṃbhava prasaṅgāt ācārya bhāva vivekaḥ dūṣaṇam āha tat atra prasaṅga vākya tvāt sādhya sādhana viparyayam kṛtvā svatas ubhayatas ahetutaḥ vai utpadyante bhāvāḥ kutaścid kasyacid utpatteḥ iti prāk pakṣa virodhaḥ anyathā sarvatas sarva saṃbhava prasaṅgāt iti asya sādhana dūṣaṇa anantaḥpāti tvāt asaṃgata artham etat iti etat api asaṃgata artham pūrvam eva pratipādita tvāt dūṣaṇa antar pāti tvāt ca para pratijñāta artha dūṣaṇena iti yat kiṃcid etat iti na punar yatnaḥ āsthīyate 
[12,ii_12,iii]	dvābhyām api na upajāyante bhāvāḥ ubhaya pakṣa abhihita doṣa prasaṅgāt pratyekam utpāda asāmarthyāt ca vakṣyati hi syāt ubhābhyām kṛtam duḥkham syāt ekaika kṛtam yadi iti ahetutaḥ api na utpadyante hetau asati kāryam ca kāraṇam ca na vidyate iti vakṣyamāṇa doṣa prasaṅgāt gṛhyeta na eva ca jagat yadi hetu śūnyam syāt yadvat eva gaganotpala varṇa gandhau ityādi doṣa prasaṅgāt ca 
[12,iv]	ācārya buddha pālitaḥ tu āha ahetutaḥ na utpadyante bhāvāḥ sadā ca sarvatas ca sarva saṃbhava prasaṅgāt atra ācārya bhāva vivekaḥ dūṣaṇam āha atra api prasaṅga vākya tvāt yadi viparīta sādhya sādhana vyakti vākya arthaḥ iṣyate tadā etat uktam bhavati hetutaḥ utpadyante bhāvāḥ kadācid kutaścid kasyacid utpatteḥ ārambha sāphalyāt ca sā iyam vyākhyā na yuktā prāc ukta doṣāt iti tat etat ayuktam pūrva udita parihārāt iti apare 
[12,v_13,i]	yat ca api īśvara ādīnām upasaṃgraha artham tadā api na yuktam īśvara ādīnām sva para ubhaya pakṣeṣu yathā abhyupagamam antarbhāvāt iti tasmāt prasādhitam etat na asti utpādaḥ iti utpāda asaṃbhavāt ca siddhaḥ anutpāda ādi viśiṣṭa pratītyasamutpādaḥ iti atra āha yadi evam anutpāda ādi viśiṣṭaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ vyavasthitaḥ bhavadbhiḥ yat tarhi bhagavatā uktam avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ avidyā nirodhāt saṃskāra nirodhaḥ iti tathā anityāḥ ca bata saṃskārāḥ utpāda vyaya dharmiṇaḥ utpadya hi nirudhyante teṣām vyupaśamaḥ sukhaḥ 
[13,ii]	tathā utpādāt vā tathāgatānām anutpādāt vā tathāgatānām sthitā eva eṣā dharmāṇām dharmatā ekaḥ dharmaḥ sattva sthitaye yat uta catvāraḥ āhārāḥ dvau dharmau lokam pālayataḥ hrīḥ ca apatrāpyam ca ityādi tathā para lokāt iha āgamanam iha lokāt ca para loka gamanam iti evam nirodha ādi viśiṣṭaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ deśitaḥ bhagavatā sa katham na virudhyate iti yatas evam nirodha ādayaḥ pratītyasamutpādasya upalabhyante atas eva idam madhyamaka śāstram praṇītam ācāryeṇa neya nīta artha sūtra anta vibhāga upadarśana artham tatra ye ete pratītyasamutpādasya utpāda ādayaḥ uktāḥ na te vigata avidyā timirān āsrava viṣaya svabhāva apekṣayā kim tarhi avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana jñāna viṣaya apekṣayā 
[13,iii]	tattva darśana apekṣayā tu uktam bhagavatā etat hi bhikṣavaḥ paramam satyam yat uta amoṣa dharma nirvāṇam sarva saṃskārāḥ ca mṛṣā moṣa dharmāṇaḥ iti tathā na asti atra tathatā vā avitatha tā vā moṣa dharmaka mapi etat pralopa dharmakam api etat mṛṣā api etat māyā iyam bāla lāpinī iti tathā phena piṇḍa upamam rūpam vedanā budbuda upamā marīci sadṛśī saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ kadalī nibhāḥ māyā upamam ca vijñānam uktam āditya bandhunā iti evam dharmān vīkṣamāṇaḥ bhikṣuḥ ārabdha vīryavān divā vā yadi vā rātrau saṃprajānan pratismṛtaḥ pratividhyet padam śāntam saṃskāra upaśamam śivam iti nirātmaka tvāt ca dharmāṇām ityādi 
[13,iv_13,v]	yasya evam deśanābhiprāya anabhijña tayā saṃdehaḥ syāt kā hi atra deśanā tattva arthā kā nu khalu ābhiprāyikī iti yaḥ ca api manda buddhi tayā neyārthām deśanām nīta arthām avagacchati tayoḥ ubhayoḥ api vineya janayoḥ ācāryaḥ yukti āgamābhyām saṃśaya mithyā jñāna apākaraṇa artham śāstram idam ārabdhavān tatra na svatas ityādinā yuktiḥ upavarṇitā 
[13,vi_14,i]	tat mṛṣā moṣa dharma yat bhagavān iti abhāṣata sarve ca moṣa dharmāṇaḥ saṃskārāḥ tena te mṛṣā pūrvā prajñāyate koṭiḥ na iti uvāca mahā muniḥ saṃsāraḥ anavara agraḥ hi na asti ādiḥ na api paścimam kātyāyanau avāde ca asti na asti iti ca ubhayam pratiṣiddham bhagavatā bhāva abhāva vibhāvinā ityādinā āgamaḥ varṇitaḥ uktam ca ārya akṣayam atisūtre 
[14,ii_14,iii]	katame sūtrāntāḥ neyārthāḥ katame nīta arthāḥ ye sūtrāntāḥ mārgavatārāya nirdiṣṭāḥ ime ucyanteḥ neyārthāḥ ye sūtrāntāḥ phala avatārāya nirdiṣṭāḥ ime ucyante neyārthāḥ yāvat ye sūtrāntāḥ śūnyatā nimitta apraṇihita anabhisaṃskāra ajāta anutpāda abhāva nirātmaniḥ sattva nirjīvaniḥ pudgalāsvāmika vimokṣa mukhāḥ nirdiṣṭāḥ te ucyante nīta arthāḥ iyam ucyate bhadanta śāradvatī putra nīta artha sūtra anta pratiśaraṇa tā na neyārtha sūtra anta pratiśaraṇa tā iti tathā ca ārya samādhi rāja sūtre nīta artha sūtra anta viśeṣa jānati yathā upadiṣṭā sugatena śūnyatā yasmin punar pudgala sattva pūruṣāḥ neyārthataḥ jānati sarva dharmān tasmāt utpāda ādi deśanām mṛṣā arthām pratipādayitum pratītyasamutpāda anudarśanam ārabdhavān ācāryaḥ 
[14,iv]	nanu ca utpāda ādīnām abhāve sati yadi sarva dharmāṇām mṛṣā tva pratipādana artham idam ārabdhavān ācāryaḥ nanu evam sati yat mṛṣā na tat asti iti na santi akuśalāni karmāṇi tad abhāvāt na santi durgatayaḥ na santi kuśalāni karmāṇi tad abhāvāt na santi sugatayaḥ sugati durgati asaṃbhavāt ca na asti saṃsāraḥ iti sarva ārambha vaiyarthyam eva sthāt ucyate saṃvṛti satya vyapekṣayā lokasya idaṃsatya abhiniveśasya pratipakṣa bhāvena mṛṣārtha tā bhāvānām pratipādyate asmābhiḥ na eva tu āryāḥ kṛta kāryāḥ kiṃcid upalabhante yat mṛṣā amṛṣā vā syāt iti api ca yena hi sarva dharmāṇām mṛṣā tvam parijñātam kim tasya karmāṇi santi saṃsāraḥ vā asti na ca api asau kasyacid dharmassya astitvam nāstitvam vā upalabhate yathā uktam bhagavatā ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre 
[14,v]	cittam hi kāśyapa parigaveṣyamāṇam na labhyate yat na labhyate tat na upalabhyate yat na upalabhyate tat na eva atītam na anāgatam na pratyutpannam yat na eva atītam na anāgatam na pratyutpannam tasya na asti svabhāvaḥ yasya na asti svabhāvaḥ tasya na asti utpādaḥ yasya na asti utpādaḥ tasya na asti nirodhaḥ iti vistaraḥ 
[15,i_15,ii]	yaḥ tu viparyāsa anugamāt mṛṣā tvam na avagacchati pratītya bhāvānā svabhāvam abhiniviśate sa dharmeṣu idaṃsatyā abhiniveśāt abhiniviṣṭaḥ san karmāṇi api karoti saṃsāre api saṃsarati viparyāsa avasthita tvāt na bhavyaḥ nirvāṇam adhigantum kim punar mṛṣā svabhāvāḥ api padārthāḥ saṃkleśa vyavadāna nibandhanam bhavanti tat yathā māyā āyuvatiḥ tad svabhāva anabhijñānām tathāgata nirmitaḥ ca upacita kuśala mūlānām uktam hi dṛḍha adhyāśaya paripṛcchā sūtre 
[15,iii_15,vii]	tat yathā kula putra māyā ākāra nāṭake pratyupasthite māyā kāra nirmitām striyam dṛṣṭvā kaścid rāga parīta cittāḥ parṣad śāradya bhayena utthāya āsanāt apakrāmet saḥ apakramya tām eva striyam aśubhataḥ manasikuryāt anityataḥ duḥkhataḥ śūnyataḥ anātmataḥ manasikuryāt iti vistaraḥ vinaye ca yantra kāra kāritā yantra yuvatiḥ sadbhūta yuvati śūnyā sadbhūta yuvati rūpeṇa pratibhāsate tasya ca citrakārasya kāma rāga āspadībhūtā tathā mṛṣā svabhāvāḥ api bhāvāḥ bālānām saṃkleśa vyavadāna nibandhanam bhavanti tathā ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre atha khalu tāni pañca mātrāṇi bhikṣu śatāni bhagavataḥ dharma deśa nāmanavataranti anavagāhamānāni anadhimucyamānāni utthāya āsanebhyaḥ prakrāntāni atha bhagavān tasyām velāyām yena mārgeṇa ete bhikṣavaḥ gacchanti sma tasmin mārge dvau bhikṣū nirmimīte sma 
[15,viii^1]	atha tāni pañca bhikṣu śatāni yena mārgeṇa tau dvau bhikṣū nirmitakau tena upasaṃkrāmanti sma upasaṃkramya tau avocan kutra āyuṣmantau gamiṣyathaḥ nirmitakau avocatām gamiṣyāvaḥ āvām araṇya āyataneṣu tatra dhyāna sukha sparśa vihāraiḥ vihariṣyāvaḥ yam hi bhagavān dharmam deśayati tam āvām na avatarāvaḥ na avagāhāvahe na adhimucyāmahe uttrasya avaḥ saṃtrāsam āpadyāvahe atha tāni pañca bhikṣu śatāni etat avocan vayam api āyuṣmantaḥ bhagavataḥ dharma deśanām na avatarāmaḥ na avagāhāmahe na adhimucyāmahe uttrasyāmaḥ saṃtrasyāmaḥ saṃtrāsam āpadyāmahe tena vayam araṇya āyataneṣu dhyāna sukha sparśa vihāraiḥ vihariṣyāmaḥ nirmitakau avocatām tena hi āyuṣmantaḥ saṃgāsyāmaḥ na vivadiṣyāmaḥ avivāda paramāḥ hi śramaṇasya dharmāḥ kasya āyuṣmantaḥ prahāṇāya pratipannāḥ tāni avocan rāga dveṣa mohānām prahāṇāya vayam pratipannāḥ nirmitakau avocatām kim punar āyuṣmatām saṃvidyante rāga dveṣa mohāḥ yān kṣapayiṣyatha 
[15,viii^2]	tāni avocan na te adhyātmam na bahirdhāḥ na ubhayam antareṇa upalabhyante na api te aparikalpitāḥ utpadyante nirmitakau avocatām tena hi āyuṣmantaḥ mā kalpayata mā vikalpayata yadā ca āyuṣmantaḥ na kalpayiṣyatha na vikalpayiṣyatha tadā na raṃkṣyatha na viraṃkṣyatha yaḥ ca na raktaḥ na viraktaḥ sa śāntaḥ iti ucyate śīlam āyuṣmantaḥ na saṃsarati na parinirvāti samādhiḥ prajñā vimuktiḥ vimukti jñāna darśanam āyuṣmantaḥ na saṃsarati na parinirvāti ebhiḥ ca āyuṣmantaḥ dharmaiḥ nirvāṇam sūcyate ete ca dharmāḥ śūnyāḥ prakṛti viviktāḥ prajahīta etām āyuṣmantaḥ saṃjñām yat uta parinirvāṇam iti mā ca saṃjñāyām saṃjñā kārṣṭa mā ca saṃjñāyām saṃjñām parijñāsiṣṭa yaḥ hi saṃjñāyām saṃjñām parijānāti saṃjñā bandhanam eva asya tat bhavati saṃjñā vedayita nirodha samāpattim āyuṣmantaḥ samāpadyadhvam saṃjñā vedayita nirodha samāpatti samāpannasya bhikṣoḥ na asti uttarīkaraṇīyam iti vadāvaḥ 
[16,i_16,ii^1]	atha teṣām pañcānām bhikṣu śatānām anupādāya āśravebhyaḥ cittāni vimuktāni abhūvan tāni vimukta cittāni yena bhagavān tena upasaṃkrāntāni upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā abhivandya ekānte nyasīdan atha āyuṣmān subhūtiḥ tān bhikṣūn etat avocat kutra āyuṣmantaḥ gatāḥ kutas vā āgatāḥ te avocan na kvacid gamanāya na kutaścid āgamanāya bhadanta subhūte bhagavatā dharmaḥ deśitaḥ āha kaḥ nāma āyuṣma tām śāstā āhuḥ yaḥ na utpannaḥ na parinirvāsyati āha katham yuṣmābhiḥ dharmaḥ śrutaḥ āhuḥ na bandhanāya na mokṣāya āha kena yūyam vinītāḥ āhuḥ yasya na kāyaḥ na cittam āha katham yūyam prayuktāḥ āhuḥ na avidyā prahāṇāya na vidyā utpādanāya āha kasya yūyam śrāvakāḥ āhuḥ yena na prāptam nābhisaṃbuddham āha ke yuṣmākam sabrahmacāriṇaḥ āhuḥ ye traidhātuke na upavicaranti āha kiyat cireṇa āyuṣmantaḥ parinirvāsyanti āhuḥ yadā tathāgata nirmitāḥ parinirvāsyanti āha kṛtam yuṣmābhiḥ karaṇīyam āhuḥ aham kāramamakāra parijñānataḥ 
[16,ii^2]	āha kṣīṇāḥ yuṣmākam kleśāḥ āhuḥ atyanta kṣayāt sarva dharmāṇām āha dharṣitaḥ yuṣmābhiḥ māraḥ āhuḥ skandha māra an upalambhāt āha dharṣitaḥ yuṣmābhiḥ māraḥ āhuḥ skandha māra an upalambhāt āha paricaritaḥ yuṣmābhiḥ śāstā āhuḥ na kāyena na vācā na manasā āha viśodhitā yuṣmābhiḥ dakṣiṇīya bhūmiḥ āhuḥ agrāhataḥ apratigrāhataḥ āha uttīrṇaḥ yuṣmābhiḥ saṃsāraḥ āhuḥ anucchedataḥ aśāśvatatas āha pratipannā yuṣmābhiḥ dakṣiṇīya bhūmiḥ āhuḥ sarva grāha vinirmuktitaḥ āha kiṃgāminaḥ āyuṣmantaḥ āhuḥ yaṃgāminaḥ tathāgata nirmitāḥ iti hi āyuṣmataḥ subhūteḥ paripṛcchataḥ teṣām bhikṣūṇām prativisarjayatām tasyām parṣadi aṣṭānām bhikṣu śatānām anupādāya āśravebhyaḥ cittāni vimuktāni dvātriṃśataḥ ca prāṇi sahasrāṇām virajaḥ vigata malam dharma cakṣuḥ viśuddham iti 
[16,iii_16,v]	iti evam mṛṣā svabhāvābhyām tathāgata nirmitābhyām bhikṣubhyām pañcānām bhikṣu śatānām vyavadāna nibandhanam kṛtam iti uktam ca ārya vajramaṇḍāyām dhāraṇyām tat yathā mañjuśrīḥ kāṇḍam ca pratītya mathanīm ca pratītya puruṣasya hasta vyāyāmam ca pratītya dhūmaḥ prādurbhavati iti agniḥ abhinirvartate sa ca agni saṃtāpaḥ na kāṇḍa saṃniśritaḥ na mathanī saṃniśritaḥ na puruṣa hasta vyāyāma saṃniśritaḥ evam eva mañjuśrīḥ asat viparyāsa mohitasya puruṣa pudgalasya utpadyate rāga paridāhaḥ dveṣa paridāhaḥ moha paridāhaḥ sa ca paridāhaḥ na adhyātmam na bahirdhā na ubhayam antareṇa sthitaḥ 
[16,vi]	api tu mañjuśrīḥ yat ucyate mohaḥ iti tat kena kāraṇena ucyate mohaḥ iti atyanta muktaḥ hi mañjuśrīḥ sarva dharmaiḥ mohaḥ tena ucyate mohaḥ iti tathā naraka mukhāḥ mañjuśrīḥ sarva dharmāḥ idam dhāraṇī padam āha katham bhagavan idam dhāraṇī padam āha narakāḥ mañjuśrīḥ bāla pṛthagjanaiḥ asat viparyāsa viṭhapitāḥ sva vikalpa saṃbhūtāḥ āha kutra bhagavat narakāḥ samavasaranti bhagavān āha ākāśa samavasaraṇāḥ mañjuśrīḥ narakāḥ tat kim manyase mañjuśrīḥ sva vikalpa saṃbhūtāḥ narakāḥ uta svabhāva saṃbhūtāḥ āha sva vikalpena eva bhagavan sarva bāla pṛthagjanām naraka tiryagyoni yama lokam saṃjānanti te ca asat samāropeṇa duḥkhām vedanām vedayanti duḥkham anubhavanti triṣu api apāyeṣu 
[17,i]	yathā ca aham bhagavat narakān paśyāmi tathā nārakam duḥkham tat yathā bhagavan kaścid eva puruṣaḥ suptaḥ svapna antara gataḥ naraka gatam ātmānam saṃjānīte sa tatra kvathitāyām saṃprajvalitāyām aneka pauruṣāyām loha kumbhyām prakṣiptam ātmānam saṃjānīyāt sa tatra kharām kaṭukām tīvrām duḥkhām vedanām vedayet sa tatra mānasam paridāham saṃjānīyāt uttraset saṃtrāsam āpadyeta sa tatra pratibuddhaḥ samānaḥ aho duḥkham aho duḥkham iti krandet śocet paridevet atha tasya mitra jñāti sālohitāḥ paripṛccheyuḥ kena tat te duḥkham iti sa tān mitra jñāti sa ālohitān evam vadet nairayikam duḥkham anubhūtam sa tān ākrośet paribhāṣet aham ca nāma nairayikam duḥkham anubhavāmi yūyam ca me uttari paripṛcchatha kena etat tava duḥkham iti atha te mitra jñāti sa ālohitāḥ tam puruṣam evam vadeyuḥ mā bhairmoḥ puruṣa suptaḥ hi tvam na tvam itas gṛhāt kvacid nirgataḥ tasya punar api smṛti rutpadyate suptaḥ aham abhūvam vitatham etat mayā parikalpitam iti sa punar api saumanasyam pratilabhate 
[17,ii]	tat yathā bhagavan sa puruṣaḥ asat samāropeṇa suptaḥ svapna antara gataḥ naraka gatam ātmānam saṃjānīyāt evam eva bhagavan sarva bāla pṛthagjanāḥ asat bhāga paryavanaddhāḥ strī nimittam kalpayanti te strī nimittam kalpayitvā tābhiḥ sārdham ramamāṇam ātmānam saṃjānanti tasya bāla pṛtha janasya evam bhavati aham puruṣaḥ iyam strī mama eṣā strī tasya tena cchanda rāga paryavasthitena cittena bhoga paryeṣṭim cittam krāmayanti sa tatonidānam kalaha vigraha vivādam saṃjanayati tasya praduṣṭa indriyasya vairam saṃjāyate sa tena saṃjñā viparyāsena kālagataḥ samānaḥ bahūni kalpa sahasrāṇi narakeṣu duḥkhām vedanām vedayamānam ātmānam saṃjānāti 
[17,iii]	tat yathā bhagavan tasya puruṣasya mitra jñāti sa ālohitāḥ evam vadanti mā bhaiḥ mā bhaiḥ bho puruṣa suptaḥ hi tvam na tvam itas gṛhyat kutaścid nirgataḥ iti evam eva buddhāḥ bhagavantaḥ catur viparyāsa viparyastānām sattvānām evam dharmam deśayanti na atra strī na puruṣaḥ na sattvaḥ na jīvaḥ na puruṣaḥ na pudgalaḥ vitathāḥ ime sarva dharmāḥ asantaḥ ime sarva dharmāḥ viṭhapitāḥ ime sarva dharmāḥ māyā upamāḥ ime sarva dharmāḥ svapna upamāḥ ime sarva dharmāḥ nirmita upamāḥ ime sarva dharmāḥ udaka candra upamāḥ ime sarva dharmāḥ iti vistaraḥ te imām tathāgatasya dharma deśanām śrutvā vigata rāgān sarva dharmān paśyanti vigata mohān sarva dharmān paśyanti asvabhāvān anāvaraṇān te ākāśa sthitena cetasā kālam kurvanti te kālagatāḥ samānāḥ nirupadhi śeṣe nirvāṇa dhātau parinirvānti evam aham bhagavat narakān paśyāmi iti 
[18,i]	uktam ca ārya upāli paripṛcchāyām bhaya darśita nairayikam me sattva sahasra sa vejita na eke na ca vidyati kaściha sattva yaḥ cyutu gacchati ghoram apāyam na ca kāraku kāraṇa santi yehi kṛtāḥ asi tomara śastrāḥ kalpa vaśena tu paśyati tatra kāyi patanti apāyita śastrāḥ citra manorama sajjita puṣpāḥ svarṇa vimāna jalanti manojñāḥ teṣu api kāraku na astiha kaści te api ca sthāpita kalpa vaśena kalpa vaśena vikalpitu lokaḥ saṃjña gaheṇa vikalpitu bālaḥ saḥ ca gahaḥ agahaḥ asa bhūtaḥ māya marīci samāḥ hi vikalpāḥ 
[18,ii_18,iv]	tat evam ete asvabhāvāḥ bhāvāḥ sva viparyāsa viṭhapitā bālānām saṃkleśa hetavaḥ bhavanti saṃsāre iti sthitam yathā ca mṛṣā svabhāvānām padārthānām saṃkleśa vyavadāna hetu tvam tathā madhyamaka avatārāt vistareṇa avaseyam atra āha yadi svatas paratas ubhayatas ahetutaḥ ca na asti bhāvānām utpādaḥ tatra katham avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ iti uktam bhagavatā ucyate saṃvṛtiḥ eva na tattvam 
[18,v]	kim saṃvṛteḥ vyavasthānam vaktavyam idaṃpratyaya tā mātreṇa saṃvṛteḥ siddhiḥ abhyupagamyate na tu pakṣa catuṣṭaya abhyupagamena sa svabhāva vāda prasaṅgāt tasya ca ayukta tvāt idaṃpratyaya tā mātra abhyupagame hi sati hetu phalayoḥ anyonya apekṣa tvāt na asti svābhāvikī siddhiḥ iti na asti sa svabhāva vādaḥ atas eva uktam svayam kṛtam para kṛtam dvābhyām kṛtam ahetukam tārkikaiḥ iṣyate duḥkham tvayā tu uktam pratītyajam 
[19,i_19,iii]	iha api vakṣyati pratītya kārakaḥ karma tam pratītya ca kārakam karma pravartate na anyat paśyāmaḥ siddhi kāraṇam iti bhagavatā api etāvat mātram eva uktam tatra ayam dharma saṃketaḥ yat uta asmin sati idam bhavati asya utpādāt idam utpadyate yat uta avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃskāra pratyayam vijñānam ityādi 
[19,iv]	atra kecid paricodayanti anutpannāḥ bhāvāḥ iti kim ayam pramāṇa jaḥ niścayaḥ uta apramāṇa jaḥ tatra yadi pramāṇa jaḥ iṣyate tadā idam vaktavyam kati pramāṇāni kiṃlakṣaṇāni kiṃviṣayāṇi kim svatas utpannāni kim paratas ubhayatas ahetutaḥ vā iti atha apramāṇa jaḥ sa na yuktaḥ pramāṇa adhīna tvāt prameya adhigamasya anadhigataḥ hi arthaḥ na vinā pramāṇaiḥ adhigantum śakyate iti pramāṇa abhāvāt artha adhigama abhāve sati kutas ayam samyak niḥ cayaḥ iti na yuktam etat aniṣpannāḥ bhāvāḥ iti yatas vā ayam niścayaḥ bhavataḥ anutpannāḥ bhāvāḥ iti bhaviṣyati tatas eva mama api sarva bhāvāḥ santi iti yathā ca ayam te niścayaḥ anutpannāḥ sarva dharmāḥ iti tathā eva mama api sarva bhāva utpattiḥ bhaviṣyati atha te na asti niścayaḥ anutpannāḥ sarva bhāvāḥ iti tadā svayam aniścitasya para pratyāyana asaṃbhavāt śāstra ārambha vaiyarthyam eva iti santi apratiṣiddhāḥ sarva bhāvāḥ iti 
[19,v]	ucyate yadi kaścid niścayaḥ nāma asmākam syāt sa pramāṇa jaḥ vā syāt apramāṇa jaḥ vā na tu asti kim kāraṇam iha aniścaya saṃbhave sati syāt tad pratipakṣaḥ tad apekṣaḥ niścayaḥ yadā tu aniścayaḥ eva tāvat asmākam na asti tadā kutas tad viruddha aviruddhaḥ niścayaḥ syāt saṃbandhi antara nirapekṣa tvāt khara viṣāṇasya hrasva dīrgha tāvat yadā ca evam niścayasya abhāvaḥ tadā kasya prasiddhayartham pramāṇāni parikalpayiṣyāmaḥ kutas vā eṣām saṃkhyā lakṣaṇam viṣayaḥ vā bhaviṣyati svatas paratas ubhayatas ahetutaḥ vā samutpattiḥ iti sarvam etat na vaktavyam asmābhiḥ 
[19,vi]	yadi evam niścayaḥ na asti sarvatas katham punar idam niścita rūpam vākyam upalabhyate bhavatām na svatas na api paratas na dvābhyām na api ahetutaḥ bhāvāḥ bhavanti iti ucyate niścitam idam vākyam lokasya sva prasiddhayā eva upapattyā nāryāṇām kim khalu āryāṇām upapattiḥ na asti kena etat uktam asti vā na asti vā iti parama arthaḥ hi āryāṇām tūṣṇīṃbhāvaḥ tatas kutas tatra prapañca saṃbhavaḥ yat upapattiḥ anupapattiḥ vā syāt 
[19,vii^1]	yadi hi āryāḥ upapattim na varṇayanti kena khalu idānīm parama artham lokam bodhayiṣyanti na khalu āryāḥ loka saṃvyavahāreṇa upapattim varṇayanti kim tu lokataḥ eva yā prasiddha upapattiḥ tām para avabodha artham abhyupetya tayā eva lokam bodhayanti yathā eva hi vidyamānām api śarīra aśuci tām viparyāsa anugatāḥ rāgiṇaḥ na upalabhante śubha ākāram ca abhūtam adhyāropya parikliśyante teṣām vairāgya artham tathāgata nirmitaḥ devaḥ vā śubha saṃjñayā prāk pracchāditān kāya doṣān upavarṇayet santi asmin kāye keśāḥ ityādinā te ca tasyāḥ śubha saṃjñāyāḥ vimuktāḥ vairāgyam āsādayeyuḥ 
[19,vii^2]	evam iha api āryaiḥ sarvathā api anupalabhyamāna ātmakam bhāvānām avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana tayā viparītam svabhāvam adhyāropya kvacid ca kaṃcid viśeṣam atitarām parikliśyanti pṛthagjanāḥ tān idānīm āryāḥ tad prasiddhayā eva upapattyā paribodhayanti yathā vidyamānasya ghaṭasya na mṛd ādibhyaḥ utpādaḥ iti abhyupetam evam utpādāt pūrvam vidyamānasya vidyamāna tvāt na asti utpādaḥ iti avasīyatām yathā ca para bhūtebhyaḥ jvālā aṅgāra ādibhyaḥ aṅkurasya utpattiḥ na asti iti abhyupetam evam vivakṣitebhyaḥ api bīja ādibhyaḥ na asti iti avasīyatām 
[20,i]	atha api syāt anubhavaḥ eṣaḥ asmākam iti etat api uktam yasmāt anubhavaḥ eṣa mṛṣā anubhava tvāt taimirika dvi candra ādi anubhava vat iti tatas ca anubhavasya api sādhya sama tvāt tena pratyavasthānam na yuktam iti tasmāt anutpannāḥ bhāvāḥ iti evam tāvat viparīta svarūpa adhyāra upapratipakṣeṇa prathama prakaraṇa ārambhaḥ idānīm kvacid yaḥ kaścid viśeṣaḥ adhyāropitaḥ tad viśeṣa apākaraṇa artham śeṣa prakaraṇa ārambhaḥ gantṛ gantavya gamana ādikaḥ api niravaśeṣaḥ viśeṣaḥ na asti pratītyasamutpādasya iti pratipādana artham 
[20,ii]	atha syāt eṣaḥ eva pramāṇa premeya vyavahāraḥ laukikaḥ asmābhiḥ śāstreṇa anuvarṇitaḥ iti tad anuvarṇanasya tarhi phalam vācyam ku tārkikaiḥ sa nāśitaḥ viparīta lakṣaṇa abhidhānena tasya asmābhiḥ samyak lakṣaṇam uktam iti ced etat api ayuktam yadi hi kutārkikaiḥ viparīta lakṣaṇa praṇayanāt kṛtam lakṣya vaiparītyam lokasya syāt tad artham prayatna sāphalyam syāt na ca etat evam iti vyarthaḥ eva ārya prayatnaḥ iti 
[20,iii_20,iv]	api ca yadi pramāṇa adhīnaḥ prameya adhigamaḥ tāni pramāṇāni kena paricchidyante ityādinā vigraha vyāvartanyām vihitaḥ doṣaḥ tad aparihārāt samyak lakṣaṇa dyotaka tvam api na asti kim ca yadi sva sāmānya lakṣaṇa dvaya anurodhena pramāṇa dvayam uktam yasya tad lakṣaṇa dvayam kim tat lakṣyam asti atha na asti yadi asti tadā tad aparam prameyam asti iti katham pramāṇa dvayam atha na asti lakṣyam tadā lakṣaṇam api nirāśrayam na asti iti katham pramāṇa dvayam vakṣyati hi lakṣaṇa asaṃpravṛttau ca na lakṣyam upapadyate lakṣyasya anupapattau ca lakṣaṇasya api asaṃbhavaḥ iti 
[20,v_20,vi]	atha syāt na lakṣyate anena iti lakṣaṇam kim tarhi kṛtyalyuṭaḥ bahulam iti karmaṇi lyuṭam kṛtvā lakṣyate tat iti lakṣaṇam evam api tena etasya lakṣyamāṇa tva asaṃbhava ādyena etat lakṣyate tasya karaṇasya karmaṇaḥ artha antara tvāt saḥ eva doṣaḥ atha syāt jñānasya karaṇa tvāt tasya ca sva lakṣaṇa antarbhāvāt ayam adoṣaḥ iti ucyate iha bhāvānām anyāsa ādhāraṇam ātmīyam yat svarūpam tat sva lakṣaṇam tat yathā pṛthivyāḥ kāṭhinyam vedanāyāḥ viṣaya anubhavaḥ vijñānasya viṣaya prativijñaptiḥ tena hi tat lakṣyate iti kṛtvā prasiddha anugatām ca vyutpattim avadhūya karma sādhanam abhyupagacchati vijñānasya ca karaṇa bhāvam pratipadyamānena iti uktam bhavati sva lakṣaṇasya eva karma tā sva lakṣaṇa antarasya karaṇa bhāvaḥ ca iti tatra yadi vijñāna sva lakṣaṇam karaṇam tasya vyatiriktena karmaṇā bhavitavyam iti saḥ eva doṣaḥ 
[21,i]	atha syāt yat pṛthivī ādi gatam kāṭhinya ādikam vijñāna gamyam tat tasya karma asti eva tat ca sva lakṣaṇa avyatiriktam iti evam tarhi vijñāna sva lakṣaṇasya karma tva abhāvāt prameya tvam na syāt karma rūpasya eva sva lakṣaṇasya prameya tvāt tatas ca dvividham prameyam sva lakṣaṇam sāmānya lakṣaṇam ca iti etat viśeṣya vaktavyam kiṃcid sva lakṣaṇam prameyam yat lakṣyate iti evam vyapadiśyate kiṃcid aprameyam yat lakṣyate anena iti vyapadiśyate iti atha tat api karma sādhanam tadā tasya anyena karaṇena bhavitavyam jñāna antarasya karaṇa bhāva parikalpanāyām anavasthā doṣaḥ ca āpadyate 
[21,ii]	atha manyase sva saṃvittiḥ asti tatas tayā sva saṃvityā grahaṇāt karmatāyā satyām asti eva prameya antarbhāvaḥ iti ucyate vistareṇa madhyamaka avatāre sva saṃvitti niṣedhāt sva lakṣaṇam sva lakṣaṇa antareṇa lakṣyate tat api sva saṃvittyā iti na yujyate api ca tat api nāma jñānam sva lakṣaṇa vyatirekeṇa asiddheḥ asaṃbhavāt lakṣya abhāve nirāśraya lakṣaṇa pravṛtti asaṃbhavāt sarvathā na asti iti kutas sva saṃvittiḥ tathā ca uktam ārya ratna cūḍa paripṛcchāyām 
[21,iii]	sa cittam asam anupaśyan citta dhārām paryeṣate kutaścittasya utpattiḥ iti tasya evam bhavati ālambane sati cittam utpadyate tat kim anyat ālambanam anyat cittam atha yat eva ālambanam tat eva cittam yadi tāvat anyat ālambanam anyat cittam tadā dvi citta tā bhaviṣyati atha yat eva ālambanam tat eva cittam tat katham cittena cittam samanupaśyati na ca cittam cittam samanupaśyati tat yathā api nāma tayā eva asidhārayā sā eva asi dhārā na śakyate chettum na tena eva aṅgulī agreṇa tat eva aṅgulī agram śakyate spraṣṭum evam eva na tena eva cittena tat eva cittam śakyam draṣṭum tasya evam yoniśas prayuktasya yā cittasya anavasthāna tā anuccheda aśāśvata tā na kūṭastha tā na ahetukī na pratyaya viruddhāḥ na tatas na anyatas na sā eva na anyā tām citta dhārām citta latām citta dharma tām cittān avasthita tām citta apracāra tām citta adṛśyatām citta sva lakṣaṇa tām tathā jānāti tathā paśyati yathā tathatām na ca nirodhayati tām ca citta viveka tām tathā prajānāti tathā paśyati iyam kula putra bodhisattvasya citte citta an upaśyanā smṛti upasthānam iti 
[21,iv_21,v]	tat evam na asti sva saṃvittiḥ tad abhāvāt kim kena lakṣyate kim ca bhedena vā tad lakṣaṇam lakṣyāt syāt abhedena vā tatra yadi tāvat bhedena tadā lakṣyāt bhinna tvāt alakṣaṇa vat lakṣaṇam api na lakṣaṇam lakṣaṇāt ca bhinna tvāt alakṣya vat lakṣyam api na lakṣyam tathā lakṣyāt bhinna tvāt lakṣaṇasya lakṣaṇa nirapekṣam lakṣyam syāt tatas ca na tat lakṣyam lakṣaṇa nirapekṣa tvāt kha puṣpa vat atha abhinne lakṣya lakṣaṇe tadā lakṣaṇāt avyatiriktattvāt lakṣaṇa sva ātma vat vihīyate lakṣyasya lakṣyatā lakṣyāt ca avyatirikta tvāt lakṣya sva ātma vat lakṣaṇam api na lakṣaṇa svabhāvam yathā ca uktam lakṣyāt lakṣaṇam anyat ced syāt tat lakṣyam alakṣaṇam tayoḥ abhāvaḥ ananya tve vispaṣṭam kathitam tvayā iti 
[22,i_22,ii]	na ca vinā tattva anya tvena lakṣya lakṣaṇa siddhau anyā gatiḥ asti tathā ca vakṣyati ekībhāvena vā siddhiḥ nānā bhāvena vā yayoḥ na vidyate tayoḥ siddhiḥ katham nu khalu vidyate iti athavā ucyate avācya tayā siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced na etat evam avācya tā hi nāma paraspara vibhāga parijñāna abhāve sati bhavati yatra ca vibhāga parijñānam na asti tatra idam lakṣaṇam idam lakṣyam iti viśeṣataḥ pariccheda asaṃbhave sati dvayoḥ api abhāvaḥ eva iti tasmāt avācyatayā api na asti siddhiḥ 
[22,iii_22,iv]	api ca yadi jñānam karaṇam viṣayasya paricchede kaḥ kartā na ca kartāram antareṇa asti karaṇa ādīnām saṃbhavaḥ chidi kriyāyām iva atha cittasya tatra kartṛ tvam parikalpyate tat api na yuktam yasmāt artha mātra darśanam cittasya vyāpāraḥ artha viśeṣa darśanam caitasānām tatra artha dṛṣṭiḥ vijñānam tad viśeṣe tu caitasāḥ iti abhyupagamāt ekasyām hi pradhāna kriyāyām sādhyāyām yathāsvam guṇa kriyā nirvṛtti dvāreṇa aṅgībhāva upagamāt karaṇa ādīnām karaṇa ādi tvam na ca iha jñāna vijñānayoḥ ekā pradhāna kriyā kim tarhi artha mātra paricchittiḥ vijñānasya pradhāna kriyā jñānasya tu artha viśeṣa paricchedaḥ iti na asti jñānasya karaṇa tvam na api cittasya kartṛ tvam tatas ca saḥ eva doṣaḥ atha syāt anātmānaḥ sarva dharmāḥ iti āgamāt kartuḥ sarvathā abhāvāt kartāram antareṇa api vidyate eva kriyā ādi vyavahāraḥ iti etat api na asti āgamasya samyak artha anavadhāraṇāt etat eva uktam madhyamaka avatāre 
[22,v^1]	atha api syāt yathā śilāputrakasya śarīram rāhoḥ śiraḥ iti śarīra śiraḥ vyatirikta viśeṣaṇā saṃbhave api viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ asti evam pṛthivyāḥ sva lakṣaṇam iti sva lakṣaṇa vyatirikta pṛthivī asaṃbhave api bhaviṣyati iti na etat evam atulya tvāt śarīra śiraḥ śabdayohi buddhayā ādi pāṇi ādi vat sahabhāvi padārtha antara sā apekṣatā pravṛttau śarīraśiraḥ śabda mātra ālambanaḥ buddhayupajananaḥ sahacāri padārtha antara sā ākāṅkṣaḥ eva vartate kasya śarīram kasya śiraḥ iti itaraḥ api viśeṣaṇa antaraḥ saṃbandha nirācikīrṣayā śilā putra karāhu viśeṣaṇa dhvaninā laukika saṃketa anuvidhāyinā pratikartuḥ kāṅkṣām apahanti iti yuktam iha tu kāṭhinya ādi vyatirikta pṛthivī ādi asaṃbhave sati na yuktaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ tīrthikaiḥ vyatirikta lakṣya abhyupagamāt tad anurodhena viśeṣaṇa abhidhānam aduṣṭam iti ced na etat evam 
[22,v^2]	na hi tīrthika parikalpitāḥ yukti vidhurāḥ padārthāḥ sva samaye abhyupagantum nyāyyāḥ pramāṇa antara ādeḥ api abhyugama prasaṅgāt api ca pudgala ādi prajñapti vat sa śarīra upādānasya śilāputrakasya upādātuḥ laukika vyavahāra aṅga bhūtasya viśeṣaṇasya avicāra prasiddhasya sadbhāvāt śiraupādānasya ca rāhoḥ upādātuḥ sadbhāvāt ayuktam etat nidarśanam śarīra śiraḥ vyatiriktasya artha antarasya asiddheḥ tanmātrasya upalambhāt siddham eva nidarśanam iti ced na etat evam laukike vyavahāre ittham vicāra apravṛtteḥ avicārataḥ ca laukika padārthānām astitvāt yathā eva hi rūpa ādi vyatirekeṇa vicāryamāṇaḥ ātmā na saṃbhavati api ca loka saṃvṛtyā skandhān upādāya asya astitvam evam rāhu śilā putrakayoḥ api iti na asti nidarśana siddhiḥ 
[23,i]	evam pṛthivī ādīnām yadi api kāṭhinya ādi vyatiriktam vicāryamāṇam lakṣyam na asti lakṣya vyatirekeṇa ca lakṣaṇam nirāśrayam tathā api saṃvṛtiḥ eva iti paraspara apekṣayā tayoḥ siddhayā siddhim vyavasthāpayāṃbabhūvuḥ ācāryāḥ avaśyam ca etat evam abhyupeyam anyathā hi saṃvṛtiḥ upapattyā na viyujyeta tat eva tattvam eva syāt na saṃvṛtiḥ na ca upapattyā vicāryamāṇānām śilā putraka ādīm eva asaṃbhavaḥ kim tarhi vakṣyamāṇayā yuktyā rūpa vedanā ādīnām api na asti saṃbhavaḥ iti teṣām api saṃvṛtyā śilā putraka ādi vanna astitvam āstheyam syāt na ca etat evam iti asat etat 
[23,ii]	atha syāt kim anayā sūkṣma īkṣikayā na eva hi vayam sarva pramāṇa prameya vyavahāram satyam iti ācakṣmahe kim tu loka prasiddhiḥ eṣā amunā nyāyena vyavasthāpyate iti ucyate vayam api evam brūmaḥ kim anayā sūkṣma īkṣikayā laukika vyavahāre avatāritayā tiṣṭhatu tāvat eṣā viparyāsa mātra āsādita ātma bhāva sattākā saṃvṛtiḥ mumukṣūṇām mokṣa āvāhaka kuśala mūla upacaya hetuḥ yāvat na tattva adhigamaḥ iti bhavān tu etām saṃvṛti parama artha satya vibhāga durvidagdha buddhi tayā kvacid upapattim avatārya anyāyataḥ nāśayati saḥ aham saṃvṛti satya vyavasthā vaicakṣaṇyāt laukikaḥ eva pakṣe sthitvā saṃvṛti eka deśa nirākaraṇa upakṣipta upapatti antaram upapatti antareṇa vinivartayan loka vṛddhaḥ iva loka cārāt paribhraśyamānam bhavantam eva nivartayāmi na tu saṃvṛtim tasmāt yadi laukikaḥ vyavahāraḥ tadā avaśyam lakṣaṇa vat lakṣyeṇa api bhavitavyam tatas ca saḥ eva doṣaḥ atha parama arthaḥ tadā lakṣya abhāvāt lakṣaṇa dvayam api na asti iti kutas pramāṇa dvayam 
[23,iii_23,iv]	atha śabdānām evam kriyā kāraka saṃbandha pūrvikā vyutpattiḥ na aṅgīkriyate tat idam ati kaṣṭam taiḥ eva kriyā kāraka saṃbandha pravṛttaiḥ śabdaiḥ bhavān vyavaharati śabda artham kriyā karaṇa ādikam ca na icchati iti aho vataḥ icchā mātra pratibaddha pravṛttiḥ bhavataḥ yadā ca evam prameya dvayam avyavasthitam tadā sva sāmānya lakṣaṇa aviṣaya tvena āgama ādīnām pramāṇa antara tvam kim ca ghaṭaḥ pratyakṣaḥ iti evam ādikasya laukika vyavahārasya asaṃgrahāt anārya vyavahāra abhyupagamāt ca avyāpitā lakṣaṇasya iti na yuktam etat 
[24,i^1]	atha syāt ghaṭa upādāna nīla ādayaḥ pratyakṣāḥ pratyakṣa pramāṇa paricchedya tvāt tatas ca yathā eva kāraṇe kārya upacāram kṛtvā buddhānām sukhaḥ utpādaḥ iti vyapadiśyate evam pratyakṣa nīla ādi nimittakaḥ api ghaṭaḥ kārye kāraṇa upacāram kṛtvā pratyakṣaḥ iti vyapadiśyate na evaṃviṣaye upacāraḥ yuktaḥ utpādaḥ hi loke sukha vyatirekeṇa upalabdhaḥ sa ca saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa svabhāva tvāt aneka duṣkara śata hetu tvāt asukhaḥ eva sa sukhaḥ iti vyapadiśyamānaḥ asaṃbaddhaḥ eva iti evaṃviṣaye yuktaḥ upacāraḥ ghaṭaḥ pratyakṣaḥ iti atra tu na hi ghaṭaḥ nāma kaścid yaḥ apratyakṣaḥ pṛthak upalabdhaḥ yasya upacārāt pratyakṣa tvam syāt 
[24,i^2]	nīla ādi vyatiriktasya ghaṭasya abhāvāt aupacārikam pratyakṣa tvam iti ced evam api sutarām upacāraḥ na yuktaḥ upacaryamāṇasya āśrayasya abhāvāt na hi khara viṣāṇe taikṣṇyam upacaryate api ca loka vyavahāra aṅga bhūtaḥ ghaṭaḥ yadi nīla ādi vyatiriktaḥ na asti iti kṛtvā tasya aupacārikam pratyakṣa tvam parikalpyate nanu evam sati pṛthivī ādi vyatirekeṇa nīla ādikam api na asti iti nīla ādeḥ asi a aupacārikam pratyakṣa tvam kalpyatām yathā uktam rūpa ādi vyatirekeṇa yathā kumbhaḥ na vidyate vāyu ādi vyatirekeṇa tathā rūpam na vidyate iti tasmāt evam ādikasya loka vyavahārasya lakṣaṇena asaṃgrahāt avyāpitā eva lakṣaṇasya iti tattva vid apekṣayā hi pratyakṣa tvam ghaṭa ādīnām nīla ādīnām ca na iṣyate 
[24,ii]	loka saṃvṛtyā tu abhyupagantavyam eva pratyakṣa tvam ghaṭa ādīnām yathā uktam śatake sarve eva ghaṭaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ rūpe dṛṣṭe hi jāyate brūyāt kaḥ tattva vid nāma ghaṭaḥ pratyakṣaḥ iti api etena eva vicāreṇa sugandhi madhuram mṛdu pratiṣedhayitavyāni sarvāṇi uttama buddhinā iti api ca aparokṣa artha vāci tvāt pratyakṣa śabdasya sākṣāt abhimukhaḥ arthaḥ pratyakṣaḥ pratigatam akṣam asmin iti kṛtvā ghaṭa nīla ādīnām aparokṣāṇām pratyakṣa tvam siddham bhavati tad paricchedakasya jñānasya tṛṇa tuṣa agni vat pratyakṣa kāraṇa tvāt pratyakṣa tvam vyapadiśyate yaḥ tu akṣam akṣam prati vartate iti pratyakṣa śabdam vyutpādayati tasya jñānasya indriya aviṣaya tvāt viṣaya viṣaya tvāt ca na yuktā vyutpattiḥ prativiṣayam tu syāt pratyartham iti vā 
[24,iii^1]	atha syāt yathā ubhaya adhīnāyām api vijñāna pravṛtau āśrayasya paṭu manda tā anuvidhānāt vijñānānām tad vikāra vikāri tvāt āśrayeṇa eva vyapadeśaḥ bhavati cakṣuḥ vijñānam iti evam yadi api artham artha prati vartate tathā api akṣamakṣam āśritya vartamānam vijñānam āśrayeṇa vyapadeśāt pratyakṣam iti bhaviṣyati dṛṣṭaḥ hi asādhāraṇena vyapadeśaḥ bherī śabdaḥ yava aṅkuraḥ iti na etat pūrveṇa tulyam tatra hi viṣayeṇa vijñāne vyapadiśyamāne rūpa vijñānam iti evamādinā vijñāna ṣaṭkasya bhedaḥ na upadarśitaḥ syāt manaḥ vijñānasya cakṣuḥ ādi vijñānaiḥ saha eka viṣaya pravṛtta tvāt 
[24,iii^2]	tathā hi nīla ādi vijñāna ṣaṭke vijñānam iti ukte sa ākāṅkṣaḥ eva pratyayāt jāyate kim etat rūpi indriya jam vijñānam āhosvit mānasam iti āśrayeṇa tu vyapadeśe manaḥ vijñānasya cakṣuḥ ādi vijñāna viṣaye pravṛtti saṃbhave api paraspara bhedaḥ siddhaḥ bhavati iha tu pramāṇa lakṣaṇa vivakṣayā kalpanā apoḍha mātrasya pratyakṣa tva abhyupagame sati vikalpāt eva tad viśeṣa tva abhimata tvāt asādhāraṇa kāraṇena vyapadeśe sati na kiṃcid prayojanam upalakṣyate prameya paratantrāyām ca pramāṇa saṃkhyā pravṛttau prameya ākāra anukāritā mātra tayā ca samāsādita ātma bhāva sattākayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ svarūpasya vyavasthāpanāt na indriyeṇa vyapadeśaḥ kiṃcid upakaroti iti sarvathā viṣayeṇa eva vyapadeśaḥ nyāyyaḥ 
[25,i]	loke pratyakṣa śabdasya prasiddha tvāt vivakṣite arthe pratyartha śabdasya aprasiddha tvāt āśrayeṇa eva vyutpattiḥ āśrīyate iti ced ucyate asti ayam pratyakṣa śabdaḥ loke prasiddhaḥ sa tu yathā loke tathā asmābhirucyataḥ eva yathā sthita laukika padārtha tiraskāreṇa tu tad vayutpāde kriyamāṇe prasiddha śabda tiraskāraḥ prasiddhaḥ syāt tatas ca pratyakṣam iti evam na syāt ekasya ca cakṣuḥ vijñānasya eka indriya kṣaṇa āśrayasya pratyakṣa tvam na syāt vīpsā artha abhāvāt ekaikasya ca pratyakṣa tva abhāve bahūnām api na syāt 
[25,ii]	kalpanā apoḍhasya eva ca jñānasya pratyakṣa tva abhyupagamāt tena ca lokasya saṃvyavahāra abhāvāt laukikasya ca pramāṇa prameya vyavahārasya vyākhyātum iṣṭa tvāt vyarthā eva pratyakṣa pramāṇa kalpanā saṃjāyate cakṣuḥ vijñāna sāmaṅgī nīlam jānāti no tu nīlam iti ca āgamasya pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa abhidhāna arthasya aprastuta tvāt pañcānām indriya vijñānānām jaḍa tva pratipādaka tvāt ca na āgamāt api kalpanā apoḍhasya eva vijñānasya pratyakṣa tvam iti na yuktam etat tasmāt loke yadi lakṣyam yadi vā sva lakṣaṇam sāmānya lakṣaṇam vā sarvam eva sākṣāt upalabhyamāna tvāt aparokṣam atas pratyakṣam vyavasthāpyate tad viṣayeṇa jñānena saha dvi candra ādīnām tu ataimirika jñāna apekṣayā apratyakṣa tvam taimirika ādi apekṣayā tu pratyakṣa tvam eva 
[25,iii_25,iv]	parokṣa viṣayam tu jñānam sādhya avyabhicāri liṅga utpannam anumānam sākṣāt atīndriya artha vidām a āptānām yat vacanam saḥ āgamaḥ sādṛśyāt ananubhūta arthadhigamaḥ upamānam gauḥ iva gavayaḥ iti yathā tat evam pramāṇa catuṣṭayāt lokasya artha adhigamaḥ vyavasthāpyate tāni ca paraspara apekṣayā sidhyanti satsu pramāṇeṣu prameya arthāḥ satsu prameyeṣu artheṣu pramāṇāni no tu khalu svābhāvikī pramāṇa prameyayoḥ siddhiḥ iti tasmāt laukikam eva astu yathādṛṣṭam iti alam prasaṅgena prastutam eva vyākhyāsyāmaḥ laukikaḥ eva darśane sthitvā buddhānām bhagavatām dharma deśanā 
[25,v_26,i]	atra āhuḥ sva yūthyāḥ yat idam uktam na svatas utpadyante bhāvāḥ iti tat yuktam svatas utpatti vaiyarthyāt yat ca uktam na dvābhyām iti tat api yuktam eka aṃśa vaikalyāt ahetupakṣaḥ tu ekānta nikṛṣṭaḥ iti tad pratiṣedhaḥ api yuktaḥ yat tu khalu idam ucyate na api paratas iti tat ayuktam yasmāt para bhūtāḥ eva bhagavatā bhāvānām utpādakāḥ nirdiṣṭāḥ catvāraḥ pratyayāḥ hetuḥ ca ālambanam anantaram tathā eva ādhipateyam ca pratyayaḥ na asti pañcamaḥ 
[26,ii]	tatra nirvartakaḥ hetuḥ iti lakṣaṇāt yaḥ hi yasya nirvartakaḥ bīja bhāvena avasthitaḥ sa tasya hetu pratyayaḥ utpadyamānaḥ dharmaḥ yena ālambanena utpadyate sa tasya ālambana pratyayaḥ kāraṇasya anantaraḥ nirodhaḥ kāryasya utpatti pratyayaḥ tat yathā bījasya anantaraḥ nirodhaḥ aṅkurasya utpāda pratyayaḥ yasmin sati yat bhavati tat tasya ādhipateyam iti te ete catvāraḥ pratyayāḥ ye ca anye puras jāta saha jāta paścāt jāta ādayaḥ te eteṣu eva antarbhūtāḥ īśvara ādayaḥ tu pratyayāḥ eva na saṃbhavanti iti atas eva avadhārayati pratyayaḥ na asti pañcamaḥ iti tasmāt ebhyaḥ para bhūtebhyaḥ bhāvānām utpattiḥ asti paratas utpattiḥ iti 
[26,iii]	atra ucyate na eva hi bhāvānām para bhūtebhyaḥ pratyayebhyaḥ utpattiḥ iti yasmāt na hi svabhāvaḥ bhāvānām pratyaya ādiṣu vidyate avidyamāne svabhāve para bhāvaḥ na vidyate iti yadi hi hetu ādiṣu para bhuteṣu pratyayeṣu samasteṣu vyasteṣu vyasta samasteṣu hetu pratyaya sāmagyā anyatra vā kvacid bhāvānām kāryāṇām utpādāt pūrvam sattvam syāt syāt tebhyaḥ utpādaḥ na ca evam yat utpādāt pūrvam saṃbhavaḥ syāt yadi syāt gṛhyeta ca utpāda vaiyarthyam ca syāt tasmāt nam ca asti bhāvānām pratyaya ādiṣu svabhāvaḥ avidyamāne ca svabhāve na asti para bhāvaḥ bhavanam bhāvaḥ utpādaḥ parebhyaḥ utpādaḥ para bhāvaḥ sa na vidyate tasmāt ayuktam etat para bhūtebhyaḥ bhāvānā mutpattiḥ iti 
[26,iv_26,v]	athavā bhāvānām kāryāṇām aṅkura ādīnām vīja ādiṣu pratyayeṣu satsu a vikṛta rūpeṣu na asti svabhāvaḥ nirhetuka tva prasaṅgāt tat kim apekṣam paratvam pratyaya ādīnām vidyamānayoḥ eva hi maitra upagrāhakayoḥ paraspara apekṣam paratvam na ca evam bīja aṅkurayoḥ yaugapadyam tasmāt avidyamāne svabhāve kāryāṇām para bhāvaḥ paratvam bīja ādīnām na asti iti para vyapadeśa abhāvāt eva na paratas utpādaḥ iti tasmāt āgama abhiprāya anabhijña tā eva parasya na hi tathāgatāḥ yukti viruddham vākyam udāharanti āgamasya ca abhiprāyaḥ prāk eva upavarṇitaḥ 
[26,vi]	tat evam pratyayebhyaḥ utpāda vādini pratiṣiddhe kriyātaḥ utpāda vādī manyate na cakṣu ūru upādayaḥ pratyayāḥ sākṣāt vijñānam janayanti vijñāna jani kriyā niṣpādaka tvāt tu pratyayāḥ ucyante sā ca kriyā vijñānam janayati tasmāt pratyayavatī vijñāna jani kriyā vijñāna janikā na pratyayāḥ yathā pacikriyā odanasya iti ucyate kriyā na pratyayavatī
[26,vii]	yadi kriyā kācid syāt sā cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ pratyayaiḥ pratyayavatī vijñānam janayet na tu asti katham kṛtvā iha kriyā iyam iṣyamāṇāḥ jāte vā vijñāne iṣyate ajāte vā jāyamāne vā tatra jāte na yuktā kriyā hi bhāva niṣpādikā bhāvaḥ ced niṣpannaḥ kim asya kriyayā jātasya janma punar eva ca na eva yuktam ityādinā ca madhyamaka avatāre pratipāditam etat ajāte api na yuktā kartrā vinā janiḥ iyam na ca yukta rūpā ityādi vacanāt jāyamāne api bhāve kriyā na saṃbhavati jāta ajāta vyatirekeṇa jāyamāna abhāvāt yathā uktam jāyamāna artha jāta tvāt jāyamānaḥ na jāyate atha vā jāyamāna tvam sarvasya eva prasajyate iti yatas ca evam triṣu kāleṣu jani kriyāyāḥ asaṃbhavaḥ tasmāt na asti sā atas eva āha kriyā na pratyayavatī iti 
[27,i_27,iii]	viśeṣaṇam na asti vinā viśeṣam ityādinā pratipāditam etat madhyamaka avatāre na hi vandhyā putraḥ gomān iti ucyate yadi evam apratyayavatī tarhi bhaviṣyati iti etat api ayuktam iti āha na apratyayavatī kriyā yadā pratyayavatī na asti tadā katham apratyayavatī nirhetukā syāt na hi tantu mayaḥ paṭaḥ na yuktaḥ iti vīraṇa mayaḥ abhyupagamyate tasmāt kriyā na bhāva janikā 
[27,iv_27,vi]	atra āha yadi evam kriyāyāḥ asaṃbhavaḥ pratyayāḥ tarhi janakāḥ bhaviṣyanti bhāvānām iti ucyate pratyayāḥ na akriyāvantaḥ yadā kriyā na asti tadā kriyā rahitāḥ akriyāvantaḥ nirhetukāḥ pratyayāḥ katham janakāḥ atha kriyāvantaḥ eva janakāḥ iti ucyate kriyāvantaḥ ca santi uta na iti prakṛtena abhisaṃbandhaḥ uta śabdaḥ avadhāraṇe tatra kriyāyāḥ abhāvaḥ uktaḥ katham kriyāvat tvam pratyayānām iti yathā ca vijñāna jani kriyā uktā evam parikriyā ādayaḥ api bhāvāḥ uktāḥ veditavyāḥ iti na asti kriyātas api samutpattiḥ bhāvānām iti bhavati utpāda abhidhānam artha śūnyam 
[27,vii]	atra āha kim na etena kriyāvantaḥ pratyayāḥ ityādi vicāreṇa yasmāt cakṣuḥ ādīn pratītya pratyayān vijñāna ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ jāyante tasmāt cakṣuḥ ādīnām pratyaya tvam tebhyaḥ ca utpādaḥ vijñāna ādīnām iti etat api ayuktam iti āha utpadyate pratītyemāniti ime pratyayāḥ kila yāvat na utpadyate ime tāvat na apratyayāḥ katham 
[28,i_28,ii]	yadi cakṣuḥ ādīn pratyayān pratītya vijñānam utpadyate iti asya ime pratyayāḥ ucyante nanu yāvat tad vijñāna ākhyam kāryam na utpadyate tāvat ime cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ katham na apratyayāḥ apratyayāḥ eva iti abhiprāyaḥ na ca apratyayebhyaḥ utpattiḥ sikatābhyaḥ iva tailasya atha matam pūrvam apratyayāḥ santaḥ kiṃcid anyam pratyayam apekṣya pratyaya tvam pratipadyante iti etat api ayuktam yat tat pratyaya antaram apratyayasya tasya pratyaya tvena kalpyate tat api pratyaya tve sati asya pratyayaḥ bhavati tatra api eṣā eva cintanā iti na yuktam etat 
[28,iii_28,vi]	kim ca iha ime cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ vijñānasya pratyayāḥ kalpyamānāḥ sataḥ vai asya kalpyeran asataḥ vā sarvathā ca na yujyate iti āha na eva asataḥ na eva sataḥ pratyayaḥ arthasya yujyate kasmāt iti āha asataḥ pratyayaḥ kasya sataḥ ca pratyayena kim asataḥ hi arthasya avidyamānasya katham pratyayaḥ syāt bhaviṣyatā vyapadeśaḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced na evam bhaviṣyatā ced vaya padeśaḥ iṣṭaḥ śaktim vinā na asti hi bhāvitāsya ityādinā ukta doṣa tvāt sataḥ api vidyamānasya labdha janmanaḥ niṣphalā eva pratyaya kalpanā evam samastānām pratyayānām kārya utpādana asāmarthyena apratyaya tvam udbhāvya atas param vyastānām apratyaya tvam pratipādyate 
[28,vii]	atra āha yadi api evam pratyayānām asaṃbhavaḥ tathā api asti eva lakṣaṇa upadeśāt pratyaya prasiddhiḥ tatra nirvartakaḥ hetuḥ iti lakṣaṇam ucyate hetu pratyayasya na ca avidyamānasya lakṣaṇa upadeśaḥ yuktaḥ bandhyā sutasya iva iti ucyate syāt hetu pratyayaḥ yadi tasya lakṣaṇam syāt yasmāt na san āsan na sadasan dharmaḥ nirvartate yadā katham nirvartakaḥ hetuḥ evam sati hi yujyate 
[28,viii]	tatra nirvartakaḥ utpādakaḥ yadi nirvartyaḥ dharmaḥ nirvarteta tam utpādakaḥ hetuḥ utpādayet na tu nirvartate sat asat ubhaya rūpasya nirvartyasya abhāvāt tatra sat na nirvartate vidyamāna tvāt asan api avidyamāna tvāt sadasan api paraspara viruddhasya eka arthasya abhāvāt ubhaya pakṣa abhihita doṣa tvāt ca yatas evam kāryasya utpattiḥ na asti hetu pratyayaḥ api atas na asti tatas ca yat uktam lakṣaṇa saṃbhavāt vidyate hetu pratyayaḥ iti tat evam sati na yujyate 
[29,i_29,ii]	idānīm ālambana pratyaya niṣedha artham āha anālambanaḥ eva ayam san dharmaḥ upadiśyate atha anālambane dharme kutas ālambanam punar iha sa ālambana dharmāḥ katame sarva citta caittāḥ iti āgamāt citta caittāḥ yena ālambanena utpadyante yathāyogam rūpa ādinā sa teṣām ālambana pratyayaḥ ayam ca vidyamānānām vā parikalpyeta avidyamānānām vā tatra vidyamānānām na arthaḥ tad ālambana pratyayena dharmasya hi utpatti artham ālambanam parikalpyate sa ca ālambanāt pūrvam vidyamānaḥ eva iti atha evam anālambane dharme sva ātmanā prasiddhe kim asya ālambana yogena parikalpitena iti anālambanaḥ eva ayam san vidyamānaḥ dharmaḥ citta ādikaḥ kevalam sa ālambanaḥ iti ucyate bhavadbhiḥ sva manīṣikayā na tu asya ālambanena kaścid saṃbandhaḥ asti atha avidyamānasya ālambanam parikalpyate tat api na yuktam anālambanaḥ eva ayam ityādi avidyamānasya hi na asti ālambanena yogaḥ 
[29,iii_29,v]	anālambanaḥ eva ayam san dharmaḥ upadiśyate bhavadbhiḥ sa ālambanaḥ iti vākya śeṣaḥ atha anālambane dharme kutas ālambanam punar athaśabdaḥ praśne kutas iti hetau tena ayam arthaḥ atha evam anālambane dharme asati avidyamāne bhūyas kutas ālambanam ālambanaka abhāvāt ālambanasya api abhāvaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ katham tarhi sa ālambanāḥ citta caittāḥ sāṃvṛtam etat lakṣaṇam na pārama arthi kam ityadoṣaḥ 
[29,vi_29,vii]	idānīm samanantara pratyaya niṣedha artham āha anutpanneṣu dharmeṣu nirodhaḥ na upapadyate na anantaram atas yuktam niruddhe pratyayaḥ ca kaḥ tatra paścime ślokasya ardhe pāda vyatyayaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ caśabdaḥ ca bhinna kramaḥ niruddhe ca iti tena evam pāṭhaḥ niruddhe ca pratyayaḥ kaḥ na anantaram atas yuktam iti śloka bandha artham tu evam uktam 
[29,viii]	tatra kāraṇasya anantaraḥ nirodhaḥ kāryasya utpāda pratyayaḥ samanantara pratyaya lakṣaṇam atra vicāryate anutpanneṣu dharmeṣu kārya bhūteṣu aṅkura ādiṣu nirodhaḥ na upapadyate kāraṇasya bīja ādeḥ yadā etat evam tadā kāraṇasya nirodha abhāvāt aṅkurasya kaḥ samanantara pratyayaḥ atha anutpanne api kārye bīja nirodhaḥ iṣyate evam sati niruddha bīje abhāvībhūte aṅkurasya kaḥ pratyayaḥ kaḥ vā bīja nirodhasya pratyayaḥ iti ubhayam etat ahetukam iti āha niruddhe ca kaḥ pratyayaḥ iti caśabdaḥ anutpanna śabda apekṣaḥ tena anutpanne ca aṅkure bīja ādīnām nirodhe iṣyamāṇe api ubhayam etat ahetukam apadyate iti na anantaram atas yuktam atha vā na svatas na api paratas ityādinā utpādaḥ niṣiddhaḥ tam abhisaṃdhāya āha anutpanneṣu dharmeṣu nirodhaḥ na upapadyate na anantaram atas yuktam iti api ca niruddhe pratyayaḥ ca kaḥ iti atra pūrvakam eva vyākhyānam 
[30,i_30,ii]	idānīm adhipati pratyaya svarūpa niṣedha artham āha bīja ādīnām bhāvānām niḥsvabhāvānām na sattā vidyate yatas sati idam asmin bhavati iti etat na eva upapadyate iha yasmin sati yat bhavati tat tasya ādhipateyam iti adhipati pratyaya lakṣaṇam bhāvānām ca pratītyasamutpanna tvāt svabhāva abhāve kutas tada yat asmin iti kāraṇa tvena vyapadiśyate kutas tat yat idam iti kāryatvena tasmāt na asti lakṣaṇataḥ api pratyaya siddhiḥ 
[30,iii]	atra āha tantu ādibhyaḥ paṭa ādikam upalabhya paṭa ādeḥ tantu ādayaḥ pratyayāḥ iti ucyate paṭa ādi phala pravṛttiḥ eva svarūpataḥ na asti kutas pratyayānām pratyaya tvam setsyati yathā ca paṭa ādi phala pravṛttiḥ asatī tathā pratipādayan āha na ca vyasta samasteṣu pratyayeṣu asti tad phalam pratyayebhyaḥ katham tat ca bhavet na pratyayeṣu yat 
[30,iv]	tatra vyasteṣu tantu turī vemata sara śalāka ādiṣu pratyayeṣu paṭaḥ na asti tatra anupalabhyamāna tvāt kāraṇa bahu tvāt ca kārya bahutva prasaṅgāt samuditeṣu api tantu ādiṣu na asti paṭaḥ pratyekam avayaveṣu avidyamāna tvāt ekasya kāryasya khaṇḍaśas utpatti prasaṅgāt tasmāt phala abhāvāt na santi pratyayāḥ svabhāvataḥ iti 
[30,v_30,vi]	atha āsat api tat tebhyaḥ pratyayebhyaḥ pravartate iti abhiprāyaḥ syāt apratyayebhyaḥ api kasmāt phalam na abhipravartate apratyayeṣu api na asti phalam iti apratyayebhyaḥ api vīraṇa ādibhyaḥ kasmāt na abhipravartate paṭaḥ iti na asti phala pravṛttiḥ svarūpataḥ 
[30,vii_30,viii]	atra āha yadi anyat phalam syāt anye ca pratyayāḥ tadā kim pratyayeṣu phalam asti na asti iti cintā syāt na asti tu vyatiriktam phalam kim tarhi pratyaya mayam eva iti ucyate phalam ca pratyaya mayam pratyayāḥ ca asvayaṃmayāḥ phalam asvamayebhyaḥ yat tat pratyaya mayam katham yadi pratyaya mayam pratyaya vikāraḥ phalam iti vyavasthāpyate tat ayuktam yasmāt te api pratyayāḥ asvayaṃmayā apratyaya svabhāvāḥ iti arthaḥ tantu mayaḥ hi paṭaḥ iti ucyate syāt paṭaḥ yadi tantavaḥ eva svabhāva siddhāḥ syuḥ te hi aṃśumayāḥ aṃśu vikārāḥ na svabhāva siddhāḥ tatas ca tebhyaḥ asvayaṃmayebhyaḥ asvabhāvebhyaḥ yat phalam paṭa ākhyam tat katham tantu mayam bhaviṣyati yathā uktam paṭaḥ kāraṇataḥ siddhaḥ siddham kāraṇam anyatas siddhiḥ yasya svatas na astaḥ tat anyat janayet katham iti 
[31,i_31,ii]	tasmāt na pratyaya mayam phalam saṃvidyate apratyaya mayam tarhi astu na apratyaya mayam phalam saṃvidyate iti tantu mayaḥ yadā paṭaḥ na asti tadā katham vīraṇa mayaḥ syā atra āha mā bhūt phalam pratyaya apratyaya niyamaḥ tu vidyate tathā ca bhavān bravīti yadi asat phalam pratyayebhyaḥ pravartate apratyayebhyaḥ api kasmāt na abhipravartate iti na ca asati phale paṭakaṭa ākhye tantu vīraṇānām pratyayānām pratyaya tvam yuktam atas phalam api asti iti ucyate syāt phalam yadi pratyaya apratyayāḥ eva syuḥ sati hi phale ime asya pratyayāḥ ime apratyayāḥ iti syāt tat ca vicāryamāṇam na asti iti phala abhāvāt pratyaya apratyayāḥ kutas 
[31,iii]	pratyayāḥ ca apratyayāḥ ca iti samāsaḥ tasmāt na asti bhāvānām svabhāvataḥ samutpattiḥ iti yathā uktam ārya ratnākara sūtre śūnyavidya na hi vidyate kvaci antarīkṣi śakunasya vā padam yaḥ na vidyati sabhāvataḥ kvaci saḥ na jātu para hetu bheṣyati yasya na eva hi sabhāvu labhyati saḥ asvabhāvu para paccayaḥ katham asvabhāvu paru kim janīṣyati eṣa hetu sugatena deśitaḥ sarva dharma acalāḥ dṛḍham sthitāḥ nirvikāra nirupadravāḥ śivāḥ antarīkṣa patha tulya ajānakā tatra muhyati jagam ajānakam śailaparvata yathā akampiyāḥ evam dharmaḥ avikampiyāḥ sadā no cyavati na pi ca upapadyayu evam dharmata jinena deśitā ityādi 
[32,i]	tathā yaḥ na pi jāyati nā cupapadyī no cyavate na pi jīryati dharmaḥ tam jinu deśayatī narasiṃhaḥ tatra niveśayi sattva śatāni yasya sabhāvu na vidyati kaści no para bhāvatu kenaci labdhaḥ na antarataḥ na pi bāhiratas vā labhyati tatra niveśayi nāthaḥ śānta gatī kathitā sugatena no ca gati upalabhyati kāci tatra ca voharasī gati muktaḥ muktaku mocayamī bahu sattvān iti vistaraḥ 
[33,i]	atra āha yadi api utpāda pratiṣedhāt pratītya samutpādasya anirodha ādi viśeṣaṇa siddhiḥ tathā api anāgama nirgama pratītyasamutpāda siddhaye loka prasiddha gamana āgamana kriyā pratiṣedha artham kiṃcid upapatti antaram ucyatām iti ucyate yadi gamanam nāma syāt niyatam tat gate vai adhvajāte parikalpyeta agate gamyamāne vā sarvathā ca na yujyate iti āha gatam na gamyate tāvat agatam na eva gamyate gatāgata vinirmuktam gamyamānam na gamyate 
[33,ii]	tatra uparata gami kriyam adhvajātam gatam iti ucyate āviśyamānam gami kriyayā vartamānam gamyate iti ucyate yat gatam uparata gami kriyam tad vartamāna gami kriyā yoga vācinā gamyate iti anena śabdena ucyamānam asaṃbaddham iti kṛtvā gatam tāvat gamyate iti na yujyate tāvat śabdena ca pratiṣedha kramam darśayati 
[33,iii_33,iv]	agatam api na gamyate agatam hi anupajāta gami kriyam anāgatam ucyate gamyate iti ca vartamānam atas anāgata vartamānayoḥ atyanta bhedāt agatam api gamyate iti na yujyate yadi agatam katham gamyate atha gamyate na tat agatam iti gamyamāne api na asti gamanam yasmāt gatāgata vinirmuktam gamyamānam na gamyate 
[33,v]	iha hi gantā yam deśam atikrāntaḥ sa tasya deśaḥ gataḥ yam ca na atikrāntaḥ saḥ asya anāgataḥ na ca gatāgata vyatirekeṇa tṛtīyam aparama dhvajātam paśyāmaḥ gamyamānam nāma yatas ca evam gamyamānam na gamyate gamyate iti na prajñāyate tasmāt na asti gamyamānam atas na tat gami kriyayā āviśyate na gamyate iti na asti gamyamāne api gamanam 
[33,vi]	atha syāt gantuḥ gacchataḥ yaḥ caraṇa ākrāntaḥ deśaḥ sa gamyamānaḥ syāt iti na evam caraṇayoḥ api paramāṇu sāṃghāta tvāt aṅguli agra avasthitasya paramāṇoḥ yaḥ pūrvaḥ deśaḥ sa tasya gate antargataḥ pārṣṇi avasthitasya carama paramāṇoḥ yaḥ uttaraḥ deśaḥ sa tasya agate antargataḥ na ca paramāṇu vyatirekeṇa caraṇam asti tasmāt na asti gatāgata vyatirekeṇa gamyamānam yathā ca evam caraṇe vicāraḥ evam paramāṇūnām api pūrva apara diś bhāga saṃbandhena vicāraḥ kāryaḥ iti atha ardha gatam gamyamānam uktam uttaram jāyamāna vicāreṇa tasmāt gamyamānam na gamyate iti siddham 
[33,vii_34,i]	tatra āha gamyate eva gamyamānam iha hi ceṣṭā yatra gatiḥ tatra gamyamāne ca sā yatas na gate na āgate ceṣṭā gamyamāne gatiḥ tatas tatra ceṣṭā caraṇa utkṣepa parikṣepa lakṣaṇā yatas vrajataḥ gantuḥ yatra deśe ceṣṭā gatiḥ tatra eva deśe sā ca ceṣṭā na gate adhvani saṃbhavati na api agate kim tu gamyamānaḥ eva tatas ca gamyamāne gatiḥ yatra hi gatiḥ upalabhyate tat gamyamānam tat ca gami kriyayā āviśyate tasmāt gamyamānam eva gamyate iti ekaḥ atra gamiḥ jñāna arthaḥ aparaḥ ca deśa antara saṃprāpti arthaḥ iti 
[34,ii_34,iii]	evam api parikalpyamāne gamyamānam na gamyate iti āha gamyamānasya gamanam katham nāma upapatsyate gamyamāne dvi gamanam yadā na eva upapadyate iha hi gami kriyā yogāt eva gamyamāna vyapadeśam icchati bhavān tat ca iti gamyata bravīti ekā ca atra gami kriyā tayā gamyamāna vyapadeśaḥ bhavatu kāmam adhvanaḥ gamyate iti bhūyas kriyā saṃbandhaḥ gamyamānasya na yujyate iti gamyamānasya gamanam katham nāma upapatsyate kāraṇam āha gamyamāne dvi gamanam yadā na eva upapadyate iti 
[34,iv]	gamyamānam iti gamyate iti arthaḥ dvi gatam gamanam dvi gamanam ekasyāḥ gami kriyāyāḥ gamyamānam iti atra upayukta tvāt dvitīyāyāḥ abhāvāt ca gamyate iti ayam vyapadeśaḥ vinā gamanena yadā na eva upapadyate tadā gamyamānam gamyate iti paripūrṇaḥ vākya arthaḥ na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ gamyamānam iti etāvat mātram eva saṃbhavati dvitīya kriyā bhāvāt na tu gamyate iti 
[34,v_34,vi]	atha gamyate iti atra eva gami kriyā saṃbandhaḥ iṣyate evam sati gamyamāna vyapadeśe na asti kriyā saṃbandhaḥ iti na paripūrṇa tā vākya arthasya iti āha gamyamānasya gamanam yasya tasya prasajyate ṛte gateḥ gamyamānam gamyamānam hi gamyate yasya vādinaḥ gamyamānasya gamanam iti pakṣaḥ gamyamāne saṃjñā bhūte gami kriyā śūnye yaḥ gami kriyām ādheya bhūtām icchati tasya pakṣe ṛte gateḥ gamyamānam iti prasajyate gati rahitam gamanam syāt yasmāt asya gamyamānam hi gamyate hi śabdaḥ yasmāt arthe yasmāt gati rahitam eva gamyamānam sat tasya vādinaḥ gamyate gamyate iti atra kriyā upayogāt tasmāt gati rahitam gamanam prasajyate 
[34,vii_34,viii]	atha ubhayatra api kriyā saṃbandhaḥ iṣyate gamyamāne gamyate iti atra ca evam api gamyamānasya gamane prasaktam gamana dvayam yena tat gamyamānam ca yat ca atra gamanam punar yena gamanena yogāt gamyamāna vyapadeśam pratilabhate adhvā tat ekam gamanam tatra gamyamāne adhikaraṇa bhute dvitīyam gamanam yena saḥ adhvā gamyate etat gamana dvayam gamyamānasya gamane sati prasaktam 
[35,i_35,iii]	bhavatu gamana dvayam kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced ayam doṣaḥ yasmāt dvau gantārau prasajyete prasakte gamana dvaye kim punar kāraṇam gantṛ dvaya prasaṅge iti āha gantāram hi tiraskṛtya gamanam na upapadyate yasmāt avaśyam kriyā sva sādhanam apekṣate karma kartāram vā gamikriyā ca evam kartari avasthitā atas gantāram apekṣate na asti ca ekasmin eva gacchati devadatte dvitīyaḥ kartā iti atas kartṛ dvaya abhāvāt na asti gamana dvayam tatas ca gamyamānam gamyate iti na upapadyate 
[35,iv]	atha syāt yadā ayam devadattaḥ sthitaḥ sa na bhāṣate paśyati na tadā ekaḥ aneka kriyaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ evam ekasmin gantari kriyā dvayam bhaviṣyati iti na evam śaktiḥ hi kārakaḥ na dravyam kriyā bhedāt ca tad sādhanasya api śakteḥ siddhaḥ eva bhedaḥ na hi sthiti kriyayā vaktā syāt dravyam ekam iti ced bhavatu evam na tu dravyam kārakaḥ kim tarhi śaktiḥ sā ca bhidyate eva api ca sadṛśa kriyā dvaya kāraka tvam na eka deśikasya dṛṣṭam atas na ekasya gantuḥ gamana dvayam 
[35,v_35,vi]	atra āha yadi api evam tathā api gantari devadatte gamanam upalabhyate devadattaḥ gacchati iti vyapadeśāt tatas ca vidyate eva gamanam gamana āśraya gantṛ sadbhāvāt ucyate syāt evam yadi gamana āśrayaḥ gantā syāt na tu asti katham iti āha gantāram cetiḥ askṛtya gamanam na upapadyate gamane asati gantā atha kutas eva bhaviṣyati gantāram antareṇa nirāśrayam gamanam asat iti uktam tatas ca gantāram cetiraskṛtya pratyākhyāya gamanam na asti asati gamane kutas nirhetukaḥ gantā atas na asti gamanam
