[35,vii]	atra āha vidyate eva gamanam tadvataḥ tena vyapadeśāt iha gantā gamanena yuktaḥ tad yogāt ca gacchati yadi gamanam na syāt gamanavataḥ devadattasya gacchati iti vyapadeśaḥ na syāt daṇḍa abhāve daṇḍi vyapadeśa abhāva vat ucyate syāt gamanam yadi gacchati iti evam vyapadeśaḥ syāt yasmāt gantā na gacchati tāvat agantā na eva gacchati anyaḥ gantuḥ agantuḥ ca kaḥ tṛtīyaḥ hi gacchati 
[35,viii]	iha gacchati iti gantā sa tāvat na gacchati yathā ca na gacchati tathā uttareṇa śloka trayeṇa pratipādayiṣyati agantā api na gacchati agantā hi nāma yaḥ gami kriyā rahitaḥ gacchati iti ca gami kriyā yoga pravṛttaḥ śabdaḥ yadi asā avagantā katham gacchati atha gacchati na asau agantāḥ iti tad ubhaya vyatiriktaḥ gacchati iti ced na evam kaḥ hi gantuḥ agantuḥ vinirmuktaḥ tṛtīyaḥ asti yaḥ gacchati iti kalpyeta tasmāt na asti gamanam 
[36,i_36,ii]	atra āha na āgantā gacchati na api ubhaya rahitaḥ kim tarhi gantā eva gacchati iti etat api asat kim kāraṇam yasmāt gantā tāvat gacchati iti katham eva upapatsyate gamanena vinā gantā yadā na eva upapadyate gantā gacchati iti atra vākye ekā eva gami kriyā tayā ca gacchati iti vyapadiśyate gantā iti tu vyapadeśe na asti dvitīyāḥ gami kriyā iti gamanena vinā gantā agacchan gantā iti yadā na saṃbhavati tadā gantā gacchati iti na yujyate kāmam gacchati iti astu gantā iti tu na saṃbhavati iti tat ayuktam 
[36,iii_36,iv]	atha gati yogāt sa gatikaḥ eva gantā tathā api dvitīya gami kriyā abhāvadgacchati iti vyapadeśaḥ na syāt iti āha pakṣaḥ gantā gacchati iti yasya tasya prasajyate gamanena vinā gantā gantuḥ gamanam icchataḥ yasya vādinaḥ gami kriyā yogāt eva gantā iti pakṣaḥ tasya gantuḥ gamanam icchataḥ sa gamana gantṛ vyapadeśāt gamanena vinā gantā gacchati iti syāt dvitīya gami kriyā bhāvāt atas gantā gacchati iti na yujyate gacchati iti etasya arthe gantā iti śabdaḥ gamanena vinā gantā iti atra vākye 
[36,v_36,vi]	atha ubhayatra api gati yogaḥ iṣyate gantā gacchati iti evam api gamane dve prasajyete gantā yadi uta gacchati gantā iti ca ucyate yena gantā san yat ca gacchati yena gamanena yogāt gantā iti ucyate vyapadiśyate tat ekam gamanam gantā bhavan yat ca gacchati yām ca gati kriyām karoti tat etat gamana dvayam prasaktam atas gantṛ dvaya prasaṅgaḥ iti pūrvavat dūṣaṇam vaktavyam tasmāt na asti gacchati iti vyapadeśaḥ 
[36,vii_36,viii]	atra āha yadi api evam tathā api devadattaḥ gacchati iti vyapadeśa sadbhāvāt gamanasti iti na evam yasmāt devadatta āśrayā eva eṣā cintā kim asau gantā san gacchati uta agantā gacchati tat vayatiriktaḥ vā iti sarvathā ca na upapadyate iti yat kiṃcid etat atra āha vidyate eva gamanam tad ārambha sadbhāvāt iha devadattaḥ sthiti upamardena gamanam ārabhate na ca avidyamāna kūrma roma prāvāra ādikam ārabhate ucyate syāt gamanam yadi tadāramme eva syāt yasmāt gate na ārabhyate gantum gatam na ārabhyate agate na ārabhyate gamyamāne gantum ārabhyate kuha 
[37,i]	yadi gamana ārambhaḥ bhavet tat gate vā adhvanyāramyeta agate vā gamyamāne vā tatra gate gamanam na ārabhyate tat hi nāma uparata gami kriyam yadi tatra gamanam ārabhyeta tat gatam iti evam na syāt atīta vartamānayoḥ virodhāt agate api gamanam na ārabhyate anāgata vartamānayoḥ virodhāt na api gamyamāne tad abhāvāt kriyā dvaya prasaṅgāt kartṛ dvaya prasaṅgāt ca tat evam sarvatra gamana ārambham apaśyan āha gantum ārabhyate kuha iti 
[37,ii_37,iv]	yathā ca gamanam na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha na pūrvam gamana ārambhāt gamyamānam na vā gatam yatra ārabhyeta gamanam agate gamanam kutas iha devadattaḥ yadā avasthitaḥ āste sa tadā gamanam na ārabhate tasya gamana ārambhāt pūrvam na gamyamānam adhu ajātam asti na ca gatam yatra gamanam ārabhyeta tasmāt gata gamyamāna abhāvāt enayoḥ na gamana ārambhaḥ atha syāt yadi api gamana ārambhāt pūrvam na gatam na gamyamānam tathā api agatam asti tatra gamana ārambhaḥ syāt iti ucyate agate gamanam kutas anupajāta gami kriyam anārabdha gami kriyama gatam tatra gamana ārambhaḥ iti asaṃbaddham etat iti āha agate gamanam kutas iti 
[37,v_37,vi]	yadi api gatāgata gamyamāneṣu gamana ārambhaḥ na asti gatāgata gamyamānāni tu santi na ca asati gamane etāni yujyante iti ucyate syāt gamanam yadi etāni eva syuḥ sati hi gami kriyā prārambhe yatra uparatā gami kriyā tat gatam iti parikalpyeta yatra vartamānā tat gamyamānam yatra ajātā tat agatam iti yadā tu gami kriyā prārambhaḥ eva na asti tadā gatam kim gamyamanam kim agatam kim vikalpyate adṛśyamānaḥ ārambhe gamanasya eva sarvathā prārambhe anupalabhyamāne kim mithyā adhva trayam parikalpyate kutas vā tad vayapadeśa kāraṇam gamanam iti ayuktam etat 
[37,vii]	atra āha vidyate eva gamanam tad pratipakṣa sadbhāvāt yasya ca pratipakṣaḥ asti tat asti āloka andhakāra vat pārāvāra vat saṃśaya niścaya vat ca asti ca gamanasya pratipakṣaḥ sthānam iti ucyate syāt gamanam yadi tad pratipakṣaḥ sthānam syāt katham iha idam sthānam gantuḥ agantuḥ tad anyasya vā parikalpyeta sarvathā ca na yujyate iti āha gantā na tiṣṭhati tāvat agantā na eva tiṣṭhati anyaḥ gantuḥ agantuḥ ca kaḥ tṛtīyaḥ atha tiṣṭhati 
[37,viii]	yathā gantā na tiṣṭhati tathā uttareṇa ślokena ākhyāsyati agantā api na tiṣṭhati sa hi tiṣṭhati eva tasya kim aparayā sthityā prayojanam agantā api na tiṣṭhati sa hi tiṣṭhati eva tasya kim aparayā sthityā prayojanam ekayā sthityā agantā aparayā tiṣṭhati iti sthiti dvaya prasaṅgāt sthātṛ dvaya prasaṅgaḥ iti pūrvavat doṣaḥ gantra gantṛ rahitaḥ ca anyaḥ na asti 
[38,i_38,ii]	atra āha na āgantā tiṣṭhati na api gantuḥ agantuḥ ca anyaḥ kim tarhi gantā eva tiṣṭhati iti na evam yasmāt gantā tāvat tiṣṭhati iti katham eva upapatsyate gamanena vinā gantā yadā na eva upapadyate yadā ayam tiṣṭhati iti ucyate tadā sthiti virodhi gamanam asya na asti vinā ca gamanam gantṛ vyapadeśaḥ na asti atas gantā tiṣṭhati iti na upapadyate 
[38,iii_38,iv]	atra āha vidyate eva gamanam tad nivṛtti sadbhāvāt iha gateḥ nivartamānaḥ sthitim ārabhate gamana abhāve tu na tatas nivarteta ucyate syāt gamanam yadi tad nivṛttiḥ eva syāt na tu asti yasmāt na tiṣṭhati gamyamānāt na gatāt na āgatāt api tatra gantā gatāt adhvanaḥ na nivartate gati abhāvāt agatāt api gati abhāvāt eva gamyamānāt api na nivartate tad anupalabdheḥ gami kriyā bhāvāt ca tasmāt na gati nivṛttiḥ 
[38,v]	atra āha yadi gamana pratidvan dvi sthiti abhāvāt gatiḥ asatī evam tarhi gamana prasiddhaye sthiti sādhayāmaḥ tad siddhau gamana siddhiḥ tasmāt vidyate eva sthānam pratidvandvi sadbhāvāt sthiteḥ hi pratidvandvi gamanam tat asti tatas ca sthitiḥ api pratidvandvi sadbhāvāt etat api ayuktam yasmāt gamanam saṃpravṛttiḥ ca nivṛttiḥ ca gateḥ samā 
[38,vi]	atra hi yat gamanam sthiti siddhaye varṇitam tad gatyā samam gati dūṣaṇena tulyam iti arthaḥ yathā gantā na tiṣṭhati tāvat ityādinā gati prasiddhaye sthiteḥ hetu tvena upāttāyāḥ dūṣaṇam uktam evam iha api sthiti prasiddhaye gamanasya hetu tvena upāttasya sthātā na gacchati tāvat ityādinā śloka dvaya pāṭha parivartena dūṣaṇam vaktavyam iti na asti gamanam tad abhāvāt pratidvandvinī sthitiḥ api iti evam tāvat gamanam gatyā tulyam pratyākhyeyam 
[38,vii]	atha syāt vidyate eva sthānam tad ārambha sadbhāvāt iha gati upamardena sthānam ārabhyate katham tat na syāt ucyate saṃpravṛttiḥ ca gateḥ samā vācyā tatra yathā pūrvam gate na ārabhyate gantum ityādinā gamana ārambhaḥ niṣiddhaḥ evam iha api sthite na ārabhyate sthātum sthātum na ārabhyate asthite na ārabhyate sthīyamāne sthātum ārabhyate kuha ityādinā śloka traya parivartena sthāna saṃpravṛttiḥ api gateḥ samā sthāna nivṛttiḥ api gati nivṛttyā samā pratyākhyeyā yathā gati niṣedhe na tiṣṭhati gamyamānāt na gatāt na āgatāt api iti gateḥ dūṣaṇam uktam evam sthiti niṣedhe api na gacchati sthīyamānāt na sthita anna āsthitāt api iti gatyā tulyam dūṣaṇam iti na asti sthitiḥ tad abhāvāt kutas gati pratipakṣa sthiti sadbhāva vādinām gateḥ siddhiḥ iti 
[39,i_39,iii]	api ca yadi gamanam syāt gantṛ vyatirekeṇa vā syāt avyatirekeṇa vā sarvathā ca vicāryamāṇam na saṃbhavati iti āha yat eva gamanam gantā saḥ eva iti na yujyate anyaḥ eva punar gantā gateḥ iti na yujyate katham punar na yujyate iti āha yat eva gamanam gantā saḥ eva hi bhavet yadi ekībhāvaḥ prasajyeta kartuḥ karmaṇaḥ eva ca yā iyam gami kriyā sā yadi gantuḥ avyatiriktā na anyā syāt tadā kartuḥ kriyāyāḥ ca eka tvam syāt tatas ca iyam kriyā ayam kartā iti viśeṣaḥ na syāt na ca chidi kriyāyāḥ chettuḥ ca eka tvam atas yat eva gamanam saḥ eva gantā iti na yujyate 
[39,iv_39,v]	anyatram api gantṛ gamanayoḥ yathā na asti tathā pratipādayan āha anyaḥ eva punar gantā gateḥ yadi vikalpyate gamanam syāt ṛte gantuḥ gantā syāt gamanāt ṛte yadi hi gantṛ gamanayoḥ anya tvam syāt tadā gamana nirapekṣaḥ gantā syāt gantṛ nirapekṣam ca gamanam gṛhyeta pṛthak siddham ghaṭāt iva paṭaḥ na ca gantuḥ pṛthak siddham gamanam gṛhyate iti anyaḥ eva punar gantā gateḥ iti na yujyate iti prasādhitam etat 
[39,vi_39,vii]	tat evam ekībhāvena vā siddhiḥ nānā bhāvena vā yayoḥ na vidyate tayoḥ siddhiḥ katham nu khalu vidyate yayoḥ gantṛ gamanayoḥ yathā udita nyāyena ekībhāvena vā nānā bhāvena vā na asti siddhiḥ tayoḥ idānīm kena anyena prakāreṇa siddhiḥ astu atas āha tayoḥ siddhiḥ katham nu khalu vidyate iti na asti gantṛ gamanayoḥ siddhiḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[40,i_40,ii]	atra āha iha devadattaḥ gantā gacchati iti loka prasiddham tatra yathā vaktā vācam bhāṣate kartā kriyām karoti iti prasiddham evam yayā gatyā gantā iti abhivyajyate tām gacchati iti na yathā ukta doṣaḥ tat api asat yasmāt gatyā yayā ucyate gantā gatim tām sa na gacchati yayā gatyā devadattaḥ gantā iti abhivyajate sa gantā san tām tāvat na gacchati na prāpnoti yadi vā na karoti iti arthaḥ 
[40,iii_40,v]	yasmāt na gati pūrvaḥ asti gateḥ pūrvaḥ gati pūrvaḥ yadi gantā gateḥ pūrvam siddhaḥ syāt sa tām gacchet katham yasmāt kaścid kiṃcid hi gacchati kaścid devadattaḥ kiṃcid artha antara bhūtam grāmam nagaram vā gacchati iti dṛṣṭam na ca evam yayā gatyā gantā iti ucyate tasyāḥ pūrvam siddha rūpaḥ gati nirapekṣaḥ gantā nāma asti yaḥ tām gacchet 
[40,vi_40,vii]	atha manyase yayā gatyā gantā iti abhivyajyate tām eva asau na gacchati kim tahi tatas anyām iti etat api asat yasmāt gatyā yayā ucyate gantā tatas anyām sa na gacchati gatī dve na upapadyete yasmāt eke pragacchati yayā gatyā gantā abhivyajyate tatas anyām api sa gantā san na gacchati gati dvaya prasaṅgāt yayā gatyā gantā abhivyajyate gantā san yām ca aparām gacchati iti etat gati dvayam prasaktam na ca ekasmin gantari gati dvayam iti uktam etat etena vaktā vācam bhāṣate kartā kriyām karoti iti pratyuktam 
[40,viii_40,ix]	tat evam sadbhūtaḥ gamanam gantā tri prakāram na gacchati na asat bhūtaḥ api gamanam tri prakāram sa gacchati gamanam sat asat bhūtaḥ tri prakāram na gacchati tatra gamyate iti gamanam iha ucyate tatra sadbhūtaḥ gantā yaḥ gami kriyā yuktaḥ asat bhūtaḥ gantā yaḥ gami kriyā rahitaḥ sat asat bhūtaḥ yaḥ ubhaya pakṣīya rūpaḥ evam gamanam api tri prakāram gami kriyā saṃbandhena veditavyam tatra sadbhūtaḥ gantā sat bhūtam asat bhūtam sat asat bhūtam tri prakāram gamanam na gacchati etat ca karma kāraka parīkṣāyām ākhyāsyate evam asat bhūtaḥ api gantā tri prakāram gamanam na gacchati sat asat bhūtaḥ api iti tatra eva pratipādayiṣyati yatas ca evam gantṛ gantavya gamanāni vicāryamāṇāni na santi tasmāt gatiḥ ca gantā ca gantavyam ca na vidyate 
[41,i_41,iii]	yathā uktam āryā kṣayam ati nirdeśa sūtre agatiḥ iti bhadanta śāradvatī putra saṃkarṣaṇa padam etat gatiḥ iti bhadanta śāradvatī putra niṣkarṣaṇa padam etat yatra na saṃkarṣaṇa padam na niṣkarṣaṇa padam tad ā āryāṇām padam apada yogena anāgatiḥ agatiḥ ca āryāṇām gatiḥ iti yadi bījam eva aṅkure saṃkramati bījam eva tat syāt na yat aṅkuraḥ śāśvata doṣa prasaṅgaḥ ca atha aṅkuraḥ anyatas āgacchati ahetuka doṣa prasaṅgaḥ syāt na ca ahetukasya utpattiḥ khara viṣāṇasya iva 
[41,iv_41,v]	atas eva āha bhagavān bījasya sataḥ yathā aṅkuraḥ na ca yaḥ bīju sa ca eva aṅkuraḥ na ca anyu tatas na ca eva tat evam anuccheda aśāśvata dharma tā iti mudrāt pratimudra dṛśyate mudra saṃkrānti na ca upalabhyate na ca tatra na ca eva sā anyatas evam saṃskāra nuccheda śāśvatāḥ iti ca tathā ādarśa pṛṣṭhe tatha taila pātre nirīkṣate nārimukham alaṃkṛtam saḥ tatra rāgam janayitva bālaḥ pradhāvitaḥ kāmi gaveṣamāṇaḥ mukhasya saṃkrānti yadā na vidyate bimbe mukham na eva kadāci labhyate mūḍhaḥ yathā saḥ janayeta rāgam tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān 
[41,vi^1]	tathā tahi kāli saḥ daśa balaḥ anaghaḥ jinu bhāṣate imu samādhi varam su pinā upamā bhagavatī sakalā na hi kaści jāyati na caḥ mriyate na ca sattvu labhyati na jīvu naraḥ imi dharma phena kadalī sadṛśāḥ māyā upamāḥ gagana vidyu samāḥ daka candra saṃnibha marīci samāḥ na ca asmi loki mṛtu kaści naraḥ para loka saṃkramati gacchati vā na ca karma naśyati kadāci kṛtam phalu deti kṛṣṇa śubha saṃsarataḥ na ca śāśvatam na ca uccheda punaḥ na ca karma saṃcayu na ca api sthitiḥ na ca saḥ api kṛtva punar āspṛśati na ca anyu kṛtva puna vedayate 
[41,vi^2]	 na ca saṃkramaḥ na ca punā āgamanam na ca sarvam asti na ca na asti punar na ca dṛṣṭaḥ sthāna gati śuddhiḥ ihaḥ na ca satvacāra supaśānta gati su pina upamam hi tri bhavam vaśikam laghu bhagnam anityena māya samam na ca āgatam na ca iha upagatam śūnya animitta sada saṃtatiyaḥ anutpāda śānta animitta padam sugatāna gocara jināna guṇā bala dhāraṇī daśa balāna balam buddhānaḥ iyam vṛṣabhitā paramā vara śukla dharma guṇa saṃnicayaḥ guṇa jñāna dhāraṇi balam paramam ṛddhī vikurvaṇa vidhiḥ paramaḥ vara pañca bhijña pratilābha nayaḥ iti vistaraḥ 
[43,i_43,iii]	atra āha yadi api gatiḥ ca gantā ca gantavyam ca na vidyate tathā api pravacana siddha yapekṣayā draṣṭṭa draṣṭavya darśana ādīnām astitvam āstheyam tathā ca abhidharme ucyate darśanam śravaṇam ghrāṇam rasanam sparśanam manaḥ indriyāṇi ṣaṭ eteṣām draṣṭavī a ādīni gocaraḥ tasmāt santi darśana ādīni svabhāvataḥ iti ucyate na santi iha hi paśyati iti darśanam cakṣuḥ tasya ca rūpam viṣaya tvena upadiśyate 
[43,iv_43,v]	yathā darśanam rūpam na paśyati tathā pratipādayan āha svam ātmānam darśanam hi tat tam eva na paśyati na paśyati yadā ātmānam katham drakṣyati tad parān tatra tat eva darśanam sva ātmānam na paśyati sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt tatas ca sva ātma adarśanāt śrotra ādi vat nīla ādikam na paśyati tasmāt na asti darśanam 
[43,vi_43,vii]	yadi api sva ātmānam darśanam na paśyati tathā aṣi agni vat parān drakṣyati tathā hi agniḥ para ātmānam eva dahati na sva ātmānam evam darśanam parān eva drakṣyati na sva ātmānam iti etat ati ayuktam yasmāt na paryāptaḥ agni dṛṣṭāntaḥ darśanasya prasiddhaye yaḥ ayam agni dṛṣṭāntaḥ darśanasya prasiddhaye bhavatā upanyastaḥ sa na paryāptaḥ na alam na samarthaḥ na yujyate iti arthaḥ yasmāt sa darśanaḥ sa pratyuktaḥ gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ 
[43,viii]	saha darśanena vartate iti sa darśanaḥ yaḥ ayam agni dṛṣṭāntaḥ darśana prasiddhaye bhavatā upanyastaḥ saḥ api saha darśanena dārṣṭa antika arthena pratyuktaḥ dūṣitaḥ kena punar iti āha gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ yathā gatam na gamyate na āgatam na gamyamānam evam agninā api dagdham na dahyate na adagdham dahyate ityādinā samam vācyam yathā ca na gatam na āgatam na gamyamānam gamyate evam na dṛṣṭam dṛśyate tāvat adṛṣṭam na eva dṛśyate dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa vinirmuktam dṛśyamānam na dṛśyate ityādi vācyam 
[43,ix]	yathā ca gantā na gacchati tāvat iti ādi uktam evam na dagdhāḥ dahati tāvat ityādi vācyam evam na draṣṭā paśyati tāvat ityādinā agni dṛṣṭāntena saha gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ yasmāt samam dūṣaṇam atas agni vat darśana siddhiḥ iti na yujyate tatas ca siddham etat sva ātma vat darśanam parān api na paśyati iti 
[44,i_44,ii]	yadā evam tadā na apaśyamānam bhavati yadā kiṃcana darśanam darśanam paśyati iti evam katham etat tu yujyate yadā ca evam apaśyan na kiṃcid darśanam bhavati tadānīm apaśyataḥ darśana ātvā ayogāt stambha ādi vat paśyati iti darśanam iti vyapadeśaḥ na yujyate yadi api darśana śabdāt anantaram śloka bandha anurodhena darśana paśyati iti pāṭhaḥ tathā api vyākhyāna kāle paśyati iti darśanam iti evam katham etat tu yujyate iti paṭhitavyam 
[44,iii_44,iv]	kim ca anyat iha paśyati iti darśanam iti ucyamāne darśana kriyayā darśana svabhāvasya vā cakṣuṣaḥ saṃbandhaḥ parikalpyeta adarśana svabhāvasya vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha paśyati darśanam na eva na eva paśyati adarśanam darśana svabhāvasya tāvat dṛśi kriyā yuktasya bhūyas paśyati ityādinā saṃbandhaḥ na upapadyate dṛśi kriyā dvaya prasaṅgāt darśana dvaya prasaṅgāt ca adarśanam api na paśyati darśana kriyā rahita tvāt aṅgūlī agravadityā abhiprāyaḥ yadā paśyati darśanam na eva na eva paśyati adarśanam tadā darśanam paśyati iti evam katham etat tu yujyate iti anena eva saṃbandhaḥ 
[44,v]	ye tu manyante nirvyāpāram hi idam dharma mātram utpadyamānam utpadyate iti na eva kiṃcid kaścid viṣayam paśyati kriyāyāḥ abhāvāt tasmāt darśanam na paśyati iti siddham etat prasādhyate iti atra ucyate yadi kriyā vyavahāra aṅga bhūtāḥ na syāt tadā dharma mātram api na syāt kriyā virahita tvāt khapuṣpa vat iti kutas kriyā rahitam dharma mātram bhaviṣyati tasmāt yadi vyavahāra satyam dharma mātra vat kriyā api abhyupagamyatām atha tattva cintā tadā kriyāvat dharma mātram api na asti iti bhavatā abhyupagamyatām yathā uktam śatake kriyāvān śāśvataḥ na asti na asti sarva gate kriyā niṣkriyaḥ nāstinā tulyaḥ nairātmyam kim na te priyam iti 
[44,vi_45,i]	tasmāt na ayam vidhiḥ bādhakaḥ parasya na api asmākam siddha sādhana doṣaḥ atra āha na eva hi paśyati iti darśanam iti kartṛ sādhanam abhyupagamyate kim tarhi paśyati anena itī darśanam iti karaṇa sādhanam tatas ca ukta doṣa aprasaṅgaḥ yaḥ ca anena darśanena karaṇa bhūtena paśyati sa draṣṭā eṣa ca vidyate vijñānam ātmā vā kartṛ sadbhāvāt ca darśanam api siddham iti ucyate vyākhyātaḥ darśanena eva draṣṭā ca api upagamyatām yathā svam ātmānam darśanam hi ityādinā dūṣaṇam uktam evam draṣṭuḥ api darśana vat dūṣaṇam veditavyam tat yathā svam ātmānam na eva draṣṭā darśanena vipaśyati na paśyati yadā ātmānam katham drakṣyati tad parān ityādi vācyam tasmāt darśana vat draṣṭā api na asti iti siddham 
[45,ii]	atra āha vidyate eva draṣṭā tad karma karaṇa sadbhāvāt iha yat na asti iti na tasya karma karaṇe vidyete tat yathā vandhyā sūnoḥ asti ca draṣṭuḥ karaṇam darśanam draṣṭavyam ca karma tasmāt chettṛ vat vidyamāna karma karaṇaḥ vidyate eva draṣṭā iti ucyate na eva hi draṣṭavya darśane vidyete tad kutas draṣṭā syāt draṣṭu sāpekṣe hi draṣṭavya darśane sa ca nirūttyamāṇaḥ tiraskṛtya draṣṭā na asti atiraskṛtya ca darśanam 
[45,iii]	iha draṣṭā nāma yadi kaścid syāt sa darśana sāpekṣaḥ vā syāt nirapekṣaḥ vā tatra yadi darśana sāpekṣaḥ atiraskṛtya darśanam iṣyate tadā siddhasya vā darśana apekṣā syāt asiddhasya vā tatra siddhaḥ draṣṭā na hi darśanam apekṣate kim siddhasya sataḥ draṣṭuḥ punar darśana apeś ṣā kuryāt na hi siddham punar api sādhyate iti atha asiddhaḥ apekṣeta asiddha tvāt vandhyā suta vat darśanam na apekṣate evam tāvat atiraskṛtya darśanam apekṣya draṣṭā na asti tiraskṛtya api darśana nirapekṣa tvāt iti uktam prāk tat evam tiraskṛtya atiraskṛtya vā darśanam yadā draṣṭā na asti tadā draṣṭavyam darśanam ca eva draṣṭari asati te kutas 
[45,iv_45,vi]	draṣṭari asati nirhetuke draṣṭavya darśane na saṃbhavataḥ iti kutas tad sadbhāvāt draṣṭā prasetsyati atra āha vidyete eva draṣṭavya darśane tad kārya sadbhāvāt tatra pratītya mātā pitarau yathā uktaḥ putra saṃbhavaḥ cakṣū rūpe pratītyā evam uktaḥ vijñāna saṃbhavaḥ iti draṣṭavyam darśanam ca pratītya vijñānam utpadyate trayāṇām saṃnipātāt sa āsrava sparśaḥ sparśa sahajāḥ vedanā tad pratyayā tṛṣṇā iti evam catvāri api bhava aṅgāni draṣṭavya darśana hetukāni vidyante tasmāt kārya sadbhāvāt draṣṭavya darśane vidyete iti 
[45,vii_46,i]	ucyate syātām ete yadi vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayam eva syāt yasmāt draṣṭavya darśana abhāvāt vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayam na asti iti iha draṣṭuḥ abhāvāt draṣṭavya darśane api na staḥ iti uktam atas kutas vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayam vijñāna sparśa vedanā tṛṣṇā ākhyam tasmāt na santi vijñāna ādīni atra āha santi evatāni tad kārya sadbhāvāt iha tṛṣṇā pratyayam upādānam ityādinā upādāna bhava jāti jarā maraṇa ādikam vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayāt utpadyate tasmāt santi vijñāna ādīni tad kārya sadbhāvāt ucyate syuḥ upādāna ādīni yadi vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayam eva syāt yadā tu draṣṭavya darśana abhāvāt vijñāna ādi catuṣṭayam na eva asti tadā upādāna ādīni bhaviṣyanti punar katham na santi upādāna ādīni iti arthaḥ 
[46,ii_46,iii]	idānīm darśana vat śeṣa āyatana vyākhyāna atideśa artham āha vyākhyātam śravaṇam ghrāṇam rasanam sparśanam manaḥ darśanena eva jānīyāt śrotṛ śrotavyaka ādi ca iti uktam hi bhagavatā na cakṣuḥ prekṣate rūpam manaḥ dharmāt na vetti ca etat ta paramam satyam yatra lokaḥ na gāhate sāmagryā darśanam yatra prakāśayati nāyakaḥ prāha upacāra bhūmim tām parama arthasya buddhimān iti 
[46,iv]	tathā cakṣuḥ ca pratītya rūpataḥ cakṣu vijñānam iha upajāyate no cakṣuṣi rūpa niśritam rūpa saṃkrānti na ca eva cakṣuṣi nairātmya aśubhāḥ ca dharmime teṣu ātmā iti śubhāḥ ca kalpitāḥ viparītam asat vikalpitam cakṣu vijñāna tatas api jāyate vijñāna nirodha saṃbhavam vijñāna aupāda vayam vipaśyati na kahiṃci gatam na ca āgatam śūnya māyā upama yogi paśyati 
[46,v_47,i]	tathā ācārya upāli pṛcchāyām sarva sa yogi tu paśyati cakṣuḥ tatra na paśyati pratyaya hīnam na eva ca cakṣu prapaśyati rūpam tena sa yoga viyoga vikalpaḥ āloka samāśrita paśyati cakṣuḥ rūpa manorama citra viśiṣṭam yena ca yoga samāśrita cakṣuḥ tena na paśyati cakṣu kadāci yaḥ api ca śrūyati śabdu manojñaḥ saḥ api ca na antari jātu praviṣṭaḥ saṃkramaṇam na ca labhyati tasya kalpa vaśāt tu samucchritu śabdaḥ iti tathā gītam na nṛtyam api vādya rutam na grāhyam svapna upamāḥ hi ratayaḥ abudha mohanāḥ ca saṃkalpa lālasa gatāḥ abudhā atra nāśam kim kleśa dāsaḥ iva bāla janaḥ bhavāmi iti 
[48,i_48,ii]	atra āha yadi evam cakṣuḥ ādīni indriyāṇi na santi na skandhāḥ apratiṣedhāt tad antargatāni ca indriyāṇi atas tāni api bhaviṣyanti iti ucyate syuḥ eva yadi skandhāḥ syuḥ tatra rūpa skandham adhikṛtya āha rūpa kāraṇa nirmuktam na rūpam upalabhyate rūpeṇa api na nirmuktam dṛśyate rūpa kāraṇam tatra rūpam bhautikam tasya kāraṇam catvāri mahābhūtāni tadvayatiriktam pṛthak bhūtam rūpam rūpa śabda gandha rasa spraṣṭavya ākhyam na upalabhyate ghaṭāt iva paṭaḥ rūpeṇa api na nirmuktam rūpāt pṛthak bhūtam rūpa kāraṇam upalabhyate 
[48,iii_48,iv]	tat etat pratijñā dvayam prasādhayitu kāmaḥ āha rūpa kāraṇa nirmukte rūpe rūpam prasajyate āhetukam na ca asti arthaḥ kaścid āhetukaḥ kvacid yathā ghaṭāt artha antara bhūtaḥ paṭaḥ na ghaṭa hetukaḥ evam rūpa kāraṇa catur mahābhūta vyatirikta bhautikam rūpam iṣyamāṇam na bhūta hetukam syāt na ca asti arthaḥ kaścid āhetukaḥ kvacid tasmāt ahetuka tva doṣa prasaṅgāt na rūpa kāraṇa nirmuktam rūpam abhyupetavyam iti 
[48,v_48,vi]	idānīm rūpeṇa api vinirmuktam yathā rūpa kāraṇam na asti tathā pratipādayan āha rūpeṇa tu vinirmuktam yadi syāt rūpa kāraṇam yadi kārya rūpa vinirmuktam rūpa kāraṇam syāt tadā yathā ghaṭāt kuṇḍam pṛthak siddham ghaṭa hetukam na bhavati evam kāryāt pṛthak bhūtam kāraṇam iṣyamāṇam akāryakam kāraṇam syāt nirhetukam syāt kāraṇasya hi kāraṇa tve kārya pravṛttiḥ hetuḥ kārya nirapekṣāt ca kāraṇāt pṛthak siddhā na asti kārya pravṛttiḥ yat ca akāryakam kāraṇam tat nirhetuka tvāt nara uraga turaga viṣāṇa vat na asti eva iti āha na asti akāryam ca kāraṇam iti 
[48,vii_48,viii]	atha ca idam rūpasya kāraṇam iṣyamāṇam sati vā rūpe kāraṇa tvena iṣyate asati vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha rūpe sati eva rūpasya kāraṇam na upapadyate rūpe asati eva rūpasya kāraṇam na upapadyate sati vā saṃvidyamāne rūpe kim rūpa kāraṇena prayojanam asati asaṃvidyamāne rūpe kim kim rūpa kāraṇena prayojanam kasya vā tad kāraṇam parikalpyate tasmāt asati api rūpe rūpa kāraṇam na upapadyate 
[49,i_49,iii]	atha syāt yadi api evam rūpa kāraṇam na saṃbhavati tathā api kāryam rūpam saṃvidyate sadbhāvāt kāraṇam api bhaviṣyati iti syāt evam yadi kāryam rūpam syāt na tu asti yasmāt niṣkāraṇam punā rūpam na eva na eva upapadyate rūpa kāraṇam yathā na asti tathā uktam asati kāraṇe kutas nirhetukam kāryam rūpam bhavet na eva na eva iti anena sa avadhāraṇena pratiṣedha dvayena ahetuka tvāt asya ati aniṣṭa tām darśayati yatas ca evam rūpam sarvathā vicāryamāṇam na saṃbhavati tasmāt tattva darśī yogī rūpa gatān kāṃścid na vikalpān vikalpayet sa pratighā pratighasa nidarśana anidarśana atīta anāgata nīla pīta ādi vikalpān rūpa ālambanāt na kāṃścid parikalpayitum arhati iti arthaḥ 
[49,iv_49,v]	api ca idam rūpa kāraṇam iṣyamāṇam sadṛśam kāryam niṣpādayet asadṛśam vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha na kāraṇasya sadṛśam kāryam iti upapadyate na kāraṇasya asadṛśam kāryam iti upapadyate tatra rūpa kāraṇam kaṭhina drava uṣṇa tarala svabhāvam bhautikam tu cakṣuḥ ādhyātmikam pañca cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādi āśrayaka rūpa prasāda ātmakam bāhyam tu rūpa ādi āyatana ādikam cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādi grāhya lakṣaṇam na mahābhūta svabhāvam iti atas bhinna lakṣaṇa tvāt nirvāṇa vat kārya kāraṇayoḥ sādṛśyam eva na asti iti na kāraṇasya sadṛśam kāryam iti upapadyate na ca api sadṛśānām śāli bīja ādīnām paraspara kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti atas na kāraṇasya sadṛśam kāryam iti upapadyate tathā api na kāraṇasya asadṛśam kāryam iti upapadyate bhinna lakṣaṇa tvāt nirvāṇa vat eva iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[49,vi_49,vii]	yathā ca idam rūpam vicāryamāṇam sarvathā na upapadyate evam vedanā ādayaḥ api iti atidiśan āha vedanā citta saṃjñānām saṃskārāṇām ca sarvaśas sarveṣām eva bhāvānām rūpeṇa eva samaḥ kramaḥ vedanā ādikam api sarvam rūpa vicāreṇa eva samam yojyam yathā eva hi ekasya dharmasya śūnyatā pratipādayitum iṣṭā mādhyamikena tathā eva sarva dharmāṇām api iti 
[49,viii_50,i]	atas vigrahe yaḥ parīhāram kṛte śūnyatayā vadet sarvam tasya aparihṛtam samam sādhyena jāyate tatra para pakṣa dūṣaṇam vigrahaḥ śūnyatayā kāraṇa bhūtayā rūpam niḥsvabhāvam iti evam sa svabhāva vāde pratiṣiddhe yadi paraḥ parihāram brūyāt vedanā ādayaḥ tāvat santi tadvat rūpam api asti iti tat etat sarvam tasya aparihṛtam bhavati yasmāt vedanā ādīnām api sadbhāvaḥ sādhyena rūpa sadbhāvena samaḥ veditavyaḥ yathā rūpam sva kāraṇāt tattva anyatvena vicāryamāṇam asat evam sparśa pratyayā vedanā vijñāna sahajā saṃjñā avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃskāra pratyayam ca vijñānam sva kāraṇāt sparśa ādeḥ tattva anyatva ādinā vicāryamāṇam na asti iti sarvam etat sādhya samam bhavati yathā vedanā ādayaḥ sādhya samāḥ evam lakṣya lakṣaṇa kārya kāraṇa avaya vya vayava ādayaḥ api sarve eva padārthāḥ rūpeṇa sādhyena samāḥ iti kutas parasya parīhāra saṃbhavet sarvam vacanam asya sādhya samam bhavati iti sarvatra śāstre parīhāreṇa sādhya sama tvam mādhyamikenā grāhaṇīyam iti ācāryaḥ śikṣayati 
[50,ii_50,iii]	yathā ca para pakṣa dūṣaṇe vihi atoyam vidhiḥ evam vyākhyāna kāle api iti āha vyākhyāne yaḥ upālambham kṛte śūnyatayā vadet sarvam tasya anupālabdham samam sādhyena jāyate vyākhyāna kāle api yaḥ śiṣya deśīyaḥ ca udyam upālambham kuryāt tasya api tat ca udyam upālambha ākhyam pūrvavat sādhya samam veditavyam yathā uktam bhāvasya ekasya yaḥ draṣṭā draṣṭā sarvasya sa smṛtaḥ ekasya śūnyatā yā eva sā eva sarvasya śūnyatā iti 
[50,iv_50,v]	ārya gagana gañja samādhi sūtre api ekena dharmeṇa tu sarva dharmān anugacchate māya marīci sādṛśān agrāhya tucchānalikānaśāśvatān saḥ bodhimaṇḍam nacireṇa gacchati iti samādhi rāja sūtre api yathaḥ ñāta tayā ātma saṃjña tathā eva sarvatra peṣitā buddhiḥ sarve ca tad svabhāvāḥ dharma viśuddhāḥ gagana kalpāḥ ekena sarvam jānāti sarvam ekena paśyati kiyat bahu pi bhāvetvā na tasya utpadyate madaḥ iti 
[51,i]	atra āha dhātavaḥ santi pratiṣedha abhāvāt uktam ca bhagavatā ṣaṣ dhātuḥ ayam mahā rāja puruṣa pudgalaḥ ityādi tatas ca pravacana pāṭhāt dhātu vat skandha āyatanāni eva santi iti ucyate syuḥ skandha āyatanāni yadi dhātavaḥ eva syuḥ katham iti āha na ākāśam vidyate kiṃcid pūrvam ākāśa lakṣaṇāt alakṣaṇam prasajyeta syāt pūrvam yadi lakṣaṇāt 
[51,ii_51,iii]	tatra ṣaṭ dhātavaḥ uktāḥ pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśa vijñāna ākhyāḥ tatra ākāśam adhikṛtya ucyate dūṣaṇam svarūpa nirūpaṇāt iha ākāśasya anāvaraṇam lakṣaṇam ucyate yat yasmāt pūrvam ākāśam anāvaraṇa lakṣaṇāt lakṣyam syāt tatra lakṣaṇa pravartanāt anāvaraṇa lakṣaṇāt pūrvam na ākāśam lakṣya rūpam iti yadā ca evam na ākāśam vidyate kiṃcid pūrvam ākāśa lakṣaṇāt alakṣaṇam prasajyeta syāt pūrvam yadi lakṣaṇāt tathā hi alakṣaṇam pravartatām tad abhāve kha puṣpa vat na asti ākāśam iti āha alakṣaṇaḥ na kaścid ca bhāvaḥ saṃvidyate kvacid iti atra āha lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ lakṣye bhavet tad sadbhāvāt lakṣyam api asti iti etat api na asti yasmāt asatya lakṣaṇe bhāve kramatām kuha lakṣaṇam lakṣaṇāt pūrvam alakṣaṇaḥ bhāvaḥ na asti iti uktam tatas ca asati asaṃvidyamāne alakṣaṇe lakṣaṇa rahite bhāve kuha idānīm lakṣaṇaṃpravartatām iti na asti lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ 
[51,iv_51,v]	api ca idam lakṣaṇam pravartamānam sa lakṣaṇe vā pravarteta alakṣaṇe vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha na alakṣaṇe lakṣaṇasya pravṛttiḥ na sa lakṣaṇe sa lakṣaṇa alakṣaṇābhyām na api anyatra pravartate tatra alakṣaṇe khara viṣāṇa vat na lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ sa lakṣaṇe api bhāve na lakṣaṇa pravṛtti rūpapadyate prayojana abhāvāt kim hi lakṣaṇavataḥ prasiddhasya bhāvasya punar lakṣaṇa kṛtyam syāt iti anavasthāḥ atiprasaṅgaḥ ca evam syāt na hi asau kadācid na sa lakṣaṇaḥ syāt iti sadā eva lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ prasajyeta na ca etat iṣṭam tasmāt sa lakṣaṇe api bhāve na lakṣaṇa pravṛtti parupadyate prayojana abhāvāt tatra evam syāt sa lakṣaṇa alakṣaṇābhyām anyatra pravartiṣyate iti ucyate 
[51,vi_51,vii]	sa lakṣaṇa alakṣaṇābhyām na api anyatra pravartate kim kāraṇam asadbhāvāt yadi sa lakṣaṇaḥ na alakṣaṇaḥ atha alakṣaṇaḥ na sa lakṣaṇaḥ atas sa lakṣaṇaḥ ca alakṣaṇaḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham etat na ca vipratiṣiddham saṃbhavati tasmāt asaṃbhavāt eva sa lakṣaṇe ca alakṣaṇe ca lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ na upapadyate iti 
[52,i_52,iv]	atha api syāt yadi api na lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ tathā api lakṣyam asti iti etat api na asti yasmāt lakṣaṇa asaṃpravṛttau ca na lakṣyam upapadyate yadā lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ eva na asti tadā katham lakṣyam syāt na eva saṃbhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ atra āha lakṣaṇa pravṛttiḥ tvayā niṣiddhāḥ na tu lakṣaṇam tatas ca vidyate lakṣyam lakṣaṇa sadbhāvāt ucyate lakṣyasya anupapattau ca lakṣaṇasya api asaṃbhavaḥ lakṣaṇa asaṃpravṛttau ca na lakṣyam upapadyate iti pratipāditam tadā lakṣyasya anupapattau ca lakṣaṇasya api asaṃbhavaḥ nirāśraya tvāt 
[52,v_52,vii]	yadā ca evam lakṣaṇam na asti tadā lakṣaṇa sadbhāvāt vidyate lakṣyam iti yat uktam tat na yatas ca etat evam tasmāt na vidyate lakṣyam lakṣaṇam na eva vidyate iti nigamanam atra āha yadya api lakṣya lakṣaṇe na staḥ tathā api ākāśam asti bhāva rūpam ca bhavat ākāśa lakṣyam lakṣaṇam vā syāt tasmāt lakṣya lakṣaṇe api ṣṭaḥ iti etat api ayuktam iti āha lakṣya lakṣaṇa nirmuktaḥ na eva bhāvaḥ api vidyate lakṣya lakṣaṇe yathā na staḥ tathā uktam prāk yadā anayoḥ abhāvaḥ tadā lakṣya lakṣaṇa rahita tvāt ākāśa kusuma vat na asti ākāśam 
[52,viii_52,ix]	yadi ākāśam bhāvaḥ na bhavati abhāvaḥ tarhi astu etat api na asti yasmāt avidyamāne bhāve ca kasya abhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati yadā ākāśam bhāvaḥ na bhavati tadā bhāvasya asattve kasya abhāvaḥ kalpyatām vakṣyati hi bhāvasya ced aprasiddhiḥ abhāvaḥ na eva sidhyati bhāvasya hi anyathābhāvam abhāvam bruvate janāḥ iti 
[52,x_53,i]	tasmāt bhāva abhāvāt abhāvaḥ api ākāśam na saṃbhavati rūpa abhāvaḥ ca ākāśam iti vyavasthāpyate yadi api rūpam syāt tadā rūpa abhāvaḥ ākāśam iti syāt yadā ca yathā uktena nyāyena rūpam eva na asti tadā kasya abhāvaḥ ākāśam syāt atra āha vidyete eva bhāva abhāvau tad parīkṣaka sadbhāvāt asti ca bhavān bhāva abhāvayoḥ parīkṣakaḥ yaḥ eva āha avidyamāne bhāve ca kasya abhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt bhavataḥ bhāva abhāva parīkṣakasya sadbhāvāt parīkṣyau api bhāva abhāvau vidyete iti ucyate etat api ayuktam yasmāt bhāva abhāva vidharmā ca bhāva abhāvam avaiti kaḥ 
[53,ii_53,iii]	syātām bhāva abhāvau yadi tadā tayoḥ parīkṣakaḥ bhāvaḥ va syāt abhāvaḥ vā yadi bhāvaḥ iṣyate tasya lakṣya lakṣaṇa nirmuktaḥ na eva bhāvaḥ api vidyate iti uktam dūṣaṇam atha abhāvaḥ avidyamāne bhāve ca kasya abhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati iti atra uktam etat duṣaṇam na ca bhāva abhāva visadṛśa dharmā kaścid tṛtīyaḥ padārthaḥ asti yaḥ anayoḥ avagamakaḥ iti na asti bhāva abhāvayoḥ parīkṣakaḥ atas eva uktam bhagavatā bhāvān abhāvān iti yaḥ prajānati sa sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate yaḥ sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate saḥ ānimittam bhajate samādhim iti tathā yaḥ api ca cintayi śūnyaka dharmān saḥ api kumārga papannaku balaḥ akṣara kīrtita śūnyaka dharmāḥ te ca anakṣara akṣaraḥ uktāḥ śānta paśānta yaḥ cintayi dharmān saḥ api ca cinta na jātu na bhūtaḥ citta vitarkaṇa sarvi papañcāḥ sūkṣma acintiya budhyatha dharmān iti vistaraḥ 
[53,iv]	idānīm pratipāditam artham nigamayan āha tasmāt na bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ na lakṣyam na api lakṣaṇam ākāśam iti yathā ca ākāśam evam ākāśa samāḥ dhātavaḥ pañca ye pare pṛthivī ādi dhātavaḥ ye pañca pare avaśiṣyante te api ākāśa vat bhāva abhāva lakṣya lakṣaṇa parikalpa svarūpa rahitāḥ parijñeyāḥ iti arthaḥ 
[54,i]	tat evam padārthānām svabhāve vyavasthite avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana tayā anādi saṃsāra abhyasta tayā bhāva abhāva ādi viparīta darśanāḥ nirvāṇa anugāmi aviparītanaiḥ svabhāvya darśana sat mārga paribhraṣṭāḥ astitvam ye tu paśyanti nāstitvam ca alpabuddhayaḥ bhāvānām te na paśyanti draṣṭavya upaśamam śivam 
[54,ii]	draṣṭavya upaśamam śiva lakṣaṇam sarva kalpanā jāla rahitam jñāna jñeya nivṛtti svabhāvam śivam parama artha svabhāvam parama artham ajaram amarama prapañcam nirvāṇam śūnyatā svabhāvam te na paśyanti manda buddhi tayā astitvam nāstitvam ca abhiniviṣṭāḥ santaḥ iti yathā uktam ārya ratna āvalyām nāstikaḥ durgatim yāti sugatim yāti anāstikaḥ yathābhūta parijñānāt mokṣam advaya niśritaḥ iti 
[54,iii_54,iv]	ārya samādhi rāje ca uktam bhagavatā asti iti na asti iti ume api antā śuddhī aśuddhi iti ime api antā tasmāt ume anta vivarjayitvā madhye api sthānam na karoti paṇḍitaḥ asti iti na asti iti vivādaḥ eṣaḥ śuddhī aśuddhi iti ayam vivādaḥ vivāda prāptyā na dukham praśāmyate avivāda prāptyā ca duḥkham nirudhyate iti tasmāt asaṃbhavaḥ eva yat sāṃsārikeṇa mārgeṇa nirvāṇam adhigamyate iti 
[55,i]	atra āha vidyante eva skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ kutas tad āśraya saṃkleśa upalabdheḥ iha yat na asti na tad āśraya saṃkleśa upalabdhiḥ asti bandhyā duhituḥ iva vandhyā sūnoḥ santi ca rāga ādayaḥ kleśāḥ saṃkleśa nibandhanam yathā uktam bhagavatā bālaḥ bhikṣave aśrutavān pṛthagjanaḥ prajñaptim anupatitaḥ cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭvā saumanasya sthānīyāni abhiniviśate saḥ abhiniviṣṭaḥ san rāgam utpādayati raktaḥ san rāga jam dveṣa jam moha jam karma abhisaṃskaroti kāyena vācā manasā iti vistaraḥ ucyate syuḥ skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ yadi rāga ādayaḥ eva kleśāḥ syuḥ iha ayam rāgaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ bāla pṛthagjanaiḥ sati rakte nare parikalpyeta asati vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha rāgāt yadi bhavet pūrvam raktaḥ rāga tiraskṛtaḥ tam pratītya bhavet rāgaḥ rakte rāgaḥ bhavet sati 
[55,ii]	tatra rāgaḥ saktiḥ adhyavasānam saṅgaḥ abhiniveśaḥ iti paryāyāḥ raktaḥ rāga āśrayaḥ sa yadi raktaḥ rāgāt pūrvam rāga tiraskṛtaḥ rāga rahitaḥ bhavet tadā tam rāga tiraskṛtam raktam pratītya rāgaḥ bhavet evam sakti rakte rāgaḥ bhavet iti yuktam na tu evam saṃbhavati yad rāga rahitaḥ raktaḥ syāt arhatām api rāga prasaṅgāt 
[55,iii_55,v]	yadi evam sati rakte na rāgaḥ asati tarhi rakte rāgaḥ astu etat api ayuktam iti āha rakte asati punā rāgaḥ kutas eva bhaviṣyati yadā sati rakte rāgaḥ na asti tadā katham asati rakte nirāśrayaḥ rāgaḥ setsyati na hi asati phale tat pakva tā saṃbhavati iti atra āha yadi api tvayā rāgaḥ niṣiddhaḥ tathā api raktaḥ asti apratiṣedhāt na ca rāgam antareṇa raktaḥ yuktaḥ tasmāt ayam api asti iti ucyate syāt rāgaḥ yadi raktaḥ syāt yasmāt ayam raktaḥ iṣyamāṇaḥ sati vā rāge parikalpyeta asati vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha sati vā asati vā rāge rakte api eṣa samaḥ kramaḥ 
[55,vi_55,vii]	tatra yadi sati rāge raktaḥ parikalpyeta tatra api eṣaḥ eva rāga anupapatti kramaḥ anantara uktaḥ rakte api tulyaḥ raktāt yadi bhavet pūrvam rāgaḥ rakta tiraskṛtaḥ ityādi atha asati rāge raktaḥ iṣyate etat api ayuktam yasmāt rāge asati punā raktaḥ kutas eva bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt raktaḥ api na asti rāga rakta abhāvāt ca skandha ādayaḥ api na santi iti 
[56,i_56,iii]	atra āha na eva hi rāga raktayoḥ paurvāparyeṇa saṃbhavaḥ yatas idam dūṣaṇam syāt kim tarhi rāga raktayoḥ saha eva udbhavaḥ citta saha bhūtena rāgeṇa hi cittam rajyate tat ca raktam iti atas vidyete eva rāga raktau iti ucyate evam api saha eva punar udbhūtiḥ na yuktā rāga raktayoḥ saha utpādaḥ api na yuktaḥ rāga raktayoḥ yasmāt bhavetām rāga raktau hi nirapekṣau parasparam sahabhāvāt savya itara go viṣāṇa vat iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[56,iv_56,viii]	api ca anayaḥ rāga raktayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ eka tve parikalpyeta pṛthaktve vā tatra yadi ekatve tat na yujyate yasmāt na ekatve sahabhāvaḥ asti kasmāt punar na asti iti āha na tena eva hi tat saha na hi rāgasva ātmā rāgāt avyatiriktaḥ rāgeṇa saha iti vyapadiśyate idānīm pṛthaktve api sahabhāva abhāvam āha pṛthaktve sahabhāvaḥ atha kutas eva bhaviṣyati na hi pṛthak bhūtayoḥ āloka andhakārayoḥ saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ vā sahabhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti 
[56,ix_56,x]	kim ca anyat eka tve sahabhāvaḥ ced syāt sahāyam vinā api saḥ pṛthaktve sahabhāvaḥ ced syāt sahāyam vinā api saḥ yadi eka tve sahabhāvaḥ syāt tadā yatra yatra ekatvam tatra tatra sahabhāvaḥ iti ekasya api sahabhāvaḥ syāt pṛthaktve api sahabhāve iṣyamāṇe yatra yatra pṛthaktvam tatra tatra sahabhāvaḥ iti aśva ādi vyatiriktasya pṛthak avasthitasya goḥ asahāyasya sahabhāvaḥ syāt 
[56,xi_56,xii]	kim ca pṛthaktve sahabhāvaḥ ca yadi kim rāga raktayoḥ siddhaḥ pṛthak pṛthagbhāvaḥ sahabhāvaḥ yatas tayoḥ pṛthaktve sahabhāvaḥ ca rāga raktayoḥ parikalpyate kim anayoḥ siddhaḥ pṛthak pṛthagbhāvaḥ kim rāga nirapekṣaḥ raktaḥ siddhaḥ yatas tayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ syāt pṛthak pṛthak siddhayoḥ eva hi gavāśvayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na tu evam rāga raktau pṛthak pṛthak siddhau iti na asti anayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ 
[56,xiii_57,i]	athavā pṛthak pṛthak asiddhayoḥ na sahabhāvaḥ iti kṛtvā siddhaḥ pṛthak pṛthagbhāvaḥ yadi vā rāga raktayoḥ parikalpyate bhavatā kim idānīm sahabhāvena akiṃcitkareṇa parikalpitena iti āha sahabhāvam kim artham tu parikalpayase tayoḥ rāga raktayoḥ siddhayartham sahabhāvaḥ parikalpyate sa ca pṛthak pṛthak asiddhayoḥ na asti iti pṛthak pṛthak siddhiḥ abhyupagamyate tvayā nanu evam sati siddha tvāt kim anayoḥ saha bhāvena kṛtyam 
[57,ii_57,iv]	atha pṛthak na sidhyati iti evam sahabhāvam vikāṅkṣasi pṛthak pṛthak rāga raktayoḥ siddhiḥ na asti iti kṛtvā yadi anayoḥ sahabhāvam icchasi sa ca pṛthak pṛthak asiddhayoḥ na asti iti sahabhāva prasiddhayartha pṛthaktvam bhūyas icchasi nanu evam sati itaretara āśrayāyām siddhau sthitāyām kasya idānīm siddhau satyām kasya siddhiḥ astu 
[57,v_57,vi]	yāvatā pṛthak bhāva aprasiddheḥ ca sahabhāvaḥ na sidhyati katamasmin pṛthagbhāve sahabhāvam sati icchasi na asti eva sa pṛthak bhāvaḥ sahabhāva anapekṣaḥ yasmin pṛthagbhāve sati sahabhāva siddhiḥ syāt iti asaṃbhāvayan āha katamasmin pṛthagbhāve sahabhāvam sati icchasi 
[57,vii_57,viii]	tat evam yathā udita vicāra parāmarśena rāga raktayoḥ asiddhim nigamayan āha evam raktena rāgasya siddhiḥ na saha na asaha iti yathā ca rāga raktayoḥ na paurvāparyeṇa siddhiḥ na api saha bhāvena evam sarva bhāvānām api iti atidiśan āha rāga vat sarva dharmāṇām siddhiḥ na saha na asaha iti dveṣa dviṣṭa moha mūḍha ādīnām rāga rakta vat asiddhiḥ yojyate atas eva uktam bhagavatā 
[57,ix_58,i]	yaḥ rajyeta yatra vā rajyeta yena vā rajyeta yaḥ duṣyeta yatra vā duṣyeta yena vā duṣyeta yaḥ muhyeta yatra vā muhyeta yena vā muhyeta sa tam dharma na samanupaśyati tam dharma na upalabhate sa tam dharmam asam anupaśyan anupalabhamānaḥ araktaḥ aduṣṭaḥ amūḍhaḥ aviparyasta cittaḥ samāhitaḥ iti ucyate tīrṇaḥ pāragaḥ iti ucyate kṣema prāptaḥ iti ucyate abhaya prāptaḥ iti ucyate yāvat kṣīṇa āsravaḥ iti ucyate niḥkleśaḥ vaśībhūtaḥ su vimukta cittaḥ su vimukta prajñaḥ ājāneyaḥ mahābhāgaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ kṛta karaṇīyaḥ apahata bhāraḥ anuprāpta svaka arthaḥ parikṣīṇa bhava saṃyojanaḥ samyak ājñā su vimukta cittaḥ sarva cetaḥ vaśitā parama pārami prāptaḥ śramaṇaḥ iti ucyate iti vistaraḥ tathā ye rāga doṣa mada moha sabhāva jñātvā saṃkalpa hetu janitam vitatha pravṛttam na vikalpayanti na virāgam api iha teṣām āśu sarva bhava bhāva vibhāvitānām 
[59,i]	atra āha vidyante eva saṃskṛta svabhāvāḥ skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ utpāda ādi saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa sadbhāvāt uktam hi bhagavatā trīṇi imāni saṃskṛtasya saṃskṛta lakṣaṇāni saṃskṛtasya bhikṣavaḥ utpādaḥ api prajñāyate vyayaḥ api sthiti anyathātvam api iti na ca avidyamānasya khara viṣāṇasya iva jāti ādi lakṣaṇam asti tasmāt saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa upadeśāt vidyante eva skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ iti ucyate syuḥ skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ saṃskṛta svabhāvāḥ tāvakena matena yadi jāti ādi lakṣaṇam eva bhavet iha ayam utpādaḥ saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tvena iṣyamāṇaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ vā tad lakṣaṇa tvena iṣyate asaṃskṛtaḥ vā tatra yadi saṃskṛtaḥ utpādaḥ tatra yuktā tri lakṣaṇī 
[59,ii]	trayāṇām lakṣaṇānām samāhāraḥ tri lakṣaṇī iyam ca utpāda sthiti bhaṅga samāhāra svabhāva sarva saṃskṛta avyabhicāriṇī iti kṛtvā yadi utpādaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ iti parikalpyate tadā utpāde api tri lakṣaṇī prasajyate tatas ca rūpa ādi vat lakṣya tvam utpādasya syāt na saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tvam atha utpāde api tri lakṣaṇī na iṣyate tadā tri lakṣaṇī rahita tvāt ākāśa vat saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tvam asya avahīyate iti āha atha asaṃskṛtaḥ utpādaḥ katham saṃskṛta lakṣaṇam iti na etat saṃskṛta lakṣaṇam iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[59,iii_59,iv]	api ca ime utpāda ādayaḥ saṃskṛtasya lakṣaṇa tvena parikalpyamānāḥ vyastāḥ vā pṛthak vā lakṣaṇa tvena parikalpyeran samastāḥ vā saha bhūtā vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha utpāda ādyāḥ trayaḥ vyastāḥ na alam lakṣaṇa karmaṇi saṃskṛtasya samastāḥ syuḥ ekatra katham ekadā tatra vyastāḥ lakṣaṇa karmaṇi na yujyante yadi utpāda kāle sthiti bhaṅgau na syātām tadā sthiti bhaṅga rahitasya ākāśasya iva saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tvena anupapadya eva utpādaḥ atha sthiti kāle utpāda bhaṅgau na staḥ tadā tat rahitasya sthitiḥ syāt utpāda bhaṅga rahitaḥ ca padārthaḥ na asti eva iti na asya avidyamānasya kha puṣpa vat sthitiḥ yujyate kim ca sthiti yuktasya paścāt anitya tayā api yogaḥ na syāt tad virodhi dharma ākrānta tvāt atha syāt pūrvam śāśvataḥ bhūtvā paścāt aśāśvataḥ iti na ca eka padārthaḥ śāśvataḥ ca aśāśvataḥ ca yuktaḥ iti na utpāda bhaṅga rahitasya sthitiḥ tathā yadi bhaṅga kāle sthiti utpādau na syātām evam api anutpannasya sthiti rahitasya khapuṣpasya vināśaḥ api na asti iti evam tāvat utpāda ādayaḥ vyastāḥ na alam lakṣaṇa karmaṇi na alam na paryāptāḥ iti arthaḥ 
[59,v_60,i]	idānīm samastāḥ api na yujyante iti āha samastāḥ syuḥ ekatra katham ekadā ekatra padārthe ekasmin kāle paraspara viruddha tvāt rāga vairāgya vat āloka andhakāra vat vā na yujyante iti abhiprāyaḥ yasmin eva kṣaṇe padārthaḥ jāyate tasmin eva tiṣṭhati vinaśyati ca iti kaḥ sa cetāḥ pratipadyeta tasmāt samastānām api utpāda ādīnām saṃskṛtasya lakṣaṇa karmaṇi na asti sāmarthyam 
[60,ii_60,iii]	atha yat uktam yadi saṃskṛtaḥ utpādaḥ ityādi tena yadi utpāda ādīnām tri lakṣaṇī prāptā prasaktā tatas kaḥ doṣaḥ atha asaṃskṛtaḥ evam api adoṣaḥ iti ucyate utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām anyat saṃskṛta lakṣaṇam asti ced anavasthā evam na asti ced te na saṃskṛtāḥ nanu ca pakṣa dvaye api vihitaḥ eva doṣaḥ tatra kim punar ukta abhidhānena iti satya muktaḥ doṣaḥ sa khalu na ācāryeṇa kim tarhi vṛtti kāreṇa atha pūrva pratijñātam eva dūṣaṇa antara abhidhānena spaṣṭīkaraṇa artham punar ācāryaḥ abhihitavān yadi utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām anyat utpāda ādikam saṃskṛta lakṣaṇam iṣyate tadā teṣām api anyat teṣām api anyat iti aparyavasāna doṣaḥ syāt sati ca aparyavasāna doṣe kim pūrvam syāt yatas uttara kālam aparam bhavet iti vyavasthā bhāvāt asaṃbhavaḥ evam utpāda ādīnām iti abhiprāyaḥ athavā pūrvam mukhya tvāt utpādasya eva dūṣaṇam uktam adhunā tu sāmānyena iti na asti ced te na saṃskṛtāḥ iti gata artham etat 
[60,iv]	atra āhuḥ sāṃmitīyāḥ santi ca utpāda ādīnām utpāda ādayaḥ na ca anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ lakṣaṇa anulakṣaṇānām paraspara niṣpādaka tvāt yasmāt iha saṃskṛta dharmaḥ kuśalaḥ kliṣṭaḥ vai utpadyamānaḥ ātmanā pañcadaśaḥ utpadyate sa dharmaḥ tasya ca utpādaḥ samanvāgamaḥ sthitiḥ jarā anitya tā yadi asau dharmaḥ kliṣṭaḥ bhavati tasya mithyā vimuktiḥ atha śubhaḥ tasya samyak vimuktiḥ yadi nairyāṇikaḥ bhavati tasya nairyāṇika tā atha anairyāṇikaḥ tasya anairyāṇika tā iti eṣa parivāraḥ idānīm utpāda sya aparaḥ utpādaḥ yāvat anaiḥ yāṇika tānaiḥ yāṇikatā iti eṣa parivārasya parivāraḥ tatra yaḥ ayam maulaḥ utpāda saḥ ātmānam vihāya anyān caturdaśa dharmān janayati utpāda utpāda saṃjñakaḥ tu anulakṣaṇa bhūtaḥ utpādaḥ maulam eva utpādam janayati evam yāvat anaiḥ yāṇika tā caturdaśa dharmāt na niryāṇayati na tat nirvāṇam prāpayati iti arthaḥ anairyāṇika tā naiḥ yāṇika tā tu na niryāṇayati tat evam utpāda ādīnām anavasthām pariharan āha utpāda utpādaḥ utpādaḥ mūla utpādasya kevalam utpāda utpāda sutpādaḥ maulaḥ janayate punar 
[60,v]	dvividhaḥ hi utpādaḥ ekaḥ maulaḥ utpādaḥ aparaḥ ca utpāda utpāda saṃjñakaḥ utpādasya utpādaḥ iti kṛtvā tatra yaḥ ayam utpāda utpāda saṃjñakaḥ utpādaḥ sa mūla utpādasya kevalam utpādakaḥ tam ca idānīm utpāda upāda ākhyam utpādam maulaḥ utpādaḥ janayati tat evam paraspara nirvartanāt asti ca tri lakṣaṇī utpāda ādīnām na ca anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ iti 
[61,i_61,ii]	atra ucyate utpāda utpādaḥ utpādaḥ mūla utpādasya te yadi maulena ajanitaḥ tam te sa katham janayiṣyati yadi tava utpādasya utpādaḥ mūla utpādasya janakaḥ iti matam sa katham idānīm maulena utpādena anutpāditaḥ san utpāda utpādaḥ maulam janayiṣyati 
[61,iii_61,iv]	atha manyase utpāditaḥ eva maulena utpādena utpāda utpādaḥ maulam janayiṣyati etat api asat iti āha sa te maulena janitaḥ maulam janayate yadi maulaḥ sa tena ajanitaḥ tam utpādayate katham saḥ utpāda utpāda saṃjñakaḥ utpādaḥ maulena janitaḥ yadi maulam janayati sa maulaḥ utpāda utpādena ajanitaḥ avidyamānaḥ katham utpāda utpādam janayiṣyati tasmāt maulena janitaḥ san utpāda utpādaḥ maulam janayati ite na yujyate tatas ca paraspara nirvartya nirvartaka tva abhāvāt saḥ eva anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ iti na asti utpādaḥ 
[61,v_61,vi]	atra āha utpadyamānaḥ eva mūla utpādaḥ utpāda utpādam utpādayati saḥ eva utpāda utpādaḥ mūla utpādam janayiṣyati iti ucyate ayam utpadyamānaḥ te kāmam utpādayet imam yadi imam utpādayitum ajātaḥ śaknuyāt ayam kāma mayam mūla utpādaḥ utpadyamānaḥ utpādayet utpādam yadi ayam eva ajātaḥ śaknuyāt aparama jātam utpādayitum utpadyamānaḥ hi nāma anāgataḥ sa ca ajātaḥ katham utpādayiṣyati iti na yuktam eva etat iti abhiprāyaḥ evam utpāda utpāde api vācyam 
[61,vii_61,viii]	atra āha na eva hi utpādasya aparaḥ utpādaḥ asti yatas anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ syāt kim tarhi pradīpaḥ sva para ātmānau saṃprakāśayitā yathā utpādaḥ sva para ātmānau ubhau utpādayet tathā yathā pradīpaḥ prakāśa svabhāva tvāt ātmānam prakāśayati ghaṭa ādīn ca evam utpādaḥ api utpāda svabhāva tvāt ātmānam utpādayiṣyati param ca iti 
[61,ix_62,i]	ucyate syāt etat evam yadi pradīpaḥ sva para ātmānau saṃprakāśayet na ca evam yasmāt pradīpe na andhakāraḥ asti yatra ca asau pratiṣṭhitaḥ kim prakāśayati dīpaḥ prakāśaḥ hi tamaḥ vadhaḥ iha prakāśaḥ nāma tamasaḥ vadhaḥ tamaḥ ca pradīpasva ātmani tāvat na saṃbhavati virodhāt yattamaḥ nighnataḥ sva ātma prakāśa tvam syāt na ca api pradīpaḥ yatra deśe tiṣṭhati tatra tamaḥ asti yattamaḥ nighnataḥ pradīpasya para prakāśaka tvam syāt atas api na asti pradīpasya sva para ātma prakāśaka tvam yadā ca evam tadā pradīpa vat utpādasya sva para ātmā utpādaka tvam na saṃbhaviṣyati iti ayuktam etat 
[62,ii]	atra āha yat etat uktam pradīpe na andhakāraḥ asti iti etat asati andhakāra dhāte yuktam eva vaktum yasmāt tu utpadyamānena eva pradīpena tamaḥ nihatam tatra pradīpe na andhakāraḥ asti yatra ca pradīpaḥ asti tatra api andhakāraḥ na asti iti yujyate yadi pradīpena na andhakāra dhātar kṛtaḥ tadā anutpanne iva pradīpe utpanne api ghaṭa ādayaḥ na upalabhyeran andhakāra ghāta abhāvāt prāc avasthām iva tasmāt asti eva andhakāra ghāta lakṣaṇam prakāśanam pradīpasya tat ca anena utpadyamānena pradīpena kṛtam iti ucyate katham utpadyamānena pradīpena tamaḥ hatam na utpadyamānaḥ hi tamaḥ pradīpaḥ prāpnute yadā 
[62,iii]	iha āloka andhakārayoḥ yaugapadya abhāvāt prāpteḥ abhāvaḥ yadā ca evam prāpteḥ abhāvaḥ tadā katham kena prakāreṇa idānīm utpadyamānena pradīpena tamaḥ hatam iti yuktam parikalpayitum yasmāt ca evam utpadyamāna pradīpaḥ tamaḥ na prāpnoti tasmāt na eva aprāpta tvāt pradīpaḥ kiṃcid api prakāśayati iti avasīyatām 
[62,iv_62,v]	atha manyase yathā aprāptām eva avidyām jñānam nihanti aprāptam eva rūpam cakṣuḥ paśyati aprāptam eva ayaḥ ayaskāntaḥ maṇiḥ ākarṣati evam eva aprāptam eva andhakāram pradīpaḥ nihaniṣyati iti etat api asāram iti āha aprāpya eva pradīpena yadi vā nihatam tamaḥ ihasthaḥ sarva loka stham sa tamaḥ nihaniṣyati yadi aprāpya eva pradīpena tamaḥ nihatam evam sati ihasthaḥ eva pradīpaḥ sarva loka stham tamaḥ nihaniṣyati aprāpta tvāt samīpa stham iva iti abhiprāyaḥ etena nyāyena jñānena avidyā ghātaḥ cakṣuṣā rūpa darśanam ayaskānta maṇinā ayaākarṣaṇam iva iti evam ādikam sādhya samam jñeyam 
[62,vi]	atha aprāptau api satyām ayaskānta maṇi prabhṛtīnām yogya deśa avasthānām eva sva kārya kṛtvam debha viṣyati iti ced tat api na yuktam aprāptau hi satyām viprakṛṣṭa deśa antara avasthita vat avyavahita śāntara avasthita vat ca aprāpta tvāt yogya deśa avasthitānām api yogya deśa avasthita tvam na yuktam iti kutas yogya deśa avasthitānām sva kārya kṛt tvam prasetsyati 
[63,i_63,ii]	dṛṣṭam etat lokataḥ iti ced na etat evam yathā hi bhavān parikalpayati na tathā loke dṛṣṭam yasmāt na lokaḥ prāpti aprāpti cintām evam ādau viṣaye avatārya pradīpa ādīnām prakāśaka tva ādikam kalpayati yathā uditam tu vicāram anavatārya pradīpena tamaḥ hatam cakṣuṣā rūpa darśanam ayaskānta maṇinā ayaa ākarṣaṇam ityādi icchati paśyatu vā loke evam tattva vicāra kāle tu lokasya aprāmāṇyāt na tena bādhā śakyate kartum evam tāvat aprāpya prakāśanam ayuktam prāptau api viṣaya ādi grahaṇam ayuktam eva prāptiḥ hi eka tve sati bhavati yadā ca eka tvam tadā sva rūpa vat darśana ākarṣaṇa ādikam na asti yadi api ca iyam prāpti aprāpti ādi cintā laukika vyavahāre na avatarati iti nirupapattika tvena mṛṣā artha tvāt asya tathā api tattva vicāre avatāryā mā bhūt paramārthataḥ api nirupapattika pakṣa abhyupagamaḥ iti alam prasaṅgena 
[63,iii_63,iv]	yadi ca sva para ātmānau pradīpaḥ prakāśayati iti parikalpyate tvayā tamasaḥ api tarhi pratipakṣa bhūtasya sva para ātmanoḥ pracchādanam prakalpyatam iti āha pradīpaḥ sva para ātmānau saṃprakāśayate yadi tamaḥ api sva para ātmānau chādayiṣyati asaṃśayam pratidvandvi tvāt pradīpa vat tamaḥ api sva para ātma gatam vyāpāram kariṣyati tatas ca para vat ātmānam api chādayiṣyati yadi ca ātmānam chādayet tamaḥ tasya eva anupalabdhiḥ syāt ghaṭa ādi vat tamasā pracchādita tvāt atas eva uktam ārya upāli pṛcchāyām iha sāsani sūramaṇīye pravrajathā gṛhiliṅga jahitvā phalavantu bhaviṣyatha śreṣṭhaḥ eṣu nideśitu kāruṇikena pravrajitvā gṛhiliṅga jahitvā sarva phalasya bhaviṣyati prāptiḥ puna dharma sabhāva tulitvā sarva phalāna phalāna ca prāptiḥ alabhanta phalam tatha prāptim āścariyam puna jāyati teṣām aho atikāruṇikaḥ narasiṃhaḥ suṣṭhupadeśita yukti jinena iti 
[64,i]	tathā ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre yathā hi dīpaḥ layane cirasya kṛtaḥ hi gehe puruṣeṇa kenacid tatra andhakārasya na bhoti evam cira sthitaḥ na aham itas gamiṣye tamondhakārasya na śaktiḥ asti kṛte pradīpe na vigacchanāya pratītya dīpam ca vinaśyate tamaḥ ubhayam pi śūnyam na ca kim ca manyati jñānam tathā ārya pratītya na āsravam ajñāna kleśa upacitam vigacchati saṃparka teṣām na kadāci vidyate jñānasya kleśasya ca nityakālam jñānam na kalpa iti añānu naḥ bhavet jñānam pratītya eva vinaśyate tamaḥ bhayam pi agrāhya kha puṣpa saṃnibham jñānam tathā ājñānu bhayam pi śūnyam iti 
[64,ii_64,iii]	kim ca anyat iha ayam utpādaḥ yadi ātmānam utpādayet saḥ utpannaḥ vā sva ātmānam utpādayet anutpannaḥ vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha anutpannaḥ ayam utpādaḥ sva ātmānam janayet katham atha utpannaḥ janayate jāte kim janyate punar yadi anutpannaḥ utpādaḥ sva ātmānam utpādayet maṇḍūka jaṭā śiromaṇiḥ api ātmānam utpādayet atha utpannaḥ utpādayet kim utpannasya apareṇa utpādena prayojanam iti evam tāvat utpādaḥ ātmānam na utpādayati 
[64,iv_65,i]	idānīm param api yathā na utpādayati tathā pratipādayan āha na utpadyamānam na utpannam na anutpannam kathaṃcana utpadyate tathā ākhyātam gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ yadi hi kiṃcid utpadyeta tad utpādaḥ utpādayet na tu kiṃcid utpadyate adhva traye api utpāda asaṃbhavāt etat ca gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ prāk eva uktam tatra yathā gatam na gamyate atīta vartamānayoḥ virodhāt na api agatam gamyate anāgata vartamānayoḥ virodhāt na api gamyamānam gamyate gatāgata vyatirikta gamyamāna anupalambhāt iti uktam evam utpadyamānaḥ bhāvaḥ na utpadyate utpanna an utpanna vyatirekeṇa utpadyamāna abhāvāt utpannaḥ api na utpadyate atīta vartamānayoḥ virodhāt utpannaḥ iti uparata utpatti kriyaḥ ucyate utpadyate iti vartamāna kriyā āviṣṭaḥ tatas ca utpannaḥ utpadyate iti ucyamāne atīta vartamānayoḥ eka kālatā syāt anutpannaḥ api na utpadyate anāgata vartamānayoḥ virodhāt tasmāt utpādaḥ param utpādayati iti na yuktam 
[65,ii]	atra āha utpadyamānam eva utpadyate na utpannam na api anutpannam iti atha manyase utpanna anutpanna vyatirekeṇa utpadyamāna asaṃbhavāt na utpadyamānam utpadyate iti etat ca na asti yasmāt iha utpatti kriyā yuktam utpadyamānam iti vyapadiśyate tasmāt utpattau satyām utpattim pratītya utpadyamāna siddheḥ utpadyamānam eva utpadyate tat ca utpadyamānam utpādaḥ utpādayati iti ucyate utpadyamānam utpattau idam na kramate yadā katham utpadyamānam tu pratītya utpattim ucyate 
[65,iii]	yat uktam utpattim pratītya utpadyamānam bhavati tat ca utpadyate iti nanu viśeṣate etat vaktavyam syāt asya utpattim pratītya idam nāma utpadyamānam bhavati iti na ca evam ucyate na hi tat utpadyamānam viśeṣataḥ nirdhārayitum śakyate idam tat utpadyamānam iti anutpanna tvāt tad nimitta grahaṇataḥ tatas ca utpadyamānā asaṃbhavāt utpatti kriyā api na asti iti katham asatyām utpattau tām pratītya utpadyamānam syāt tasmāt utpadyamānam utpadyate tat ca utpādaḥ utpādayati iti ayuktam 
[65,iv^1]	atra āha aho bata aham atīva bhavataḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa padārtha nirapekṣāt atyanta nāstikāt vibhemi yaḥ hi nāma bhavān tathāgata pravacana vyākhyāna vyājena dūṣaṇa mātra kauśalam eva ātmanaḥ prakaṭayan parama ṛṣi gaditam idam pratyaya tā pratītya samutpāda lakṣaṇam parama artha satyam tathāgatānām nihanti iha bhagavatā tathāgatena prakṛti īśvara svabhāva kāla aṇu nārāyaṇa jaimini kaṇāda ka pila ādi tīrtha kara kartṛ vāda nirāsena sarva bhāvānām tattvam ādarśitam yat uta asmin sati idam bhavati asya utpādāt idam utpadyate yat uta avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ ityādya viparītam pratītyasamutpādam prakaṭayatā 
[65,iv^2]	tasya ca tvayā na utpadyamānam na utpannam na anutpannam ityādinā dūṣaṇam vidadhatā tathāgata jananyāḥ pratītyasamutpatti mātuḥ vadhaḥ eva ācaritaḥ iti alam bhavatā sarva nāstikena tvayā iti ucyate na aham sakala daśa bala jananīm pratītyasamutpatti mātaram nihanmi bhavān eva tu parama gambhīra pratītya samutpāda adhimukti virahāt viparītam tad artham avadhārya asmākam eva adhilayam karoti nanu ca idam pratītya idam bhavati iti evam abhidhānena bhagavatā tathāgatena niḥsvabhāva tvam eva sarva dharmāṇām spaṣṭam āveditam yasmāt pratītya yat yat bhavati tat tat śāntam svabhāvataḥ 
[66,i]	yaḥ hi padārthaḥ vidyamānaḥ sa sa svabhāvaḥ svena ātmanā svam svabhāvam anapāyinam bima rti sa saṃvidyamāna tvāt na eva anyat kiṃcid apekṣate na api utpadyate iti kṛtvā sa svabhāva bhāva abhyupagame sati kutas pratītyasamutpādaḥ iti bhavatā iva sa svabhāva tām bhāvānām abhyupagacchatā sarvathā pratītyasamutpādaḥ eva bādhitaḥ bhavati tatas ca parama dharma buddha darśanam api bādhitam bhavati yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam paśyati sa dharmam paśyati yaḥ dharmam paśyati sa buddham paśyati iti āgamāt mayā tu yat pratītya bīja ākhyam kāraṇam yat bhavati aṅkura ākhyam kāryam tat ca ubhayam api śāntam svabhāva virahitam pratītyasamutpannam pratipādayatā sarvathā bhagavatām tathāgatānām pratītyasamutpatti mātā dyotitā bhavati yatas evam tasmāt utpadyamānam ca śāntam utpattiḥ eva ca iti sphuṭam avasīyatām 
[66,ii_66,iii]	atra āha yat uktam utpadyamānam utpattau idam na kramate yadā katham utpadyamānam tu pratītya utpattim ucyate iti tat ayuktam yasmāt idam utpadyamānam iti eva saṃbhavati tathā hi ghaṭotpattim pratītya ghaṭaḥ utpadyamānaḥ bhavati tam ca utpadyamānam utpādaḥ utpādayati iti ucyate etat api ayuktam yasmāt yadi kaścid anutpannaḥ bhāvaḥ saṃvidyate kvacid utpadyeta sa kim tasmin bhāvaḥ utpadyate asati yadi kaścid anutpannaḥ utpādāt pūrvam ghaṭaḥ nāma kvacid saṃvidyeta saḥ utpatti kriyām pratītya utpadyeta na ca evam kaścid utpādāt pūrvam kvacid asti tasmin asati ghaṭe kim utpadyate 
[66,iv]	atha syāt yadi utpādāt pūrvam ghaṭaḥ na asti tathā api utpannaḥ san ghaṭa saṃjñām pratilapsyate tad bhāvinyā saṃjñayā na doṣaḥ iti etat api ayuktam yadi hi utpatti kriyā pravarteta tadā vartamānībhūtaḥ bhāvaḥ ghaṭa ākhyām pratilabheta yadā tu anāgata bhāva asaṃbandhena kriyāyāḥ apravṛttiḥ tadā kutas vartamāna tā atha aghaṭa āśrayeṇa kriyā prārabhyeta tat vaktavyam yaḥ asau aghaṭaḥ sa kim bhavituḥ mahati paṭaḥ uta na eva kiṃcid yadi paṭe utpadyamānaḥ sa katham utpannaḥ san ghaṭaḥ bhaviṣyati iti atha na evam kiṃcid katham tad āśrayā kriyā kriyā pravartate katham vā saḥ utpannaḥ san ghaṭaḥ bhavet iti sarvathā bhāvita tva kalpanā apya yuktā tasmāt utpadyamānam api utpādaḥ na utpādayat iti siddham 
[66,v_67,i]	api ca evam na yujyamānāyām api utpadyamānasya utpattau bhavataḥ matam abhyupetya ucyate utpadyamānam utpādaḥ yadi ca utpādayati ayam utpādayet tam utpādam utpādaḥ katamaḥ punar yadi api utpadyamānam padārtham utpādaḥ utpādayet bhavat matena idam tu vaktavyam tam idānīm utpādaḥ katamaḥ aparaḥ utpādam utpādayiṣyati iti 
[67,ii_67,iii]	atha syāt utpādasya aparaḥ utpādaḥ utpādakaḥ parikalpyeta tadā anavasthā doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti āha anyaḥ utpādati enam yadi utpādaḥ anavasthitiḥ etat ca uktam atha na asya aparaḥ utpādaḥ iṣyate nanu evam sati vinā utpādena utpādaḥ utpadyate iti evam prāpnoti tatas ca utpāda utpādyānām api padārthānām vinā eva utpādena utpattiḥ astu bhāva tvāt utpāda vat iti pratipādayan āha atha anutpādaḥ utpannaḥ sarvam utpadyate tathā iti 
[67,iv_67,v]	api ca utpādaḥ ātmānam parān ca utpādayati iti atra pakṣe dūṣaṇam eva na vaktavyam adhunā asmābhiḥ yasmāt atra pakṣe dūṣaṇam sataḥ ca tāvat utpatti rasataḥ ca na yujyate na sataḥ ca asataḥ ca iti pūrvam eva upapāditam na eva asataḥ na eva sataḥ pratyayaḥ arthasya yujyate iti na san āsan na sadasan dharmaḥ nirvartate yadā ityādinā utpādaḥ niṣiddhaḥ eva pūrvam tatas ca evam utpāde niṣiddhe utpadyamānam utpādaḥ utpādayati sva para ātmānau vā utpādayati iti asyāḥ kalpanāyāḥ na asti eva avatāraḥ iti kutas etat prasetsyati utpādaḥ utpadyate utpadyamānam utpadyate sva para ātmānau ca utpādayati iti 
[67,vi_67,vii]	kim ca anyat iha ayam utpādaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ nirudhyamānasya anitya tā anugatasya vartamānasya vā bhāvasya parikalpyate anirudhyamānasya vai atīta anāgatasya anitya tā virahitasya ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha nirudhyamānasya utpattiḥ na bhāvasya upapadyate yaḥ ca anirudhyamānaḥ tu sa bhāvaḥ na upapadyate tatra nirudhyamānasya vartamānasya vidyamāna tvāt utpādaḥ na upapadyate anirudhyamānasya api vināśa rahitasya atīta anāgatasya bhāva lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇasya khapuṣpasya iva na asti utpādaḥ iti 
[67,viii_68,i]	evam bhāvānām utpāda abhāvam pratipādya atas param sthitiḥ vicāryate atra āha vidyate eva bhāvānām utpādaḥ tad bhāva bhāvi dharma sadbhāvāt na anutpannasya sthiti saṃbhavati iti utpāda bhāvena sthiteḥ bhāvāt sthitiḥ utpāda bhāva bhāvinī bhavati tasmāt utpādaḥ api asti tad bhāva bhāvi dharma sadbhāvāt iha yat na asti na tad bhāva bhāvi dharma sadbhāvaḥ tat yathā gagana kusuma saurabhyasya iti ucyate syāt utpādaḥ yadi tad bhāva bhāvinī sthitiḥ eva syāt na tu asti tat evam na sthita bhāvaḥ tiṣṭhati asthita bhāvaḥ na tiṣṭhati na tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhamānaḥ kaḥ anutpannaḥ ca tiṣṭhati 
[68,ii_68,iii]	tatra sthitam na tiṣṭhati tatra sthiti kriyā nirodhāt asthita bhāvaḥ api na tiṣṭhati sthiti rahita tvāt tiṣṭhamānam api na tiṣṭhati sthiti dvaya prasaṅgāt sthita āsthita vyatirikta saṃtiṣṭhamāna abhāvāt ca api ca kaḥ anutpannaḥ ca tiṣṭhati iha utpāda pratiṣedhāt kaḥ asau anutpannaḥ padārthaḥ yaḥ tiṣṭhet iti sarvathā na asti sthitiḥ 
[68,iv_68,v]	api ca iyam sthitiḥ nirudhyamānasya bhāvasya syāt anirudhyamānasya vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti pratipādayan āha sthitiḥ nirudhyamānasya na bhāvasya upapadyate yaḥ ca anirudhyamānaḥ tu sa bhāvaḥ na upapadyate nirudhyamānasya nirodha abhimukhasya tāvat bhāvasya virodhinī sthitiḥ na saṃbhavati yaḥ ca api anirudhyamānaḥ sa bhāvaḥ eva na bhavati kutas tasya sthitiḥ bhaviṣyati 
[68,vi_68,vii]	api ca jarasā maraṇena ca sarve eva bhāvāḥ kṣaṇam api na tyajyante yadā ca etat evam tadā jarā maraṇa virodhinyāḥ sthiteḥ bhāveṣu pravṛtti avakāśaḥ eva na asti iti pratipādayan āha jarā maraṇa dharmeṣu sarva bhāveṣu sarvadā tiṣṭhanti katame bhāvāḥ ye jarā maraṇam vinā ke hi nāma jarā maraṇa rahitāḥ bhāvāḥ yeṣām sthitiḥ syāt tasmāt na asti eva sthitiḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[68,viii_68,ix]	yadi ca asyāḥ sthiteḥ anyā vā sthitiḥ sthiti artham parikalpyeta svayam vā sva ātmānam sthāpayet ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha sthityā anyayā sthiteḥ sthānam tayā eva ca na yujyate utpādasya yathā utpādaḥ na ātmanā na para ātmanā anutpannaḥ ayam utpādaḥ sva ātmānam janayet katham ityādinā yathā utpādaḥ ātmānam na janayati iti uktam evam sthitiḥ api na ātmānam sthāpayati iti vaktavyam 
[69,i_69,vi]	asthitā sthitiḥ eṣā ced sva ātmānam sthāpayet katham sthitā ced sthāpayati eṣā sthitāyām sthāpyate atha kim iti yojyam yathā ca anyaḥ utpādayati enam yadi utpādaḥ anavasthitiḥ iti utpāde vyākhyātam evam sthitau api vyākhyeyam atha anyā sthāpayati enām sthitiḥ yadi anavasthitiḥ iti evam sthitiḥ api na yuktā atas eva uktam bhagavatā asthitāḥ hi ime dharmāḥ sthitiḥ ca eṣām na vidyate asthitiḥ sthiti śabdena svabhāvena na vidyate na sthitiḥ na api caḥ jātiḥ lokanāthena deśitā lokanātham viditvā evam samādhim tena jānathā iti uktam ca ārya sa carya gāthāsu ākāśa niśrita sa mārutaḥ āpakhandho tad niśritā iya mahī pṛthivī jagat ca sattvāna karma aupabhoga nidānam evam ākāśatha anu kṛta cittamaḥ etam artham yāvat sthānam maya anu ayu tha anu jinena uktaḥ iti vistaraḥ 
[69,vii]	atra āha vidyete eva sthiti utpādau tad sahacāri dharma sadbhāvāt iha utpāda sthiti lakṣaṇa sahacāriṇī saṃskṛtānām anitya tā asti tasmāt sthiti utpādau api staḥ iti ucyate syāta sthiti utpādau yadi anitya tā eva syāt na tu asti katham iti yasmāt nirudhyate na aniruddham na niruddham nirudhyate tathā api nirudhyamānam kim ajātam nirudhyate 
[69,viii]	yadi anitya tā iti kācid syāt sā niruddhasya bhāvasya aniruddhasya vā nirudhyamānasya vā syāt tatra niruddham nirudhyate iti na yuktam atīta vartamānayoḥ virodhāt aniruddham api na yuktam nirodha virahita tvāt yat aniruddham eva tat katham nirudhyate iti paraspara virodhāt ca tathā api nirudhyamānam na nirudhyate iti anena saṃbandhaḥ nirudhyamānam api na nirudhyate nirudhyamāna abhāvāt nirodha dvaya prasaṅgāt ca yatas ca evam triṣu api kāleṣu nirodha asaṃbhavaḥ tasmāt na asti eva nirodhaḥ iti kutas tad sahacāri sthiti utpāda saṃbhavaḥ syāt api ca prāk utpāda pratiṣedhāt asaṃbhavaḥ eva nirodhasya iti āha kim ajātam nirudhyate iti 
[70,i_70,iv]	api ca ayam nirodhaḥ sthitasya vā bhāvasya syāt asthitasya vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha sthitasya tāvat bhāvasya nirodhaḥ na upapadyate sthitasya nirodha viruddhasya na asti nirodhaḥ na asthitasya api bhāvasya nirodhaḥ upapadyate asthitasya abhāvasya avidyamānasya nirodhaḥ na asti iti sarvathā na asti nirodhaḥ 
[70,v_70,vi]	kim ca anyat yadi iha nirodhaḥ syāt sa tayā eva avasthayā tasyāḥ eva avasthāyāḥ syāt anyayā vai anyasyāḥ avasthāyāḥ syāt sarvathā ca na upapadyate iti pratipādayan āha tayā eva avasthayā avasthā na hi sā eva nirudhyate anyayā avasthayā avasthā na ca anyā eva nirudhyate tayā eva tāvat kṣīra avasthayā sā eva kṣīra avasthā na nirudhyate sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt na api anyayā dadhi avasthayā kṣīra avasthā nirudhyate yadi hi kṣīra dadhi avasthayoḥ yaugapadyam syāt syāt tayoḥ vināśi avināśaka bhāvaḥ na tu dadhi avasthāyām kṣīra avasthā asti yadā ca na asti tadā kāma satī vināśayet yadi vināśayet khara viṣāṇa tīkṣṇa tām api vināśayet tasmāt anyayā api avasthayā na eva anya avasthā nirudhyate 
[70,vii]	atra āha yadi api tayā eva avasthayā sā eva avasthyā anyayā vā avasthayā anya avasthā na nirudhyate tathā api kṣīra avasthāyāḥ tāvat nirodhaḥ asti tatas ca utpādaḥ api syāt iti ucyate aho bata ati jaḍa tām ātmanaḥ bhavān prakaṭayati nanu ca pūrva uktena nyāyena yadā evam sarva dharmāṇām utpādaḥ na upapadyate iti uktam tadā evam sarva dharmāṇām nirodhaḥ na upapadyate iti sphuṭataram eva pratipāditam bhavati 
[70,viii_71,i]	api ca nirodhaḥ nāma yadi kaścid syāt sa sataḥ vā bhāvasya syāt asataḥ vā tatra sataḥ ca tāvat bhāvasya nirodhaḥ na upapadyate svabhāvāt apracyutasya bhāvasya nirodhaḥ na yuktaḥ yasmāt eka tve na hi bhāvaḥ ca na abhāvaḥ ca upapadyate nirodhaḥ hi nāma abhāvaḥ sa yasya bhavati sa na eva bhavati tatas ca sataḥ bhāvasya nirodhaḥ iti bruvatā bhāva abhāvayoḥ eka adhikaraṇa tā abhyupagatā bhavati eka tve sati ubhayam na yujyate yadi tadānīm bhāvaḥ syāt tadā nirodhena abhāvena āveśāt bhāva vyapadeśaḥ ayuktaḥ atha abhāvaḥ saḥ api asya na yujyate abhāva virodhinā bhāva rūpeṇa aviyogāt tasmāt ekatve sati bhāva abhāvayoḥ sa padārthaḥ na eva bhāvaḥ na api abhāvaḥ iti yujyate athavā paraspara viruddha tvāt āloka andhakāra vat eka tve sati na hi bhāvaḥ ca na abhāvaḥ ca upapadyate evam tāvat sataḥ bhāvasya nirodhaḥ na yuktaḥ 
[71,ii_71,iv]	idānīm asataḥ api na bhāvasya nirodhaḥ upapadyate avidyamānasya abhāvasya na vināśaḥ asti vandhyā tanayasya iva avidyamāna tvāt atas eva āha na dvitīyasya śirasa chedanam vidyate yathā prasiddhā sattvasya eva narāṇām dvitīyasya śirasaḥ dṛṣṭānta tvena upādānāt nirdeśa āpūrṇa tvāt na asti iti na upāttam tat evam asataḥ bhāvasya nirodhaḥ na saṃbhavati sataḥ api na yaḥ ca ubhayathā api na saṃbhavati sa kena ātmanā sthitaḥ na asti eva nirodhaḥ iti pratīyatām 
[71,v_71,viii]	kim ca anyat yadi nirodhaḥ nāma bhāvānām nirodhakaḥ iti kalpyate tasya idānīm kim anyaḥ nirodhaḥ iṣyate uta na yadi iṣyate tat na yujyate na sva ātmanā nirodhaḥ asti nirodhaḥ na para ātmanā katham punar na asti iti pratipādayan āha utpādasya yathā utpādaḥ na ātmanā na para ātmanā tatra yathā anutpannaḥ ayam utpādaḥ sva ātmānam janayet katham 
[71,ix]	ityādinā utpādaḥ sva ātmānam na utpādayati evam nirodhaḥ api sva ātmānam na nirodhayati katham iti ucyate aniruddhaḥ nirodhaḥ ayam sva ātmānam nāśayet katham atha naṣṭaḥ nāśayati naṣṭe kim nāśyate punar iti samam utpādena vaktavyam evam ca sva ātmanā na nirodhaḥ asti nirodhaḥ idānīm para ātmanā api na asti katham tatra yathā utpāde gaditam anyaḥ utpādayati enam ityādi evam nirodhe api vaktavyam anyaḥ vināśayati enam nāśaḥ yadi anavasthitiḥ atha avināśaḥ naṣṭaḥ ayam sarvam naśyatu te tathā iti tat evam para ātmanā api nirodhaḥ na saṃbhavati iti na asti nirodhasya nirodhaḥ 
[72,i]	atha manyase na asti eva nirodhasya nirodhaḥ iti tat ayuktam yadi hi nirodhasya nirodhaḥ na syāta tadā nirodha rahita tvāt saṃskṛta lakṣaṇam avahīyate tat evam yadi vināśasya vināśaḥ parikalpyate tathā api na yuktaḥ vināśaḥ atha na parikalpyate tathā api na yuktaḥ iti katham tu idānīm vināśaḥ yokṣyate parasya atha syāt tathā api evam eva vicāre sati vināśaḥ bhavataḥ api na yujyate tatas yaḥ ubhayoḥ doṣaḥ na tena ekaḥ codyaḥ bhavati iti ucyate na eva idam ca udyam mama āpatati kim kāraṇam ye sva ātmanā niḥsvabhāvāḥ bhāvāḥ te ca niḥsvabhāvāḥ eva santaḥ bālānām idaṃsatya abhiniveśinām vyavahāra patham upayānti avicāra prasiddhena eva nyāyena iti teṣu na asti yathā udita vicāra avatāraḥ asmākam māyā svapna gandharvanagara ādi vat tu laukikāḥ padārthāḥ nirupapattikāḥ eva santaḥ sarva lokasya avidyā timira upahatam ati nayanasya prasiddhim upagatāḥ iti paraspara apekṣayā eva kevalam prasiddhim upagatāḥ bālaiḥ abhyupagamyante yathā uktam śatake alāta cakra nirmāṇa svapna māyā ambu candrakaiḥ dhūmikā antar pratiśrutkā marīci abhraiḥ samaḥ bhavaḥ 
[72,ii_72,iii]	tasmāt sati utpāde utpādyam sati utpādye utpādaḥ sati nirodhe nirodhyam sati nirodhye nirodhaḥ iti evam laukikasya vyavahārasya abhyupagamāt kutas asmad pakṣe sama prasaṅgitā bhavitum arhati yaḥ tu vināśasya ahetuka tvam abhyupetya kṣaṇika tām saṃskārāṇām āha tasya nirhetuka tvāt kha puṣpa vat vināśa abhāvāt kutas kṣaṇika tvam bhāvānām setsyati kutas vināśa rahitānām saṃskṛta tvam api iti sarvam eva asamañjasam tasya jāyate jāti pratyayam jarā maraṇam saṃskṛta lakṣaṇānām ca saṃskāra skandha antar bhāva varṇayatā bhagavatā nanu sa hetuka tvam spaṣṭam ādarśitam vināśasya jāti mātra apekṣa tvāt ca asya kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ api sukha sādhyaḥ iti sarvam sustham jāyate 
[72,iv]	atha syāt vināśaḥ hi nāma abhāvaḥ yaḥ ca abhāvaḥ kim tasya hetunā kartavyam atas nirhetukaḥ vināśaḥ iti nanu ca bhāve api hetvabhāva prasaṅgaḥ bhavati bhāvaḥ hi nāma vidyamānaḥ yaḥ ca vidyamānaḥ tasya ca kim hetunā prayojanam na hi jātam punar api janyate tasmāt sarvatra eva hetvabhāva prasaṅgāt ayuktam etat 
[72,v^1]	api ca yathā utpādaḥ sa hetukaḥ pūrvam abhāvāt paścāt ca bhāvāt evam vināśaḥ api iṣyatām vināśaḥ hi na sarvadā bhavati utpādāt pūrvam abhāvāt paścāt ca bhāvāt yat ca ucyate yaḥ ca abhāvaḥ tasya kim hetunā kartavyam iti tat ayuktam yasmāt na vayam vināśasya hetunā kiṃcid kriyamāṇam icchāmaḥ kim tarhi vināśaḥ eva kriyate iti varṇayāmaḥ nanu evam sati kriyamāṇa tvāt vināśaḥ api bhāvaḥ prāpnoti iti ced iṣyate eva etat vināśaḥ hi svarūpa apekṣayā bhāvaḥ rūpa ādi dharma nivṛtti svabhāva tvāt tu na bhāvaḥ api ca 
[72,v^2]	maraṇam api dvividha kārya pratyupasthāpanam saṃskāra vidhvaṃsanam ca karoti aparijñāna anupacchedam ca iti āgamāt katham na sa hetukaḥ vināśaḥ api ca kalpita abhāva lakṣaṇāyāḥ ca śūnyatāyāḥ pareṇa bhāva rūpa tām abhyupagacchatā katham abhāvasya bhāva tvam na abhyupagatam bhavati bhāva tvāt ca katham asaṃskṛta tvam śūnyatāyāḥ syāt atas sarvam abhyupetam vihīyate bhavatā atas eva vakṣyati bhavet abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam ubhayam katham na saṃskṛtam hi nirvāṇam bhāva abhāvau ca saṃskṛtau iti alam prasaṅgena prakṛtam eva vyākhyāsyāmaḥ 
[73,i]	atra āha yadi utpāda sthiti bhaṅgāḥ saṃskṛtasya niṣiddhāḥ tathā api saṃskṛtam asti viśeṣa lakṣaṇa yuktam tathā hi kāṭhinya ādikam sāsnādikam ca tasya viśeṣa lakṣaṇam upadiśyate tasmāt saṃskṛtasya sadbhāvāt tad lakṣaṇam api asti iti ucyate syāt evam yadi saṃskṛtam eva vastu syāt kutas yasmāt utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām asiddheḥ na asti saṃskṛtam 
[73,ii_73,iv]	yadā yathā uktena nyāyena utpāda sthiti bhaṅgāḥ eva niṣiddhāḥ tadā kutas saṃskṛtam vastu tad viśeṣa lakṣaṇam api asti iti atra āha vidyate eva saṃskṛtam tad pratipakṣā saṃskṛta sadbhāvāt ucyate syāt etat evam yadi asaṃskṛtam eva syāt yasmāt saṃskṛtasya aprasiddhau ca katham setsyati asaṃskṛtam atra eke ākāśa apratisaṃkhyā nirodha nirvāṇāni asaṃskṛtāni iti kalpayanti apare śūnyatām tathatā lakṣaṇām asaṃskṛtām parikalpayanti tat etat sarvam saṃskṛtasya aprasiddhau satyām na asti eva iti spaṣṭam ādarśitam 
[73,v]	atra āha yadi utpāda sthiti bhaṅgāḥ na santi iti avadhāritam yat tarhi idam anāvaraṇa jñāninā muninā saṃskṛtasya bhikṣavaḥ utpādaḥ api prajñāyate vyayaḥ api sthiti anyathātvam api iti udāhṛtam tat katham veditavyam iti ucyate yathā māyā yathā svapnaḥ gandharvanagaram yathā tathā utpādaḥ tathā sthānam tathā bhaṅgaḥ udāhṛtam 
[74,i]	yathā māyā ādayaḥ svabhāvena anutpannāḥ avidyamānāḥ māyā ādi śabda vācyāḥ māyā ādi vijñāna gamyāḥ ca lokasya evam ete api loka prasiddhi mātreṇa utpāda ādayaḥ svabhāvena avidyamānā api bhagavatā tathāvidha vineya jana anugraha cikīrṣuṇā nirdiṣṭāḥ iti atas eva uktam tvac snāyu māṃsa asthi samucchraye ca utpādya saṃjñām mama patniḥ eṣā mūḍhāḥ hi balāḥ janayanti rāgam striyaḥ na jānanti yathā eva māyām yathā kumārī supina antarasmim sā putra jātam ca mṛtam ca paśyati jāte ati tuṣṭā mṛti daurmana sthitā tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān yathā eva gandharvapuram marīcikāḥ yathā eva māyā supinam yathā eva svabhāva śūnyā tu nimitta bhāvanā tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān saṃskṛta asaṃskṛta dharma viviktā na asti vikalpana teṣam ṛṣīṇām sarva gatīṣu asaṃskṛta prāptā dṛṣṭi gata ihi sadā eva viviktā nityam araktaḥ aduṣṭa amūḍhāḥ tasya sa bhāva samāhita cittā eṣa samādhi balī balavantaḥ yaḥ imu jānati śūnyaka dharmān iti 
[75,i_75,iii]	atra āha vidyante eva saṃskṛta svabhāvataḥ vijñāna ādayaḥ saṃskṛtāḥ dharmāḥ tad hetuka karma kāraka sadbhāvāt uktam hi bhagavatā avidyā anugataḥ ayam bhikṣavaḥ puruṣa pudgalaḥ puṇyān api saṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti apuṇyān api āniñjayān api saṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti ityādinā karmaṇām kārakaḥ vyapadiṣṭaḥ tad karma phalam ca vijñāna ādikam upadiṣṭam yasya ca kārakaḥ asti tat asti tat yathā ghaṭaḥ yat na asti na tasya kārakaḥ tat yathā kūrma roma prāvārasya iti ucyate syāt vijñāna ādikam saṃskṛtam yadi tasya niṣpādaka karma kārakau syātām na tu staḥ yasmāt sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ karma sadbhūtam na karoti ayam kārakaḥ na api asadbhūtaḥ karma asadbhūtam īhate 
[75,iv]	tatra karoti iti kārakaḥ kartā kurvāṇasya eva kiṃcid kāraka vyapadeśaḥ na akurvāṇasya tat ca karaṇam sadbhūtasya vā kartuḥ parikalpyeta asat bhūtasya vā sat asat bhūtasya vā kriyate iti karma kartuḥ īpsitatamam tat api trividham sadbhūtam asat bhūtam sat asat bhūtam ca tatra sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ kriyā yuktaḥ sadbhūtam kriyā yuktam karma na karoti iti ekā pratijñā idānīm asat bhūtaḥ api kriyā kāraka rahitaḥ asadbhutam kriyā rahitam karma na karoti iti aparā pratijñā 
[75,v_75,vi]	tatra ādyām prasādhayitum āha sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti karma ca syāt akartṛkam kriyā nibandhana tvāt kāraka vyapadeśasya karoti kriyā yuktaḥ eva kaścid sadbhūtaḥ kāraka vyapadeśam labhate tatas ca tasya evaṃvidhasya kriyā hetuka labdha kāraka vyapadeśasya aparā kriyā na asti yayā karma kuryāt kriyā bhāvāt ca yadā kārakaḥ karma na karoti tadā kāraka nirapekṣam akartṛkam karma syāt na ca akartṛkam karma saṃbhavati bandhyā sūnoḥ iva ghaṭa karaṇam iti evam tāvat sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti karma ca syāt akartṛkam iti doṣa prasaṅgāt sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ karma na karoti 
[75,vii_75,viii]	idānīm sadbhūtam api karma kārakaḥ na karoti iti pratipādayan āha sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti kartā ca syāt akarmakaḥ sadbhūtam nāma karma kriyā yuktam tasya idānīm kriyā nibandhana labdha karma vyapadeśasya aparā kriyā na asti yayā karma kriyeta iti evam tāvat sadbhūtasya karmaṇaḥ kriyā na asti yadā na asti parā kriyā tadā kārakaḥ tad sat bhūtam karma na eva karoti yadā ca na karoti karmaṇaḥ dvitīya kriyā bhāvāt tadā akarmakaḥ eva avidyamāna karmakaḥ eva tasya karmaṇaḥ kārakaḥ syāt na ca etat yaktam na hi akṛta ānantarya karmaṇaḥ ānantarya karma kāraka tvam dṛṣṭam iti 
[76,i_76,ii]	evam sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ sadbhūtam karma na karoti iti saṃsādhya idānīm yathā asat bhūtam api karma asat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ na karoti tathā pratipādayan āha karoti yadi asat bhūtaḥ asat bhūtam karma kārakaḥ ahetukam bhavet karma kartā ca ahetukaḥ bhavet asat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ yaḥ kriyā rahitaḥ kriyā ca kāraka vyapadeśe hetuḥ iti kriyā rahita kārakaḥ api nirhetukaḥ syāt karma api asadbhūtam nirhetukam syāt 
[76,iii_76,iv]	sati ca ahetuka vāda abhyupagame kāryam ca kāraṇam ca sarvam apoditam syāt iti āha hetau asati kāryam ca kāraṇam ca na vidyate sati eva hi hetoḥ abhyupagame hetunā yat niṣpādyate tat kāryam tasya ca yaḥ niṣpādakaḥ tad kāraṇam iti yujyate tat yathā ghaṭasya mṛd hetuḥ ghaṭaḥ kāryam tasya ca cakra ādayaḥ sahakāri kāraṇam ahetuka vāda abhyupagame tu hetu anapekṣa tvāt maṇḍūka jaṭā śiraḥ maṇi maya ghaṭa vat na syāt ayam ghaṭaḥ asati ghaṭe kutas tat kāraṇam iti evam hetau asati kāryam ca kāraṇam ca na vidyate 
[76,v_76,vii]	tatas ca tad abhāve kriyā kartā karaṇam ca na vidyate tad abhāve kārya kāraṇa bhāve kim kurvāṇasya kriyā saṃbhavet kasyām vā kriyāyām kumbhakārasya svātantryāt kartṛ tvam syāt na ca api mṛdām tādātmya pravṛttyā sādhakatama tvena karaṇa tvam yujyate iti evam tāvat tad abhāve kriyā kartā karaṇam ca na vidyate tatas ca dharma adharmau na vidyete kriyā ādīnām asaṃbhave 
[76,viii_77,i]	iha yadā devadattaḥ prāṇa atipāta virati kriyā svātantryāt kartā san svatantra kāryeṇa karaṇa bhūtena prāṇa atipāta virati kriyām karoti tadā asya dharmaḥ upajāyate evam daśasu api kuśaleṣu karma patheṣu kuśala kriyā niṣpādyeṣu ratnatraya mātā pitṛ tad anya pūjya pūjā ādi lakṣaṇeṣu ca kuśala dharma prārambheṣu yojyam evam adharme api prāṇa atipāta ādi lakṣaṇe kuśala viparyayeṇa kriyā kartṛ karaṇānām abhāve sati karmaṇā ām abhāva prasaṅgaḥ udbhāvanīyaḥ yadā ca evam dharma adharmau na saṃbhavataḥ tadā tad phalam api na asti eva iti pratipādayan āha dharme ca asati adharme ca phalam tad jam na vidyate dharma adharma janitam iṣṭa aniṣṭa phalam sugati durgatyoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ abhāve sati na syāt 
[77,ii_77,iii]	tatas ca phale asati na mokṣāya na svargāya upapadyate mārgaḥ yadi hi phalam iṣṭa aniṣṭam syāta syāt laukikasya mārgasya dhyāna ārūpya samādhi samāpatti lakṣaṇam svargaḥ tadānīm tad artham laukika mārga bhāvanā jyāyasī syāt kugati gamana karma patha virati sāphalyam ca syāt yadi ca mokṣa lakṣaṇam nirvāṇam phalam syāt tad artha loka uttara ārya aṣṭa aṅga mārga bhāva nāsā phalyam syāt yadā tu phalam na asti tadā phale asati na mokṣāya na svargāya upapadyate mārgaḥ
[77,iv_77,v]	kim ca evam phala abhāve sati sarva kriyāṇām ca nairarthakyam prasajyate yāḥ api hi etāḥ kṛṣi vāṇijya bhṛti gata ādikāḥ kriyāḥ phala artha prārabhyante tāḥ api sarvāḥ phala abhāve sati na upapadyante iti evam sarva kriyāṇām nairarthakyam prasajyate bhavatām na ca āsām nairarthakyam tasmāt niravaśeṣa doṣa viṣa vṛkṣa ākara bhūtaḥ ayam svarga apavarga apavādī naraka ādi mahāpāya prapāta vartana hetuḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa hetu padārtha virodhī iti kṛtvā saddhiḥ asat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ asat bhūtam karma karoti iti pakṣaḥ nikṛṣṭaḥ eva iti tyājyaḥ 
[77,vi_77,viii]	tat evam pratijñā dvayam saṃsādhya idānīm ubhaya rūpaḥ kārakaḥ ubhaya rūpam api karma na karoti iti āha kārakaḥ sat asat bhūtaḥ sat asat kurute na tat tatra yat etat asat bhūtam karma kriyā yuktam akriyā yuktam ca tat sat asat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ na karoti iti yasmāt paraspara viruddham hi sat ca asat ca ekatas kutas ekaḥ padārthaḥ ekasmin kāle kriyā yuktaḥ ca akriyā yuktaḥ ca iti na yujyate eva etat tatas ca sat asat bhūtaḥ api kārakaḥ sadasat bhūtam karma na karoti avidyamāna tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[77,ix_78,iii]	evam same pakṣe dūṣaṇam udbhāvya viṣama pakṣasya api nirācikīrṣayā āha satā ca kriyate na āsat nāsatā kriyate ca sat kartrā satā sat bhūtena tāvat kartrā kriyā yuktena asat bhūtam asat akriyā yuktam karma na kriyate yasmāt sarve prasajyante doṣāḥ tatra te eva hi sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti karma ca syāt akartṛkam iti evam tāvat sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ karma na karoti na api asadbhūtam karma kriyate asat bhūtam hi karma ahetukam bhavet tatas ca hetau asati kāryam ca kāraṇam ca na vidyate ityādinā sarvam dūṣaṇam āpadyate tasmāt pūrva uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ dūṣita tvāt asya viṣama pakṣasya na punar hetoḥ upādānam anuṣṭhīyate yathā ca etat satā kartrā asat karma na kriyate iti pratipāditam evam asatā kartrā akriyā yuktena satkarma na kriyate iti vyākhyeya m ukta patha anusāreṇa 
[78,iv_78,v]	evam tāvat viṣama pakṣe eka eka pada parāmarśena dūṣaṇam abhidhāya idānīm ekaikasya padasya pada dvaya parāmarśena dūṣaṇa abhidhānam āha na asat bhūtam na sadbhūtaḥ sadasat bhūtam eva vā karoti kārakaḥ karma pūrva uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ sa kārakaḥ sadbhūtaḥ asat bhūtam karma sadasat bhūtam eva vā na karoti iti katham iti āha pūrva uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ iti tatra sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti ityādinā sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ na karoti asat bhūtam api karma na kriyate ahetukam bhavet karma hetau asati kāryam ca ityādinā vihita doṣāt sat asat bhūtam api karma na kriyate paraspara viruddham hi sat ca asat ca ekatas kutas iti vacanāt evam tāvat sadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ asat bhūtam sat asadbhutam ca karma na karoti 
[78,vi_78,viii]	idānīm asat bhūtaḥ api kārakaḥ sadbhūtam karma sat asat bhūtam ca karma na karoti iti āha na asat bhūtaḥ api sadbhūtam sat asat bhūtam eva vā karoti kārakaḥ karma pūrva uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ asat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ nirhetukaḥ bhavet hetau asati kāryam ca ityādinā ukta doṣāt asadbhūtaḥ kārakaḥ na karoti sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti kartā ca syāt akarmakaḥ iti prasaṅgāt sadbhūtam karma na kriyate sat asat bhūtam api karma na kriyate paraspara viruddham hi sat ca asat ca ekatas kutas iti vacanāt 
[79,i_79,ii]	idānīm sat asat bhūtaḥ api kārakaḥ ekaikaḥ eva ubhaya rūpaḥ san yathā sat bhūtam asat bhūtam ca bhinna saṃketam karma na karoti tathā pratipādayan āha karoti sat asat bhūtaḥ na sat na asat ca kārakaḥ karma tat tu vijānīyāt pūrva uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ paraspara viruddham hi sat ca asat ca ekatas kutas iti vacanāt sadasat bhūtaḥ kārakaḥ na karoti
