[79,iii]	sadbhūtasya kriyā na asti kartā ca syāt akarmakaḥ iti prasaṅgāt sadbhūtam karma na kriyate asat bhūtam api karma ahetukam hetau asati kārya ca ityādinā ukta doṣāt na kriyate yatas ca evam sama pakṣeṣu viṣama pakṣeṣu ca kartuḥ karmaṇaḥ ca sarvathā siddhiḥ ayuktā tasmāt yat uktam vidyante eva vijñāna ādayaḥ saṃskṛtāḥ dharmāḥ saṃskṛta svabhāvāḥ tad hetuka karma kāraka sadbhāvāt iti tat ayuktam 
[79,iv]	atra āha kim avadhāritam etat bhavatā na santi bhāvāḥ iti na hi bhavataḥ tu sa svabhāva vādinaḥ svabhāvasya bhāvānām vaidhuryāt sarva bhāva apavādaḥ saṃbhāvyate vayam tu pratītya utpanna tvāt sarva bhāvānām svabhāvam evana upalabhāmahe tat kasya apavādam kariṣyāmaḥ yathā uktam ārya ratna āvalyām marīci toyam iti etat iti matvā āgataḥ atra san yadi na asti iti tat toyam gṛhṇīyāt mūḍhaḥ eva saḥ marīci pratimam lokam evam asti iti gṛhṇataḥ na asti iti ca api mohaḥ ayam sati mohe na mucyate ajñāna kalpitam pūrvam paścāt tatva artha nirṇaye yadā na labhate bhāvam eva abhāvaḥ tadā kuha iti 
[79,v]	tat evam niḥsvabhāvānām sarva bhāvānām kutas yathā ukta prakāra siddhiḥ tasmāt laukikam viparyāsam abhyupetya sāṃvṛtānām padārthānām marīcikā jala kalpānām idaṃpratyaya tā mātra abhyupagamena eva prasiddhiḥ na anyena iti āha pratītya kārakaḥ karma tam pratītya ca kārakam karma pravartate na anyat paśyāmaḥ siddhi kāraṇam 
[79,vi]	iha akurvāṇasya karma nirapekṣasya kāraka tva abhāvāt karma apekṣya kārakasya kāraka tvam bhavati kārakeṇa ca akriyamāṇasya kasyacid karma tva abhāvāt kriyamāṇasya eva karma vyapadeśāt tam kārakam pratītya karma pravartate iti evam karma kārakayoḥ paraspara āpekṣikīm siddhim muktvā na anyat siddhi kāraṇam paśyāmaḥ 
[79,vii_80,i]	yathā ca karma kārakayoḥ paraspara āpekṣikī siddhiḥ evam anyeṣām api bhāvānām iti ati diśan āha evam vidyāt upādānam vyutsargāt iti karmaṇaḥ kartuḥ ca evam iti anena anantarām karma kāraka prajñaptim darśayati upāttiḥ upādānam anena ca upātti kriyām āha sā ca sva sādhanam kartāram upādātāram karma ca upādānam saṃnidhāpayati tayoḥ ca upādeya upādātroḥ paraspara apekṣayoḥ karma kāraka vat eva siddhiḥ na svābhāvikī kasmāt punar svābhāvikī na bhavati iti āha vyutsargāt iti karmaṇaḥ kartuḥ ca iti iti śabdaḥ hetu parāmarśī vyutsargaḥ vyudāsaḥ tatas ca ayam arthaḥ upapadyate yaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ karmaṇaḥ ca vyutsargaḥ asmābhiḥ uktaḥ taiḥ eva hetubhiḥ upādātāḥ upādeyam ca pratiṣiddham veditavyam na ca kevala m anayoḥ anyonya āpekṣikī siddhiḥ katurḥ ca karmaṇaḥ ca pratiṣedhena avaseyā api ca karma kartṛbhyām śeṣān bhāvān vibhāvayet 
[80,ii_80,iii]	prājñaḥ iti vākya śeṣaḥ karmakāra kopa ādeya upādātṛ vyatiriktāḥ ye anye bhāvāḥ janya janaka gantṛ gamana draṣṭavya darśana lakṣya lakṣaṇa utpādya utpādakāḥ tathā avayava avayavi guṇa guṇi pramāṇa prameya ādayaḥ niravaśeṣāḥ bhāvāḥ teṣām kartṛ karma vicāreṇa svabhāvataḥ astitvam pratiṣidhya paraspara āpekṣikīm eva siddhi prājñaḥ nirmumukṣuḥ jāti jarā maraṇa ādi bandhanebhyaḥ mokṣāya vibhāvayet eṣām ca vistareṇa vicāraḥ madhyamaka avatāra ādibhyaḥ avaseyaḥ 
[80,iv]	nanu ca śeṣān bhāvān vibhāvayet iti anena eva upādāna upādāt na uradhi gata tvāt upādāna upādānam punar ayuktam satyam etat tathā api tattva vicāre prādhānya jñāpana artham upādāna upādātra ubhedena upādānam tathā hi uttareṣu prakaraṇeṣu bhūyasā anayoḥ eva vicāraḥ bhaviṣyati iti atas eva uktam bhagavatā ārya upāli paripṛcchāyām bhaya darśita nairayikam me sattva sahasra sa vejita na eke na ca vidyati kaściha sattva yaḥ cyutu gacchati ghoram apāyam na ca kāraku kāraṇam santi yehi kṛtāḥ asi tomara śastrāḥ kalpa vaśena tu paśyati tatra kāyi patanti apāyita śastrāḥ citra manorama sajjita puṣpāḥ svarṇa vimāna jalanti manojñāḥ teṣu api kāraku na astiha kaści te api ca sthāpita kalpa vaśena kalpa vaśena vikalpitu lokaḥ saṃjña gaheṇa vikalpitu bālaḥ saḥ ca gahaḥ agahaḥ asa bhūtaḥ māya marīci samāḥ hi vikalpāḥ iti 
[81,i_81,ii]	atra āha yat uktam evam vidyāt upādānam vyutsargāt iti karmaṇaḥ kartuḥ ca iti tat ayuktam yasmāt darśana śravaṇa ādīni vedanā ādīni ca api atha bhavanti yasya prāgebhyaḥ saḥ asti iti eke vadanti uta yasya upādātuḥ darśana śravaṇa ghrāṇa rasana ādīni vedanā sparśa manaskāra ādīni ca bhavanti saḥ upādātā pūrvam ebhyaḥ upādānebhyaḥ asti iti sāṃmitīyāḥ vadanti 
[81,iii_81,iv]	kim kāraṇam yasmāt katham hi avidyamānasya darśana ādi bhaviṣyati bhāvasya tasmāt prāgebhyaḥ saḥ asti bhāvaḥ vyavasthitaḥ iha vidyamānaḥ eva devadattaḥ dhana upādānam kurute na avidyamānaḥ vandhyā tanayaḥ evam yadi tāvat pudgalaḥ darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam vyavasthitaḥ na syāt na asau darśana ādikasya upādānam akariṣyat tasmāt asti asau dhanāt prāk eva sthita deva datta vat darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam pudgalaḥ yaḥ asya upādānam kariṣyati iti 
[81,v_81,vi]	ucyate darśana śravaṇa ādibhyaḥ vedanā ādibhyaḥ eva ca yaḥ prāc vyavasthitaḥ bhāvaḥ kena prajñapyate atha saḥ yaḥ asau pudgalaḥ darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam asti iti vyavasthāpyate sa kena prajñapyatām pudgala prajñapteḥ hi darśana ādikam kāraṇam sa yadi tebhyaḥ prāc vyavasthitaḥ asti iti kalpyate tadā darśana nirapekṣaḥ syāt ghaṭāt iva paṭaḥ yaḥ ca sva kāraṇa nirapekṣaḥ sa nirhetukaḥ dhana ādi nirapekṣaḥ dhanika vat na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[81,vii_81,viii]	kim ca anyat vinā api darśana ādīni yadi ca asau vyavasthitaḥ amūni api bhaviṣyanti vinā tena na saṃśayaḥ yadi manyase darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam pudgalaḥ nāma asti sa darśana ādikam upādānam upādatte iti nanu evam sati nirasta saṃśayam amūni api darśana ādīni vinā pudgalena bhaviṣyanti tathā hi devadattaḥ dhana saṃbandhāt pūrvam dhana vyatiriktaḥ vyavasthitaḥ san artha antara bhūtam eva pṛthak siddham dhanam upādatte evam upādātuḥ api sva ātma vyatirekeṇa artha antara bhūtam darśana ādikam upādānam syāt 
[81,ix_82,i]	na tu saṃbhavati iti āha ajyate kenacid kaścid kiṃcid kenacid ajyate kutas kiṃcid vinā kaścid kiṃcid kaṃcid vinā kutas iha bīja ākhyena kāraṇena kiṃcid kāryam abhivyajyate aṅkura ākhyam tena ca kāryeṇa kiṃcid kāraṇam abhivyajyate bīja ākhyam asya idam kāraṇam idam asya kāryam iti evam yadi kenacid darśana ādikena upādānena kaścid ātma svabhāvaḥ abhivyajyate asya ayam upādātā iti kenacid ca ātmanā kiṃcid upādānam darśana ādikam abhivyajyate idam asya upādānam iti tadānīm syāt paraspara apekṣayoḥ upādāna upādātroḥ siddhiḥ yadā tu upādātāram vinā pṛthak siddham darśana ādikam abhyupagamyate tadā tat nirāśrayam asat eva tasmāt na asti ubhayoḥ api siddhiḥ iti na yuktam etat darśana ādibhyaḥ pṛthak avasthitaḥ upādāta iti 
[82,ii_82,iii]	atra āha yat uktam darśana śravaṇa ādibhyaḥ ityādi atra ucyate yadi sarvebhyaḥ darśanādibhya prāk avasthitaḥ iti abhyupagatam syāt syāt eṣa doṣaḥ yadā tu sarvebhyaḥ darśana ādibhyaḥ kaścid pūrvaḥ na vidyate kim tarhi ekaikasmāt pūrvaḥ vidyate yadā ca evam tadā ajyate darśana ādīnām anyena punar anyadā yadā darśanena draṣṭā iti abhivyajyate na tadā śravaṇa ādīni upādāya prajñapyate tatas ca pūrva ukta doṣa an avasaraḥ iti 
[82,iv_82,v]	ucyate etat api na yuktam darśana ādi rahitasya nirupādānasya nirhetukasya nirañjanasya astitva asaṃbhavāt sarvebhyaḥ darśana ādibhyaḥ yadi pūrvaḥ na vidyate iti parikalpyate evam api ekaikasmāt katham pūrvaḥ darśana ādeḥ sa vidyate yaḥ hi sarvebhyaḥ pūrvaḥ na bhavati saḥ ekaikasmāt api na bhavati tat yathā sarvebhyaḥ vṛkṣebhyaḥ prāk vanam na asti tadā ekaikasmāt api na asti sarvāsām ca sikatānām taila janana abhāve sati ekaikasyāḥ api sikatāyāḥ tailam na asti api ca yaḥ hi ekaikasmāt pūrvaḥ bhavati nanu sa sarvebhyaḥ api pūrvam eva iti abhyupagatam bhavati ekaika vyatirekeṇa sarvasya abhāvāt tasmāt na yuktam ekaikasmāt pūrvaḥ vidyate iti 
[82,vi_82,viii]	itas ca na yuktam yasmāt draṣṭā saḥ eva sa śrotā saḥ eva yadi vedakaḥ tadā ekaikasmāt bhavet pūrvam na ca yuktam vaktum saḥ eva draṣṭā saḥ eva śrotā iti yadi syāt tadā darśana kriyā rahitasya api śrotuḥ draṣṭṭa tvam syāt śravaṇa kriyā rahitasya api draṣṭuḥ śrotṛ tvam syāt na ca evam dṛṣṭam yad darśana kriyā rahitaḥ api draṣṭā syāt śravaṇa kriyā rahitaḥ ca śrotā iti atas eva āha evam ca etat na yujyate iti pratikriyam ca kāraka bhedāt kutas etat evam bhaviṣyati iti pratipādayan āha evam ca etat na yujyate iti 
[83,i]	ācārya buddha pālitaḥ tu vyācaṣṭe eka tve hi ātmanaḥ indriya antara gamana prasaṅgaḥ puruṣasya syāt vātāyana antara upagamana vat iti asya ācārya bhāva vivekaḥ dūṣaṇam āha sarva gatasya ātmanaḥ na indriya antara gamanam asti iti ayuktaḥ prasaṅga doṣaḥ iti tat etat ayuktam sva yūthya parikalpita pudgala vāda nirāsasya prastuta tvāt tasya ca sarva gata tva apratijñānāt tasmāt yuktaḥ eva prasaṅga doṣa 
[83,ii_83,iii]	atha api yathā ukta doṣa parijihīrṣayā draṣṭā anyaḥ eva śrotā anyaḥ vedakaḥ anyaḥ punar yadi parikalpyate tat api na yuktam evam hīṣyamāṇe sati syāt draṣṭari śrotā bahu tvam ca ātmanām bhavet tat yathā goḥ anyaḥ aśvaḥ na hi gavi sati na bhavati yaugapadyena evam yadi draṣṭuḥ anyaḥ śrotā syāt sa draṣṭari api sati syāt yaugapadyena na ca evam iṣyate iti na asti anya tvam api ca evam sati bahavaḥ eva ātmānaḥ prāpnuvanti draṣṭṭa śrotṛ vedaka ādīnām pṛthak pṛthak siddhayupagamāt tasmāt ekaikasmāt api darśana ādeḥ pūrvam na asti pudgalaḥ nāma kaścid 
[83,iv]	atra āha vidyate eva pūrvam sa sarvebhyaḥ darśana ādibhyaḥ ātmā atha matam yadi asti kena prajñapyate saḥ iti yat ucyate iha darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam nāma rūpa avasthāyām catvāri mahābhūtāni santi yatas kramāt nāma rūpa pratyayam ṣaṣ āyatanam iti darśana śravaṇa ādīni utpadyante tasmāt darśana ādibhyaḥ pūrvam catur mahābhūta upādānam eva asti iti evam api darśana śravaṇa ādīni vedanā ādīni ca api atha bhavanti yebhyaḥ teṣu eṣa bhūteṣu api na vidyate 
[83,v]	yebhyaḥ mahābhūtebhyaḥ darśana ādikam utpadyate teṣu api mahābhūta upādāna nimittakaḥ api eṣa na yujyate pūrveṇa eva hetunā iti abhiprāyaḥ tatra yathā pūrvam uktam kutas kiṃcid vinā kaścid kiṃcid kaṃcid vinā kutas iti iha api tathā eva vaktavyam mahābhūta upādāna āt yaḥ ca ātmā pūrvam siddhaḥ syāt sa mahābhūtāni upādāya syāt na ca evam nirhetuka tvāt yaḥ ca na asti sa katham mahābhūtāni upādāsyati iti darśana upādāna vat bhūta upādāne api dūṣaṇam uktam eva iti na punar ucyate 
[83,vi_84,i]	atra āha yadi api evam ātmā pratiṣiddhaḥ tathā api darśana ādikam asti apratiṣedhāt na ca anātma svabhāvānām ghaṭa ādīnām darśana ādi saṃbandhaḥ asti tasmāt saṃbandhī vidyate eva ātmā iti ucyate syāt ātmā yadi darśana ādīni eva syuḥ na tu santi yasya darśana ādīni upādānam sa yadā na asti iti pratipāditam tadā tasmin ātmani upādātari asati kutas darśana ādīnām upādāna bhūtānām astitvam iti āha darśana śravaṇa ādīni vedanā ādīni ca api atha na vidyate ced yasya sa na vidyante imāni api yasya darśana ādīni parikalpyante sa yadā na asti iti uktam nanu tadā eva darśana ādikam api na asti iti spaṣṭam ādarśitam bhavati tatas ca darśana ādi abhāvāt na asti eva ātmā iti 
[84,ii]	atra āha kim khalu bhavataḥ niścitam etat na asti eva ātmā iti kena etat uktam nanu ca anantaram eva uktam darśana ādi abhāvāt ātmā api na asti iti uktam etadā īsmābhiḥ na tu asya arthaḥ bhavatā samyak niḥ citaḥ yatas bhāva rūpaḥ ātmā iti parikalpitaḥ sa svabhāvataḥ na vidyate tasya ca mayā svabhāva abhiniveśa nivartakam eva vacanam uktam asat viparyāsa pratipakṣeṇa na tu asya abhāvaḥ parikalpitaḥ dvayam hi etat parityājyam yaḥ ca bhāveṣu abhiniveśaḥ yaḥ ca abhāveṣu abhiniveśaḥ iti yathā uktam ārya devena yaḥ tava ātmā mama anātmā tena ātma aniyamān na saḥ nanu anityeṣu bhāveṣu kalpanā nāma jāyate iti 
[84,iii_84,iv]	etat eva pratipādayan āha prāk ca yaḥ darśana ādibhyaḥ sāṃpratam ca ūrdhvam eva ca na vidyate asti na asti iti nivṛttāḥ tatra kalpanāḥ prāk tāvat darśana ādibhyaḥ ātmā na asti tatra hi tasya astitva abhāvāt darśana ādi saha bhūtaḥ api na asti pṛthak pṛthak asiddhayoḥ sahabhāva adarśanāt śaśa śṛṅgayoḥ iva ātma upādānayoḥ ca paraspara nirapekṣayaḥ pṛthak pṛthak asiddha tvāt sāṃpratam api na asti urdhvam api yadi hi pūrvam darśana ādīni syuḥ uttara kālam ātmā syāt tadānīm ūrdhvam saṃbhavet na ca evam akartṛkasya karmaṇaḥ asiddha tvāt yaḥ ca evam ātmā darśana ādibhyaḥ prāk paścāt yugapad ca parīkṣyamāṇaḥ na asti tasya idānīm anupalabdha svabhāvasya astitvam nāstitvam vā kaḥ parikalpayet prājñaḥ tasmāt karma kāraka vat eva upādāna upādātroḥ paraspara apekṣā siddhiḥ na svābhāvikī iti sthitam 
[84,v]	atas eva uktam bhagavatā ārya samādhi rāja bhaṭṭārake tahi kāli saḥ daśa balaḥ anaghaḥ jinu bhāṣate imu samādhi varam su pinā upamā bhagavatī sakalā na hi kaści jāyati na caḥ mriyate na ca sattvu labhyati na jīvu naraḥ imi dharma phena kadalī sadṛśāḥ māyā upamāḥ gagana vidyu samāḥ daka candra saṃnibha marīci samāḥ na ca asmi loki mṛtu kaści naraḥ para loka saṃkramati gacchati vā na ca karma naśyati kadāci kṛtam phalu deti kṛṣṇa śubha saṃsarataḥ na ca śāśvatam na ca uccheda punaḥ na ca karma saṃcayu na ca api sthitiḥ na ca saḥ api kṛtva punar āspṛśati na ca anyu kṛtva puna vedayate na ca saṃkramaḥ na ca punā āgamanam na ca sarvam asti na ca na asti punar na ca dṛṣṭi sthāna gati śuddhiḥ iha na ca sattva cāra supaśānta gati anutpāda śānta animitta padam sugatāna gocara jināna guṇā bala dhāraṇī daśa balāna balam buddha aniyam vṛṣamitā paramā 
[86,i]	atra āha yat idam uktam tasmāt karma kāraka vat eva upādāna upādātroḥ api na svābhāvikī siddhiḥ iti tat ayuktam sa apekṣāṇām api padārthānām sa svābhāvya darśanāt tathā hi agniḥ indhanam apekṣya bhavati na ca niḥsvabhāvaḥ agniḥ tasya auṣṇya dāhaka tva ādi svabhāva kārya upalambhāt evam agnim apekṣyaḥ indhanam bhavati na ca tad niḥsvabhāvam bāhya mahābhūta catuṣṭaya svabhāva tvāt evam upādāna sāpekṣaḥ api upādātā svabhāvataḥ bhaviṣyati upādātṛ sāpekṣam ca upādānam iti agni in dhana vat etau bhaviṣyate upādāna upādātārau iti ucyate syāt etat evam yadi agni indhane eva syātām na tu staḥ katham iha yadi agni indhane syātām niyatam te eka tvena vā syātām anya tvena vā ubhayathā tu na yujyate iti āha yat indhanam sa ced agniḥ ekatvam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ anyaḥ ced indhanāt agniḥ indhanāt api ṛte bhavet 
[86,ii]	tatra idhyate yat tad indhanam dāhyam kāṣṭha ādika saṃbhūtam tasya dagdhā kartā agniḥ tatra yadi tāvat yat indhanam saḥ eva agniḥ iti parikalpyate tadā kartṛ karmaṇoḥ ekatvam syāt na ca evam dṛṣṭam ghaṭa kumbhakārayoḥ chet tṛ chettavyayoḥ ca eka tva prasaṅgāt tasya ca anabhyupagamāt atha anya tvam evam api yadi indhanāt anyaḥ agniḥ syāt tadā indhana nirapekṣasya agneḥ upalabdhiḥ syāt na hi ghaṭāt anyaḥ paṭaḥ tad nirapekṣaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ na ca evam indhana nirapekṣaḥ agniḥ iti na yuktam etat 
[86,iii_86,iv]	api ca yadi indhanāt anyaḥ agniḥ syāt tadānīm nitya pradīptaḥ eva syāt apradīpana hetukaḥ punar ārambha vaiyarthyam evam ca akarmakaḥ sati indhanāt pṛthak bhūtaḥ agniḥ iṣyamāṇaḥ nitya pradīptaḥ eva syāt apradīpana hetukaḥ ca syāt punar ārambha vaiyarthyam ca syāt evam ca sati akarmakaḥ eva syāt 
[86,v]	amum eva artham pratipādayitu kāmaḥ āha paratra nirapekṣa tvāt apradīpana hetukaḥ punar ārambha vaiyarthyam nitya dīptaḥ prasajyate iti tatra pradīpyate tat iti pradīpanam indhanam pradīpanam hetuḥ asya iti pradīpana hetuka na pradīpana hetukaḥ apradīpana hetukaḥ yadi pradīpanāt anyaḥ agniḥ syāt tadā indhana nirapekṣaḥ syāt yaḥ hi yasmāt anyaḥ sa tad nirapekṣaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ghaṭāt iva paṭaḥ tatas ca paratra nirapekṣa tvāt apradīpana hetukaḥ syāt pradīpana sa apekṣasya hi agneḥ tad abhāve syāt nirvāṇam yadā tu pradīpana nirapekṣa tadā nirvāṇa pratyaya vaikalyāt nitya pradīptaḥ eva bhavet nitya pradīpte ca agnau sati agneḥ aparinirvāṇa artham ca asya upādāna saṃdhukṣaṇa ādikam vyartham eva syāt evam ca sati akarmakaḥ agniḥ kartā syāt na ca avidyamāna karmakasya kartṛ tvam vandhyā sutasya iva tasmāt indhanāt agneḥ anyatvam iti na yujyate 
[87,i]	atra āha yat etat uktam anyaḥ ced indhanāt agniḥ indhanāt api ṛte bhavet iti tat ayuktam iha anya tve api sati agni indhanayoḥ na vinā eva indhanena agneḥ astitvam yasmāt jvālā parigataḥ arthaḥ dāhya tva lakṣaṇaḥ indhanam tad āśrayeṇa ca agniḥ upalabhyate na pṛthak yadā ca etat evam agni saṃbandhāt eva indhana vyapadeśaḥ bhavati indhana āśrayeṇa ca agniḥ upalabhyate na pṛthak tadā anyaḥ ced indhanāt agniḥ ityādi doṣa prasaṅgasya na asti eva avasaraḥ iti asya pakṣasya āṣya yukta tām udbhāvayan āha tatra etasmāt idhyamānam indhanam bhavati iti ced kena idhyatām indhanam tat tāvat mātram idam yadā 
[87,ii_87,iii]	yadi manyase jvālā parigataḥ arthaḥ dāhya lakṣaṇaḥ indhanam tad āśrayaḥ ca agniḥ iti evam api parikalpyamāne indhanam agniḥ dahati iti na upapadyate yasmāt kena idhyatām indhanam tat tāvat mātram idam yadā iha indhanam agniḥ dahati iti parikalpyamāne jvālā parigatam dāhyam indhanam iti na ca etat vayatirekeṇa aparam agnim paśyāmaḥ yena indhanam dahyeta yasmāt etāvat mātram idam upalabhyate yat uta jvālā parigatam dāhya mātram yadā ca etat vayatiriktaḥ na asti agniḥ tadā kena tat indhanam dāhyatām tāvat mātram idam yadā idhyamāna mātram idam yadā iti arthaḥ tasmāt na agniḥ indhanam dahati tadvayati rikta agni abhāvāt yadā ca evam tadā kutas kasyacid jvālā parigatiḥ iti saḥ eva doṣaḥ na vepate 
[87,iv_87,v]	api ca anya tva abhyupagame agni indhanayoḥ idhyamāna vyapadeśa abhāvāt kutas idhyamānam indhanam kutas vai indhanam agniḥ dhakṣyati iti pratipādayan āha anyaḥ na prāpsyate aprāptaḥ na dhakṣyati adahan punar na nirvāsyati anirvāṇaḥ sthāsyate vā sva liṅgavān yadi indhanāt anyaḥ agniḥ syāt saḥ anya tvāt andhakāram iva indhanam na prāpnuyāt na ca dhakṣyati aprāpta tvāt viprakṛṣṭa deśa avasthitam iva iti abhiprāyaḥ evam ca idhyamānam indhanam bhavati iti na upapannam eva tatas ca agneḥ nirvāṇam na syāt anirvāṇaḥ ca sva liṅgavān eva sthāsyati pradīptaḥ iti arthaḥ vā śabdaḥ avadhāraṇe draṣṭavyaḥ vikalpa arthaḥ vā sva liṅgavān eva agniḥ sthāsyati yadi vā na asti anya tvam agneḥ indhanāt iti samuccaye vā anyaḥ na prāpsyati na dhakṣyati na ca nirvāsyati sva liṅgavān ca sthāsyati tasmāt ayuktam indhanāt anya tvam agneḥ 
[88,i_88,ii]	atra āha ayuktam agni indhanayoḥ anya tvam yasmāt na prāpsyate aprāptaḥ na dhakṣyati adahan punar ityādi tat ayuktam dṛṣṭā hi anya tve strī puruṣayoḥ prāptiḥ evam agni indhanayoḥ api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate anyaḥ eva indhanāt agniḥ indhanam prāpnuyāt yadi strī saṃprāpnoti puruṣam puruṣaḥ ca striyam yathā syāt etat evam yadi strī puruṣa vat paraspara anapekṣāḥ agni indhanayoḥ siddhiḥ syāt 
[88,iii_88,iv]	na tu asti iti āha anyaḥ eva indhanāt agniḥ indhanam kāmam āpnuyāt agni indhane yadi syātām anyonyena tiraskṛte na tu evam saṃbhavati yat indhana nirapekṣaḥ agniḥ syāt agni nirapekṣam ca indhanam iti tasmāt dṛṣṭānta vaiyarthyam anyonya apekṣā adhīna janmanām sati anya tve yeṣām prāptiḥ siddhā teṣām eva dṛṣṭānta tvena upādānam nyāyyam syāt te ca na saṃbhavanti iti na yuktam etat anya tve sati prāptiḥ asti iti 
[88,v]	atra āha yadi api agni indhanayoḥ strī puruṣa vat paraspara nirapekṣā siddhiḥ na asti tathā api paraspara apekṣā tāvat asti tatas ca asti eva agni in dhanayoḥ svarūpa siddhiḥ paraspara sāpekṣa tvāt na hi avidyamānayoḥ vandhyā putra duhitroḥ paraspara apekṣa tā dṛṣṭā iti ucyate evam api yadi indhanam apekṣya agniḥ apekṣya agnim yadi indhanam katarat pūrva niṣpannam yat apekṣya agniḥ indhanam 
[88,vi]	asya indhanasya ayam agniḥ dāhakaḥ kartā iti evam yadi indhanam apekṣya agniḥ vyavasthāpyate asya agneḥ idam indhanam karma iti evam agnim apekṣya yadi indhanam tat katarat anayoḥ pūrva niṣpannam kim indhanam yat apekṣya agni syāt uta agniḥ yam apekṣya indhanam syāt tatra yadi indhanam pūrva niṣpannam iti kalpyate tat ayuktam agni nirapekṣasya anidhyamānasya indhana tva abhāvāt tṛṇa ādeḥ sarvasya ca eva indhana tva prasaṅgāt atha pūrvam agniḥ paścāt indhanam iti tat api ayuktam indhanāt pūrva siddhasya agneḥ asaṃbhavāt nirhetuka tva prasaṅgāt paścāt ca apekṣayā niṣprayojana tvāt tasmāt na asti atra kiṃcid pūrva siddham yat apekṣyaḥ itarasya siddhi syāt 
[88,vii_89,i]	atha api manyase pūrvam indhanam paścāt agniḥ iti evam api yadi indhanam apekṣya agniḥ agneḥ siddhasya sādhanam bhaviṣyati yadi indhanam apekṣya agniḥ bhaviṣyati iti parikalpyate evam tarhi siddhasya sataḥ agneḥ punar api sādhanam syāt vidyamānasya eva padārthasya siddha rūpasya apekṣā yujyate na hi avidyamānaḥ devadattaḥ gṛhe kaṃcid apekṣate evam yadi agniḥ vidyamānaḥ na syāt na asau indhanam apekṣate tasmāt astitvam agne rambhu peyam tadā ca kim asya indhanasya apekṣayā punar kartavyam na hi siddhaḥ agniḥ punar indhanena kartavyaḥ yad artham indhana apekṣā sāphalyam syāt tasmāt indhanam apekṣya agniḥ bhavati iti na yuktam api ca yadi indhanam apekṣya agniḥ bhavati iti parikalpyate evam sati indhanam ca api bhaviṣyati niragnikam yadi indhanam asiddham syāt na eva tad agninā apekṣyeta asiddhasya apekṣā yogāt tasmāt niragnikasya indhanasya siddhiḥ abhyupeyā na ca evam etat iti na yuktam etat iti 
[89,ii]	atha matam yaugapadyena eva indhana siddhayā agni siddhiḥ agni siddhayā ca indhana siddiḥ tatas ca ekasya api pūrva siddhayanabhyupagamāt tatra yat uktam katarat pūrva niṣpannam yat apekṣya agniḥ indhanam iti tat ayuktam iti ucyate evam apīṣyamāṇe ubhayasya api na asti siddhiḥ yasmāt yaḥ apekṣya sidhyate bhāvaḥ tam eva apekṣya sidhyati yadi yaḥ apekṣitavyaḥ sa sidhyatām kam apekṣya kaḥ 
[89,iii]	tatra yadi yaḥ agni ākhyaḥ bhāvaḥ yam indhana ākhyam bhāvam apekṣya sidhyati indhana ākhyaḥ ca bhāvaḥ yaḥ agninā ātma siddhayartham apekṣitavyaḥ sa yadi tam eva agni ākhyam padārtham apekṣya sidhyati kathyatām idānīm sidhyatām kam apekṣya kaḥ iti yadā ca agni abhāve sati indhanasya siddhiḥ eva na asti tadā akāraṇasya indhanasya abhāvāt kutas tad hetukaḥ agniḥ prasetsyati evam yaḥ indhana ākhyaḥ bhāvaḥ yamagni ākhyam bhāvam apekṣya sidhyati agni ākhyaḥ ca bhāvaḥ yaḥ indhana ākhyena ātma siddhayartham apekṣitavyaḥ sa yadi tam eva indhana ākhyam bhāvam apekṣya sidhyati kathyatām kim idānīm sidhyatām kam apekṣya kaḥ iti yadā hi indhana abhāve sati agneḥ siddhiḥ na asti tadā niṣkāraṇasya agneḥ abhāvāt kutas tat hetukam indhanam 
[89,iv_89,v]	itas ca agni indhanayoḥ paraspara apekṣayā api siddhiḥ asatī siddha asiddhayoḥ apekṣā bhāvāt iti pratipādayan āha yaḥ apekṣya sidhyate bhāvaḥ saḥ asiddhaḥ apekṣate katham atha api apekṣate siddhaḥ tu apekṣā asya na yujyate yaḥ hi agni ākhyaḥ bhāvaḥ indhana ākhyam bhāvam apekṣya sidhyati saḥ asiddhaḥ vai indhanam apekṣate siddhaḥ vā yadi asiddhaḥ tadā asiddha tvāt khara viṣāṇa vat na indhanam apekṣeta atha siddhaḥ siddha tvāt kim asya indhana apekṣayā na hi siddham punar api sādhyate vaiyarthyāt evam indhane api vācyam tasmāt na agni in dhanayoḥ paraspara apekṣayā yaugapadyena vā siddhiḥ iti 
[89,vi_90,ii]	yatas ca evam tasmāt apekṣya indhanam agniḥ na atha syāt anapekṣya agniḥ tarhi bhaviṣyati iti etat api na yuktam iti āha na anapekṣya agniḥ indhanam anya tva pratiṣedhāt ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt ca yathā ca agniḥ apekṣya vā anapekṣya vā indhanam saṃbhavati evam indhanam api iti āha apekṣya indhanam agnim na na anapekṣya agnim indhanam etat ca anantaram eva gata artha tvāt na punar ucyate 
[90,iii]	atra āha kim anayā asmākam ati sūkṣma īkṣikayā prayojanam ye vayam brūmaḥ yasmāt agninā idhyamānam indhanam pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyate tasmāt te eva agni indhane iti ucyate syāt etat evam yadi agniḥ indhanam dahet yadi indhane agniḥ saṃbhavet saḥ indhanam dahet na tu saṃbhavati iti āha āgacchati anyatas na agniḥ indhane agniḥ na vidyate 
[90,iv]	indhana vyatiriktāt tāvat kutaścid anyatas agneḥ āgamanam na asti tasya adṛṣṭa tvāt nirindhanasya ca ahetukasya agneḥ āgamana abhāvāt sa indhanasya ca āgamane prayojana abhāvāt tatra api ca indhane tulya paryanuyogāt anavasthā prasaṅgāt ca āgacchati anyatas na agniḥ tathā indhane api agniḥ na saṃbhavati tatra anupalabhyamāna tvāt 
[90,v]	atha syāt vidyamānasya api mūla udaka ādi vat abhivyañjaka pratyaya vaikalyāt pūrvam anupalabhyamāna tvam araṇi nigharṣaṇāt abhivyañjaka pratyaya saṃbhavāt tu paścāt upalabdhiḥ iti idam eva tāvat saṃpradhāryate kim punar mūla udaka ādīnām abhivyañjakaiḥ pratyayaiḥ kriyate iti tatra svarūpam tāvat na kriyate vidyamāna tvāt abhivyaktiḥ kriyate iti ced kā iyam abhivyaktiḥ nāma prakāśa ta iti ced evam tarhi sā eva kriyate pūrvam avidyamāna tvāt asyāḥ satkārya vāda tyāgaḥ ca evam jāyate abhivyakteḥ pūrvam avidyamāna tvāt paścāt ca bhāvāt svarūpasya ca utpatti pratyaya nirapekṣa tvāt khapuṣpa vat abhivyakti pratyaya sāpekṣatā api na syāt api ca iyam abhivyaktiḥ abhivyaktasya vā bhāvasya parikalpyeta anabhivyaktasya vā tatra tāvat yat abhivyaktam tat na abhivyajyate tasya abhivyakti vaiyarthyāt aniṣṭa doṣa prasaṅgāt ca anabhivyaktam api na abhivyajyate kha puṣpa vat ana bhivyakta tvāt iti evam abhivyaktiḥ na saṃbhavati 
[90,vi]	atha api syāt vidyamānasya eva pratyayaiḥ sthaulyam kriyate iti evam api yat eva sthaulyam pūrvam na asti iti tat eva kriyate iti kutas sthaulya āpādanam abhivyaktiḥ saukṣmyasya ca nirhetukasya asaṃbhavāt kasya sthūla tā āpādanāt abhivyaktiḥ syāt iti tat evam sarvathā indhane agneḥ na saṃbhavaḥ iti indhane agniḥ na vidyate na ca avidyamāna agninā indhanasya dahanam upajāyate iti asatyam eva etat upalabhate bhavān 
[90,vii_90,viii]	api ca yathā pūrvam gatāgata gamyamānānām dūṣaṇam uktam atra indhane śeṣa m uktam gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ agninā indhanam dahyamānam upalabhyate iti atra indhana prastāve śeṣam dūṣaṇam gamyamāna gata āgata dūṣaṇena veditavyam ukta pāṭha viparyayeṇa dagdham na dahyate tāvat adagdham na eva dahyate dagdhā dagdha vinirmuktam dahyamānam na dahyate ityādinā yatas evam atas na asti agninā indhanasya dahanam iti veditavyam 
[91,i_91,ii]	idānīm yathā upapāditam artham nigamayan āha indhanam punar agniḥ na na agniḥ anyatra ca indhanāt na agniḥ indhanavān na agnau indhanāni na teṣu saḥ tatra yat indhanam sa ced agniḥ ekatvam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ bhavet iti anena agni indhanayoḥ aka tva pratiṣedhāt indhanam punar agniḥ na anyaḥ ced indhanāt agniḥ indhanāt api ṛte bhavet ityādinā anya tvasya pratiṣedhāt na agniḥ anyatra ca indhanāt tattva anyatva ubhaya pakṣa pratiṣedhāt eva tadvat pakṣa ādhāra ādheya pakṣāṇām api arthataḥ pratiṣiddha tvāt tān api nigamayan āha na agniḥ indhanavān na agnau indhanāni na teṣu saḥ iti tatra agniḥ indhanavān na bhavati indhanam asya asmin vā vidyate iti vyatirekeṇa vā vyutpādena avyatirekeṇa vā tatra vyatirekeṇa tat yathā gomān devadattaḥ avyatirekeṇa buddhimān devadattaḥ rūpavān ityādi agni indhanayoḥ ca pakṣa dvayasya api pratiṣiddha tvāt indhanavān agniḥ iti pratiṣedhaḥ vihitaḥ anyat ca kuṇḍam dadhnaḥ ādhāra tām pratipadyate na ca indhanāt anya tvam agneḥ asti iti na agnau indhanāni iti yujyate na api indhane asti agniḥ anya tva pratiṣedhāt iti evam ādhāra ādheya tā pratiṣedhaḥ api arthataḥ upapāditaḥ eva 
[91,iii_91,iv]	yathā ca agniḥ pañcadhā vicāryamāṇaḥ na saṃbhavati evam ātmā api iti atidiśan āha agni indhanābhyām vyākhyātaḥ ātma upādānayoḥ kramaḥ sarvaḥ niravaśeṣeṇa tatra upādīyate iti upādānam pañca upādāna skandhāḥ yaḥ tān upādāya prajñapyate saḥ upādātā grahītā niṣpādakaḥ ātmā iti ucyate ahaṃkāra viṣaya tvāt āhitaḥ utpāditaḥ ahaṃmānaḥ asmin iti tat asya ātmanaḥ upādānasya ca yaḥ kramaḥ siddhiḥ sa sarvaḥ agni indhanābhyām vyākhyātaḥ avagantavyaḥ niravaśeṣeṇa 
[92,i]	kaḥ punar sarvasya niravaśeṣasya ca bhedaḥ sarva grahaṇena eva pañca pakṣāḥ samanantara prakrānta abhisaṃbadhyante sarve ete pañca api pakṣāḥ agni indhana vat ātma upādānayoḥ api avikalāḥ ḍhaukanīyāḥ yaḥ ca eyā pratipādane upapatti kramaḥ prāk upavarṇitaḥ tena niravaśeṣeṇa ātma upādānayoḥ pratiṣedhaḥ veditavyaḥ iti anena sarva ātmanā pratiṣedha sāmyam agni indhanābhyām ātma upādānayoḥ veditavyam iti upadarśana artham sarvaḥ nirava śeṣeṇa iti āha tatra yat eva upādānam saḥ eva ātmā iti evam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ ekatva prasaṅgāt na yujyate na api anyat upādānam anyaḥ upādātā skandha vyatirekeṇa api ātma upalabdhi prasaṅgāt paratra nirapekṣa tvāt itya ādi prasaṅgāt ca ekatva anyatva pratiṣedhāt ca skandhavān aṣya ātmā na bhavati anya tva abhāvāt ca na ātmani skandhāḥ na skandheṣu ātmā yatas evam pañcasu prakāreṣu ātmanaḥ na sattvam tasmāt karma kāraka vat eva ātma upādānayoḥ paraspara āpekṣikī siddhiḥ iti sthitam 
[92,ii_92,iii]	yaḥ ca ayam ātma upādānayoḥ kramaḥ sa na anayoḥ eva kim tarhi sārdham ghaṭa paṭa ādibhiḥ niravaśeṣaiḥ padārthaiḥ sarvathā vyākhyātaḥ veditavyaḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ hi kārya kāraṇa bhūta avayava avayavi bhūtāḥ lakṣaṇa lakṣya bhūtāḥ guṇa guṇi bhūtāḥ vā syuḥ tatra mṛd daṇḍa cakra sūtra salila kulāla karavyāyāma ādayaḥ ghaṭasya kāraṇa bhūtāḥ ghaṭaḥ kārya bhūtaḥ kapāla ādayaḥ nīla ādayaḥ vā avayava bhūtāḥ ghaṭaḥ avayavī pṛthu budhna lamba oṣṭha dīrgha grīva tva ādīni lakṣaṇāni ghaṭaḥ lakṣyaḥ śyāma tva ādayaḥ guṇāḥ ghaṭaḥ guṇī iti evam vyavasthāpya agni indhana vat kramaḥ yojyaḥ eṣām ca ghaṭa ādīnām ātma upādānayoḥ ca madhyamaka avatāra prakaraṇāt vyākhyānam avaseyam 
[92,iv]	tat evam karma kāraka vat ātma upādānayoḥ ghaṭa ādīnām ca paraspara apekṣikyām siddhau vyavasthitāyām tathāgata vacanā viparīta artha avabodha abhimāni tayā tīrthyamata upa kalpita padārtha vyavasthām saugata pravacana artha tvena upanīya ati mūḍha tayā ātmanaḥ ca sa tattvam ye bhāvānām ca pṛthak pṛthak nirdiśanti na tān manye śāsanasya artha kovidān 
[92,v]	tatra saha tena vartate iti satat satataḥ bhāvaḥ satattvam apṛthak tvam ananya tvam eka tvam iti arthaḥ tat etat satattvam ye varṇayanti na tān ācāryaḥ śāsana artha paṇḍitān manyate tat yathā ātmā upādānena prajñapyate yena saha eva tena upādānena saṃbhavati sa na pṛthak avyatirekeṇa eva bhavati iti arthaḥ evam yena kāraṇena mṛdādinā ghaṭaḥ prajñapyate tat avyatirekeṇa eva sa bhavati na pṛthak evam ātmanaḥ bhāvānām ca satattvam ye varṇayanti na te parama gambhīrasya pratītyasamutpāda stha śāśvata uccheda rahitasya upādāya prajñapti abhidhānasya tattvam paśyanti pṛthak pṛthak ca ye nirdiśanti pṛthak iti ātmānam pṛthak upādānam pṛthak kāryam pṛthak kāraṇam ityādinā anya tvam paśyanti amūn api na śāsanasya artha kovidāna ācāryaḥ manyate yathā uktam ekatva anyatva rahitam pratiśrutka upamam jagat saṃkrāntim āsādya gatam buddhavān tvam aninditaḥ 
[93,i]	evam ca agni indhana parīkṣayā adhigata dharma tattva paramasya yoginaḥ kalpena akāla ālipsitaiḥ api na eva vapuḥ dahyate rāga dveṣa moha hutāśanaiḥ api vā iti yathā uktam bhagavatā yatha gagaṇu na jātu dagdha pūrvam su bahubhi kalpa śataiḥ hi dahyamānam gagana sama vijānamāna dharmān saḥ api na dahyati jātu sa agni madhye sarvi hi jvalamāṇi buddha kṣetre praṇidhi karoti samādhiye sthihitvā jvalate ayu praśāmyatām aśeṣa pṛthivi vinaśyipi na evasya anyathātvam 
[93,ii]	tathā araṇim yatha ca uttara araṇim hasta vyāyāmu trayebhi saṃgatiḥ iti pratyayataḥ agni jāyate jātu kṛtu kārya laghū nirudhyate atha paṇḍitu kaści mārgate kutas ayam āgatu kutra yāti vā vidiśaḥ diśa sarvi mārgataḥ na agatiḥ na asya gatiḥ ca labhyati skandha āyatanāni dhātavaḥ śūnyaḥ ādhyātmika śūnya bāhirāḥ sarva ātma vivikta nālayā dharmaḥ ākāśa sabhāva lakṣaṇāḥ imu īdṛśa dharma lakṣaṇā buddhaḥ dīpaṃkara darśane tvayā anubuddha yatha tvayā ātmanā tatha bodhehi sa deva mānuṣān viparīta abhūta kalpitaiḥ rāga doṣaiḥ paridahyate jagat kṛpa megha śama ambu śītalām muñca dhārām amṛtasya nāyaka iti vistaraḥ 
[95,i]	atra āha vidyate eva ātmā saṃsāra sadbhāvāt yadi hi ātmā na syāt kasya pañcagatike ājavaṃjavībhāvena janma maraṇa paraṃparayā saṃsaraṇam syāt uktam hi bhagavatā anavara agraḥ hi bhikṣavaḥ jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāraḥ iti avidyā nīvaraṇānām sattvānām tṛṣṇā saṃyojanānām tṛṣṇā gaṇḍuḥ a baddhānām saṃsaratām saṃdhāvatām pūrvā koṭiḥ na prajñāyate iti yadā ca bhagavat upadeśāt saṃsāraḥ asti tadā saṃsartā api asti sa ca ātmā ucyate iti ucyate syāt ātmā yadā saṃsāraḥ eva syāt katham yasmāt asya pūrvā prajñāyate koṭiḥ na iti uvāca mahā muniḥ saṃsāraḥ anavara agraḥ hi na asya ādiḥ na api paścimam 
[95,ii]	koṭiḥ bhāgaḥ deśaḥ iti paryāyāḥ pūrvā koṭiḥ pūrvaḥ deśaḥ iti arthaḥ yadi hi saṃsāraḥ nāma kaścid syāt niyatam tasya pūrvam api syāt paścimam api ghaṭa ādīnām iva uktam ca bhagavatā anavara agraḥ hi bhikṣavaḥ jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāraḥ iti yat eva avara agre na staḥ saṃsārasya anavara agra vacanāt saṃsāraḥ eva na asti iti nanu spaṣṭam ādeśayāmāsa bhagavān tasmāt na asti saṃsāraḥ pūrva apara koṭayanupalambhāt alāta cakra vat iti sthitam 
[95,iii]	atra idam vicāryate yadi pūrvam ca aparam ca saṃsārasya niṣiddham bhagavatā katham punar idam āha tasmāt tarhi saṃsāra kṣayāya pratipatsyāmahe iti evam vaḥ bhikṣavaḥ śikṣitavyam iti ucyate avidyā nīvaraṇānām sattvānām ityādi viśeṣaṇa upādānāt teṣām eva ayam anavara agraḥ saṃsāraḥ iti pratīyate na punar tattva jñāna anila balāt samunmūlita avidyā nīvaraṇa tarūṇām teṣām tu loka uttara mārga jñāna agninā dagdha aśeṣa kleśa vāsanā mūla niḥśeṣa pādapānām bhavati eva antaḥ iti vijñeyam 
[95,iv_96,i]	katham punar ādiḥ ahitānām anta upadeśaḥ iti yāvat dṛṣṭam etat bāhyeṣu vrīhi ādiṣu ādi a bhāve api dahana ādi saṃparkāt anta sadbhāvaḥ yathā uktam ārya deva pādaiḥ yathā bījasya dṛṣṭaḥ antaḥ na ca ādiḥ tasya vidyate tathā kāraṇa vaikalyāt janmanaḥ api na saṃbhavaḥ iti sa ca anta upadeśaḥ laukikaḥ eva vyavahāre sthitvā saṃsāra cāraka avabaddhānām utsāhana artham sattvānām deśitaḥ laukika jñāna apekṣayā vastuka cintāyām tu saṃsāraḥ eva na asti tad kutas asya parikṣayaḥ pradīpa avasthāyām rajjūra ga parikṣaya vat atra āha yadi evam laukika jñāna apekṣayā antavat ādiḥ api kim na ucyate ucyate ahetuka doṣa prasaṅgāt laukika jñāna apekṣayā api saṃsārasya ādeḥ abhāvaḥ iti ubhayathā api ādeḥ abhāvaḥ eva iti vijñeyam 
[96,ii_96,iii]	atra āha yadya api avara agre na staḥ saṃsārasya tathā api madhyam asti apratiṣedhāt tatas ca asti saṃsāraḥ madhya sadbhāvāt iha yat na asti na tasya madhyam asti tat yathā kūrma roma prāvaraṇasya iti hāsyaḥ khalu asi nanu ca bhoḥ na eva agram na avaram yasya tasya madhyam kutas bhavet agram iti ādiḥ pūrvam prathamam ucyate avaram iti avasānam antar vyavacchedaḥ ucyate yasya saṃsārasya ādiḥ antaḥ ca pratiṣiddhaḥ tasya kutas madhyam bhaviṣyati tatas ca saṃjñā mātrakam eva viparyāsa para vaśa mānasānām saṃsāraḥ ādi madhya avasāna virahita tvāt ākāśa vat alāta cakra ādi vat iti bhāvaḥ saṃsāra abhāvāt ca na asti ātmā iti yatas evam saṃsārasya ādi madhya avasānāni na santi atas eva saṃsāra abhāvāt jāti jarā maraṇa ādīnām pūrva apara sahakramāḥ api na eva santi iti āha tasmāt na atra upapadyante pūrva apara saha kramāḥ 
[96,iv_96,v]	yathā ca na upapadyante tathā pratipādayan āha pūrvam jātiḥ yadi bhavet jarā maraṇam uttaram nirjara amaraṇā jātiḥ bhavet jāyeta ca amṛtaḥ yadi pūrvam jātiḥ bhavet tadā maraṇa sahitā syāt na ca jarā ādi rahitā jātiḥ yujyate asaṃskṛta tva prasaṅgāt jarā maraṇa rahitasya bhāvasya jātau parikalpyamānāyām anyatra amṛtasya eva devadattasya prathamam iha jātiḥ parikalpyamānā syāt tatas ca ādimān saṃsāraḥ syāt ahetuka doṣaḥ ca abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti evam pūrva anta kalpanā ca na syāt abhūtvā ca pūrvam paścāt iha utpādaḥ syāt 
[96,vi_96,viii]	atha syāt āmra ādīnām yathā pūrvam vinā api jarā maraṇa saṃbandhāt prathamam eva utpādaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ evam ātmānaḥ api iti na evam sādhya sama tvāt āmra ādīnām api hi sva bīja nirodhe samutpadyamāna tvāt na anyatra avinaṣṭānām utpādaḥ iti samam etat pūrveṇa atha syāt anyat eva vṛkṣāt bījam atas anyatra avināśa pūrvakaḥ eva vṛkṣasya utpādaḥ iti na evam kārya kāraṇayoḥ anyatvasya asiddha tvāt tathā ca vakṣyati pratītya yat yat bhavati na hi tāvat tat eva tat na ca anyat api tat tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam na ca bījāt vṛkṣasya anya tvam atas sādhya samam etat yatas ca anyatra amṛtasya iha utpādaḥ na asti na pūrvam jātiḥ abhyupeyā 
[97,i_97,ii]	atha pūrvam jarā maraṇam paścāt jātiḥ evam api paścāt jātiḥ yadi bhavet jarā maraṇam āditas ahetukam ajātasya syāt jarā maraṇam katham jāti pratyayam jarā maraṇam iti vacanāt jāti hetukam jarā maraṇam uktam bhagavatā yadi etat pūrvam syāt tadā nirhetukam syāt tasmāt na yuktam etat yatas api uktam yathaḥ ukkhitte loḍhammi ukkheve atthi kāraṇam paḍane kāraṇam ṇatthi aṇṇam ukkheva kāraṇā iti 
[97,iii]	yathā aṣyatra utkṣepaḥ patana kāraṇam na anyat evam iha api jātim evakāraṇa tvena vināśasya varṇayāmaḥ na anyat iti na asti ahetuka tā vināśasya jāti hetuka tvāt ca asya udgamanam eva vināśasya hetuḥ iti kṛtvā eṣā api gāthā sunītā bhavati evime saṃkhatāḥ dhammā saṃbhavanti sa kāraṇā sa bhāvaḥ eva dhammāṇam yam vibhonti samuggatā iti 
[97,iv_97,v]	idānīm sahabhāvena api jāti jarā maraṇānām asadbhāvam pratipādayan āha na jarā maraṇena eva jātiḥ ca saha yujyate mriyeta jāyamānaḥ ca syāt ca ahetu katobhayoḥ yadi sahabhāvaḥ jāti jarā maraṇānām syāt tadā jāyamānasya maraṇam syāt na ca etat yuktam na ca paraspara viruddha tvāt āloka andhakāra vat eka kālatā yuktā na ca evam loke dṛṣṭam yat jāyamānaḥ eva mriyate iti api ca ahetuka tvam jāti ādīnām sahabhāva kalpanāyām syāt na hi saha bhūtayoḥ savya itara go viṣāṇayoḥ anyonya hetuka tā dṛṣṭā iti na yuktam etat 
[97,vi_97,vii]	tat evam yatra na prabhavanti ete pūrva apara sahakramāḥ prapañcayanti tām jātim tad jarā maraṇam ca kim yasyām jātau yatra jarā maraṇe ete pūrva apara sahakramāḥ na santi tām jātim anupalabhamānāḥ āryāḥ kim prapañcayanti kiṃśabdaḥ asaṃbhave na eva prapañcayanti iti arthaḥ athavā evam avidyamāneṣu jāti ādiṣu tām jāti bha vidyamānām bālāḥ kim prapañcayanti tat ca jarā maraṇam yat na saṃvidyate tasmāt avastukaḥ eva bālānām prapañcaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[98,i_98,ii]	yathā ca saṃsārasya pūrvā koṭiḥ na asti evam anyeṣām api bhāvānām iti āha kāryam ca kāraṇam ca eva lakṣyam lakṣaṇam eva ca vedanā vedakaḥ ca eva santi arthāḥ ye ca kecana pūrvā na vidyate koṭiḥ saṃsārasya na kevalam sarveṣām api bhāvānām pūrvā koṭiḥ na vidyate tatra yadi pūrvam kāraṇam paścāt kāryam syāt akāryakam kāraṇam nirhetukam syāt atha pūrvam kāryam paścāt kāraṇam evam api kāraṇāt pūrvam kāryam nirhetukam eva syāt atha yugapad kārya kāraṇe syātām evam ubhayam api ahetukam syāt evam lakṣya lakṣaṇe vedanā vedakau ca yojyau na ca kevalam saṃsārasya vyākhyānena kārya kāraṇa ādikam vyākhyātam veditavyam api ca ye api ante padārthāḥ jñāna jñeya pramāṇa prameya sādhana sādhya avayava avayavi guṇa guṇī ādayaḥ teṣām api pūrvā koṭiḥ na vidyate iti yojyam atas eva ārya ratna megha sūtre ārya sarva nīvaraṇa viṣkambhiṇāḥ mahā bodhisattvena bhagavān stutaḥ ādi śāntāḥ hi anutpannāḥ prakṛtyā eva ca nirvṛtāḥ dharmāḥ te vivṛtā nātha dharma cakra pravartane iti 
[98,iii]	tathā ādita śūnya anāgata dharmāḥ naḥ gata asthita sthāna viviktāḥ nityam asāraka māyasa bhāvāḥ śuddha viśuddha nabha upama sarvi yam ca pabhāṣati dharma jinasya tam ca na paśyati saḥ akṣayatāya ādiniḥ ātma nisattvimi dharmāḥ tān ca ca pabhāṣati no ca kṣapā iti kalpita buccati kalpita mātram antu na labhyati saṃsaramāṇe koṭi alakṣaṇa yā puri āsīt a iti anāgati pratyaya tāye karma kriyā ca pravartati evam hīna autkṛṣṭa tayā samudenti jaḍḍaka dharma sadā prakṛtīye śūnya nirātma vijānatha sarvān ityādi 
[100,i_100,ii]	atra āha vidyate eva ātmā tad saṃbandhi duḥkha sadbhāvāt iha hi pañca upādāna skandhā duḥkham iti ucyate tat ca asti tena ca duḥkhena kasyacid bhavitavyam na nirāśrayeṇa iti atas vidyate eva duḥkhasya āśrayaḥ sa ca ātmā iti ucyate syāt ātmā yadi duḥkham eva syāt tat hi bhavet svayam kṛtam vā para kṛtam vā ubhaya kṛtam vā hetu rahitam vā sarvathā ca iṣyamāṇam tat kāryam eva na asti iti pratipādayan āha svayam kṛtam para kṛtam dvābhyām kṛtam ahetukam duḥkham iti ekaḥ icchanti tat ca kāryam na yujyate tatra eke vādinaḥ svayam kṛtam duḥkham iti pratipannāḥ apare punar para kṛtam anye ca ubhaya kṛtam kecid ahetu samutpannam eva duḥkham iti pratipannāḥ sarvathā ca tad duḥkham iṣyamāṇam kāryam kartavyam na yujyate tat etat pratijñā mātrakam iti 
[100,iii_100,iv]	tat pratipādayan āha svayam kṛtam yadi bhavet pratītya na tatas bhavet skandhān imānamī skandhāḥ saṃbhavanti pratītya hi yasmāt imān maraṇa antikān skandhān pratītya ime aupapattyā aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ utpadyante tasmāt svayam kṛtam duḥkham iti na upapadyate 
[100,v_100,vi]	idānīm para kṛtam api duḥkham yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha yadi amībhyaḥ ime anye syuḥ ebhyaḥ vā amī pare yadi bhavet para kṛtam duḥkham paraiḥ ebhiḥ amī kṛtāḥ yadā amībhyaḥ maraṇa antikebhyaḥ skandhebhyaḥ ime aupapattyā aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ anye syuḥ ebhyaḥ vā aupapattyā aṃśikebhyaḥ amī maraṇa antikā skandhāḥ pare syuḥ syāt tadānīm para kṛtam duḥkham na ca eṣām anya tvam dṛṣṭam hetu phala saṃbandha avasthānāt vakṣyati hi pratītya yat yat bhavati na hi tāvat tat eva tat na ca anyat api tat tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam iti atas para kṛtam api duḥkham na saṃbhavati yadi hi anya tvam syāt tadā sati anya tve etaiḥ para bhūtaiḥ skandhaiḥ amī para bhūtāḥ kṛtā iti yuktam vaktum syāt na ca etat evam iti para kṛtam api duḥkham na saṃbhavati 
[101,i]	atha syāt na brūmaḥ yasmāt duḥkhena eva duḥkham kṛtam atas svayam kṛtam iti kim tarhi sva pudgalena yasmāt svayam eva kṛtam na apareṇa kṛtvā dattam iti atas svayam kṛtam duḥkham iti brūmaḥ ucyate sva pudgala kṛtam duḥkham yadi duḥkham punar vinā sva pudgalaḥ sa katamaḥ yena duḥkham svayam kṛtam 
[101,ii]	yat etat manuṣya duḥkham pañca upādāna skandha lakṣaṇam svayam pudgalena kṛtam iti parikalpyate kalpyatām asau pudgalaḥ yena tad duḥkham svayam kṛtam yadi tāvat yena duḥkhena sva pudgalaḥ prajñapyate tat eva duḥkham tena kṛtam iti sa bhedena kathyatām idam tat duḥkham ayam asya kartā iti atha api manuṣya duḥkha upādānena pudgalena tat eva duḥkham kṛtam syāt na tarhi sva pudgala kṛtam tat para pudgala kṛtam eva syāt atha upādāna bhede api pudgala abhedaḥ iṣyate etat ca na asti upādāna vyatiriktasya bhinnasya pudgalasya darśayitum aśakyatvāt evam tāvat sva pudgala kṛtam duḥkham na bhavati 
[101,iii_101,iv]	atra āha kaḥ evam āha sva pudgala kṛtam duḥkham iti kim tarhi para pudgala jam duḥkham anyaḥ eva deva duḥkhāt manuṣya pudgalaḥ manuṣya pudgalaḥ ca deva duḥkham kṛtvā yasmāt deva pudgalāya dadāti tena ca deva duḥkhena deva pudgalaḥ prajñapyate tasmāt tasya pudgalasya tad duḥkham para pudgala jam eva bhavati ucyate para pudgala jam duḥkham yadi yasmai pradīyate pareṇa kṛtvā tad duḥkham sa duḥkhena vinā kutas yadi deva duḥkham manuṣya pudgala kṛtam tena ca manuṣya pudgalena tad duḥkham kṛtvā parasmai deva pudgalāya pradīyate iti sa deva pudgalaḥ deva duḥkha vinirmuktaḥ kutas yasmai pradīyeta iti evam tāvat apara pudgala jasya duḥkhasya pratigrāhakaḥ eva na asti 
[101,v_101,vi]	idānīm yaḥ ca dadāti asau api na asti iti āha para pudgala jam duḥkham yadi kaḥ para pudgalaḥ vinā duḥkhena yaḥ kṛtvā parasmai prahiṇoti tat yena upādānena sa manuṣya pudgalaḥ prajñapyate sa manuṣya upādāna vyatiriktaḥ katamaḥ yaḥ deva pudgalāya deva duḥkham kṛtvā praheṣyati tasmāt para pudgala jam api duḥkham na saṃbhavati 
[101,vii_102,i]	tatas ca svayaṃkṛtasya aprasiddheḥ duḥkham para kṛtam kṛtaḥ paraḥ hi duḥkham yat kuryāt tat tasya syāt svayam kṛtam yadi deva pudgala duḥkham manuṣya pudgalena kṛta tvāt para kṛtam bhavati nanu manuṣya pudgalasya svayaṃkṛtam eva tat bhavati etat ca na asti iti uktam tatas svayaṃkṛtasya aprasiddheḥ yadā manuṣya pudgalena svayam tat duḥkham na kṛtam tadā kutas para pudgalasya deva ākhyasya tad duḥkham para kṛtam bhaviṣyati iti atas api para kṛtam duḥkham na saṃbhavati 
[102,ii_102,iii]	idānīm prakaraṇa antareṇa api pakṣa dvaya asaṃbhavam pratipādayan āha na tāvat sva kṛtam duḥkham na hi tena eva tat kṛtam paraḥ na ātma kṛtaḥ ced syāt duḥkham para kṛtam katham itas ca sva parābhyām duḥkhasya karaṇam na yujyate yasmāt na tāvat sva kṛtam duḥkham kim kāraṇam yasmāt na tena eva hi tat kṛtam sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt atas sva kṛtam na asti na para kṛtam api yasmāt yaḥ asau paraḥ karoti iti parikalpyate saḥ eva tāvat na ātmanā kṛtaḥ na ātmanā niṣpannaḥ tasya api hetu antara apekṣaṇāt yaḥ ca sva ātmanā na niṣpannaḥ sa katham avidyamāna svabhāvaḥ san param kariṣyati iti na yuktam etat 
[102,iv_102,vii]	idānīm ubhaya kṛtam api duḥkham asat iti āha syāt ubhābhyām kṛtam duḥkham syāt ekaika kṛtam yadi yadi hi ekaikena duḥkhasya karaṇam syāt syāt tadānīm ubhābhyām kṛtam duḥkham na ca ekaika kṛtam tat ukta doṣāt na ca ekaikena prāṇa atipāte kṛte dvābhyām kṛtaḥ iti vyapadeśaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ idānīm nirhetukam api duḥkham yathā na asti tathā pratipadayan āha para ākāra asvayaṃkāram duḥkham ahetukam kutas pareṇa akāraḥ akaraṇam yasya iti para ākāram na svayaṃkāraḥ asya iti asvayaṃkāram yadi duḥkham svayaṃkṛtam na asti para kṛtam api na asti yathā uktena nyāyena tat idānīm kutas eva nirhetukam bhaviṣyati kha puṣpa saugandhya vat duḥkha abhāvāt kutas tasya āśraya bhūtaḥ ātmā 
[102,viii_102,ix]	yathā ca caturdhā vicāryamāṇam duḥkham asat evam bāhyāḥ api bīja aṅkura ghaṭa paṭa ādayaḥ bhāvāḥ veditavyāḥ iti pratipādayan āha na kevalam hi duḥkhasya cāturvidhyam na vidyate sarveṣām bāhyānām api bhāvānām cāturvidhyam na vidyate pūrvavat sarva samam yojyam yadi khalu eṣām duḥkha ādīnām cāturvidhyā saṃbhavaḥ tat katamena tarhi idānīm prakāreṇa eṣām siddhiḥ iti ucyate svabhāvataḥ yadi etāni duḥkha ādīni syuḥ niyatam eṣām caturṇām prakārāṇām anyatamena prakāreṇa siddhiḥ syāt na tu asti tasmāt svabhāvataḥ na santi duḥkha ādīni iti avasīyate atha viparyāsa mātra labdha ātma sattākāyāḥ duḥkha ādi saṃvṛteḥ pratītyasamutpāda vyavasthā mṛgyate tadā karma kāraka parīkṣā prakaraṇa vihita vidhinā yathā udita pakṣa catuṣṭaya tiraskāreṇa idaṃpratyaya tā mātra artha pratītyasamutpāda siddhayā siddhiḥ abhyupeyā yathā uktam svayaṃkṛtam para kṛtam dvābhyām kṛtam ahetukam tārkikaiḥ iṣyate duḥkham tvayā tu uktam pratītyajam iti 
[103,i_103,ii]	uktam ca bhagavatā ārya upāli pṛcchāyām tathā saṃvṛti bhāṣitu dharma jinena saṃskṛta asaṃskṛta paśyatha eva na astiha bhūtatu ātma naraḥ vai et taku lakṣaṇa sarva jagasya kṛṣṇa śubham ca na naśyati karma ātmana kṛtva ca vedayitavyam naḥ api tu saṃkrama karma phalasya no ca ahetuka pratyanubhoti sarvi bhavāḥ alikāḥ vasikāḥ ca riktaka tucchaka phena samāḥ ca māya marīci samā sada śūnyāḥ deśituḥ saṃvṛtu te ca viviktāḥ śaila guhā giri durga nadīṣu yat va pratiśruka jāyi pratītya evimu saṃskṛta sarvi vijāna māya marīci samam jagu sarvam ityādi 
[104,i]	yatas ca evam samanantara atikrānta prakaraṇa vidhinā sva para ubhaya kṛta tvam ahetu samutpana tvam ca nirūpyamāṇam bhāvānām asat anyaḥ ca utpādakaḥ vidhiḥ asan utpanna rūpa tvena ca ete bhāvāḥ avidyā timira upahatam ati nayanānām bāla pṛthagjanānām khyānti tasmāt niḥsvabhāvāḥ eva santaḥ bālānām visaṃvādakāḥ māyā kari tu raga ādi vat tad anabhijñānām na tu vijñānām atas eva sarva dharma svābhāva avyāparokṣadhī nayanaḥ samunmūlita aśeṣa avidyā vāsanaḥ catur viparyāsa viparyastā trāṇa sattva paritrāṇāya aviparītanaiḥ svābhāvya upadeśa tatparaḥ buddhaḥ jagat vibodhakaḥ mahākāruṇikaḥ tat mṛṣā moṣa dharma yat bhagavān iti abhāṣata sarve ca moṣa dharmāṇaḥ saṃskārāḥ tena te mṛṣā 
[104,ii]	sūtre uktam tat mṛṣā moṣa dharma yat idam saṃskṛtam etat hi khalu bhikṣavaḥ paramam satyam yat idamamoṣa dharma nirvāṇam sarva saṃskārāḥ ca mṛṣā moṣa dharmāṇaḥ iti tathā na asti atra tathatā avitatha tā vā moṣa dharmakam api etat pralopa dharmakam api etat iti tat anena nyāyena yat moṣa dharma tat mṛṣā iti evam yasmāt uktavān tathāgataḥ bhagavān sarve ca moṣa dharmāṇaḥ saṃskārāḥ tasmāt moṣa dharmaka tvena te saṃskārāḥ mṛṣā bhavanti citrakarayantra dārikā vat lakṣaṇa upeta yantra maya vāraṇa vañcita udayana vat sarāja vat tatra visaṃvādakam moṣa dharmakam vitatha khyātyā alāta cakra vat atas niḥsvabhāva tvena mṛṣā sarva saṃskārāḥ moṣa dharmaka tvāt marīcika ādi jala vat yat tu satyam na tad moṣa dharmakam tat yathā nirvāṇam ekam tatas ca vihitayā upapattyā asmāt ca āgamāt siddham sarva bhāvānām naiḥsvābhāvyam śūnyāḥ sarva dharmā niḥsvabhāva yogena iti ca prajñāpāramitā ardha śatikā pāṭhāt 
[104,iii]	atra āha yadi evam moṣa dharmaka tvena sarva saṃskārāṇām mṛṣā tvam pratipāditam bhavatā nanu evam sati na santi sarve bhāvāḥ iti sarva padārtha apavādinī mithyā dṛṣṭiḥ eva syāt ucyate satyam moṣa dharmakāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ ye adya api bhavantam muṣṇanti nanu ca bhoḥ tat mṛṣā moṣa dharma yat yadi kim tatra muṣyate 
[104,iv_104,v]	yadā asmābhiḥ tat mṛṣā moṣa dharmakam iti uktam tadā kim tatra muṣyate kim tatra abhāvaḥ bhavati kaścid yadi padārthaḥ abhaviṣyat syāt tasya apavādāt abhāva darśanāt mithyādṛṣṭiḥ yadā tu padārtham eva kaṃcid na paśyāmaḥ tadā kim tatra muṣyate na eva kiṃcid abhāvaḥ bhavati iti ayuktaḥ ayam upālambhaḥ bhavataḥ atra āha yadi abhāva darśanam api na pratipādyate kim punar anena āgamena pratipādyate iti ucyate etat tu uktam bhagavatā śūnyatā paridīpakam 
[104,vi]	yat etat uktam bhagavatā tat na bhāvānām abhāva paridīpakam kim tarhi śūnyatā paridīpakam svabhāva anutpāda paridīpakam iti arthaḥ yathā uktam anavatapta hradāpa saṃkramaṇa sūtre yaḥ pratyayaiḥ jāyati sa hi ajātaḥ no tasya utpādu sabhāvataḥ asti yaḥ pratyaya adhīnu sa śūnye uktaḥ yaḥ śūnyatām jānati saḥ apramattaḥ iti 
[105,i_105,ii]	atra āha na ayam āgamaḥ bhāva svabhāva anutpādam paridīpayati kim tarhi niḥsvabhāva tvam svabhāvasya anavasthāyi tvam vināśi tvam iti kutas etat iti ced bhāvānām niḥsvabhāva tvam anyathā bhāva darśanāt vicāryamāṇānām anyathātvam vipariṇāma darśanāt iti arthaḥ etat uktam bhavati yadi bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ na syāt tadānīm na eva eṣām anyathātvam upalabhyeta upalabhyate ca pariṇāmaḥ tasmāt svabhāvān ava sthāyi tvam eva sūtra arthaḥ iti vijñeyam 
[105,iii_105,iv]	itas ca etat evam yasmāt asvabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ na asti bhāvānām śūnyatā yatas yaḥ hi asvabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ sa na asti bhāvānām ca śūnyatā dharmaḥ iṣyate na ca asati dharmiṇi tad āśritaḥ dharmaḥ upapadyate na hi asati vandhyā tanaye tad śayāmata upapadyate iti tasmāt asti eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ iti 
[105,v_105,vii]	api ca kasya syāt anyathā bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ ced na vidyate yadi bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ na syāt yaḥ ayam vipariṇāma lakṣaṇaḥ anyathā bhāvaḥ sa kasya syāt iti atra ucyate evam api parikalpyamāne kasya syāt anyathā bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ yadi vidyate iha yaḥ dharmaḥ yam padārtham na vyabhicarati sa tasya svabhāvaḥ iti vyapadiśyate apara pratibaddha tvāt agneḥ auṣṇyam hi loke tat avyabhicāri tvāt svabhāvaḥ iti ucyate tat eva auṣṇyam apsu upalabhyamānam para pratyaya saṃbhūta tvāt kṛtrima tvāt na svabhāvaḥ iti yadā ca evam avyabhicāriṇā svabhāvena bhavitavyam tadā asya avyabhicāri tvāt anyathā bhāvaḥ syāt abhāvaḥ na hi agniḥ śaityam pratipadyate evam bhāvānām sati svabhāva abhyupagame anyathātvam eva na saṃbhavet upalabhyate ca eṣām anyathātvam atas na asti svabhāvaḥ 
[105,viii_106,i]	api ca ayam anyathā bhāvaḥ bhāvānām na eva saṃbhavati yad darśanāt sa svabhāva tā syāt yathā ca na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha tasya eva na anyathā bhāvaḥ na api anyasya eva yujyate yuvā na jīryate yasmāt yasmāt jīrṇaḥ na jīryate tasya eva tāvat prāgvat prāc avasthāyām vartamānasya bhāvasya anyathātvam na upapadyate tathā hi yūnaḥ yuvā avasthāyām eva vartamānasya na asti anyathātvam atha api avasthā antara prāptasya eva anyathātvam parikalpyate tat api na upapadyate anyathātvam nāma jarāyāḥ paryāyaḥ tat yadi yūnaḥ na iṣyate anyasya eva jīrṇasya bhavati iti tat api na yujyate yasmāt na hi jīrṇasya punar jarayā saṃbandhaḥ niṣprayojana tvāt kim hi jīrṇasya punar jarayā saṃbandhaḥ kuryāt tad āgamana antareṇa jīrṇa tā bhāvāt jīrṇaḥ jīryate iti na yujyate atha yūnaḥ eva anyathā bhāvaḥ tat ayuktam aprāpta jarā avasthasya yuvā iti vyapadeśāt avasthā dvayasya ca paraspara viruddha tvāt 
[106,ii_106,iv^1]	api ca tasya ced anyathā bhāvaḥ kṣīram eva bhavet dadhi atha syāt kṣīra avasthā parityāgena dadhi avasthā bhavati atas na kṣīram eva dadhi bhavati iti ucyate yadi kṣīram dadhi bhavati iti na iṣyate paraspara virodhāt kṣīrāt anyasya kasya atha dadhibhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati kim udakasya dadhi bhāvaḥ bhavatu tasmāt asaṃbaddham eva tad anyasya dadhibhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati iti tat evam anyathātva asaṃbhavāt kutas tad darśanāt sa svabhāva tā bhāvānām prasetsyati iti na yuktam etat yathā uktam ārya ratnākara mahāyāna sūtre yaḥ na pi jāyati no cupapadyī no cyavate na pi jīryati dharmaḥ tam jinu darśayatī narasiṃha tatra nideśayi sattva mahā ṛṣī yasya svabhāva na vidyati kaści naḥ apara bhāvatu kenaci labdhaḥ na antarataḥ na pi bāhiratas vā labhyati tatra niveśayi nāthaḥ śānta gatī kathitā sugatena no ca gatī upapadyati kāci tatra ca vyoharasī gati muktaḥ muktaku mocayasī bahu sattvān sarvi vadesi nirātmaka dharmān sattvatu grāhatu mocasi lokam 
[106,iv^2]	mukta svayam gatitaḥ gati muktaḥ tenasi pāra gataḥ na ca tīrṇaḥ pāra gataḥ asi bhava arṇava tīrṇaḥ pāra gataḥ na ca labhyati kaści pāru na vidyati na api apāru pāra gataḥ asmi vadesi ca vākyam vāca na vidyati yām ca vadesi yam pi vadesi na vidyati tam pi yasya vadesi na vidyati saḥ api yaḥ api vijānati saḥ api asantaḥ tatra praṇaṣṭu jagam imu sarvam vitatha vikalpa niveśa vaśena śānta vijānati yaḥ naru dharmām stehi tathā agatu dṛṣṭa svayaṃbhūḥ śānta prajānati dharma praṇītān prīti sa vindati toṣati sattvān saḥ bhavatī jinu jitvena kleśān ātma tena vijānita bodhi jinānām buddhiya bodhayate sa jagam pi ityādi 
[107,i_107,ii]	yat ca uktam asvabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ na eva asti śūnyatā ca bhāvānām iṣyate tasmāt asti śūnyatā āśrayaḥ bhāva svabhāvaḥ iti etat api na yujyate iti āha yadi aśūnyam bhavet kiṃcid syāt śūnyam iti kiṃcana na kiṃcid asti aśūnyam ca kutas śūnyam bhaviṣyati yadi śūnyatā nāma kācid syāt tadā tad āśrayaḥ bhāva svabhāvaḥ syāt na tu evam iha hi śūnyatā nāma iti sarva dharmāṇām sāmānya lakṣaṇam iti abhyupagamāt aśūnya dharma abhāvāt aśūnyata eva na asti yadā ca aśūnyāḥ padārthāḥ na santi aśūnyatā ca na asti tadā pratipakṣa nirapekṣa tvāt śūnyatā api kha puṣpa mālā vat na asti iti avasīyatām yadā ca śūnyatā na asti tadā atad āśrayāḥ api padārthāḥ na santi iti sthitam avikalam 
[108,i]	atra āha trīṇi vimokṣa mukhāni śūnyatā nimitta apraṇihita ākhyāni vimuktaye vineyebhyaḥ bhagavatā nirdiṣṭāni sarva tīrthika samayāsādhāraṇāni saugataḥ eva pravacane samupalabhyante yeṣām upadeśa artham eva buddhāḥ bhagavantaḥ aśeṣa tīrthya vāda mahā moha andhakāra anugata jagati jagat eka pradīpāḥ nairātmya upadeśa avicchinna śikhāḥ utpadyante sa bhavān tathāgata pravacana vyākhyāna vyājena idānīm tām eva śūnyatām pratikṣeptum ārabdhavān iti alam bhavatā svarga apavarga mārga samucchedakena iti ucyate aho vata bhavān ati unmukhaḥ iva atyanta viparyāsāt nirvāṇa pura gāminam śivam ṛjum paramam panthānam avadhūya bhāva abhiniveśavyā kulitam saṃsāra kāntāra anugameva mārgam mokṣa pura gāmi tvena samāśritaḥ nirmumukṣuḥ san saṃsāra aṭavī kāntāraḥ sadbhiḥ upālabhyaḥ eva san abhimāna abhiniveśa graha pavaraśatayā tān eva upālabhate nanu bhoḥ niravaśeṣa kleśa vyādhi cikitsakaiḥ mahā vaidya rājaiḥ śūnyatā sarva dṛṣṭīnām proktā niḥsaraṇam jinaiḥ yeṣām tu śūnyatā dṛṣṭiḥ tān a sādhyān babhāṣire 
[108,ii]	iha sarveṣām eva dṛṣṭi kṛtānām sarva graha abhiniveśānām yaniḥsaraṇam apravṛttiḥ sā śūnyatā na ca dṛṣṭi kṛtānām nivṛtti mātram bhāvaḥ ye tu tasyām api śūnyatāyām bhāva abhiniveśinaḥ tān prati avācakāḥ vayam iti kutas asmad upadeśāt sakala kalpanā vyāvṛttyā mokṣaḥ bhaviṣyati yaḥ na kiṃcid api te paṇyam dāsyāmi iti uktaḥ sa ced dehi bhoḥ tat eva mahyam nakiṃcid nāma paṇyam iti brūyāt sa kena upāyena śakyaḥ paṇya abhāvam grāhayitum evam yeṣām śūnyatāyām api bhāva abhiniveśaḥ kena idānīm sa teṣām tasyām bhāva abhiniveśaḥ niṣidhyatām iti atas mahā bhaiṣajye api doṣa saṃjñi tvāt parama cikitsakaiḥ mahā vaidyaiḥ tathāgataiḥ pratyākhyātāḥ eva te yathā uktam bhagavatā ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre 
[108,iii_108,iv]	yat na śūnyatayā dharmān śūnyān karoti api tu dharmāḥ eva śūnyāḥ yat na animittena dharmān animittān karoti api tu dharmāḥ eva animittāḥ yat na apraṇihitena dharmān apraṇihitān karoti api tu dharmāḥ eva apraṇihitāḥ yā evam pratyavekṣā iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā pratipad dharmāṇām bhūta pratyavekṣā ye hi kāśyapa śūnyatā upalambhena śūnyatām pratisaranti tān aham naṣṭa praṇaṣṭān iti vadāmi iti pravacanāt tathā 
[108,v]	varam khalu kāśyapa sumeru mātrā pudgala dṛṣṭiḥ āśritā na tu eva abhāva abhiniveśikasya śūnyatā dṛṣṭiḥ tat kasya hetoḥ sarva dṛṣṭi kṛtānām hi kāśyapa śūnyatā niḥsaraṇam yasya khalu punar śūnyatā eva dṛṣṭiḥ tam aham acikitsyam iti vadāmi tat yathā kāśyapa glānaḥ puruṣaḥ syāt tasmai vaidyaḥ bhaiṣajyam dadyāt tasya tat bhaiṣajyam sarva doṣān uccārya svayam koṣṭha gatam na niḥsaret tat kim manyase kāśyapa api tu sa puruṣaḥ tatas glānyāt muktaḥ bhavet no hi idam bhagavan gāḍhataram tasya puruṣasya glānyam bhavet yasya tat bhaiṣajyam sarva doṣān uccārya koṣṭha gatam na niḥsaret bhagavān āha evam eva kāśyapa sarva dṛṣṭi kṛtānām śūnyatā niḥsaraṇam yasya khalu punar śūnyatā eva dṛṣṭiḥ tam aham acikitsyam iti vadāmi iti 
[110,i_110,ii]	atra āha asti eva bhāva svabhāvaḥ tad saṃsarga upadeśāt iha yat na asti na tasya saṃsargaḥ tat yathā vandhyā suta duhitroḥ asti ca saṃskārāṇām saṃsarga upadeśaḥ cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpāṇi ca utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam trayāṇām saṃnipātaḥ sparśaḥ sparśa sahajā vedanā iti vistaraḥ tathā saṃjñā ca vedanā ca saṃsṛṣṭau etau dharmau na asaṃsṛṣṭau iti saṃskārāṇām saṃsarga upadeśaḥ tat evam saṃsarga upadeśāt vidyate eva bhāva svabhāvaḥ iti ucyate syāt etat evam yadi saṃsargaḥ eva bhavataḥ bhavet na tu asti yasmāt draṣṭavyam darśanam draṣṭā trīṇi etāni dviśas dviśas sarvaśas ca na saṃsargam anyonyena brajanti uta tatra draṣṭavyam rūpam darśanam cakṣuḥ draṣṭā vijñānam eṣām trayāṇām dviśas dviśas saṃsargaḥ na asti cakṣuṣaḥ rūpasya ca cakṣuṣaḥ vijñānasya ca vijñānasya rūpasya ca saṃsargaḥ na asti iti evam dviśas dviśas saṃsargaḥ na bhavati sarvaśas api trayāṇām api eṣām yugapad ca saṃsargaḥ na asti 
[110,iii_110,iv]	yathā ca draṣṭavya darśana draṣṭaṇām dviśas dviśas sarvaśas ca saṃsarga abhāvaḥ evam rāgaḥ ca raktaḥ ca rañjanīyam ca dṛśyatām rāgasya raktasya ca saṃsargaḥ na asti rāgasya rañjanīyasya ca trayāṇām api yugapad saṃsargaḥ na asti yathā ca eṣām evam traidhena śeṣāḥ kleśāḥ ca śeṣāṇi āyatanāni ca anyonyena saṃsargam na vrajanti trayaḥ prakārāḥ tridhā tridhā bhāvaḥ traidham tena traidhena śeṣāḥ kleśāḥ dveṣa moha ādayaḥ te ete dveṣa dviṣṭa dveṣaṇīya ādinā traidhena śrotra śrotṛ śrotavyādinā ca 
[110,v_110,vi]	kasmāt punar eteṣām saṃsargaḥ na asti iti āha anyena anyasya saṃsargaḥ tat ca anya tvaṃna vidyate draṣṭavya prabhṛtīnām yat na saṃsargam vrajanti atas yat iti ayam yasmāt arthe yadi draṣṭavī a ādīnām parasparam anya tvam syāt tadā kṣīrodakayoḥ iva anyena anyasya saṃsargaḥ syāt tat ca anya tvam yasmāt eṣām draṣṭavya prabhṛtīnām na saṃbhavati atas na ete saṃsarga brajanti 
[110,vii_110,viii]	api ca na ca kevalam anya tvam draṣṭavī ādeḥ na vidyate kasyacid kenacid sārdham na anya tvam upapadyate na ca kevalam kārya kāraṇa bhāva sthitānām draṣṭavī a ādīnām anya tvam na saṃbhavati ghaṭa paṭa ādīnām api padārthānām sarveṣām na eva saṃbhavati iti avasīyatām 
[111,i_111,ii]	yathā ca eṣām draṣṭavya prabhṛtīnām parasparataḥ anya tvam asat tathā pratipādayan āha anyat anyat pratītya anyat na anyat anyat ṛte anyatas yat pratītya ca yat tasmāt tat anyat na upapadyate iha yat etat ghaṭa ākhyam vastu paṭāt anyat iti vyapadiśyate tat etat anyat anyat pratītya anyat bhavati anya vastunaḥ ṛte ṛte anyatas vinā anyat anyat anyat na bhavati yat ca paṭa ākhyam vastu anyat ghaṭa ākhyam vastu pratītya anyat bhavati tasmāt paṭa ākhyāt vastunaḥ tat ghaṭa ākhyam vastu na anyat bhavati iti avasīyatām yasmāt yat pratītya yat bhavati tasmāt tat anyat na bhavati sa apekṣa tvāt bīja aṅkura vat hrasva dīrgha vat ca iti tathā ca vakṣyati pratītya yat yat bhavati na hi tāvat tat eva tat na ca anyat api tat tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatat iti 
[111,iii_111,iv]	atra āha yadi ghaṭāt anyaḥ paṭaḥ syāt tam ca pṛthak bhūtam paṭam apekṣya anyaḥ ghaṭaḥ syāt tadā kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ucyate yadi anyat anyat anyasmāt anyasmāt api ṛte bhavet tat anyat anyat anyasmāt ṛte na asti ca na asti atas ekaḥ atra anya śabdaḥ upadarśane aparaḥ ca artha antara parāmarśī anyaḥ ca prasiddha uccāraṇam iti anya śabda traya upādānam yadi hi etat ghaṭa ākhyam vastu paṭāt anyasmāt anyat syāt tat ghaṭa ākhyam vastu anyasmāt api paṭa ākhyāt ṛte anyat bhavet tadā ca paṭa nirapekṣasya eva ekaikasya ghaṭasya anya tvam bhavet yat hi yasmāt anyat tat tena vinā api siddhayati tat yathā saḥ eva ghaṭaḥ na sva rūpa niṣpattau anyam paṭam apekṣate evam anya tvam api yadi ghaṭasya anyasmāt paṭāt ṛte bhavet tadānīm paṭa nirapekṣasya ghaṭasya paratvam syāt na tu ekaikasya paṭa nirapekṣasya ghaṭasya anya tvam dṛṣṭam tasmāt anyat bhavati iti bruvatā yat apekṣya yat anyat tatas tad anyat na bhavati iti sphuṭam abhyupetam bhavati 
[111,v]	atra āha yadi khalu anya tvam evam kutaścid kasyacid na asti nanu idam api tadā na saṃbhavati vaktum yasmāt anyat pratītya anyat anyat bhavati iti tasmāt eva tat anyat anyat na bhavati iti ucyate yatas eva hi paraspara āpekṣikī bhāvānām anya tva siddhiḥ atas eva anyat iti ucyate laukike vyavahāre sthitvā vastutas tu parīkṣyamāṇam anya tvam na saṃbhavati iti brūmaḥ 
[111,vi]	yadi tarhi evam api avidyamāne api anya tve loka saṃvṛtyā paṭāt anyaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti vyapadiśyate atha kasmāt bīja aṅkurayoḥ api evam anya tvam na vyapadiśyate ucyate na eva hi lokaḥ ghaṭa paṭayoḥ iva bīja aṅkurayoḥ anya tvam pratipadyate ghaṭa paṭayoḥ iva janya janaka tva abhāva prasaṅgāt yaugapadya bhāva prasaṅgāt api ca yasmāt bīja mātramu tvā bīja kāryam vṛkṣam upadarśayati pumān loke ayam vṛkṣaḥ mayā uptaḥ iti tasmāt loke api kārya kāraṇa bhūtānām na asti eva paratvam iti vyavasthāpyate 
[112,i]	atra āha yadi padārtha antare padārtha antara sāpekṣā para buddhiḥ syāt syāt eṣa doṣaḥ tasmāt tat anyat na bhavati iti na tu evam brūmaḥ kim tarhi iha anya tvam nāma sāmānya viśeṣaḥ asti tat yatra samavetam sa padārthaḥ padārtha antara nirapekṣayā api paraḥ iti ucyate tasmāt ukta doṣa an avasaraḥ asmat pakṣe iti ucyate syāt etat evam yadi anya tvam eva syāt na tu asti iha idam anya tvam kalpyamānam anyasmin vā kalpyeta ananyasmin vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti pratipādayan āha na anyasmin vidyate anya tvam ananyasmin na vidyate 
[112,ii]	tatra anyasmin anya tvam asti iti kalpyate kim tadānīm anyatva parikalpanayā anya vyapadeśa siddhayartham hi bhavatā anya tvam parikalpyate sa ca anya vyapadeśaḥ vinā api anyatvena siddhaḥ eva yasmāt labdha ani avyapadeśaḥ eva padārthe anyasmin anya tvam kalpyate iti evam tāvat anyasmin anya tvam na saṃbhavati idānīm ananyasmin api anya tvam na asti yasmāt ananyaḥ ucyate ekaḥ tatra ca anya tva viruddham eka tvam asti iti yatas virodhāt ananyasmin api anya tvam na saṃbhavati yat ca idānīm na anyasmin ananyasmin vidyate tadvayatiriktasya padārtha antarasya asaṃbhavāt etat vayatirikte api padārthe na saṃbhavati tatra eva asti yadā ca evam anya tvam eva na asti tadā anya tva samavāya nibandhanaḥ anya buddhi dhvani pravṛtti hetuḥ anyaḥ api padārthaḥ na asti iti siddham 
[112,iii_112,iv]	atra āha yadi api anya tvam na asti tathā api anyaḥ tāvat asti na ca asati anya tve anyaḥ bhavitum arhati atas anya tvam bhaviṣyati iti ucyate avidyamāne ca anya tve na asti anyat vā tat eva vā yadā anya tvam eva na asti iti prāk pratipāditam tadā kutas asati anya tve anyat vā tat eva vā bhaviṣyati tat eva iti ananya tvam iti arthaḥ tasmāt na asti anyat vā tat eva vā 
[112,v]	atra āha vidyante eva darśana ādayaḥ saṃsarga sadbhāvāt iha darśana ādīnām yadi api anya tvam na asti iti pratipāditam tathā api trayāṇām saṃnipātaḥ saṃgatiḥ sparśaḥ iti saṃsargaḥ asti tatas ca saṃsarga sadbhāvāt vidyante eva darśana ādayaḥ iti ucyate syuḥ evam yadi teṣām saṃsargaḥ eva syāt na tu asti yathā ca na asti tathā pratipādayan āha na tena tasya saṃsargaḥ na anyena anyasya yujyate 
[112,vi]	iha yadi darśana ādīnām saṃsargaḥ syāt saḥ eka tvena vā parikalpyeta anya tvena vā tatra eka tve na asti saṃsargaḥ na hi ekakam kṣīram udaka nirapekṣam udakena saṃsṛjyate iti ucyate pṛthaktve api saṃsargaḥ na asti na hi udakāt pṛthak avasthitam kṣīram udakena saṃsṛjyate iti kathyate evam darśana ādīnām yadi eka tve sati saṃsargaḥ parikalpyate saḥ anupapannaḥ ekakasya api cakṣuṣaḥ saṃsṛṣṭi prasaṅgāt atha pṛthaktvam evam api anupapannaḥ ekakasya api cakṣuṣaḥ rūpa ādibhyaḥ pṛthak bhūtasya saṃsṛṣṭi prasaṅgāt asati saṃsarge na asti darśana ādikam iti siddham 
[112,vii^1]	atra āha yadi api saṃsargaḥ na asti tathā api saṃsṛjyamānam saṃsṛṣṭam saṃsraṣṭā ca asti tat apratiṣedhāt na ca saṃsargam antareṇa saṃsṛjyamānam saṃsṛṣṭam saṃsraṣṭā ca saṃbhavati tasmāt saṃsargaḥ api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate etat api na yuktam yasmāt yadā saṃsargaḥ eva na asti iti pratipāditam asati ca saṃsarge tadā kutas saṃsṛjyamāna ādikam tatra vartamāna saṃsarga kriyā sādhana karma bhūtam saṃsṛjyamānam saṃsṛṣṭam niṣpanna saṃsarga kriyam saṃsraṣṭā kartā kriyā niṣpattau svātantryeṇa avasthitaḥ tat atra saṃsarga abhāvāt eva saṃsṛjyamāna ādikam apaśyan tat pratiṣedham nigamayan āha saṃsṛjyamānam saṃsṛṣṭaṃsaṃsraṣṭā ca na vidyate 
[112,vii^2_113,i]	 iti yathā uktam bhagavatā sarva sayogi tu paśyati cakṣuḥ tatra na paśyati pratyaya hīnam na eva ca cakṣu papaśyati rūpam tena sa yoga viyoga vikalpaḥ āloka samāśrita paśyati cakṣu rūpa manorama citra vicitram yena ca yoga samāśrita cakṣuḥ tena na paśyati cakṣu kadāci te parinirvṛta laukika śūrāḥ yehi svabhāvata jñātibhi dharmāḥ kāma guṇaiḥ hi caranti asaṅgāḥ saṅga vivarjiya sattva vinenti no pi ca sattva na jīviha kaści sattva hitam ca karonti jinendrāḥ sattvu na asti karonti ca artham saṅgu na vidyati atra kadāci tasya na vidyati vedana loke tathā bhāvitu mārga pavartitu jñāna śūnyaka dharma nirātmaka sarvi yena vibhāvita bhontimi dharmāḥ tasya bhavet pratibhānam anantam 
[114,i]	atra āha vidyate eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ tad niṣpādaka hetu pratyaya upādānāt iha yat na asti na tasya niṣpādaka hetu pratyaya upādānam asti yathā khapuṣpasya upādīyante ca bīja avidyā ādayaḥ hetu pratyayāḥ aṅkara saṃskāra ādīnām niṣpādakāḥ iti atas vidyate eva bhāva svabhāvaḥ iti ucyate yadi bhāvānām saṃskāra aṅkura ādīnām svabhāvaḥ asti kim idānīm vidyamānānām hetu pratyayaiḥ prayojanam yathā vartamānībhūtānām saṃskāra aṅkura ādīnām bhūyas niṣpattaye avidyā bīja ādīnām upādānam kriyate evam anyat api tad utpattaye na kartavyam syāt tad svabhāvasya vidyamāna tvāt iti pratipādayan āha na saṃbhavaḥ svabhāvasya yuktaḥ pratyaya hetubhiḥ 
[114,ii_114,iii]	atha syāt na eva utpādāt pūrvam kasyacid bhāvasya svabhāvaḥ asti yatas asya vidyamāna tvāt utpatti vaiyarthyam syāt kim tarhi utpādāt pūrvam avidyamānasya eva svabhāvasya hetu pratyayān pratītya paścāt utpādaḥ bhavati iti evam apīṣyamāṇe hetu pratyaya saṃbhūtaḥ svabhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ bhavet atha syāt iṣyate eva hetu pratyaya saṃbhūta tvāt svabhāvasya kṛtaka tvam tasmāt kṛtakasya eva svabhāvasya abhyupagamāt kṛtaka tva prasaṅgaḥ na asmākam bādhakaḥ iti etat api na yuktam iti āha svabhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ nāma bhaviṣyati punar katham 
[114,iv]	kṛtakaḥ ca iti svabhāvaḥ ca iti paraspara viruddha tvāt asaṃgata artham etat iha hi svaḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti vyutpatteḥ yaḥ kṛtakaḥ padārthaḥ sa loke na eva svabhāvaḥ iti vyapadiśyate tat yathā apāmauṣpyam dhātu piśāca pratyaya niṣpāditaḥ karkeṭana ādīnām padmarāga ādi bhāvaḥ ca yaḥ tu akṛtakaḥ sa svabhāvaḥ tat yathā agneḥ auṣṇyam jātānām padmarāga ādīnām padmarāga ādi svabhāvaḥ ca sa hi teṣām padārtha antara saṃparkā janita tvāt svabhāvaḥ iti ucyate tat evam akṛtakaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti loka vyavahāre vyavasthite vayam idānīm brūmaḥ yat etat auṣṇyam tat aṣi agneḥ svabhāvaḥ na bhavati iti gṛhyatām kṛtaka tvāt iha maṇi indhana āditya samāgama ādaraṇi nirdharṣaṇa ādeḥ ca agneḥ hetu pratyaya sāpekṣatā eva upalabhyate na ca agni vyatiriktam auṣṇyam saṃbhavati tasmāt auṣṇyam api hetu pratyaya janitam tatas ca kṛtakam kṛtaka tvāt ca apām auṣṇya vat svabhāvaḥ na eva bhavati iti sphuṭam avasīyate 
[114,v^1]	nanu ca gopāla aṅganā jana prasiddham etat agneḥ auṣṇyam svabhāvaḥ iti kim khalu asmābhiḥ uktam na prasiddham iti etat tu vayam brūmaḥ na ayam svabhāvaḥ bhavitum arhati svabhāva lakṣaṇa viyukta tvāt avidyā viparyāsa anugamāt tu lokaḥ niḥsvabhāvam eva bhāva jātam sa svabhāva tvena pratipannaḥ yathā hi taimirikāḥ timira pratyayāt asantam eva keśa ādi svabhāvam sa svabhāva tvena abhiniviṣṭāḥ evam avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana tayā bālā niḥsvabhāvam bhāva jātam sa svabhāva tvena abhiniviṣṭāḥ yathā abhiniveśam lakṣaṇam ācakṣate agneḥ auṣṇyam sva lakṣaṇam tatas anyatra anupalambhāt asādhāraṇa tvena svam eva lakṣaṇam iti kṛtvā 
[114,v^2_115,ii]	bāla jana prasiddhayā eva ca bhagavatā tat eva eṣām sāṃvṛtam svarūpam abhidharme vyavasthāpitam sādhāraṇam tu anitya tva ādikam sāmānya lakṣaṇam iti ca uktam yadā tu vigata avidyā timira avadāta prajñā cakṣuṣām darśanam apekṣyate tadā vitimiraiḥ taimirika upalabdha keśa adarśana vat bāla jana mati parikalpita anupalabdha svabhāvaiḥ āryaiḥ puras ucyate para hita vyāpāraiḥ na ayam svabhāvaḥ bhāvānām iti yathā uktam ārya laṅka avatāra sūtre keśoṇḍukam yathā mithyā gṛhyate taimirikaiḥ janaiḥ tathā bhāva vikalpaḥ ayam mithyā bālaiḥ vikalpyate na svabhāvaḥ na vijñaptiḥ na ca vastu na ca ālayaḥ bālaiḥ vikalpitāḥ hi ete śava bhūtaiḥ kutārkikaiḥ iti tathā svabhāva anutpattim saṃdhāya mahāmate mayā sarva dharmāḥ anutpannāḥ iti uktāḥ iti vistaraḥ 
[115,iii_115,iv^1]	atra āha yadi khalu idam agni ādeḥ auṣṇya ādikam hetu pratyaya saṃbhūta tvena kṛtaka tvāt niḥsvabhāvam iti ucyate kim idānīm tad svabhāvasya lakṣaṇam kaḥ ca asau svabhāvaḥ iti vaktavyam ucyate akṛtrimaḥ svabhāvaḥ hi nirapekṣaḥ paratra ca iha svaḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti yasya padārthasya yat ā ātmīyam rūpam tat tasya svabhāvaḥ iti vyapadiśyate kim ca kasya ātmīyam yadi asya akṛtrimam yat tu kṛtrimam na tat tasya ātmīyam tat yathā apām auṣṇyam yat ca yasya āyattam tat api tat ā ātmīyam tat yathā sve bhṛtyāḥ svāni dhanāni yat tu yasya parāyattam na tat tasya ātmīyam tat yathā tāvat kālikā yācitakamasvatantram yatas ca evam kṛtrimasya para sa apekṣasya ca svabhāva tvam na iṣṭam atas eva auṣṇyam agneḥ hetu pratyaya pratibaddha tvāt pūrvaṃma bhūtvā paścāt utpādena kṛtaka tvāt na svabhāvaḥ iti yujyate 
[115,iv^2]	yatas ca etat evam atas yat eva agneḥ kāla traye api avyabhicāri nijam rūpam akṛtrimam pūrvam abhūtvā paścāt yat na bhavati yat ca hetu pratyaya sāpekṣam na bhavati apāmauṣṇya vat pārāvāra vat dīrgha hrasva vat vā tat svabhāvaḥ iti vyapadiśyate kim khalu agneḥ tat ittham svarūpam asti na tat asti na ca api na asti svarūpataḥ yadi api evam tathā api śrotṛṇām uttrāsa parivarjana artham saṃvṛtyā samāropya tat asti iti brūmaḥ yathā uktam bhagavatā anakṣarasya dharmasya śrutiḥ kā deśanā ca kā śrūyate deśyate ca api samāropāt anakṣaraḥ iti 
[115,v_116,i]	iha api ca vakṣyati śūnyam iti na vaktavyam aśūnyam iti vā bhavet ubhayam na ubhayam ca iti prajñapti artham tu kathyate yadi khalu tad adhyāropāt bhavadbhiḥ asti iti ucyate kīdṛśam tat yā sā dharmāṇām dharmatā nāma sā eva tad svarūpam atha kā iyam dharmāṇām dharmatā dharmāṇām svabhāvaḥ kaḥ ayam svabhāvaḥ prakṛtiḥ kā ca iyam prakṛtiḥ yā iyam śūnyatā kā iyam śūnyatā naiḥsvābhāvyam kim idam naiḥsvābhāvyam tathatā kā iyam tathatā tathā abhāvaḥ avikāri tvam sadā eva sthāyitā sarvathā anutpādaḥ eva hi agni ādīnām para nirapekṣa tvāt akṛtrima tvāt svabhāvaḥ iti ucyate 
[116,ii_116,iii]	etat uktam bhavati avidyā timira prabhāva upalabdham bhāva jātam yena ātmanā vigata avidyā timirāṇām āryāṇām adarśana yogena viṣaya tvam upayāti tat eva svarūpam eṣām svabhāvaḥ iti vyavasthāpyate tasya ca idam lakṣaṇam akṛtrimaḥ svabhāvaḥ hi nirapekṣaḥ paratra ca iti vyavasthāpayāṃbabhūvuḥ ācāryāḥ iti vijñeyam sa ca eṣa bhāvānām anutpāda ātmakaḥ svabhāva akiṃcittvena abhāva mātra tvāt asvabhāvaḥ eva iti kṛtvā na asti bhāva svabhāvaḥ iti vijñeyam yathā uktam bhagavatā bhāvān abhāvān iti yaḥ prajānati sa sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate yaḥ sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate saḥ ānimittam spṛśate samādhim iti 
[116,iv_116,v]	atra āha yadi api svabhāvaḥ na asti bhāvānām tathā api para bhāvaḥ tāvat asti tat apratiṣedhāt sati ca para bhāve svabhāvaḥ api bhaviṣyati svabhāvam antareṇa para bhāva aprasiddheḥ iti ucyate kutas svabhāvasya abhāve para bhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati svabhāvaḥ para bhāvasya para bhāvaḥ hi kathyate iha svabhāvaḥ eva hi loke kaścid svabhāva antara apekṣayā paraḥ iti vyapadiśyate yadi hi agneḥ auṣṇyam svabhāvaḥ syāt drava svabhāva salila sāpekṣayā para bhāvaḥ iti vyapadiśyeta yadā tu mumukṣubhiḥ vicāryamāṇasya kasyacid svabhāvaḥ eva na asti tadā kutas paratvam syāt para bhāvāt ca svabhāvaḥ api na asti iti siddham 
[116,vi_117,i]	atra āha yadi api svabhāva para bhāvau na staḥ tathā api bhāvaḥ tāvat asti apratiṣedhāt sa ca bhāvaḥ bhavan svabhāvaḥ vā bhavet para bhāvaḥ vā tasmāt svabhāva para bhāvau api bhaviṣyate iti ucyate svabhāva para bhāvābhyām ṛte bhāvaḥ kutas punar svabhāve para bhāve vā sati bhāvaḥ hi sidhyati bhāvaḥ hi parikalpyamānaḥ svabhāvaḥ vā bhavet para bhāvaḥ vā tau ca pūrva ukta vidhinā na staḥ iti tayoḥ abhāvāt bhāvaḥ api na asti iti avadhāryatām 
[117,ii]	atra āha yadi api bhavatā bhāvaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ tathā api abhāvaḥ asti pratiṣedha abhāvāt tatas ca bhāvaḥ api bhaviṣyati pratidvandvi sadbhāvāt abhāva vat iti ucyate syāt bhāvaḥ yadi abhāvaḥ eva syāt na tu asti iti āha bhāvasya ced aprasiddhiḥ abhāvaḥ na eva sidhyati bhāvasya hi anyathābhāvam abhāvam vruvate janāḥ 
[117,iii]	iha hi yadi bhāvaḥ nāma kaścid abhaviṣyat syāt tasyānyathā bhāvāt abhāvaḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ hi vartamāna avasthāyāḥ pracyutāḥ santaḥ anyathābhāvam āpannāḥ abhāva dhvani vācyāḥ bhavanti loke yadā tu amī ghaṭa ādayaḥ bhāva rūpa tvena eva asiddhāḥ tadā kutas avidyamāna svabhāvānām anyathātvam iti atas abhāvaḥ api na asti 
[117,iv_117,v^1]	tat evam sarvathā svabhāva para bhāva bhāva abhāveṣu anupapadyamāneṣu avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana tayā viparītam svabhāvam para bhāvam ca bhāvam ca abhāvam eva ca ye paśyanti na paśyanti te tattvam buddha śāsane ye hi tathāgata pravacanā viparīta vyākhyāna abhimānitayā pṛthivyāḥ kāṭhinyam svabhāvaḥ vedanāyāḥ viṣaya anubhavaḥ vijñānasya viṣaya prativijñaptiḥ svabhāvaḥ iti evam svabhāvam bhāvānām varṇayanti anyat vijñānam anyat rūpam anyā eva ca vedanā iti evam para bhāvam varṇayanti vartamāna avastham ca vijñāna ādikam bhāva tvena ye varṇayanti vijñāna ādikam eva ca atīta tām āpannam abhāvaḥ iti na te parama gambhīrasya pratītyasamutpādasya tattvam varṇayanti yasmāt yathā udita upapatti viruddham svabhāva para bhāva ādīnām astitvam na ca upapatti viruddham padārtha svabhāvam anuvarṇayanti tathāgatāḥ 
[117,v^2]	svayam aviparīta aśeṣa padārtha tattva saṃbodhāt atas eva buddhānām eva bhagavatām vacanam pramāṇam iti upavarṇayanti vicakṣaṇāḥ sa upapattika tvena avisaṃvādaka tvāt atas eva ca āptebhyaḥ prahīṇa aśeṣa doṣebhyaḥ āgata tvāt āgamayati iti samantāt tattvam gamayati iti vā āmi mukhyāt gamanāt vā tad āśrayeṇa lokasya nirvāṇa gamanāt saṃbuddha vacanasya eva āgama tvam vyavasthāpyate tad anya matānām tu upapatti viyukta tvāt na prāmāṇyam āgama ābhāsa tvam ca vyavasthāpyate 
[117,vi_118,i]	yasmāt ca etāni svabhāva para bhāva bhāva abhāva darśanāni yukti vidhura tvāt na tattvāni atas eva mumukṣūṇām vineya janānām kātyāyana avavāde ca asti iti na asti iti ca ubhayam pratiṣiddham bhagavatā bhāva abhāva vibhāvinā uktam hi bhagavatā ārya kātyāyana avavāda sūtre yat bhūyasā kātyāyana ayam lokaḥ astitām vai abhiniviṣṭaḥ na astitām ca tena na parimucyate jāti jarā vyādhi maraṇa śoka parideva duḥkha daurmanasya upāyāsebhyaḥ na parimucyate pāñcagatikāt saṃsāra cāraka āgāra bandhanāt na parimucyate mātṛ maraṇa saṃtāpa duḥkhāt na parimucyate pitṛ maraṇa saṃtāpa duḥkhāt iti vistaraḥ 
[118,ii]	idam ca sūtram sarva nikāyeṣu paṭhayate tat asmāt āgamāt yathā upavarṇitāyāḥ ca upapatteḥ na arhati prājña svabhāva para bhāva bhāva abhāva darśanam tathāgata vacanāt atyanta viruddham āsthātum bhagavatā pratiṣiddha tvāt kiṃviśiṣṭena bhagavatā bhāva abhāva vibhāvinā bhāva abhāvau vibhāvayitum śīlam asya iti bhāva abhāva vibhāvī yathā avasthita bhāva abhāva aviparīta svabhāva parijñānāt bhāva abhāva vibhāvī iti bhagavān eva ucyate tena bhagavatā bhāva abhāva vibhāvinā yasmāt astitvaṃca nāstitvam ca ubhayam etat pratiṣiddham tasmāt na yuktam bhāva abhāva darśanam tattvam iti āsthātum 
[118,iii_118,vi]	tathā asti iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ antar na asti iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ antar yat enayoḥ antayoḥ madhyam tad arūpyam anidarśanam apratiṣṭham anābhā sam aniketam avijñaptikam iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamām pratipad bhūta pratyavekṣā iti tathā asti iti na asti iti ubhe api antā śuddhī aśuddhi iti ime api antā tasmāt ubhe anta vivarjayitvā madhye api sthānam na karoti paṇḍitaḥ asti iti na asti iti vivādaḥ eṣaḥ śuddhī aśuddhi iti ayam vivādaḥ vivāda prāptyā na duḥkham praśāmyati avivāda prāptyā ca duḥkham nirudhyate iti atra āha yadi punar evam agni ādīnām svabhāvataḥ eva astitvam syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ syāt ukta doṣaḥ hetu pratyaya saṃbhūtaḥ svabhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ bhavet ityādinā 
[118,vii_119,i]	api ca yadi ayam eṣām agni ādīnām svabhāvaḥ syāt tasya vidyamānasya sataḥ na syāt punar anyathātvam iti pratipādayan āha yadi astitvam prakṛtyā syāt na bhavet asya na astitā yadi agni ādeḥ bhāvasya prakṛtyā svabhāvataḥ astitvam tadā asya svabhāvasya prakṛtyā vidyamānasya punar anyathātvam na syāt yasmāt prakṛteḥ anyathā bhāvaḥ na hi jātu upapadyate 
[119,ii]	yadi eṣām agni ādīnām iyam eva prakṛtiḥ syāt svabhāvaḥ syāt tadā prakṛteḥ avikāriṇī tvāt na kadācid punar anyathā bhāvaḥ upapadyeta na hi ākāśasya anāvaraṇa tvam kadācid api anyathātvam pratipadyate evam agni ādīnām api prakṛtyā vidyamānānām punar anyathātvam na syāt upalabhate ca bhavān eṣām anyathātva prabandha uparama lakṣaṇam vināśam tasmāt vipariṇāma dharmi tvāt apām auṣṇya vat na ayam eṣām svabhāvaḥ iti pratīyatām 
[119,iii_119,v]	atra āha yadi prakṛtyā vidyamānasya anyathātvā asaṃbhavāt anyathātvasya ca upalabhyamāna tvāt prakṛtiḥ eṣām bhāvānām na asti iti ucyate nanu ca evam api prakṛtau kasya ca asatyām anyathātvam bhaviṣyati kasya idānīm prakṛtyā sva rūpeṇa avidyamānasya khapuṣpasya iva anyathātvam bhaviṣyati tasmāt avidyamāna prakṛtikasya anyathā ātvā anupalambhāt anyathātu asya ca darśanāt asti eva svabhāvaḥ iti ucyate yadi tāvakena matena prakṛtyā svabhāvena asaṃvidyamānasya anyathātva abhāvāt anyathātu asya ca darśanāt prakṛtiḥ iti ucyate evam api prakṛtau kasya ca satyām anyathātvam bhaviṣyati kasya idānīm prakṛtyā svabhāvena vidyamānasya vartamānasya eva anyathātvam bhaviṣyati tasmāt prakṛtyā vidyamānasya anyathātvam na asti iti sarvathā anyathātvā asaṃbhavaḥ eva tatas ca na asti prakṛtiḥ bhāvānām iti vijñeyam 
[119,vi]	yat ca api uktam anyathātu asya darśanāt na asti prakṛtiḥ iti tat api para prasiddhayā anyathātva darśanam adhikṛtya uktam na tu asmābhiḥ kadācid api kasyacid anyathātvam abhyupetam tat evam atyantataḥ prakṛtau asaṃvidyamānāyām sarva dharmeṣu asaṃvidyamāneṣu asvabhāveṣu tad anyathā tve ca asaṃvidyamāne yaḥ hi idānīm astitvam nāstitvam ca bhāvānām parikalpayati tasya evam parikalpayataḥ niyatam eva asti iti śāśvata grāhaḥ na asti iti uccheda darśanam 
[119,vii_119,viii]	prasajyate iti vākya śeṣaḥ tat ca etat śāśvata uccheda darśanam svarga apavarga mārga antarāya kara tvāt yasmāt mahānartha karam tasmāt astitvana astitve na aśrīyeta vicakṣaṇaḥ kasmāt punarbhāva abhāva darśane sati śāśvata uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ bhavati iti yasmāt asti yat hi svabhāvena na tat na asti iti śāśvatam na asti idānīm abhūt pūrvam iti ucchedaḥ prasajyate 
[120,i]	yat svabhāvena asti iti ucyate svabhāvasya anapāyi tvāt na tat kadācid api na asti iti evam bhāvasya astitva abhyupagame sati śāśvata darśanam āpadyate pūrvam ca vartamāna avasthāyām bhāva svarūpam abhyupetya idānīm tat vinaṣṭa tvāt na astiti paścāt abhyupagacchataḥ uccheda darśanam prasajyate yasya tu bhāva svabhāvaḥ eva na upapadyate na tasya śāśvata uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ bhāva svabhāva anupalambhāt 
[120,ii_120,iii]	nanu ca bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ na asti iti abhyupagacchataḥ mā bhūt bhāva darśana abhāvāt śāśvata darśanam uccheda darśanam tu niyatam prasajyate iti na evam abhāva darśanam bhavati yaḥ hi pūrvam bhāva svabhāvam abhyupetya paścāt tad nivṛttim ālambate tasya pūrva upalabdha svabhāva apavādāt syāt abhāva darśanam yaḥ tu taimirika upalabdha keśeṣu iva vitaimirikaḥ na kiṃcid upalabhate sa na asti iti bruvan kiṃcid na asti iti brūyāt pratiṣedhya abhāvāt viparyastānām tu mithyā abhiniveśa nivṛtti artham ataimirikāḥ iva vayam brūmaḥ na santi sarva bhāvāḥ iti na ca evam bruvatām asmākam para hita vyāpāra parāyaṇānām uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ yathā uktam sūtre yaḥ hi bhagavan pūrvam rāga dveṣa moha bhāva abhyupagamam kṛtvā paścāt na santi rāga dveṣa moha bhāvāḥ iti bravīti sa bhagavan vai nāstikaḥ bhavati iti vistaraḥ 
[120,iv]	yaḥ tu paratantra citta caitta vaḥ tu mātram abhyupetya tasya parikalpita svabhāva abhāvāt astitva darśanam pariharati saṃkleśa vyavadāna nibandhanasya ca paratantra vastu mātra sadbhāvāt na astitva darśanam pariharati tasya parikalpitasya avidyamāna tvāt paratantrasya ca vidyamāna tvāt astitvanā astitva darśana dvayasya api upanipātāt kutas anta dvaya parihāraḥ hetu pratyaya janitasya ca sa svabhāvena ayukta tva pratipādanāt ayuktam eva asya vyākhyānam tat evam madhyamaka darśane eva astitva nā astitva dvaya darśanasya aprasaṅgaḥ na vijñāna vādi darśana ādiṣu iti vijñeyam atas eva uktam ārya ratna āvalyām sa sāṃkhī ā aullūkya nirgrantha pudgala skandha vādinam pṛccha lokam yadi vadati astināsti vyatikramam dharmayautakam iti asmāt astināsti vyatikramam viddhi gambhīram iti ukta buddhānām śāsana amṛtam iti
