[120,v]	tathāvidha vineya jana bodha anurodhāt tu parama artha darśanasya upāya bhūta tvāt neyārtha tvena bhagavatā mahā karuṇā paratantra tayā vijñāna ādi vādaḥ deśitaḥ sāṃmitīya pudgala vāda vat na nīta arthaḥ iti vijñeyam yathā uktam ārya samādhi rāja bhaṭṭārake nīta artha sūtra anta viśeṣa jānati yathā upadiṣṭā sugatena śūnyatā yasmin punar pudgala sattva pūruṣaḥ neyārthataḥ jānati sarva dharmān 
[121,i]	etat ca ārya akṣayam ati nirdeśa ādiṣu vistareṇa boddhavyam iti bhāva abhāva darśana dvaya prasaṅgaḥ yāvat tāvat saṃsāraḥ iti avetya mumukṣubhiḥ etad darśana dvaya nirāsena sadbhiḥ madhyamā pratipad bhāvanīyāḥ yathāvat iti etat ca uktam bhagavatā bhāva abhāva vibhāvayi jñānam sarvi acintiya sarvi abhūtam ye puna citta vaśa anuga bālāḥ te dukhitā bhava koṭi śateṣu bhāvān abhāvān iti yaḥ prajānatī sa sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate yaḥ sarva bhāveṣu na jātu sajjate saḥ ānimittam spṛśate samādhim iti 
[121,ii]	tathā smarāmi aham pūrvam atīta adhvani acintiye kalpi narāṇam uttamaḥ utpannu loka artha karaḥ mahā ṛṣī nāmena saḥ abhāva samudgataḥ abhūt sa jāta mātraḥ gagane sthihitvā sarvāṇa dharmāṇa bhāva deśayi tadā anurūpam kṛta nāmadheyam śabdena sarvam tri sahasra vijñayī deva api sarve pramumocu śabdam abhāva nāmā iti jinaḥ bhaviṣyati yaḥ jāta mātraḥ pada sapta prakraman abhāva dharmāṇa samam prakāśayī buddhaḥ yadā bheṣyati dharmarājaḥ sarvāṇa dharmāṇa prakāśakaḥ muniḥ tṛṇa gulma vṛkṣa oṣadhi śaila parvate abhāva dharmāṇa ravaḥ bhaviṣyati yāvanti śabdāḥ tahi lokadhātau sarve hi abhāvāḥ na hi kaści bhāvaḥ tāvanti khaḥ tasya tathāgatasya ravu niścarī loka vināyakasya iti 
[122,i_122,iii]	bhavati iti bhāvaḥ sattā na vidyate sattā svabhāvaḥ sarva bhāvānām iti abhāvāḥ sarva dharmāḥ śūnyāḥ sarva dharmā niḥsvabhāva yogena iti prajñāpāramitā pāṭhāt bhāva svabhāvasya anupapatteḥ abhāva dharmāṇa ravaḥ bhaviṣyati ityādinā sūtra arthaḥ avagantavyaḥ yāvanti śabdāḥ tahi lokadhātau sarve hi abhāvāḥ na hi kaści bhāvaḥ ityādi bhūtvā abhāva pratiṣedha vivakṣita tvāt bhāva abhāva arthaḥ eva svabhāva abhāva arthaḥ 
[123,i]	atra āha vidyate eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ saṃsāra sadbhāvāt iha saṃsaraṇam saṃsṛtiḥ gateḥ gati antara gamanam saṃsāraḥ iti ucyate yadi bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ na syāt kasya gateḥ gati antara gamanam saṃsāraḥ syāt na hi avidyamānānām vandhyā sūnu saṃskārāṇām saṃsaraṇam dṛṣṭam tasmāt saṃsāra sadbhāvāt vidyate eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ iti ucyate syāt bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ yadi saṃsāraḥ eva bhavet na tu asti iha yadi saṃsāraḥ syāt sa niyatam saṃskārāṇām vā bhavet sattvasya vā kim ca atas ubhayathā ca doṣaḥ iti āha saṃskārāḥ saṃsaranti ced na nityāḥ saṃsaranti te saṃsaranti ca na anityāḥ sattve api eṣa samaḥ kramaḥ 
[123,ii]	tatra yadi saṃskārāḥ saṃsaranti iti parikalpyate kim te nityāḥ saṃsaranti uta anityāḥ tatra na nityāḥ saṃsaranti niṣkriya tvāt anityānām ca ghaṭa ādīnām sa kriyatva upalambhāt atha anityāḥ ye hi akriyāḥ te utpāda samanantaram eva vinaṣṭāḥ ye ca vinaṣṭāḥ kutas teṣām avidyamāna tvāt vandhyā sūnu saṃskārāṇām iva kvacid gamanam iti evam anityānām api na asti saṃsāraḥ 
[123,iii]	atha api syāt anityāḥ eva santaḥ hetu phala saṃbandha paraṃparayā avicchinna kramāḥ saṃtānena ca pravartamānāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃsaranti iti etat api na upapadyate kutas yat tāvat utpadyate kāryam tasya saṃsāraḥ na asti kutaścid ana āgamanāt kvacid ca āgamanāt yat ca kāraṇam naṣṭam tasya api saṃsāraḥ na asti kutaścid ana āgamanāt kvacid ca āgamanāt saṃskāra mātra vyatirekeṇa atīta anāgatayoḥ asiddha tvāt naṣṭa ajāta tvena avidyamāna tvāt 
[123,iv^1]	uttarasmin kṣaṇe utpanne pūrvaḥ saṃsarati iti ced yadi pūrva uttarayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ eka tvam syāt syāt etat evam na tu eka tvam asti kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt cakṣū rūpa cakṣuḥ vijñānānām na asti ca kim ca eka tve sati pūrva uttara kṣaṇa vācya tā eva na syāt na hi ekaḥ devadattaḥ ekadā pūrvaḥ ca uttaraḥ ca iti vyapadiśyate evam iha api eka tvāt pūrva uttara kṣaṇa vyapadeśaḥ eva na syāt api ca pūrvakṣaṇaḥ naṣṭaḥ iti na syāt uttara kṣaṇa vat avyatirikta tvāt uttarakṣaṇaḥ utpannaḥ iti na syāt pūrvakṣaṇa vat avyatirikta tvāt atha anya tve sati saṃsaraṇam syāt evam sati arhatām api saṃsaraṇam syāt anyasya pṛthagjanasya saṃsāra utpatti sadbhāvāt nirvṛtaḥ ca pradīpaḥ pradīpa antare jvalati iti syāt 
[123,iv^2]	kim ca anyat naṣṭāt vā pūrvakṣaṇāt uttarasya kṣaṇasya udayaḥ syāt anaṣṭāt naśyamānāt vā tatra yadi naṣṭa āt iṣyate vahni dagdhāt api bījāt aṅkura udayaḥ syāt tatas ca nirhetukaḥ syāt atha anaṣṭāt evam api avikṛte api bīje aṅkura udayaḥ syāt kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca yaugapadyam syāt nirhetukaḥ ca utpādaḥ syāt naśyamānāt iti ced naṣṭān aṣṭa vyatirekeṇa naśyamāna abhāvāt naṣṭān aṣṭayoḥ ca vihita doṣa tvāt naśyamānāt api na asti utpattiḥ iti kutas kārya kāraṇa vyavasthā pūrva uttara kṣaṇa vyavasthā vā bhaviṣyati yadā ca pūrva uttara kṣaṇa vyavasthā kārya kāraṇa vyavasthā ca na asti tadā saṃtānaḥ api na asti tad abhāvāt na asti bhavatām saṃsāraḥ iti anityānām api saṃskārāṇām na asti saṃsāraḥ iti 
[124,i]	atra eke varṇayanti satyam saṃskārāḥ na saṃsaranti utpatti vidhura tvāt kim tarhi sattvaḥ saṃsarati iti ucyate sattve api eṣa samaḥ kramaḥ sattvaḥ saṃsarati iti ucyamāne kim asau nityaḥ saṃsarati uta anityaḥ iti vicāryamāṇe yaḥ eva saṃskārāṇām saṃsaraṇa anupapatti kramaḥ sa sama tvāt sattve api samaḥ nipatati tasmāt sattvaḥ api na saṃsarati 
[124,ii]	atra āha na eva hi sattva saṃskārāṇām saṃsāra anupapatti kramaḥ samaḥ bhavitum arhati yasmāt iha saṃskārāṇām nitya anitya bhūtānām saṃsaraṇam na asti iti uktam na ca evam ātmā nitya anitya bhūtaḥ tasya hi skandhebhyaḥ tattva anya tva avakta vya tāvat nitya tvena anitya tvena api avaktavyatā vyavasthāpyate tasmāt ātmā eva saṃsarati iti na ca ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti ucyate pudgalaḥ saṃsarati ced skandha āyatana dhātuṣu pañcadhā mṛgyamāṇaḥ asau na asti kaḥ saṃsariṣyati 
[124,iii]	yadi pudgalaḥ nāma kaścid syāt sa saṃsaret na tu asti yasmāt skandha āyatana dhātuṣu pañcadhā mṛgyamāṇaḥ na asti katham kṛtvā indhanam punar agniḥ na na agniḥ anyatra ca indhanāt na agniḥ indhanavān na agnau indhanāni na teṣu saḥ agni indhanābhyām vyākhyātaḥ ātma upādānayoḥ kramaḥ iti evam skandha āyatana dhātu svabhāvaḥ ātmā na bhavati na api tebhyaḥ vyatiriktaḥ na skandha āyatana dhātumān na skandha āyatana dhātuṣu ātmā na ātmani skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ iti evam pañcadhā mṛgyamāṇaḥ ātmā na saṃbhavati pūrva uditena nyāyena yaḥ ca idānīm skandha āyatana dhātuṣu evam vicāryamāṇaḥ pañcadhā na saṃbhavati sa katham avidyamānaḥ san saṃsariṣyati iti evam ātmanaḥ api na asti saṃsāraḥ vandhyā sutasya iva avidyamāna tvāt 
[124,iv_125,i]	api ca ayam ātmā upādānāt upādānam saṃsaran vibhavaḥ bhavet vibhavaḥ ca anupādānaḥ kaḥ sa kim saṃsariṣyati bhavatu kāmam ātmanaḥ saṃsāraḥ yadi anupādānasya sataḥ asya saṃsāraḥ yuktaḥ syāt katham punar asya anupādāna tā prasajyate iti pratipādayan āha upādānāt upādānam saṃsaran vibhavaḥ bhavet iti 
[125,ii]	iha hi manuṣya upādānāt deva upādānam gacchan parityajya vā manuṣya upādānam deva upādānam gacchet aparityajya vā yadi tāvat parityajya gacchati iti ucyate tadā pūrva upādānasya parityāgāt uttarasya ca anupādānāt tad antarāle vibhavaḥ syāt vigataḥ bhavaḥ vibhavaḥ bhavaḥ pañca upādāna skandhāḥ tat rahitaḥ syāt yaḥ ca vibhavaḥ anupādānaḥ sa skandha rahita tvāt prajñapti upādānakāraṇa rahita tvāt nirhetukaḥ syāt yaḥ ca anupādānaḥ nirañjanaḥ avyaktaḥ nirhetukaḥ kaḥ saḥ na kaścid saḥ na asti eva saḥ iti arthaḥ tasmin ca asati tad abhāvāt eva upādānam api nirupādātṛkam na asti iti kim saṃsariṣyati na asti eva tat yat saṃsariṣyati iti arthaḥ athavā kim iti etat saṃsaraṇa kriyā viśeṣaṇam tatas ca avidyamāna tvāt na eva saṃsaraṇa kriyām kariṣyati evam tāvat pūrva upādāna parityāgena saṃsaraṇam ayuktam atha aparityāgena tathā api na upapadyate kim kāraṇam pūrvasya aparityāgāt uttarasya ca grahaṇāt yasmāt ekasya ātmanaḥ dvaya ātmaka tā syāt na ca etat iṣyate iti tasmāt aparityāgena api saṃsaraṇam na asti 
[125,iii_125,v]	atha pūrva uttarayoḥ bhavayoḥ madhye āntarābhavika skandha saṃbhavāt taiḥ ca sa upādāna tvāt sa upādānam saṃsarataḥ api na vibhavatā prasaṅgaḥ iti tat api na yuktam pūrva bhava parityāga aparityāga abhyām āntara āmavika skandha saṃsāre api tulya prasaṅga tvāt yugapad tyāgopāt ānāt adoṣaḥ iti ced ucyate kim eka deśena pūrva upādānam tyajate eka deśena antarā abhava upādānam saṃcarati atha sarva ātmanā tatra yadi avayavena iti parikalpyate tadā dvaya ātmaka tā prasaṅgāt iti ukta doṣaḥ atha sarva ātmanā evam api saḥ eva vibhavatā aprasaṅgaḥ āpadyate etāvān tu viśeṣaḥ yad antarābhava saṃcāre atisāmīpyāt sūkṣmam kālam anupādānaḥ syāt na ca sarva ātmanā ekasya padārthasya abhinna padārthasya viṣaye yugapad tyāga upādāne dṛṣṭe na hi ekasya devadattasya sarva ātmanā gṛhāt gṛham saṃcarataḥ ekadā tyāga upādāna kriye dve saṃbhavataḥ atha ekena pādena ekasya parityāgāt aparasya ca upādānāt yugapad tyāgopa ādāne parikalpyete nanu evam sati pāda dvaya vat dvaya ātmaka tā ātmanaḥ syāt aṃśena pūrvatra avasthānāt aṃśena ca uttaratra avasthānāt aneka avayava tā prasajyeta tasmāt yaugapadyena api tyāga upādāne na saṃbhavataḥ iti aparihāraḥ eva ayam tasmāt antarā abhava upādāne api saḥ eva doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti sarvathā ātmanaḥ api na asti saṃsāraḥ yadā ca saṃskārāṇām ātmanaḥ ca saṃsāraḥ na asti tadā na asti eva saṃsāraḥ iti sthitam 
[125,vi]	atra āha vidyate eva saṃsāraḥ pratidvandvi sadbhāvāt iha yaḥ na asti na tasya pratidvandvī vidyate tat yathā vandhyā sūnoḥ iti asti ca saṃsārasya pratidvandvi nirvāṇam tasmāt asti saṃsāraḥ iti ucyate syāt saṃsāraḥ yadi tad pratidvandvi nirvāṇam syāt na tu asti iti āha saṃskārāṇām na nirvāṇam kathaṃcid upapadyate sattvasya api na nirvāṇam kathaṃcid upapadyate 
[126,i_126,ii]	yadi nirvāṇam nāma kiṃcid syāt tat parikalpyamānam saṃskārāṇām nityānām vā parikalpyeta anityānām vā tatra nityānām avikāriṇām kim nirvāṇam kuryāt anityānām api asaṃvidyamānānām kim nirvāṇam kuryāt iti sarvam pūrveṇa tulyam na kathaṃcid iti na kena api prakāreṇa iti arthaḥ atha sattvasya nirvāṇam parikalpyate tat api nityasya vā anityasya vā pūrvavat na upapadyate 
[126,iii]	atha nitya anitya tvena avācyasya parikalpyate nanu evam sati nirvāṇe api ātmā asti iti abhyupeta bhavati saṃsāraḥ iva api ca sa upādānasya eva ātmanaḥ avācya tā yujyate na ca nirvāṇe upādānam asti iti kutas asya avācya tā bhavatu vā tattva anya tva a ācya tā ātmanaḥ api tu kim asau nirvāṇe asti uta na asti yadi asti tadā mokṣe api tasya sadbhāvāt nitya tā syāt atha na asti tadā anityaḥ ātmā syāt tatas ca tattva anyatva avācya tāvat nitya anitya tvena api ātmanaḥ avaktavyatā iti na syāt atha nirvāṇe api ātmanaḥ astitva nā astitvena avācya tā eva iṣyate evam api kim asau vijñeyaḥ atha na yadi vijñeyaḥ na tarhi nirupādānaḥ asau ātmā nirvāṇe vijñeya tvāt saṃsāraḥ iva atha na vijñāyate tatra asau avijñeya svarūpa tvāt khapuṣpa vat na asti eva iti kutas asya avācya tā tat evam nirvāṇam api na asti tad abhāvāt na asti saṃsāraḥ iti atas eva uktam bhagavatyām aṣṭa sāhasrikāyām 
[126,iv_126,vi]	nirvāṇam api āyuṣman subhūte māyā upamam svapna upamam buddha dharmāḥ āyuṣman subhūte māyā upamāḥ svapna upamāḥ ityādi saceta kula putra nirvāṇāt api adhikataraḥ anyaḥ dharmaḥ abhaviṣyat tam api aham māyā upamam svapna upamam iti vadāmi tathā ārya samādhi rāja bhaṭṭārake paramārtha satya supinena samam nirvāṇam svapna samotaratī manaḥ evam otarati yena vidu mana saṃvaraḥ kathitu śreṣṭhu ayam tathā nirodha satyam supinam yathā eva svapna svabhāvām atha nirvṛtim ca yena iha vācā uttari bodhisattvaḥ ayam khu saḥ vuccati vāca saṃvaraḥ 
[127,i]	atra āha yadi api tvayā saṃsāra nirvāṇe pratiṣiddhe tathā api bandha mokṣau vidyete na ca avidyamānasya bhāva svabhāvasya bandha mokṣau saṃbhavataḥ tasmāt bandha mokṣa sadbhāvāt vidyate eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ iti ucyate syāt bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ yadi bandha mokṣau eva syātām na tu staḥ iti āha na badhyante na mucyante udaya vyaya dharmiṇaḥ saṃskārāḥ pūrvavat sattvaḥ badhyate na na mucyate 
[127,ii]	iha ye ime rāga ādayaḥ kleśāḥ baddhānām asvatantrī karaṇe bandhanam iti vyapadiśyate yaiḥ ca baddhāḥ pṛthagjanāḥ traidhātukam na atikramanti iti vyavasthāpyate tat etat rāga ādikam bandhana tvena parikalpyamānam udaya vyaya dharmiṇām tāvat kṣaṇikānām saṃskārāṇām utpāda anantara dhvaṃsinām naṣṭānām asattvāt na saṃbhavati rāga ādi bandhana viccheda lakṣaṇaḥ api mokṣaḥ anityānām saṃskārāṇām avidyamāna tvāt na eva saṃbhavati pūrvavat pūrva ukta vidhinā iti arthaḥ yathā ca pūrva ukta vidhinā saṃskārāṇām bandha mokṣau na saṃbhavataḥ evam pūrvavat eva sattvaḥ api na badhyate na api mucyate iti evam bandha mokṣau api na staḥ 
[127,iii]	atra āha yadi api saṃskārāṇām sattvasya vā bandhaḥ na asti tathā api rāga ādikam upādāna ākhyam bandhana bhūtam asti tad sadbhāvāt bandhaḥ api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate syāt upādānam bandhanam yadi kaṃcid padārtham badhnīyāt na tu badhnāti yathā ca na badhnāti tathā pratipādayan āha bandhanam ced upādānam sa upādānaḥ na badhyate badhyate na anupādānaḥ kimavasthaḥ atha badhyate 
[127,iv]	tatra vidyamāna upādānaḥ sa upādānaḥ sa tāvat bhāvaḥ na badhyate yaḥ hi sa upādānaḥ sa baddhaḥ eva tasya punar api bandhana yogaḥ kim kuryāt yaḥ ca api anupādānaḥ bandhana rahitaḥ asau api bandhana rahita tvāt tathāgatavat na badhyate anupādānaḥ bandhana rahitaḥ badhyate iti paraspara viruddha tvāt ca ayuktam etat yaḥ ca evam nirūpyamāṇaḥ sa upādānaḥ nirupādānaḥ vā na badhyate saḥ idānīm kimavasthaḥ badhyatām na asti eva asau kācid aparā asya avasthā yasyām badhyeta iti abhiprāyaḥ yadā ca evam nirūpyamāṇam bandhanam na kaṃcid api badhnāti tadā kaṃcid api abadhnate upādānasya rāga ādeḥ kutas bandhana tvam iti tasmāt bandhanam api na asti 
[127,v_127,vi]	api ca badhnīyāt bandhanam kāmam bandhyāt pūrvam bhavet yadi na ca asti tat iha bandhya vyatirekeṇa bandhanam nigaḍa ādikam pūrva siddham sat bandhyam devadattam badhnāti iti dṛṣṭam evam yadi bandhyebhyaḥ saṃskārebhyaḥ pudgalāt vā bandhyāt pūrvam rāga ādikam bandhanam siddham syāt tena pūrva siddhena bandhanam syāt saṃskārāṇām pudgalasya vā tat ca etat na saṃbhavati nirāśrayasya rāga ādikasya asiddha tvāt pūrva siddhasya ca bandhanasya paścāt bandhyena saha saṃbandhasya niṣprayojana tvāt bandhyasya ca bandhanāt pṛthak siddhasya pūva bandhana apekṣā niṣprayojana tvāt ca na asti bandhyāt bandhanasya pūrva siddhiḥ tasmāt na eva bandhanam kaṃcid api badhnāti na ca kaṃcid api abadhnataḥ bandhana tvam yuktam iti na asti bandhanam bandhana abhāvāt ca bandhyaḥ api na asti iti siddham yat punar atra śeṣam dūṣaṇam tat śeṣa m uktam gamyamāna gata āgataiḥ iti veditavyam śloka pāṭha parivartanena baddhaḥ na badhyate tāvat abaddhaḥ na eva badhyate baddha ābaddha vinirmuktaḥ badhyamānaḥ na badhyate ityādinā yojyam 
[128,i]	atra āha yadi api bhavatā bandhanam pratiṣiddham tathā api saṃsāra cāraka āgāra avabaddha anāmatrāṇānām sattvānām mahā kāruṇikaiḥ tathāgataiḥ śīla samādhi prajñā ātma kara kandha traya upadeśaḥ yad artham uktaḥ sa tāvat mokṣaḥ asti na ca abaddhasya puṃsaḥ mokṣaḥ tasmāt bandhaḥ api asti iti ucyate syāt bandhayadi mokṣaḥ eva syāt iha ayam mokṣaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ baddhasya vā parikalpyeta abaddhasya vā kicātaḥ ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha baddhaḥ na mucyate tāvat abaddhaḥ na eva mucyate syātām baddhe mucyamāne yugapad bandha mokṣaṇe 
[128,ii]	tatra baddhasya mokṣaḥ na saṃbhavati baddha tvāt atha baddhasya paścāt upāyena mokṣaḥ iti kṛtvā baddhaḥ eva mucyate iti syāt na tarhi baddhaḥ mucyate iti vaktavyam kim tarhi mokṣyate iti vartamāna sāmīpyāt eva mucyate iti ced yadi kadācid api mokṣaḥ saṃbhavet tadā samīpe syāt yadā tu kasyāṃcid api avasthāyām mokṣe iṣyamāṇe baddhasya mokṣa asaṃbhavena mokṣa abhāvaḥ pratipipādayiṣita tadā kutas vartamāna samīpa tā evam tāvat baddhaḥ na mucyate iti sthitam 
[128,iii_128,iv]	idānīm abaddhaḥ api na mucyate sa hi muktaḥ eva tasya punar api mokṣaḥ kim kuryāt muktānām ca arhatām punar api mokṣa apekṣa tvāt baddha tā eva syāt tatas ca arhataḥ api bandhaḥ syāt atha syāt abaddhasya mokṣa asaṃbhavāt baddhaḥ eva mucyate iti evam sati baddhe mucyamāne parikalpyamāne baddha tvāt mucyamāna tvāt ca yaugapadyena bandha mokṣaṇe syātām na ca paraspara viruddha tvāt āloka andhakāra vat ekasmin kāle bandha mokṣaṇe upapadyete yatas ca evam baddha ābaddhayoḥ mokṣā saṃbhava tasmāt mokṣaḥ api na asti tad abhāvāt ca bandhanam api na asti iti siddham 
[128,v^1]	atra āha yadi bhavatā eva saṃsāra nirvāṇe niṣiddhe bandha mokṣau ca pratiṣiddhau yaḥ eṣa saṃsāra vinirmumukṣūṇām avidyā sāndra andhakāra vividha kudarśana kaṭhina ati dīrgha latā saṃchādita sat patham jāti ādi vividhā paryanta vyasana aniṣṭatara vipula vipāka phalada anuśaya viṣa vṛkṣa saṃkulam viṃśati śikhara samunnata tara ati pṛthu sat kāya dṛṣṭi mahā śaila pariveṣṭita sarva diṅmukham viṣaya sukha āśāti picchila vipula mahā taṭa vivara vāhi tṛṣṇā nadī mahā parikham saṃsāra mahā aṭavī kāntāram nistitīrṣūṇām parama āśvāsa karaḥ kuśalaḥ mahā dharma chandaḥ kadā nu khalu aham anupādānaḥ nirvāsyāmi kadā nu me nirvāṇam bhaviṣyati iti nanu sa vyarthakaḥ eva saṃjāyate yaḥ ca api evam utpādita kuśala amala vipula dharma chandānām kalyāṇa mitra saṃseva ādāna śīla śruta cintā bhāvana ādi kramaḥ nirvāṇa prāptaye nanu tamyā api vaiyarthyam syāt iti ucyate 
[128,v^2]	yaḥ hi evam niḥsvabhāveṣu sarva bhāveṣu pratibimba marīcikā jala alāta cakra svapna māyā indrajāla sadṛśeṣu ātma ātmīya svabhāva rahiteṣu viparyāsa mātra anugamāt tām eva sat kāya dṛṣṭim aham mama iti ahaṃkāram amakāra samudācāra parigraheṇa utpādya manyate nirvāsyāmi anupādānaḥ nirvāṇam me bhaviṣyati iti yeṣām grahaḥ teṣām upādāna mahā grahaḥ 
[129,i]	aham anupādānaḥ sarva upādāna rahitaḥ nirvāsyāmi mama ca evam pratipannasya nirvāṇam bhaviṣyati iti evam yeṣām mumukṣūṇām grāhaḥ bhavati nanu tat eva ahaṃkāram amakāra ākhyam sat kāya dṛṣṭayupādānam eṣām mahā grahaḥ bhavati na ca evaṃvidha mahā graha abhiniviṣṭānām śāntiḥ saṃbhāvyate niravaśeṣa graha prahāṇena eva mokṣa avāptaye yāvat ahaṃmam eti grāha abhiniveśaḥ yāvat ca nirvāṇam nāma asti iti grāha abhiniveśaḥ yāvat ca upādāna tyāga abhiniveśaḥ tāvat niyatam eva anupāyena nirvāṇam prārthayatām sarve eva ārambhāḥ vyarthāḥ bhavanti tasmāt mumukṣuṇā sarvam etat parityājyam yathā uktam bhagavatā ārya dhyāyita muṣṭi sūtre 
[129,ii^1]	atha khalu bhagavān mañju śriyam kumāra bhūtam etat avocat caturṇām ārya satyānām yathābhūta artha adarśanāt caturbhiḥ viparyāsaiḥ viparyasta cittāḥ satvāḥ evam imam abhūtam saṃsāram na atikrāmanti evam ukte mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ bhagavantam etat avocat deśayatu bhagavān kasya upalambhataḥ sattvāḥ saṃsāram na atikrāmanti bhagavān āha ātma ātmīya upalambhāt mañjuśrīḥ sattvāḥ saṃsāram na atikrāmanti tat kasya hetoḥ yaḥ hi mañjuśrīḥ ātmānam param ca samanupaśyati tasya karma abhisaṃskārāḥ bhavanti bālaḥ mañju śrīraśrutavān pṛthagjanaḥ atyanta aparinirvṛtān sarva dharmānaprajānānaḥ ātmānam param ca upalabhate upalabhya abhiniviśate abhiniviṣṭaḥ san rajyate duṣyate muhyate 
[129,ii^2]	sa raktaḥ duṣṭaḥ mūḍhaḥ san trividham karma abhisaṃskaroti kāyena vācā manasā saḥ asat samāropeṇa vikalpayati aham raktaḥ aham dviṣṭaḥ aham mūḍhaḥ iti tasya tathāgata śāsane pravrajitasya evam bhavati aham śīlavān aham brahmacārī iti aham saṃsāram samatikramiṣyāmi aham nirvāṇam anuprāpsyāmi aham duḥkhebhyaḥ mokṣyāmi sa vikalpayati ime kuśalāḥ dharmāḥ ime akuśalāḥ dharmāḥ ime dharmāḥ prahātavyāḥ ime dharmāḥ sākṣāt kartavyāḥ duḥkham parijñātavyam samudayaḥ prahātavyaḥ nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ mārgaḥ bhāvayitavyaḥ sa vikalpayati anityāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ ādīptāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ yat nu aham sarva saṃskārebhyaḥ palāyeyam 
[129,ii^3]	tasya evam avekṣamāṇasya utpadyate nirvitsaha gataḥ manasikāraḥ animitta purogataḥ tasya evam bhavati eṣā sā duḥkha parijñā yā iyam eṣām dharmāṇām parijñā tasya evam bhavati yat nu aham samudayam prajaheyam saḥ ebhyaḥ dharmebhyaḥ ārtīyate jehrīyate vitarati vijugupsate uttrasyati saṃtrasyati saṃtrāsam āpadyate tasya evam bhavati iyam eṣām dharmāṇām sākṣātkriyā idam samudaya prahāṇam yat idam ebhyaḥ dharmebhyaḥ artīyanā vijugupsanā tasya eva bhavati nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ samudayam kalpayitvā nirodhe saṃjānāti tasya evam bhavati eṣā sā nirodha sākṣāt kriyā tasya evam bhavati yat nūnam aham mārgam bhāvayeyam 
[129,ii^4]	saḥ ekaḥ rahaḥ gataḥ tān dharmān manasi kurvan śamatham pratilabhate tasya tena nirvitsaha gatena manasikāreṇa śamathe utpadyate tasya sarva dharmeṣu cittam pratilīyate prativahati pratyudāvartate tebhyaḥ ca ārtīyate jehrīyate anabhinandana acittam utpadyate tasya evam bhavati muktaḥ asmi sarva duḥkhebhyaḥ na mama bhūyas uttarim kiṃcitkaraṇīyam arhan asmi iti ātmānam saṃjānāti sa maraṇa kāla samaye utpattim ātmanaḥ samanupaśyati tasya kāṅkṣā ca vicikitsā ca bhavati buddha bodhau sa vicikitsā patitaḥ kālagataḥ mahānirayeṣu prapatati tat kasya hetoḥ yathā api idam anutpannān sarva dharmān vikalpayitvā tathāgate vicikitsām vimatim ca utpādayati 
[130,i]	atha khalu mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ bhagavantam etat avocat katham punar bhagavan catvāri ārya satyāni draṣṭavyāni bhagavān āha yena mañju śrīḥ anutpannāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tena duḥkham parijñātam yena asamutthitāḥ sarva dharmāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tasya samudayaḥ prahīṇaḥ yena atyanta parinirvṛtāḥ sarva dharmāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tena nirodhaḥ sākṣātkṛtaḥ yena atyanta śūnyāḥ sarva dharmāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tena mārgaḥ bhāvitaḥ yena mañjuśrīḥ evam catvāri ārya satyāni dṛṣṭāni sa na kalpayati na vikalpayati ime kuśalāḥ dharmāḥ ime akuśalāḥ dharmāḥ ime dharmāḥ prahātavyāḥ ime dharmāḥ sākṣāt kartavyāḥ duḥkham parijñātavyam samudayaḥ prahātavyaḥ nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ mārgaḥ bhāvayitavyaḥ iti tat kasya heto tathā hi sa tam dharmam na samanupaśyati yam parikalpayet bāla pṛthagjanāḥ tu etān dharmān kalpayantaḥ rajyanti ca dviṣanti ca muhyanti ca sa na kaṃcid dharmam āvyūhati nirvyūhati tasya evamanāvyūhataḥ anirvyūhataḥ traidhātuke citta na sajjati ajāta sarva tra edhātukam samanupaśyati iti vistaraḥ 
[130,ii_130,iii]	atas eva asmāt āgamāt parama artha satyaḥ ucyate na nirvāṇa samāropaḥ na saṃsāra apakarṣaṇam yatra kaḥ tatra saṃsāraḥ nirvāṇam kim vikalpyate yatra hi nāma parama artha satye na evam na nirvāṇa samāropaḥ na nirvāṇa adhyāropaḥ saṃbhavati anupalabhyamāna tvāt na api saṃsāra apakarṣaṇam saṃsāra parikṣayaḥ na saṃbhavati kaḥ tatra saṃsāraḥ yaḥ vikalpyate kṣaya artham kim vā tatra nirvāṇam yat prāpi artham vikalpyate athavā yatra nirvāṇe kasyacid sattvasya saṃsārāt apakarṣaṇam apanayanam nirvāṇe ca samāropaṇam prayatnavatā api na śakyate kartum saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ api anupalabhyamāna tvāt tatra kim nirvāṇam vikalpyate na eva hi kiṃcid vikalpayitum yuktam avikalpayataḥ ca niyatam yathā udita saṃsāra aṭavī kāntāra atikramaḥ nirvāṇa pura prāptiḥ ca bhaviṣyati iti atas eva uktam ārya mārada mana sūtre 
[131,i]	atha mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ tasyām velāyām tathārūpam samanvāhāram samanvāharati sma yat māraḥ pāpīyān indra kīla bandhana baddhaḥ dharaṇī tala prapatitaḥ utkrośati sma gāḍha bandhana baddhaḥ asmi mañjuśrīḥ āha asti pāpīyan etasmāt bandhanāt gāḍhataram bandhanam yena tvam nitya baddhaḥ na punar badhyase tat punar katamat yat idam asmi māna viparyāsa bandhanam tṛṣṇā dṛṣṭi bandhanam idam pāpīyan bandhanam atas bandhanāt gāḍhataram bandhanam na saṃvidyate tena tvam nitya baddhaḥ na punar badhyase peyālam āha kim tvam pāpīyanna ātta manāḥ bhūyāḥ yadi mucyethāḥ āha ātta manāḥ bhaveyam parama ātta manāḥ bhaveyam 
[131,ii_131,iii]	atha khalu suyāmaḥ deva putraḥ mañju śriyam kumāra bhūtam etat avocat utsṛja mañjuśrīḥ māram pāpīyāṃsam gacchatu sva bhavanam atha khalu mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ māram pāpīyāṃsam etat avocat kena asi pāpīyan baddhaḥ yadā ātmānam utsṛjasi āha na jāne mañjuśrīḥ kena asmi baddhaḥ iti āha yathā tvam pāpīyan abaddhaḥ baddha saṃjñī evam eva sarva bāla pṛthagjanāḥ anitye nitya saṃjñinaḥ duḥkhe aduḥkha saṃjñinaḥ aśubhe śubha saṃjñinaḥ anātmani ātma saṃjñinaḥ arūpe rūpa saṃjñinaḥ avedanāyām vedanā saṃjñinaḥ asaṃjñāyām saṃjñā saṃjñinaḥ asaṃskāre saṃskāra saṃjñinaḥ avijñāne vijñāna saṃjñinaḥ api tu khalu punar pāpīyan yaḥ tvam mokṣyase kutas mokṣyase āha na aham jāne kutaścid mokṣye āha evam eva pāpīyan ye api mokṣyante nate kutaścid vimokṣyante anyatra yā asau asat bhūta saṃjñā tām parijānanti tām parijñāya vimuktāḥ iti ucyante iti atas eva āgamāt asat viparyāsa kalpanā mātra latā bandhana vicchedaḥ vimokṣaḥ nirvāṇam iti ucyate svapna upalabdha dahana jvālā nirvāpaṇa vat tad anila salilaiḥ iti 
[132,i]	atra āha vidyate eva saṃsāraḥ karma phala saṃbandha āśraya tvāt yadi iha saṃtāna aviccheda krameṇa janma maraṇa paraṃparayā hetu phala bhāva pravṛttyā saṃskārāṇām ātmanaḥ vā saṃsaraṇam syāt syāt tadānīm karma phala saṃbandhaḥ yathā āvarṇite saṃsāra abhāve tu utpatti anantara vināśi tvāt cittasya karma ākṣepa kāle ca vipākasya asadbhāvāt karma phala saṃbandha abhāvaḥ eva syāt saṃsāra sadbhāve tu sati iha kṛtasya karmaṇe janma antare api vipāka phala saṃbandhāt karmaṇām phala saṃbandhaḥ na virodhitaḥ bhavati tasmāt vidyate eva saṃsāraḥ karma phala saṃbandha āśraya tvāt iti kāni punar tāni karmāṇi kim vā tad phalam iti tad prabheda vivakṣaya it am ucyate ātma saṃyamakam cetaḥ para anugrāhakam ca yat maitram sa dharmaḥ tad bījam phalasya pretya ca iha ca 
[132,ii]	tatra āhitaḥ utpāditaḥ ahaṃmānaḥ asmin iti ātmā skandhān upādāya prajñapyamānaḥ pudgalaātmā iti ucyate cinoti upacinoti śubham aśubham karma vipāka dāna sāmarthye niyamayati iti cetaḥ cittam manaḥ vijñānam iti tasya eva paryāyāḥ ātmānam saṃyamayati viṣayeṣu asvatantrayati rāga ādi kleśa vaśena pravṛttim nivārayati iti ātma saṃyamakam tat etat ātma saṃyamakam kuśalam cetaḥ prāṇa atipāta ādiṣu pravṛtti vidhārakam durgati gamanāt dhārayati iti dharmaḥ iti ucyate 
[132,iii]	dharma śabdaḥ ayam pravacane tridhā vyavasthāpitaḥ sva lakṣaṇa dhāraṇa arthena kugati gamana vidhāraṇa arthena pāñcagatika saṃsāra vidhāraṇa arthena tatra sva lakṣaṇa dhāraṇa arthena sarve sa āsravāḥ anāsravāḥ ca dharmāḥ iti ucyante kugati gamana vidhāraṇa arthena daśa kuśala ādayaḥ dharmāḥ iti ucyante dharma cārī sukham śete asmin loke paratra ca pāñcagatika saṃsāra gamana vidhāraṇa arthena nirvāṇe dharmaḥ iti ucyate dharmam śaraṇam gacchati iti atra iha tu kugati gamana vidhāraṇa arthena eva dharma śabdaḥ abhipretaḥ 
[132,iv]	kim punar ātma saṃyamakam eva ekam cetaḥ dharmaḥ iti na iti āha kim tarhi para anugrāhakam ca maitram ca yat cetaḥ asau api dharmaḥ maitram iti atra caśabdaḥ lupta nirdiṣṭaḥ veditavyaḥ tatra param anugṛhṇāti iti para anugrāhakam cetaḥ catur saṃgraha vastu pravṛttam bhaya paritrāṇa pravṛttam ca yat cetaḥ asau api dharmaḥ mitre bhavam aviruddham sattveṣu yat cetaḥ tat maitram cetaḥ maitram yat cetaḥ tad maitra cetaḥ maitram evam vā yat ca etat trividham cetaḥ nirdiṣṭam sa dharmaḥ iti ucyate viparyayāt adharmaḥ yojyaḥ 
[133,i_133,ii]	yat ca etat nirdiṣṭa prabhedam cetaḥ tad bījam phalasya asādhāraṇam phala abhinirvṛttau yat kāraṇam tat eva bījam iti ucyate tat yathā śāli aṅkurasya śāli bījam yat tu sādhāraṇam kṣiti ādi na tat bījam kāraṇam etat yathā etat evam iha api iṣṭasya vipākasya abhinirvṛttau trividham cetaḥ bhavati bījam puruṣakāra ādayaḥ tu kāraṇam eva kasmin punar kāle bījasya phala niṣpattiḥ iti āha pretya ca iha ca pretya iti adṛṣṭe janmani iha iti dṛṣṭe janmani iti arthaḥ etat ca āgamāt vistareṇa boddhavyam 
[133,iii_133,v]	evam tāvat citta ātmakam eva ekam dharmam vyavasthāpya punar api dvividham bhagavatā cetanā cetayitvā ca karma uktam parama ṛṣiṇā parama artha darśanāt ṛṣiḥ paramaḥ ca asau ṛṣiḥ ca iti parama ṛṣiḥ sarva ākāra tayā parama artha gamanāt śrāvaka pratyekabuddhabhyaḥ api utkṛṣṭa tvāt parama ṛṣiḥ saṃbuddhaḥ bhagavān tena parama ṛṣiṇā cetanā karma cetayitvā ca karma iti uktam sūtre yat ca etat dvividham karma uktam tasya anekavidhaḥ bhedaḥ karmaṇaḥ parikīrtitaḥ katham kṛtvā tatra yat cetanā iti uktam karma tat mānasam smṛtam cetayitvā ca yat tu uktam tat tu kāyika vācikam 
[133,vi]	manasi bhavam mānasam manaḥ dvāreṇa eva niṣṭhā gamanāt kāya vāc pravṛtti nirapekṣa tvāt ca manaḥ vijñāna saṃprayuktā eva cetanā mānasam karma iti ucyate tatraśabdaḥ nirdhāraṇe yat tu dvitīyam cetayitvā ca karma iti uktam tat punar kāyikam vācikam ca veditavyam evam ca evam ca kāya vāgbhyām pravartiṣye iti evam cetasā saṃcintya yat kriyate tad cetayitvā karma iti ucyate tat punar dvividham kāyikam vācikam ca kāya vācoḥ bhava tvāt tad dvāreṇa ca niṣṭhā gamanāt evam ca trividham kāyikam vācikam mānasam ca 
[133,vii]	etat api trividham karma punar bhidyamānam saptavidham saṃjāyate iti evam tasya karmaṇaḥ bhagavatā bahu prakāraḥ bhedaḥ anuvarṇitaḥ katham kṛtvā vāc viṣpandaḥ aviratayaḥ yāḥ ca avijñapti saṃjñitāḥ avijñaptayaḥ eva anyāḥ smṛtāḥ viratayaḥ tathā paribhoga anvayam puṇyam apuṇyam ca tathāvidham cetanā ca iti saptā ete dharmāḥ karma añjanāḥ smṛtāḥ 
[133,viii^1]	tatra vyakta varṇa uccāraṇam vāc viṣpandaḥ śarīraṃceṣṭā tatra kuśala akuśalā vā vāc sarvā eva virati avirati lakṣaṇā vijñapti samutthāpikā sāmānyena vāc iti gṛhyate evam kuśalaḥ akuśalaḥ vā virati avirati lakṣaṇaḥ vijñapti samutthāpakaḥ viṣpandaḥ sāmānyena gṛhyate yathā ca etat vijñapteḥ dvidhā bhedaḥ evam avijñapteḥ api avirati lakṣaṇāḥ avijñaptayaḥ virati lakṣaṇāḥ ca iti kṛtvā tatra avirati lakṣaṇāḥ avijñaptayaḥ tat yathā adya prabhṛti mayā prāṇinam hatvā cauryam kṛtvā jīvikā parikalpayitavyā iti pāpa karma abhyupagamāt prabhṛti tat akāriṇaḥ api akuśala karma abhyupagama hetukāḥ satata samitam avijñaptayaḥ samupajāyante 
[133,viii^2]	kaivarta ādīnāṃca jāla ādi parikarma kālāt prabhṛti tat akāriṇām api yāḥ avijñaptayaḥ upajāyante tāḥ etāḥ avirati lakṣaṇāḥ avijñaptayaḥ iti ucyante yathā ca etāḥ tathā anyāḥ virati lakṣaṇāḥ kuśala svabhāvāḥ avijñaptayaḥ tat yathā adya prabhṛti prāṇa atipāta ādibhyaḥ prativiramāmi iti kāya vāc vijñapti parisamāptikā lakṣaṇāt prabhṛti tad uttara kālam pramatta ādi avasthasya api yāḥ kuśala upacaya svabhāvāḥ avijñaptayaḥ upajāyante tāḥ etāḥ virati lakṣaṇāḥ avijñaptayaḥ iti ucyante etāḥ rūpa kriyā svabhāvāḥ api satyaḥ vijñapti vat parān na vijñāpayanti iti avijñaptayaḥ 
[134,i_134,ii]	tathā paribhoga anvayam puṇyam kuśalam iti arthaḥ paribhogena anvayaḥ asya iti paribhoga anvayam paribhogaḥ parityaktasya vastunaḥ saṃgha ādibhiḥ upabhogaḥ anvayaḥ anugamaḥ dāyaka saṃtāna jaḥ kuśala upacayaḥ iti arthaḥ apuṇyam ca tathāvidham paribhoga anvayam iti arthaḥ tat yathā devakula ādi pratiṣṭhāpanam yatra sattvāḥ hanyante yathā yathā hi tad kīrtau prāṇinaḥ hanyante tathā tathā tad deva kula ādi upabhogāt tad kartṛṇām saṃtāne paribhoga an vayam apuṇyam api jāyate iti evam apuṇyam ca tathāvidham bhavati 
[134,iii_134,v]	citta abhisaṃskāra manaskarma lakṣaṇā cetanā ca iti saṃkṣepeṇa etat saptavidham karma bhavati kuśala akuśalā vāc kuśala akuśalaḥ viṣpandaḥ kuśalam avijñapti lakṣaṇam akuśalam avijñapti lakṣaṇam paribhoga anvayam puṇyam paribhoga anvayam apuṇyam cetanā ca iti ete ca sapta dharmāḥ karma añjanāḥ karma tvena abhivyaktāḥ karma lakṣaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ 
[134,vi_134,vii]	atra eke paricodayanti yat etat karma bahuvidham uktam tat kimā vipāka kālāt avatiṣṭhate atha na tiṣṭhati utpatti anantara vināśi tvāt yadi tāvat tiṣṭhatyā pāka kālāt ced karma tat nitya tām iyāt niruddham ced niruddham sat kim phalam janayiṣyati yadi utpannam sat karma āvipāka kālam svarūpeṇa avatiṣṭhate iti parikalpyate tat iyantam kālam asya nitya tā āpadyate vināśa rahita tvāt paścāt vināśa sadbhāvāt na nitya tvam iti ced na etat evam pūrvam vināśa rahitasya ākāśa ādi vat paścāt api vināśena saṃbandha abhāvāt vināśa rahitasya ca asaṃskṛta tva prasaṅgāt asaṃskṛtānām ca vipāka adarśanāt avipāka tvena sadā eva avasthānāt nitya tā abhyupagamaḥ eva karmaṇām upapadyate iti evam tāvat nitya tve doṣaḥ atha utpāda anantara vināśi tvam eva karmaṇām abhyupetam nanu evam sati niruddham ced niruddham sat kim phalam janayiṣyati abhāvībhūtam sat karma avidyamāna svabhāva tvāt na eva phalam janayiṣyati iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[135,i]	tatra eke nikāya antarīyāḥ parihāram varṇayanti utpatti anantara vināśi tvāt saṃskārāṇām anitya tva doṣaḥ tāvat asmākam na upapadyate yat ca api uktam niruddham ced niruddham sat kim phalam janayiṣyati iti atra api parihāram brūmaḥ yaḥ aṅkura prabhṛtiḥ bījāt saṃtānaḥ abhipravartate tatas phalam ṛte bījāt sa ca na abhipravartate 
[135,ii]	iha bījam kṣaṇikam api sat sva jātīya bhāvi phala viśeṣa niṣpatti sāmarthya viśeṣa yuktasya eva saṃtānasya aṅkura kāṇḍa nāla patra ādi abhidhānasya hetu bhāvam api upagamya nirudhyate yaḥ ca ayam aṅkura prabhṛtiḥ bījāt saṃtānaḥ pravartate tasmāt krameṇa sahakāri kāraṇa vaikalye sati su alpāt api hetoḥ vipula phala pracayaḥ upajāyate ṛte bījāt vinā bījāt sa ca aṅkura ādi saṃtānaḥ na abhipravartate tat evam tad bhāve bhāvi tvena tad abhāve ca abhāvi tvena bīja hetuka tvam aṅkura ādi saṃtānasya phalasya upadarśitam bhavati 
[135,iii_135,iv]	tat evam bījāt ca yasmāt saṃtānaḥ saṃtānāt ca phala udbhavaḥ bīja pūrvam phalam tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam yadi iha bījam aprasūya aṅkura ādi saṃtānam jvālā aṅgāra ādi virodhi pratyaya sāṃnidhyāt nirudhyeta tadā tatra kārya saṃtāna pravṛtti adarśanāt syāt uccheda darśanam yadi ca bījam na nirudhyeta aṅkura ādi saṃtānaḥ ca pravarteta tadā bījasya anirodha abhyupagamāt śāśvata darśanam syāt na ca etat evam iti atas na asti bījasya śāśvata uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ 
[135,v_135,vi]	yathā ca bīje ayam kramaḥ anuvarṇitaḥ evam yaḥ tasmāt citta saṃtānaḥ cetasaḥ abhipravartate tatas phalam ṛte cittāt sa ca na abhipravartate tasmāt kuśala akuśala cetanā viśeṣa saṃprayuktāt cittāt yaḥ citta saṃtānaḥ tad hetukaḥ pravartate tasmāt kuśala akuśala cetanā paribhāvitāt citta saṃtānāt sahakāri kāraṇa saṃnidhāna avaikalye sati iṣṭam aniṣṭam phalam upajāyate sugati durgatiṣu ṛte tu tad citāt cittam antareṇa sa ca na abhipravartate 
[135,vii_135,viii]	tat evam cittāt ca yasmāt saṃtānaḥ saṃtānāt ca phala udbhavaḥ karma pūrvam phalam tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam yadi arhat carama cittam iva tad hetu phala pāraṃparya avicchinna krama vartinaḥ bhāvinaḥ citta saṃtānasya hetu bhāvam anupagamya kuśalam cittam nirudhyeta tadā ucchinnam tat karma syāt atha api anāgata saṃtānasya hetu bhāvam upagamya svarūpāt apracyutam syāt syāt tadānīm karma śāśvatam na ca etat evam iti tasmāt kṣaṇika karma abhyupagame api na asti uccheda śāśvata darśana dvaya prasaṅgaḥ iti 
[136,i_136,iii]	tat atra yathā udita karma prabheda vyākhyāne daśa kuśalāḥ karma pathāḥ vyākhyātāḥ te ca dharmasya sādhana upāyāḥ śuklāḥ karma pathāḥ daśa phalam kāma guṇāḥ pañca dharmasya pretya ca iha ca te ete daśa kuśalāḥ karma pathāḥ dharmasya sādhana upāyāḥ niṣpatti hetu bhūtāḥ iti arthaḥ kaḥ punar asau kuśala karma patha vyatiriktaḥ dharmaḥ nāma yasya ete sādhana upāya tvena vyavasthāpyante ucyate citta viśeṣaḥ eva kaścid dharma śabdena uktaḥ ātma saṃyamakam cetaḥ para anugrāhakam ca yat maitram sa dharmaḥ iti anena athavā pariniṣṭhita rūpāḥ ete daśa kuśalāḥ karma pathāḥ dharma śabda vācyāḥ bhavanti kriyamāṇa rūpāḥ tu kuśala karma patha vācyāḥ bhavanti tat asya ukta lakṣaṇasya ete daśa kuśalāḥ karma pathāḥ niṣpattau hetu tvena vyavasthāpyante katham punar atra prakrānte karma vibhāge daśa kuśalāḥ karma pathāḥ iti ucyate vāc viṣpandaḥ aviratayaḥ yāḥ ca avijñapti saṃjñitāḥ ityādinā kāyikā srayaḥ karma pathāḥ vācikāḥ catvāraḥ vyākhyātāḥ cetanā ca iti anena abhidhyā vyāpāda samyak dṛṣṭayā ākhya asrayaḥ mānasāḥ vyākhyātāḥ iti evam daśā api kuśalāḥ karma pathāḥ atra vyākhyātāḥ te ca yathā uditasya dharmasya niṣpatti hetavaḥ bhavanti asya ca dharmasya rūpa śabda gandha rasa spraṣṭavya lakṣaṇāḥ pañca kāma guṇāḥ pretya ca adṛṣṭe para loke iti arthaḥ iha ca iti ihaloke iti arthaḥ phalam upabhujyate iti 
[136,iv_136,v^1]	evam tāvat aika nikāyikaiḥ ākṣepa parihāre varṇite sati tān prati apare doṣam udbhāvya anya ākṣepa parihāram varṇayantaḥ āhuḥ bahavaḥ ca mahāntaḥ ca doṣāḥ syuḥ api kalpanā yadi eṣā tena na eva eṣā kalpanātra upapadyate yadi bīja aṅkura sādharmyeṇa citta saṃtāne śāśvata uccheda darśana dvaya doṣa prasaṅga parihāraḥ syāt tadā bahavaḥ ca doṣāḥ saṃkhyā bahu tvena mahāntaḥ ca dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa virodhena para pakṣe prāpruvanti katham kṛtvā yadi hi bīja saṃtāna dṛṣṭāntena śāli bījāt śāli aṅkura ādi saṃtānaḥ eva pravartate na vijātīyaḥ śāli aṅkura ādi saṃtānāt ca śāli phalam eva upajāyate na bilva phalam bhinna jātīya tvāt evam iha api kuśala cittāt kuśala citta saṃtānaḥ eva syāt samāna jātīya tvāt na akuśala avyākṛta citta saṃtānaḥ vijātīya tvāt evam akuśala avyākṛta cittāt akuśala avyākṛta citta saṃtānaḥ eva syāt na anyaḥ bhinna jātīya tvāt 
[136,v^2]	kāmarūpā rūpya avacarān āsrava cittebhyaḥ sadṛśānām eva cittānām kāmarūpā rūpya avacarān āsravāṇām utpādaḥ syāt na bhinna jātīyānām manuṣya cittān manuṣya cittam eva syāt na deva nāraka tiryak ādi anya cittam tatas ca yaḥ devaḥ sa devaḥ eva syāt yaḥ manuṣyaḥ sa manuṣyaḥ eva syāt ityādi tatas ca akuśalam api kurvatām deva manuṣyāṇām gati yoni varṇa buddhīndriya bala rūpa bhoga ādi vaicitryam na syāt apāya patanam ca iṣyate ca etat sarvam iti evam bahavaḥ ca mahāntaḥ ca doṣāḥ yasmāt bīja saṃtāna sādharmya kalpanāyām prasajyante tasmāt na eṣā kalpanā atra upapadyate 
[137,i_137,iii]	imām punar pravakṣyāmi kalpanām yā atra yojyate buddhaiḥ pratyekabuddhaiḥ ca śrāvakaiḥ ca anuvarṇitām kā ca asau kalpanā iti āha patram yathā vipraṇāśaḥ tathā ṛṇam iva karma ca caturvidhaḥ dhātutaḥ sa prakṛtyā vyākṛtaḥ ca saḥ iha kuśalam karma kṛtam sat utpāda anantaram eva nirudhyate na ca tasmin niruddhe phala abhāva prasaṅgaḥ yasmāt yadā eva tat karma utpadyate tadā etasya karmaṇaḥ avipraṇāśaḥ nāma viprayuktaḥ dharmaḥ kartuḥ saṃtāne samupajāyate ṛṇa patra sthānīyaḥ tat evam patram yathā avipraṇāśaḥ tathā veditavyaḥ yasya ca asau avipraṇāśa ākhyaḥ dharmaḥ utpadyate ṛṇam iva tat karma veditavyam yathā ca ṛṇa patra avasthānāt prayukte api dhane dhaninaḥ na dhana nāśaḥ bhavati saṃbadhyate eva sa kāla antareṇa pañcamena dhana skandhena tathā vinaṣṭe api karmaṇi avipraṇāśa ākhya dharma antara avasthānāt tad nimittakena phalena abhisaṃbadhyate eva kartā yathā ca ṛṇa patram dātuḥ dhana abhyāgamam kṛtvā nirmuktam sat punar api vidyamānam vā avidyamānam vā na dhana abhyāgame samartham evam avipraṇāśaḥ api datta vipākaḥ san vidyamānaḥ vā avidyamānaḥ vā na śaknoti nirmukta patra vat kartuḥ punar api vipāka saṃbandham kartum 
[137,iv]	yaḥ ca ayam avipraṇāśaḥ asmābhiḥ uktaḥ sūtra antara uktaḥ caturvidhaḥ dhātutaḥ sa kāmarūpā rūpya avacara an āsrava bhedāt prakṛtyāḥ avyākṛtaḥ ca saḥ kuśala akuśala tvena avyākaraṇāt avyākṛtaḥ eva avipraṇāśaḥ yadi asau akuśalānām karmaṇā ām akuśalaḥ syāt tadā kāmam vīta rāgāṇām na syāt yadi ca kuśalānām kuśalaḥ syāt samucchinna kuśala mūlānām sa na syāt tasmāt prakṛti avyākṛtaḥ eva asau 
[137,v_137,vii]	kim ca prahāṇataḥ na praheyaḥ bhāvanā heyaḥ eva vā sa ca ayam avipraṇāśaḥ prahāṇataḥ na praheyaḥ pārthagjanikāni karmāṇi darśana mārgeṇa eva prahīyante mā bhūt āryaḥ pṛthagjana karma samanvāgataḥ iti avipraṇāśaḥ tu tad karma prahāṇe api darśana mārgeṇa na prahīyate kim tu bhāvanā mārgeṇa vā tasyāḥ prahāṇam bhavati dhātu samatikramaṇa praheyaḥ eva iti vā śabdaḥ vikalpa arthaḥ yatas ca evam avipraṇāśaḥ karma vināśe api na naśyati karma prahāṇe api na prahīyate tasmāt avipraṇāśena jāyate karmaṇām phalam 
[138,i]	yadi punar api asya avipraṇāśasya karmaṇaḥ prahāṇena prahāṇāt prahāṇataḥ prahāṇam syāt karmaṇaḥ ca saṃkrameṇa karmaṇaḥ vināśena karma antara saṃmukhībhāvena vināśaḥ syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ syāt iti ucyate prahāṇataḥ praheyaḥ syāt karmaṇaḥ saṃkrameṇa vā yadi doṣāḥ prasajyeran tatra karma vadha ādayaḥ 
[138,ii]	yadi darśana mārgeṇa pārthagjanika karma vat avipraṇāśaḥ prahīyeta tadā karmaṇaḥ vināśaḥ eva syāt karma vināśāt ca āryāṇām iṣṭa aniṣṭa karma phala vipākaḥ pūrva karma phala hetukaḥ na syāt akṛtasya eva karmaṇaḥ phala udayaḥ syāt karma phala abhāva darśanāt ca mithyā darśanam syāt iti evam karma vadha ādayaḥ doṣāḥ prasajyante prahāṇataḥ praheya tva abhyupagame sati avipraṇāśasya evam karmaṇaḥ saṃkrame api yojyam 
[138,iii_138,iv]	sarveṣām viṣa bhāgānām sa bhāgānām ca karmaṇām pratisaṃdhau sa dhātūnām ekaḥ utpadyate tu saḥ bhinna jātīyāni karmāṇi viṣa bhāgāni sadṛśāni sa bhāgāni teṣām sarveṣām eva sa bhāgānām ca viṣa bhāgānām ca karmaṇām kāmarūpa ārūpya dhātu pratisaṃdhiṣu sarva karma apamardanaḥ ekaḥ eva avipraṇāśaḥ utpadyate sa ca api sa dhātūnām samāna dhātukānām eva utpadyate na viṣa bhāga dhātukānām 
[138,v_138,vi]	karmaṇaḥ karmaṇaḥ dṛṣṭe dharmaḥ utpadyate tu saḥ dvi prakārasya sarvasya vipakke api ca tiṣṭhati sa ca ayam avipraṇāśa ākhyaḥ dharmaḥ sarvasya eva karmaṇaḥ cetanā cetayitvā asvabhāvasya sa āsravānāsrava bhedena vā dvi prakāra bhinnasya dṛṣṭe dharme iha eva janmani karmaṇaḥ karmaṇaḥ ekaikaḥ avipraṇāśaḥ utpadyate sa ca ayam avipraṇāśaḥ vipakke api vipāke na avaśyam nirudhyate nirbhukta patra vat ca vidyamānaḥ api san na śaknoti punar api vipaktum 
[138,vii_138,viii]	phala vyatikramāt vā sa maraṇāt vā nirudhyate anāsravam sa āsravam ca vibhāgam tatra lakṣayet tatra phala vyatikramāt nirudhyate yathā uktam bhāvanā heyaḥ eva iti maraṇāt nirudhyate yathā uktam pratisaṃdhau sa dhātūnām ekaḥ utpadyate tu saḥ iti sa ca ayam sa āsravāṇām sa āsravaḥ anāsravāṇām anāsravaḥ iti evam vibhāgam lakṣayet 
[138,ix_138,x]	tat evam śūnyatā ca na ca ucchedaḥ saṃsāraḥ ca na śāśvatam karmaṇaḥ avipraṇāśaḥ ca dharmaḥ buddhena deśitaḥ yasmāt karma kṛtam sat nirudhyate na svabhāvena avatiṣṭhate tasmāt karmaṇaḥ svabhāvena avasthānāt śūnyatā ca upapadyate na ca evam karmaṇaḥ anavasthānāt uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ avipraṇāśa parigraheṇa karma vipāka sadbhāvāt vipāka abhāve hi karmaṇaḥ uccheda darśanam syāt avipraṇāśa dharma sadbhāvāt bīja saṃtāna sādharmya parikalpanā bhāvāt ca nānā gati jāti yoni dhātu bheda bhinnaḥ ca pāñcagatikaḥ saṃsāraḥ vicitraḥ siddhaḥ bhavati na ca śāśvata vāda prasaṅgaḥ karmaṇaḥ sva rūpeṇa avasthāna anabhyupagamāt karmaṇām ca avipraṇāśaḥ avipraṇāśa sadbhāvāt iti evam niravaśeṣa avidyā nidrā apagamāt vibuddhena bhagavatā yasmāt ayam dharmaḥ deśitaḥ tasmāt yat pūrvaṃmuktam pareṇa tiṣṭhatyā pāka kālāt ced karma tad nitya tām iyāt niruddham ced niruddham sat kim phalam janayiṣyati iti tat asmat pakṣe na upapadyate iti tasmāt asmābhiḥ upavarṇita kalpanā eva nyāyyāḥ iti 
[139,i]	atra ucyate kim iha bhavantaḥ gandharvanagara prākāra patana atiśaṅkitayā atīva udvignāḥ tad parirakṣā pariśramāyāsam āpannāḥ ye nāma yūyam karmaṇi anupapadyamāne tad phala nimittam vipra vadadhvam yadi hi karmaṇaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva utpādaḥ syāt tasya āvipākam avasthānāt nitya tvam syāt vināśāt ucchedaḥ syāt yadā tu karma na eva utpadyate svabhāva śūnyatvāt tadā tasya kutas avasthānam vināśaḥ vā yatas eṣā cintā syāt atra āha karma na utpadyate kasmāt 
[139,ii_139,iv]	ācāryaḥ āha niḥsvabhāvam yatas tatas yasmāt niḥsvabhāvam karma tasmāt na utpadyate yadi khalu evam niḥsvabhāva tvāt karma na utpadyate tat katham evam uktam bhagavatā na praṇaśyanyi karmāṇi kalpa koṭi śataiḥ api sāmagrīm prāpya kālam ca phalanti khalu dehinām iti ucyate yasmāt ca tad anutpannam na tasmāt vipraṇaśyati iti evam bhagavataḥ abhiprāyaḥ iti atas na ayam asmākam bādhakaḥ vidhiḥ iti 
[139,v_139,vi]	avaśyam ca etat evam vijñeyam niḥsvabhāvam karma iti anyathā hi karma svabhāvataḥ ced syāt śāśvatam syāt asaṃśayam akṛtam ca bhavet karma kriyate na hi śāśvatam yadi hi karma svabhāvataḥ syāt mukta saṃśayam tat śāśvatam syāt svabhāvasya anyathā bhāva abhāvāt tatas ca akṛtam eva karma bhavet kartuḥ svatantrasya kriyayā yadīpsitatamam tat karma etat ca na yujyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt kriyate na hi śāśvatam śāśvatam hi nāma tat yat vidyamāna sattākam yat ca vidyamānam tasya karaṇa anupapatteḥ tat na eva kāraṇam apekṣate iti 
[139,vii_140,i]	śubha aśubhe karmaṇi akṛtaḥ eva sakalasya lokasya vipākaḥ yasmāt tatas ca akṛta abhyāgam abhayam syāt karma akṛtakam yadi abrahmacarya vāsaḥ ca doṣaḥ tatra prasajyate yadi hi akṛtam karma bhavet tadā akṛta abhyāgam abhayam syāt yena api hi prāṇa atipāta ādikam na kṛtam tasya api akṛtam api sat tat karma asti eva iti tena api asya saṃbandhāt akṛta abhyāgam abhayam syāt abrahmacarya vāsaḥ ca tatra pakṣe prāpnoti kim kāraṇam pariśuddha brahmacarya vāsān na kasyacid nirvāṇena bhavitavyam syāt 
[140,ii_140,iii]	kim ca atas vyavahārāḥ virudhyante sarve eva na saṃśayaḥ puṇya pāpa kṛtoḥ na eva pravibhāgaḥ ca yujyate ye hi ete kṛṣi vāṇijya gorakṣa ādayaḥ kriyā ārambhāḥ phala artham ārabhyante teṣām sarveṣām akṛtānām eva vidyamāna tvāt prārambha vaiyarthyam syāt ghaṭam kuru paṭam kuru iti evamādayaḥ ca sarve eva laukika vyavahārāḥ virudhyante ghaṭa ādīnām sarveṣām eva vidyamāna tvāt puṇya kṛt ayam pāpa kṛt ayam iti ca pravibhāgaḥ na prāpnoti ubhayoḥ api puṇya pāpa kṛtoḥ akṛtayoḥ api puṇya pāpayoḥ pratyekam vidyamāna tvāt 
[140,iv_140,v]	kim ca tad vipakva vipākam ca punar eva vipakṣyati karma vyavasthitam yasmāt tasmāt svābhāvikam yadi vipakva vipākasya api karmaṇaḥ punar vipāka dānam āpadyate sva rūpāt apracyuta tvāt avipakva vipāka avasthāyām iva tat evam yadi karma svābhāvikam iti manyase yasmāt tat karma vyavasthitam asti tasmāt niḥsaṃśayam yathā upavarṇitāḥ doṣāḥ prāpnuvanti sa svabhāva tve tasmāt niḥsvabhāvam karma yatas ca niḥsvabhāvam karma tasmāt śāśvata uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ na eva asmākam evam vyācakṣamāṇānām āpadyate iti 
[140,vi]	atra āha vidyate eva svabhāvataḥ karma tad kāraṇa sadbhāvāt iha yat na asti na tasya kāraṇam asti kūrma romakūpa prāvārasya iva asti ca karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam kleśāḥ avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ upādāna pratyayaḥ bhavaḥ iti vacanāt tasmāt vidyate eva karma svabhāvataḥ iti ucyate ayuktam eva kim kāraṇam yasmāt karma kleśa ātmakam ca idam te ca kleśāḥ na tattvataḥ na ced te tattvataḥ kleśāḥ karma syāt tattvataḥ katham 
[140,vii_140,viii]	iha idam karma kleśa ātmakam kleśa hetukam te ca kleśāḥ tattvataḥ na santi vakṣyati hi śubha aśubha viparyāsān saṃbhavanti pratītya ye te svabhāvāt na vidyante tasmāt kleśāḥ na tattvataḥ iti tat evam tāvat na tattvataḥ kleśāḥ tad hetukam karma tadānīm kutas tattvataḥ bhaviṣyati tasmāt na asti karma svabhāvataḥ 
[141,i_141,ii]	atra āha vidyante eva kleśā karmāṇi ca tad kārya sadbhāvāt iha hi kleśa karmaṇām deha ākhyam kāryam upalabhyate yasya ca kāryam upalabhyate tat asti avidyamānasya kha puṣpa ādeḥ kārya adarśanāt iti ucyate syuḥ kleśāḥ karmāṇi ca yadi tat kāryam dehāḥ vidyeran na tu vidyante iti āha karma kleśāḥ ca dehānām pratyayāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ karma kleśāḥ ca te śūnyā yadi deheṣu kā kathā yathā karma kleśāḥ ca śūnyāḥ tathā pratipāditam tatas ca karma kleśāḥ yadā na santi tadā tad kāryāṇām dehānām asattve kā kathā bhaviṣyati nāstitvam teṣām pūrvam eva siddham yasmāt tasmāt na at na kaścid vaktavya viśeṣaḥ asti iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[141,iii_141,iv]	atra āha vidyate eva svabhāvataḥ karma tad phala bhoktṛ sadbhāvāt yat na asti na tasya phala upabhoktā asti tat yathā gagana cūta phalasya iti asti ca karmaṇaḥ phala upabhoktā avidyā nivṛtaḥ jantuḥ tṛṣṇā saṃyojanaḥ ca saḥ sa bhoktā sa ca na kartuḥ anyaḥ na ca saḥ eva saḥ tatra avidyā ajñānam tamaḥ saṃmohaḥ iti paryāyāḥ avidyayā nivṛtaḥ chāditaḥ pāñcagatika saṃsāre punar punar jāyate iti jantuḥ sattvaḥ pudgalaḥ prāṇi iti tasya eva paryāyāḥ tṛṣṇā rāgaḥ saktiḥ visaktiḥ ca iti paryāyāḥ saṃyojanam bandhanam tṛṣṇā saṃyojanam asya iti tṛṣṇā saṃyojanaḥ tṛṣṇā bandhanaḥ iti arthaḥ yathā uktam sūtre avidyā nivṛtāḥ sattvāḥ tṛṣṇā saṃyojanāḥ iti atha ca punar idam pāpam karma svayam eva kṛtam asya svayam eva vipākaḥ pratyanubhavitavyaḥ iti vacanāt sa ca bhoktā karma phalasya sa ca na kartuḥ anyaḥ na ca saḥ eva saḥ tattva anyatva avācya tvāt tasmāt phala upabhoktṛ sadbhāvāt asti eva karma iti 
[141,v]	atra ucyate syāt karmaṇaḥ kartā karma phalasya ca upabhoktā yadi karma eva syāt na tu asti katham kṛtvā na pratyaya samutpannam na apratyaya samutthitam asti yasmāt idam karma tasmāt kartā api na asti atas karma ced na asti kartā ca kutas syāt karma jam phalam asatī atha phale bhoktā kutas eva bhaviṣyati 
[141,vi]	yadi karma nāma kiṃcid syāt tat pratyaya samutpannam vā bhavet apratyaya samutpannam vā yadi tāvat pratyaya samutpannam iṣyate tat na yuktam pratyaya parīkṣāyām ukta doṣa tvāt atha apratyaya janitam nirhetukam tat api hetau asati kāryam ca kāraṇam ca ityādinā karma kāraka parīkṣāyām vistareṇa pratipāditam yatas ca evam pratyaya samutpannam vā apratyaya samutpannam vā karma idam na saṃbhavati tasmāt asya karmaṇaḥ kartā api na saṃbhavati yadā ca evam karma ca kartā ca na asti tadā nirhetukam karma jam phalam kutas bhaviṣyati iti asati ca phale kutas eva phala bhoktā bhaviṣyati iti sarvam etat svabhāvataḥ asaṃvidyamānam eva iti vijñeyam 
[142,i]	atra āha yadi evam naiḥsvābhāvyam bhāvānām vyavasthāpitam bhavati yat tarhi etat uktam bhagavatā svayam kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ svayam eva vipākaḥ pratyanubhavitavyaḥ iti tat etat sarvam amunā nyāyena apākṛtam bhavati karma phala apavādāt ca pradhāna nāstikaḥ bhavān iti ucyate na vayam nāstikāḥ astitva nā astitva dvaya vāda nirāsena tu vayam nirvāṇa pura gāmi nam advaya patham vidyotayāmaḥ na ca karma kartṛ phala ādikam na asti iti brūma kim tarhi niḥsvabhāvam etat iti vyavasthāpayāmaḥ atha manyase niḥsvabhāvānām bhāvānām vyāpāra karaṇa anupapatteḥ tad avasthaḥ eva doṣaḥ iti etat api na asti sa svabhāvānām eva vyāpāra adarśanāt niḥsvabhāvānām eva vyāpāra darśanāt tathā hi niḥsvabhāvāḥ eva santaḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ loke sva kārya kṛt upalabhyante 
[142,ii_142,iii]	api ca amuṣmāt dṛṣṭāntāt spaṣṭatarāt ayam arthaḥ avasīyatām yathā nirmitakam śāstā nirmimīta ṛddhi saṃpadā nirmitaḥ nirmimīta anyam sa ca nirmitakaḥ punar tat yathā ekam nirmitakam śāstā buddhaḥ bhagavān ṛddhi saṃpadā ṛddhi prabhāveṇa nirmimīta sa ca api nirmitakaḥ punar yaḥ ayam buddhena bhagavatā nirmitaḥ sa punar bhūyas anyam aparam nirmitakam nirmimīta tatra yaḥ eṣa nirmitakaḥ aparasya nirmitakasya nirmātā sa śūnyaḥ niḥsvabhāvaḥ tathāgata svabhāva rahitaḥ iti arthaḥ yaḥ ca ayam aparaḥ nirmitakaḥ yoniḥ mitakena nirmitaḥ asau api śūnyaḥ nisvabhāvaḥ tathāgata svabhāva rahitaḥ iti arthaḥ yathā atra niḥsvabhāvānām nisvabhāva kārya kṛt tvam karma kartṛ vyapadeśaḥ ca bhavati tathā nirmitaka ākāraḥ kartā karma ca tad kṛtam tat yathā nirmitena anyaḥ nirmitaḥ nirmitaḥ tathā 
[142,iv^1]	yaḥ hi atra karmaṇaḥ kartā sa nirmitaka ākāraḥ svabhāva śūnyaḥ tena ca svabhāva śūnyena svatantra kartrā yat kiṃcid karma kriyate tat api svabhāva śūnyam tat yathā nirmitakena anyaḥ nirmitakaḥ nirmitaḥ tathā veditavyam yathoktam āgame ekasya bhāṣamāṇasya sarve bhāṣanti nirmitāḥ ekasya tūṣṇīṃbhūtasya sarve tūṣṇīṃbhavanti hi tasmāt advaya vādinām mādhyamikānām kutas mithyā darśanam uktam ca ārya samādhi rāje yada sugatu kathām kathā iti nāthaḥ vīthi gatān manujān kṛpāyamānaḥ nirmita jinu tatra nirminitva vicarati teṣu praṇīta buddha dharmān 
[142,iv^2]	 prāṇi śata sahasra tam śruṇitvā praṇidadhayiṃsu vara agra buddha jñāne kada vaya labhi jñānam eva rūpam āśaya jñātva jinaḥ asya vyākaroti raśmi śata sahasra aprameyān avasiri pāda tala ihi dharmarājā sarvi niraya śītalāḥ bhavanti dukham apanīya sukham ca vedayanti dharma daśa bala prabhāṣite atra marum anujāna viśuddha bhoti cakṣuḥ ityādi keci spṛha janenti tatra kāle paramaḥ acintya tehi labdha lābhā yehi jinu nimantritaḥ narendraḥ na ca pariyanta teṣu dakṣiṇāyāḥ ityādi vistaraḥ 
[143,i_143,iv]	tathā ārya vimala kīrti nirdeśe tad nirmita bodhisattvena gandha sugandhāyām lokadhātau samantabhadra tathā gata upabhukta śeṣam bhojanam ānītam nānā vyañjana khādya ādi saṃprayuktam pṛthak pṛthak vividha rasam eka bhojanena sarvam tad śrāvaka bodhisattva saṃgha rāja rāja amātya purohita antar pura dauvārika sārthavāha ādi janapadam saṃtarpya prīti ākāram nāma mahā samādhim lambhayāmāsa iti vinaye ca paṭhayate pāpa bhikṣuḥ apratirūpakaḥ bhagavatā bhikṣuḥ abhinirmitaḥ tad vacanena śīlavataḥ api viśuddhi pratijñā saṃvāsaḥ prajñaptaḥ iti 
[143,v_143,vi]	na ca kevalam nirmāṇa dṛṣṭāntena naiḥsvabhāvya darśanam upapadyamāna rūpam api ca amībhyaḥ dṛṣṭāntebhyaḥ sphuṭam naiḥsvabhāvyam bhāvānām pratīyatām iti pratipādayan āha kleśāḥ karmāṇi dehāḥ ca kartāraḥ ca phalāni ca gandharvanagara ākārāḥ marīci svapna saṃnibhāḥ tatra kleśāḥ rāga ādayaḥ kliśnanti sattva citta saṃtānāni iti kṛtvā karmāṇi kuśala akuśalān eñjyāni dehāḥ śarīrāṇi kartāraḥ ātmānaḥ phalāni vipāka ādhipatya niṣyanda ādīni te ete kleśa ādayaḥ arthāḥ gandharvanagara ādi vat niḥsvabhāvāḥ veditavyāḥ tasmāt mādhyamikānām eva bhāvānām svabhāva anabhyupagamāt śāśvata uccheda darśana dvaya prasaṅgaḥ na asti iti vijñeyam 
[143,vii_144,ii^1]	atra ca karma phala saṃbandha vicāre kuca udya śeṣa ākṣepa parihāraḥ madhyamaka avatārāt vistareṇa avaseyaḥ yathā uktam ārya ratna kūṭa sūtre pañca ca bhikṣu śatāni dhyāna lābhīni utthāya āsanebhyaḥ prakrāntāni imām gambhīrām dharma deśa nāmanavabudhyamānāni anavataranti anavagāhamānāni anadhimucyamānāni bhagavān āha tathā hi ete kāśyapa bhikṣavaḥ ābhimānikāḥ imām anāsravām śīla viśuddhim na avataranti na avagāhante na adhimucyante uttrasyanti saṃtrasyanti saṃtrāsam āpadyante gambhīraḥ kāśyapa gāthā abhinirhāraḥ gambhīrā ca buddhānām bhagavatām bodhiḥ sā na śakyāḥ anavaropita kuśala mūlaiḥ sattvaiḥ pāpa mitra parigṛhītaiḥ anadhi mukti bahulaiḥ adhimoktum api ca etāni kāśyapa pañca bhikṣu śatāni kāśyapasya tathāgatasya pravacane anya tīrthika śrāvakāḥ abhūvan 
[144,ii^2]	taiḥ eva tasya kāśyapasya tathāgatasya antikāt upālambha abhiprāyaiḥ eṣā dharma deśanā śrutā śrutvā ca ekacitta prasādaḥ labdhaḥ evaṃtaiḥ vāc bhāṣitā āścaryam yāvat madhurapriyamāṇī kāśyapaḥ tathāgataḥ arhan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ iti te etena eka citta prasādena pratilabdhena kālagatāḥ trāyastriṃśeṣu deveṣu upapannāḥ te tatas cyutāḥ samānāḥ iha upapannāḥ tena eva ca hetunā iha mama śāsane pravrajitāḥ tāni etāni kāśyapa pañca bhikṣu śatāni dṛṣṭi praskandhāni imām gambhīrām dharma deśanām na avataranti na avagāhante na adhimucyante uttrasyanti saṃtrasyanti saṃtrāsam āpadyante kṛtam punar eṣām anayā dharma deśanayā parikarma na bhūyas durgati vinipātam gamiṣyanti ebhiḥ eva ca skandhaiḥ parinirvāsyanti 
[144,iii^1]	atha khalu bhagavān āyuṣmantam subhūtim āmantrayate sma gaccha subhūte etān bhikṣūn saṃjña patha subhūtiḥ āha bhagavataḥ eva tāvat ete bhāṣitam vilomayanti kaḥ punar vādaḥ mama atha bhagavān tasyām velāyām yena mārgeṇa ete bhikṣāvaḥ gacchanti sma tasmin mārge drau bhikṣū nirmimīte sma atha tāni pañca bhikṣu śatāni yena mārgeṇa tau dvau bhikṣū nirmitakau tena upasaṃkrāmanti sma upasaṃkramya etat avocan kutra āyuṣmantau gamiṣyathaḥ tau avocatām gamiṣyāvaḥ āvām araṇya āyataneṣu tatra dhyāna sukha saṃsparśa vihāraiḥ vihariṣyāvaḥ tāni api pañca bhikṣu śatāni etat avocan vayam api āyuṣmantau bhagavataḥ dharma deśanām na avatarāmaḥ na avagāhāmahe na adhimucyāmahe uttrasyāmaḥ saṃtrasyāmaḥ saṃtrāsam āpadyāmahe 
[144,iii^2]	tena vayam araṇya āyataneṣu dhyāna sukha saṃsparśa vihāraiḥ vihariṣyāmaḥ iti nirmitakau avocatām tena hi āyuṣmantaḥ saṃgāsyāmaḥ na vivadiṣyāmaḥ avivāda paramaḥ hi śramaṇa dharmaḥ yat idam āyuṣmantaḥ ucyate parinirvāṇam iti katamaḥ sa dharmaḥ yaḥ parinirvāsyati kaścid punar atra kāyaḥ ātmā vā sattvaḥ vā jīvaḥ vā jantuḥ vā poṣaḥ vā puruṣaḥ vā pudgalaḥ vā manujaḥ vā mānavaḥ va yaḥ parinirvāsyati kasya vā kṣayāt parinirvāṇam te avocan rāga dveṣa moha kṣayāt parinirvāṇam nirmitakau avocatām kim punar āyuṣmatām saṃvidyante rāga dveṣa mohāḥ yān kṣayiṣyatha te avocan na te adhyātmam na bahirdhāḥ na ubhayam antareṇa upalabhyante na api te aparikalpitāḥ utpadyante 
[145,i]	atra āha yadi kleśāḥ karmāṇi ca dehāḥ ca kartāraḥ ca phalāni ca sarvam etat na tattvam kevalaṃtu gandharvanagara ādivadatta tvam eva sat tattva ākāreṇa pratibhāsate bālānām kim punar atra tattvam katham vā tattvasya avatāraḥ iti ucyate ādhyātmika bāhya aśeṣa vastu anupalambhena adhyātmam bahis ca yaḥ sarvathā ahaṃkāra mamakāra parikṣayaḥ idam atra tattvam tattva avatāraḥ punar sat kāya dṛṣṭi prabhavān aśeṣān kleśān ca doṣān ca dhiyā vipaśyan ātmānam asyāḥ viṣayam ca buddhā yogī karoti ātma niṣedham eva 
[145,ii_145,iii]	ityādinā madhyamaka avatārāt vistareṇa avaseyaḥ kāya dṛṣṭi mūlakam eva saṃsāram anupaśyan ātma anupalambhāt ca sat kāya dṛṣṭi prahāṇam tad prahāṇāt ca sarva kleśa vyāvṛttim samanupaśyan prathamataram ātmānam eva upaparīkṣate kaḥ ayam ātmā nāma iti yaḥ ahaṃkāra viṣayaḥ sa ca ayam ahaṃkārasya viṣayaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ skandha svabhāvaḥ vā bhavet skandha vyatiriktaḥ vā ādhāra ādheya tadvat pakṣāṇām api ekatva anya tva pakṣe eva antarbhāvāt saṃkṣepeṇa eva ca vivakṣita tvāt ekatva anyatva pakṣa dvaya pratiṣedhena eva ātma niṣedham ārabdhu kāmaḥ ācāryaḥ āha ātmā skandhā yadi bhavet udayavyaya bhāj bhavet skandhebhyaḥ anyaḥ yadi bhavet bhavet askandha lakṣaṇaḥ kim artha punar anyatra tathāgata parīkṣāyām agni in dhana parīkṣāyām ca pañca pañca pakṣāḥ upanyastāḥ iha tu punar pakṣa dvayam eva iti ucyate yena eva tatra prakaraṇa dvaye pañca pañca pakṣāḥ nirdiṣṭāḥ atas eva anyatra nirdiṣṭa tvāt na punar iha nirdiśyante saṃkṣepeṇa tu pakṣa dvayam upanyasyate iti 
[145,iv]	tatra yadi skandhāḥ ātmā iti parikalpyate tadā udaya vyaya bhāj utpādī ca vināśī ca ātmā prāpnoti skandhānām udaya vyaya bhāktvāt na ca evam iṣyate ātma aneka tva doṣa prasaṅgāt vakṣyati hi na api abhūtvā samutpannaḥ doṣaḥ hi atra prasajyate kṛtakaḥ vā bhavet ātmā saṃbhūtaḥ vā api ahetukaḥ iti tathā na ca upādānam eva ātmā vyeti tat samudeti ca katham hi nāma upādānam upādātā bhaviṣyati iti kim ca skandhāḥ ātmā ced atas tad bahu tvāt ātmānaḥ syuḥ te api bhūyāṃsaḥ eva dravyam ca ātmā prāpnuyāt tādṛśaḥ ca dravye vṛttau vaiparītye ca na syāt ātma ucchedaḥ nirvṛtau syāt avaśyam nāśa utpādau nirvṛteḥ prāk kṣaṇeṣu kartuḥ nāśāt tad phala abhāvaḥ eva bhuñjīta anyena arjitam karma ca anyaḥ ityādinā madhyamaka avatāre vistareṇa vihita vicārāt api pakṣaḥ boddhavyaḥ iti na iha punar vistara prapañcaḥ ārabhyate 
[146,i]	evam tāvat skandhāḥ ātmā na bhavati skandha vyatiriktaḥ api na yujyate yadi hi skandhebhyaḥ anyaḥ ātmā bhavet askandha lakṣaṇaḥ bhavet yathā hi goḥ anyaḥ aśvaḥ na go lakṣaṇe bhavati evam ātmā api skandha vyatiriktaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ askandha lakṣaṇaḥ bhavet tatra skandhāḥ saṃskṛta tvāt hetu pratyaya saṃbhūtāḥ utpāda sthiti bhaṅga lakṣaṇāḥ tatra askandha lakṣaṇaḥ ātmā bhavan bhavat matena utpāda sthiti bhaṅga lakṣaṇa ayuktaḥ syāt yaḥ ca evam bhavati saḥ avidyamāna tvāt asaṃskṛta tvāt vā kha puṣpa vat nirvāṇa badvā na eva ātma vyapadeśam pratilabhate na api ahaṃkāra viṣaya tvena yujyate iti skandha vyatiriktaḥ api ātmā na yujyate 
[146,ii]	athavā ayam anyaḥ arthaḥ yadi ātmā skandha vyatiriktaḥ syāt saḥ askandha lakṣaṇa syāt rūpaṇa anubhava nimitta udgahaṇa abhisaṃskaraṇa viṣaya prativijñapti lakṣaṇāḥ pañca skandhāḥ ātmā ca rūpāt iva vijñānam skandhebhyaḥ vyatiriktaḥ iṣyamāṇaḥ pṛthak lakṣaṇa siddhaḥ syāt pṛthak lakṣaṇa siddhaḥ ca gṛhyeta rūpāt iva cittam na ca gṛhyate tasmāt skandha vyatiriktaḥ api na asti 
[146,iii^1]	nanu ca tīrthikāḥ skandhebhyaḥ vyatiriktam ātmānam pratipannāḥ bhinna lakṣaṇam ācakṣate tasmāt teṣām abādhakaḥ eva ayam vidhiḥ iti yathā ca tīrthikāḥ ātmanaḥ bhinna lakṣaṇam ācakṣate tathā uktam madhyamaka avatāre ātmā tīrthyaiḥ kalpyate nitya rūpaḥ akartā bhoktā nirguṇaḥ niṣkriyaḥ ca kaṃcid kaṃcid vedam āśritya tasya bhedam yātā prakriyā tīrthikānām iti anena ucyate satyam bruvanti tīrthikāḥ skandha vyatiriktasya lakṣaṇam na punar te svarūpataḥ ātmānam upalabhya tasya lakṣaṇam ācakṣate kim tarhi yathāvat upādāya prajñapti anavagamena nāma mātrakam eva ātmānam trāsāt apratipadyamānāḥ saṃvṛti satyāt api paribhraṣṭāḥ mithyā kalpanayā eva kevalam anumāna ābhāsa mātra vipralabdhāḥ santaḥ mohāt parikalpayanti ātmānam tasya ca lakṣaṇam ācakṣate 
[146,iii^2]	teṣām ca karma kāraka parīkṣā ādiṣu ātma upādānayoḥ paraspara āpekṣikīm siddhim bruvatā saṃvṛtya api pratiṣedhaḥ vihitaḥ eva uktam ca yathā ādarśam upādāya sva mukha pratibimbakam dṛśyate nāma tat ca eva na kiṃcid api tattvataḥ ahaṃkāraḥ tathā skandhān upādāya upalabhyate na ca kaścid sa tattvena sva mukha pratibimba vat yathā ādarśam anādāya sva mukha pratibimbakam na dṛśyate tathā skandha ānanādāya aham iti api evaṃvidha artha śravaṇāt dharma cakṣuḥ avāptavān ārya ānandaḥ svayam ca eva bhikṣubhyaḥ abhīkṣṇam uktavān iti 
[147,i]	atas na punar tad pratipādana artham yatnaḥ ārabhyate upādāya prajñapyamānaḥ eva avidyā viparyāsa anugatānām ātma abhiniveśa āspada bhūtaḥ mumukṣubhiḥ vicāryate yasya idam skandha pañcakam upādāna tvena pratibhāsate kim asau skandha lakṣaṇaḥ uta askandha lakṣaṇaḥ iti sarvathā ca vicārayantaḥ mumukṣavaḥ na enam upalabhante bhāva svabhāvataḥ tadā eṣām ātmani asati ca ātmīyam kutas eva bhaviṣyati 
[147,ii]	ātma anupalambhāt ātma prajñapti upādānam skandha pañcakam ātmīyam iti sutarām na upalabhante yathā eva hi dagdhe rathe tad aṅgāni api dagdha tvāt na upalabhyante evam yoginaḥ yadā eva ātmanairātmyam pratipadyante tadā eva ātmīya skandha vastu nairātmyam api niyatam pratipadyante yathā uktam ratnāvalyām ahaṃkāra udbhavāḥ skandhāḥ saḥ ahaṃkāraḥ anṛtaḥ arthataḥ bījam yasya anṛtam tasya prarohaḥ satyataḥ kutas skandhān asatyān dṛṣṭvā evam ahaṃkāraḥ prahīyate ahaṃkāra prahāṇāt ca na punar skandha saṃbhavaḥ iti 
[147,iii]	yathā eva hi grīṣme madhyāhna kāla avasānam āsāditasya vidhana nabhaḥ madhya deśam āci kraṃsoḥ īṣat paribhramyamāna paṭu tara hutabhuj vitata sphuliṅgān iva virūkṣatara mahī maṇḍala uttāpana parān pradīpta kiraṇasya kiraṇān pratītya virūkṣataram avanideśam ca āsādya viparītam ca darśanam apekṣya salila ākārāḥ marīcayaḥ upalabhyamānā vidūra deśa avasthitānām janmavatām ati prasanna abhinīla jala ākāram pratyayam ādadhati na tu tad samīpa gatānām evam iha api yathā avasthita ātma ātmīya padārtha tattva darśana vidūra deśa antara sthitānām saṃsāra adhvani vartamānānām avidyā viparyāsa anugamāt mṛṣā arthaḥ eva skandha samāropaḥ satyataḥ pratibhāsamānaḥ padārtha tattva darśana samīpa sthānām na pratibhāsate yathā uktam ācārya pādaiḥ dūrāt ālokitam rūpam āsannaiḥ dṛśyate sphuṭam marīciḥ yadi vāri syāt āsannaiḥ kim na gṛhyate dūrībhūtaiḥ yathābhūtaḥ lokaḥ ayam dṛśyate yathā na dṛśyate tad āsannaiḥ ānimittaḥ marīci vat marīciḥ toya sadṛśī yathā na ambhona ca arthataḥ skandhāḥ tathā ātma sadṛśāḥ na ātmānaḥ na api te arthataḥ iti 
[148,i_148,ii]	atas eva ca ātmā ātmīya anupalambhāt parama artha darśana samīpa sthaḥ yogī niyatam bhavati nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ śamāt ātmā ātmanīnayoḥ ātmani hitam ātmanīnam skandha pañcakam ātmīyam iti arthaḥ ātmanaḥ ahaṃkāra viṣayasya ātmanīnasya ca skandha ādeḥ vastunaḥ mamakāra viṣayasya śamāt anutpādāt anupalambhāt nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ ca jāyate yogī 
[148,iii_148,iv]	nanu ca yaḥ asau evam nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ ca yogī bhavati sa tāvat asti sati ca tasmin siddhaḥ ātmā skandhāḥ ca iti na etat evam yasmāt nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ yaḥ ca saḥ api na vidyate nirmamam nirahaṃkāram yaḥ paśyati na paśyati ātmani skandheṣu ca sarvathā anupalabhyamāna svarūpeṣu kutas ta dvayatiriktaḥ apara padārthaḥ bhaviṣyati yaḥ asau nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ ca iti yaḥ tu evam asaṃvidyamāna svarūpam nirmamam nirahaṃkāram ca paśyati sa tattvam na paśyati iti vijñeyam yathā uktam bhagavatā śūnyam ādhyātmikam paśya paśya śūnyam bahis gatam na vidyate saḥ api kaścid yaḥ bhāvayati śūnyatām 
[148,v_149,i]	tathā yaḥ api ca cintayi śūnyaka dharmān saḥ api kumārga papannaku bālaḥ akṣara kīrtita śūnyaka dharmāḥ te ca anakṣara akṣaraḥ uktāḥ śānta paśānta yaḥ cintayi dharmān saḥ api ca cittu na jātu na bhūtaḥ citta vitarkiṇa sarvi papañcāḥ tasya acintiya budhyatha dharmān iti tathā skandha sabhāvatu śūnya vivikta bodhi sabhāvatu śūnya vivikta yaḥ api caret sa pi śūnya sa bhāvaḥ jñānavataḥ na tu bāla janasya iti 
[149,ii_149,iii]	tat evam mama iti aham iti kṣīṇe bahis dhā adhyātmam eva ca nirudhyate upādānam tad kṣayāt janmanaḥ kṣayaḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭi mūlakāḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭi samudayāḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭi hetukāḥ sarva kleśāḥ sūtre uktāḥ sā ca sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ ātma ātmīya anupalambhāt prahīyate tad prahāṇāt ca kāma dṛṣṭi śīla vrata ātma vāda upādāna catuṣṭayam prahīyate upādāna kṣayāt ca janmanaḥ punarbhava lakṣaṇasya kṣayaḥ bhavati 
[149,iv_149,v]	yatas ca ayam janma nivṛtti kramaḥ evam vyavasthāpitaḥ tasmāt karma kleśa kṣayāt mokṣaḥ iti sthitam upādāne hi kṣīṇe tad pratyayaḥ bhavaḥ na bhavati bhave niruddhe kutas jāti jarā maraṇa ādikasya saṃbhavaḥ iti evam karma kleśa kṣayāt mokṣaḥ bhavati iti sthitam karma kleśānām tarhi kasya kṣayāt parikṣayaḥ iti vaktavyam ucyate karma kleśāḥ vikalpataḥ te prapañcāt prapañcaḥ tu śūnyatāyām nirudhyate 
[149,vi_149,vii]	ayoniśaḥ hi rūpa ādikam vikalpayataḥ bāla pṛthagjanasya kleśaḥ upajāyate rāga ādikaḥ vakṣyati hi saṃkalpa prabhavaḥ rāgaḥ dveṣaḥ mohaḥ ca kathyate śubha aśubha viparyāsān saṃbhavanti pratītya hi uktam ca sūtre kāma jānāmi te mūlam saṃkalpāt kila jāyase na tvām saṃkalpayiṣyāmi tatas me na bhaviṣyasi iti 
[150,i^1]	evam tāvat karma kleśāḥ vikalpataḥ pravartante te ca vikalpāḥ anādimat saṃsāra abhyastād jñāna jñeya vācya vācaka kartṛ karma karaṇa kriyā ghaṭa paṭa mukuṭa ratha rūpa vedanā strī puruṣa lābha alābha sukha duḥkha yaśaḥ ayaśaḥ nindā praśaṃsā ādi lakṣaṇāt vicitrāt prapañcāt upajāyate sa ca ayam laukikaḥ prapañcaḥ niravaśeṣa śūnyatāyām sarva svabhāva śūnyatā darśane sati nirudhyate katham kṛtvā yasmāt sati hi vastunam upalambhe syāt yathā udita prapañca jālam na hi anupalabhya vandhyā duhitaram rūpa lāvaṇya yauvanavatīm tad viṣayam prapañcam avatārayanti rāgiṇaḥ na ca anavatārya prapañcam tat viṣayam ayoniśaḥ vikalpam avatārayanti na ca anavatārya kalpanā jālam ahaṃmama iti abhiniveśāt sat kāya dṛṣṭi mūlakān kleśa gaṇān utpādayanti na ca anutpādya sat kāya dṛṣṭayā ātmakān kleśa gaṇān karmāṇi śubha aśubhāniñjyāni kurvanti na ca akurvāṇāḥ karmāṇi jāti jarā maraṇa śoka parideva duḥkha daurmanasya aupāyāsa ādi rūpam ekajālībhūtam saṃsāra kāntāram anubhavanti 
[150,i^2]	evam yoginaḥ api śūnyatā darśana avasthā niravaśeṣa skandha dhātu āyatanāni svarūpataḥ na upalabhante na ca anupalabhamānāḥ vastu svarūpam tat viṣayam prapañcam avatārayanti na ca anavatārya tad viṣayam prapañcam vikalpam avatārayanti na ca anavatārya vikalpam ahaṃmama iti abhiniveśāt sat kāya dṛṣṭi mūlakam kleśa gaṇam utpādayanti na ca anutpādya satkāya dṛṣṭayā ādikam kleśa gaṇam karmāṇi kurvanti na ca akurvāṇāḥ jāti jarā maraṇa ākhyam saṃsāram anubhavanti tat evam aśeṣa prapañca upaśama śiva lakṣaṇām śūnyatām āgamya yasmāt aśeṣa kalpanā jāla prapañca vigamaḥ bhavati prapañca vigamāt ca vikalpa nivṛtiḥ vikalpa nivṛttyā ca aśeṣa karma kleśa nivṛtti karma kleśa nivṛttyā ca janma nivṛttiḥ tasmāt śūnyatā eva sarva prapañca nivṛtti lakṣaṇa tvāt nirvāṇam iti ucyate yathoktam śatake dharmam samāsatas ahiṃsām varṇayanti tathāgatāḥ śūnyatām eva nirvāṇam kevalam tat iha ubhayam iti 
[150,ii]	ācārya bhāva vivekaḥ tu śrāvaka pratyekabuddhānām yathā udita śūnyatā adhigamam apratipadyamānaḥ evam varṇayati apara utpanna pratikṣaṇa vinaśvara saṃskāra kalāpa mātram anātmā anātmīyam avalokayataḥ ārya śrāvakasya api ātma ātmīya vastu abhāvāt dharma mātram idam jāyate mriyate ca iti darśanam utpadyate ahaṃkāra viṣayaḥ hi ātmā tad abhāvāt tasya api abhāvaḥ tad abhāvāt eva na kvacid ādhyātmikam bāhyam vā vastu asti iti mamakārān utpatteḥ nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ aham iti na svarūpa viniścitiḥ upajāyate anyatra vyavahāra saṃketāt prāk eva ajāta sarva saṃskāra darśinām nirvikalpa prajñācāra vihāriṇām mahā bodhisattvānām iti atas āha nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ yaḥ ca saḥ api na vidyate iti 
[151,i_151,iii]	tat ayam ācāryaḥ yathā evaṃvidhe viṣaye na ācārya pāda mata anuvartī tathā pratipāditam madhyamaka avatāre dūraṃgamāyām tu dhiyā adhikaḥ iti atra iti na punar tad dūṣaṇe yatnaḥ āsthīyate atas eva uktam bhagavatā ārya aṣṭa sāhasrikāyām bhagavatyām śrāvaka bodhim abhisaṃboddhu krāmena subhūte asyām eva prajñāpāramitāyām śikṣitavyam pratyeka bodhim abhisaṃboddhu kāmena subhūte asyām eva prajñāpāramitāyām śikṣitavyam anuttarām samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃboddhu kāmena subhūte bodhisattvena mahāsattvena asyām eva prajñāpāramitāyām śikṣitavyam ityādi āha ca yaḥ icchatī sugata śrāvaku ham bhaveyam pratyekabuddhu bhavijā tatha dharmarājaḥ imu kṣānti na āgatya na śakyati pāpuṇotum yathaḥ āra pāra gamanīyam atīradarśī iti 
[151,iv_151,v]	atra āha yadi evam ādhyātmika bāhya vastu anupalambhāt adhyātmam bahis ca ahaṃmameti kalpanā jālānām anutpādaḥ tattvam iti vyavasthāpitam yat tarhi etat uktam bhagavatā ātmā hi ātmanaḥ nāthaḥ kaḥ nu nāthaḥ paraḥ bhavet ātmanā hi su dāntena svargam prāpnoti paṇḍitaḥ ātmā hi ātmanaḥ nāthaḥ kaḥ nu nāthaḥ paraḥ bhavet ātmā hi ātmanaḥ sākṣī kṛtasya apakṛtasya ca tathā ārya samādhi rāje kṛṣṇa śubham ca na naśyati karma ātmana kṛtva ca vedayitavyam no pi ca saṃkrama karma phalasya no ca ahetuka pratyanubhoti iti vistaraḥ tat katham na virudhyate iti ucyate idam api kim na uktam bhagavatā na asti iha sattvaḥ ātmā vā dharmāḥ tu ete sa hetukāḥ iti 
[151,vi]	tathā hi rūpam na ātmā rūpavān na api ca ātmā rūpe na ātmā na ātmani rūpam evam yāvat vijñānam na ātmā vijñānavān na ātmā vijñāne na ātmā na ātmani vijñānam iti tathā anātmānaḥ sarva dharmāḥ iti tat katham idānīm anena āgamena pūrvakasya āgamasya virodhaḥ na syāt tasmāt deśanābhiprāyaḥ bhagavataḥ anveṣyaḥ sāmānyena tu bhagavadbhiḥ buddhaiḥ pravacane neya nīta artha vistara prabhede aśeṣa jagat vineya buddhi padma ākara vibodhana paraiḥ āditya kalpa eḥ anastaṃgataiḥ mahā karuṇa upāya vijñāna gabhasti vistaraiḥ ātmā iti api prajñapitam anātmā iti api deśitam buddhaiḥ na ātmā na ca anātmā kaścid iti api deśitam 
[152,i^1]	atra ca ayam abhiprāyaḥ iha ye ātmā abhāva viparyāsa kudarśana dhana timira paṭala avacchādita aśeṣa buddhi nayana tayā laukika avadāta darśana viṣayān atikrāntam api bhāva jātam apaśyantaḥ vyavahāra satya avasthitāḥ eva santaḥ kṣiti salila jvalana pavana abhidhāna tattva mātra anuvarṇana parā mūlaudana udaka kiṇva ādi dravya viśeṣa paripāka mātra pratyaya utpanna mada murcchā ādi sāmarthya viśeṣa anugata madya pāna upalambha vat kalala ādi mahābhūta paripāka mātra saṃbhūtāḥ eva buddhīḥ anuvarṇayantaḥ pūrva anta aparānta apavāda pravṛttāḥ santaḥ para lokam ātmānam ca apavat ante na asti ayam lokaḥ na asti para lokaḥ na asti sukṛta duṣkṛtānām karmaṇām phala vipākaḥ na asti sattvaḥ upapādukaḥ ityādinā tad apavādāt ca svarga apavarga viśiṣṭa iṣṭa phala viśeṣa ākṣepa parāṅmukhāḥ satata samitam akuśala karma abhisaṃskaraṇa pravṛttāḥ naraka ādi mahā prapāta patana abhimukhāḥ 
[152,i^2]	teṣām tat asadṛṣṭi nivṛtti artha caturaśīti citta carita sahasra bheda bhinnasya sattva dhātoḥ yathā āśaya anuvartakaiḥ aśeṣa sattva dhātu uttāraṇa ākṣipta pratijñā saṃpādana tatparaiḥ prajñā upāya mahā karuṇā saṃbhāra puraḥ s araiḥ nirupamaiḥ eka jagat bandhubhiḥ niravaśeṣa kleśa mahā vyādhi cikitsakaiḥ mahā vaidya rāja bhūtaiḥ hīna madhya utkṛṣṭa vineya jana anujidhṛkṣayā hīrnānām vineyānām akuśala karma kāriṇām akuśala ādi nivartayitum buddhaiḥ bhagavadbhiḥ kvacid ātmā iti api prajñapitam loke vyavasthāpitam ahetuvāda pratiṣedha upapattiḥ ca karma kāraka parīkṣātaḥ na api ahetutaḥ iti atas madhyamaka avatārāt ca vistareṇa veditavyā iti tad pratiṣedha artha na iha punar yatnaḥ āsthīyate 
[152,ii]	ye tu sat bhūta ātma dṛṣṭi kaṭhina ati dīrgha śithila mahā sūtra baddhāḥ vihaṃgamāḥ iva su dūram api gatāḥ kuśala karma kāriṇaḥ akuśala karma patha vyāvṛttāḥ api na śaknuvanti traidhātuka bhava upapattim ativāhya śivam ajaram amaraṇam nirvāṇa puram abhigantum teṣām madhyānām vineyānām sat kāya darśana abhiniveśa śithilīkaraṇāya nirvāṇa abhilāṣa saṃjanana artham buddhaiḥ bhagavadbhiḥ vineya jana anugraha cikīrṣubhiḥ anātmā iti api deśitam 
[152,iii_152,iv]	ye tu pūrva abhyāsa viśeṣa anugata gambhīra dharma adhimokṣa labdha bīja paripākāḥ pratyāsanna vartini nirvāṇe teṣām utkṛṣṭānām vineyānām vigata ātma snehānām parama gambhīramauni indra pravacana artha tattva avagāhana samarthānām adhimukti viśeṣam avadhārya buddhaiḥ ātmā na ca anātmā kaścid iti api deśitam yathā eva hi ātma darśanam atattvam evam tad pratipakṣa bhūtam api anātma darśanam na eva tattvam iti evam na asti ātmā kaścid na ca api anātmā kaścid asti iti deśitam yathā uktam ārya ratna kūṭe 
[153,i_153,ii]	ātmā iti kāśyapa ayam ekaḥ antar nairātmyam iti ayam dvitīyaḥ antar yat etat anayoḥ antayoḥ madhyam tad arūpyam anidarśanam apratiṣṭham anābhā sam avijñaptikam aniketam iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā pratipada dharmāṇām bhūta pratyavekṣā iti uktam ca ārya ratna āvalyām na evam ātmā na ca anātmā yathābhūtena labhyate ātmānātma kṛte dṛṣṭī vavāra asmān mahā muniḥ dṛṣṭa śruta ādyam muninā na satyam na mṛṣā uditam pakṣāt hi pratipakṣaḥ syāt ubhayam tat ca na arthataḥ iti 
[153,iii]	yatas ca evam hīna madhya utkṛṣṭa vineya jana āśaya nānātvena ātmā anātma tad ubhaya pratiṣedhena buddhānām bhagavatām dharma deśanā pravṛttā tasmāt na asti āgama bādhaḥ mādhyamikānām atas eva uktam ārya deva pādaiḥ vāraṇam prāk apuṇyasya madhye vāraṇam ātmanaḥ sarvasya vāraṇam paścāt yaḥ jānīte sa buddhimān iti 
[153,iv]	tathā ācārya pādaiḥ uktam yathā eva vaiyākaraṇaḥ mātṛkām api pāṭhayet buddhaḥ avadat tathā dharma vineyānām yathākṣamam keṣāṃcid avadat dharmam pāpebhyaḥ vinivṛttaye keṣāṃcid puṇya siddhayartham keṣāṃcid dvaya niścitam dvayāniśritam ekeṣām gambhīram bhīru bhīṣaṇam śūnyatā karuṇā garbham keṣāṃcid bodhi sādhanam iti 
[153,v_153,vi]	athavā ayam anyaḥ arthaḥ ātmā iti api prajñapitam sāṃkhya ādibhiḥ pratikṣaṇa vinaśvarāṇām saṃskārāṇām karma phala saṃbandha abhāvam utprekṣya anātmā iti api prajñapitam lokāyatikaiḥ upapattyā ātmānam saṃsartāram apaśyadbhiḥ etāvān eva puruṣaḥ yāvān indriya gocaraḥ bhadre vṛka padam hi etat yat vadanti bahu śrutāḥ ityādinā taimirika upalabdha keśa maśaka ādiṣu iva vitaimirikaiḥ iva bāla jana parikalpita ātmānātma ādi vastu svarūpam sarvathā eva apaśyadbhiḥ buddhaiḥ na ātmā na ca anātmā kaścid iti api deśitam yathā uktam ārya tathāgata guhya sūtre 
[153,vii^1]	atha khalu śānta matiḥ bodhisattvaḥ bhagavantam etat avocat upaśamaḥ upaśamaḥ iti bhagavan ucyate kaḥ eṣaḥ upaśamaḥ nāma kasya ca upaśamāt upaśamaḥ iti ucyate bhagavān āha upaśamaḥ iti kula putraḥ ucyate kleśa upaśamasya etat adhivacanam kleśa upaśamaḥ iti saṃkalpa vikalpa parikalpa upaśamasya etat adhivacanam saṃkalpa vikalpa parikalpa upaśamaḥ iti saṃjñā manasikāra upaśamasya etat adhivacanam saṃjñā manasikāra upaśamaḥ iti viparyāsa upaśamasya etat adhivacanam viparyāsa upaśamaḥ iti hetu ārambaṇa upaśamasya etat adhivacanam hetu ārambaṇa upaśamaḥ iti avidyā bhava tṛṣṇā upaśamasya etat adhivacanam avidyā bhava tṛṣṇā upaśamaḥ iti ahaṃkāram amakāra upaśamasya etat adhivacanam 
[153,vii^2]	ahaṃkāram amakāra upaśamaḥ iti uccheda śāśvata dṛṣṭayupaśamasya etat adhivacanam uccheda śāśvata dṛṣṭayupaśamaḥ iti satkāya dṛṣṭayupaśamasya etat adhivacanam iti śānta mate ye kecid ārambaṇa hetu dṛṣṭi saṃyuktāḥ saṃkleśāḥ pravartante sarve te satkāya dṛṣṭeḥ utpadyante satkāya dṛṣṭayupaśamāt sarva dṛṣṭayupaśamaḥ iti sarva dṛṣṭayupaśamāt sarva praṇidhāna upaśamaḥ iti sarva prāṇi dhāna upaśamāt sarva kleśa upaśamaḥ tat yathā api nāma śānta mate vṛkṣasya mūle chinne sarva śākhā patra phalāni śuṣyanti evam eva śānta mate sat kāya dṛṣṭayupaśamāt sarva kleśāḥ upaśāmyante sat kāya dṛṣṭau śānta mate aparijñātāyām sarva upādāna upakleśāḥ utpadyante sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñātaḥ api sarva upādāna upakleśāḥ na utpadyante na bādhante 
[154,i]	śānta matiḥ āha kā punar bhagavan sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā bhagavān āha ātma asamutthānam śānta mate sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā sattva asamutthānam jivāsam utthānam pudgala asamutthānam dṛṣṭayasam utthānam sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā na khalu punar śānta mate sā dṛṣṭiḥ adhyātmam pratiṣṭhitā na bahirdhā pratiṣṭhitā sā dṛṣṭiḥ sarvatas apratiṣṭhitā yat tasyāḥ apratiṣṭhitāyāḥ dṛṣṭeḥ apratiṣṭhitā iti jñānam iyam śānta mate sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā iti śānta mate śunyatāyāḥ etat adhivacanam yat śūnyatā anulomikyā kṣāntyā tām dṛṣṭi na udgṛhṇāti iyam api śānta mate sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā satkāyaḥ iti śānta mate śūnyatā nimitta apraṇihita anabhisaṃskāra ajāta anutpāda dṛṣṭayā tām dṛṣṭim na udgṛhṇāti iyam api śānta mate sat kāya dṛṣṭi parijñā satkāyaḥ iti śānta mate akāyaḥ eṣaḥ na kasati na vikasati na cinoti na upacinoti āditas eva tat abhūtam parikalpitam yat ca abhūtam parikalpitam tat na parikalpitam na parikalpyate na vikalpyate tat na kriyate na viṭhapyate na utthāpyate na adhyavasyate tat ucyate upaśamaḥ iti 
[154,ii_154,iii]	śānta matiḥ āha upaśāntaḥ upaśāntaḥ iti bhagavan ucyate kasya upaśamāt upaśāntaḥ iti ucyate bhagavān āha ārambaṇataḥ śānta mate cittam jvalati yat na bhūyas ālambanīkaroti tat na jvalati ajvalan upaśāntaḥ iti ucyate tat yathā api nāma śānta mate agniḥ upādānataḥ jvalati anupādānataḥ śāmyati evam eva ālambanataḥ cittam jvalati anālambanataḥ śāmyati tatra śānta mate upāya kuśalaḥ ayam bodhisattvaḥ prajñāpāramitā pariśuddhaḥ ālambana sama tām ca prajānāti kuśala mūla ālambanam ca śamayati ityādi atra āha yadi buddhaiḥ bhagavadbhiḥ na ātmā iti deśitam na anā ātmā iti kim tarhi deśitam iti ucyate nivṛttam abhidhātavyam nivṛtte citta gocare anutpanna aniruddhā hi nirvāṇam iva dharma tā 
[155,i]	iha yadi kiṃcid abhidhātavyam vastu syāt tat deśyeta yadā tu abhidhātavyam nivṛttam vācām viṣayaḥ na asti tadā kiṃcid api na eva deśyate buddhaiḥ kasmāt punar abhidhātavyam na asti iti āha nivṛtte citta gocare iti cittasya gocaraḥ citta gocaraḥ gocaraḥ viṣayaḥ ārambaṇam iti arthaḥ yadi cittasya kaścid gocaraḥ syāt tatra kiṃcid nimittam adhyāropya syāt vācām pravṛttiḥ yadā tu cittasya viṣayaḥ eva anupapannaḥ tadā kva nimitta adhi āropaḥ yena vācām pravṛttiḥ syāt kasmāt punar citta viṣayaḥ na asti iti pratipādayan āha anutpanna aniruddhā hi nirvāṇam iva dharma tā 
[155,ii]	yasmāt anutpanna aniruddhā nirvāṇam iva dharmatā dharma svabhāvaḥ dharma prakṛtiḥ vyavasthāpitā tasmāt na tatra cittam pravartate cittasya apravṛttau ca kutas nimitta adhyāropaḥ tad abhāvāt kutas vācām pravṛttiḥ atas ca na kiṃcid buddhaiḥ bhagavadbhiḥ deśitam iti sthitam avikalam atas eva ca vakṣyati sarva upalambha upaśamaḥ prapañca upaśamaḥ śivaḥ na kvacid kasyacid kaścid dharmaḥ buddhena deśitaḥ iti 
[155,iii_155,vi]	evam ca etat athavā ayam anyaḥ pūrva pakṣaḥ yat uktam prapañcaḥ śūnyatāyām nirudhyate iti katham punar prapañcasya śūnyatāyām nirodhaḥ iti ucyate yasmāt nivṛttam abhidhātavyam ityādi pūrvavat vyākhyeyam athavā yat etat uktam prāc ādhyātmika bāhya vastu anupalambhena adhyātmam bahis ca yaḥ sarvadā ahaṃkāra mamakāra parikṣayaḥ idam atra tattvam iti kīdṛśam tat kiṃvat vaktum vā śakyate tasmāt nivṛttam abhidhātavyam nivṛtte citta gocare tatra tattvataḥ iti vākya śeṣaḥ kim punar kāraṇam tatra tattve nivṛttam abhidhātavyam nivṛtte citta gocare iti āha anutpanna aniruddhā hi nirvāṇam iva dharma tā iti pūrvakam eva vyākhyānam yojyam atas eva uktam ārya tathā gata guhya sūtre 
[155,vii]	yām ca śānta mate rātrim tathāgataḥ anuttarām samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbuddhaḥ yām ca rātrim anupādāya parinirvāsyati asmin antare tathāgatena eka akṣaram api na udāhṛtam na pravyāhṛtam na pravyāhariṣyati katham tarhi bhagavatā sakala sura asura nara kiṃnara siddha vidyādhara uraga prabhṛti vineya janebhyaḥ vividha prakārebhyaḥ dharma deśanā deśitā eka kṣaṇa vāc udāhāreṇa eva tad tad jana manaḥ ta maḥ haraṇī bahuvidha buddhi nalinī vana vibodhinī jarā maraṇa sarit sāgara ucchoṣiṇī kalpa kāla anala sapta arka raśmi visara hrepiṇī śarad aruṇa mahā prabhā iti 
[155,viii]	tat evam sūtre yathā yantra kṛtam tūryam vādyate pavana īritam na ca atra vādakaḥ kaścid niścaranti atha ca svarāḥ evam pūrva su śuddha tvāt sarva sattva āśaya īritā vā agniḥ carati buddhasya na ca asya asti iha kalpanā pratiśrutka ādayaḥ śabdāḥ na adhyātmam na bahis sthitāḥ vāc api evam narendrasya na adhyātmam na bahis sthitāḥ iti 
[156,i]	tathā devata codani dundubhi divya karma vipāka nivṛtta marūṇam deva pamatta vihāriṇa ñātvā dundubhi ghoṣa pamuñci nabhātaḥ sarve anitya aśāśvata kāmāḥ itvaraḥ adhruva phenasa bhāvāḥ māya marīci samāḥ daka candrāḥ sarvi bhavāḥ su pina anta sa bhāvāḥ dundubhi vādita śakramarudbhiḥ sārddhaya saṃkrami dharma sabhāyām dharma kathām pakaroti marūṇām yā katha śānta virāga nukūlā 
[156,ii_156,iii]	tathā ārya samādhi rāje buddhaḥ yadā bheṣyati dharmarājaḥ sarvāṇa dharmāṇa pakāśakaḥ muniḥ tṛṇa gulma vṛkṣa oṣadhi śaila parvata abhāva dharmāṇa ravaḥ bhaviṣyati yāvanti śabdāḥ tahi lokadhātau sarve hi abhāvāḥ na hi kaści bhāvaḥ tāvantu khaḥ tasya tathāgatasya svaru niścarī loka vināyakasya iti vistaraḥ tathā eka svarā tu tava loka hitaḥ nānā adhimukti svaru niścarati ekaikamanvimama bhāṣi jinaḥ brūhi smitam prakṛtakasya kṛte iti 
[156,iv^1]	atra eke paricodayanti nāstikā viśiṣṭāḥ mādhyamikāḥ yasmāt kuśala akuśalam karma kartāram ca phalam ca sarvam ca lokam bhāva svabhāva śūnyam iti bruvate nāstikāḥ api hi etat na asti iti bruvate tasmāt nāstikā viśiṣṭā mādhyamikāḥ iti na evam kutas pratītyasamutpāda vādinaḥ hi mādhyamikāḥ hetu pratyayān prāpya pratītya samutpanna tvāt sarvam eva ihaloka para lokam niḥsvabhāvam varṇayanti yathā svarūpa vādinaḥ na eva nāstikāḥ pratītya samutpanna tvāt bhāva svabhāva śunyatvena na para loka ādi abhāvam pratipannāḥ kim tarhi aihalaukikam vastu jātam upalabhya svabhāvataḥ tasya para lokāt iha āgamanam ihalokāt ca para loka gamana paśyantuḥ ihaloka upalabdha padārtha sadṛśa padārtha antara apavādam kurvanti tathā api vastu svarūpeṇa avidyamānasya eva te nāstitvam pratipannāḥ iti amunā tāvat darśanena sāmyam asti iti ced na hi kutas saṃvṛtyā mādhyamikaiḥ astitvena abhyupagamāt na tulya tā
