[156,iv^2]	vastutas tulya tā iti ced yadi api vastutas asiddhiḥ tulyā tathā api pratipatṛ bhedāt atulya tā yathā hi kṛta caurya puruṣam ekaḥ samyak aparijñāya eva tad amitra preritaḥ tam mithyā vyācaṣṭe cauryam anena kṛtam iti aparaḥ tu sākṣāt dṛṣṭvā dūṣayati tatra yadi api vastutas na asti bhedaḥ tathā api parijñātṛ bhedāt ekaḥ tatra mṛṣāvādī iti ucyate aparaḥ tu satya vādī iti ekaḥ ca ayaśasā ca apuṇyena ca samyak parīkṣyamāṇaḥ yujyate na aparaḥ evam iha api yathāvat vidita vastu svarūpāṇām mādhyamikānām bruvatām avagacchatām ca vastu svarūpa abhede api yathāvat avidita vastu svarūpaiḥ nāstikaiḥ saha jñāna abhidhānayoḥ na asti sāmyam yathā eva hi upekṣā sāmānye api apratisaṃkhyāya pratisaṃkhyāya upekṣakayoḥ iva pṛthagjana arhatoḥ jāti andha cakṣuṣmatoḥ ca viṣama prapāta pradeśa viniścita sāmānye api yathā asti mahān viśeṣaḥ tathā nāstikānām mādhyamikānām ca viśeṣaḥ bhaviṣyati iti pūrva ācāryāḥ iti alam prasaṅgenaḥ prakṛtam eva vyākhyāsyāmaḥ 
[157,i_157,ii]	atra āha yadi api evam anutpanna aniruddhā hi nirvāṇam iva dharma tā tasyām ca na asti vāc cittayoḥ pravṛttiḥ tathā api na eva asau adeśyamānā śakyā janaiḥ vijñātum iti avaśyam tasyām avatāraṇa artham vineya janānām saṃvṛti satya apekṣayā kadācid deśana ānupūrvyā bhavitavyam iti atas sā kathyatām iti ucyate iyam atra buddhānām bhagavatām tattva amṛta avatāra deśana ānupūrvī vijñeyā yat uta sarvam tathyam na vā tathyam tathyam ca atathyam eva ca na eva atathyam na eva tathyam etat buddha anuśāsanam 
[157,iii_157,vii]	tatra yat yat yasya priyam pūrvam tat tat tasya samācaret na hi pratihataḥ pātram saddharmasya kathaṃcana iti tathā ca bhagavatā uktam lokaḥ mayā sārdham vivadati na aham lokena sārdham vivadāmi yat loke asti saṃmatam tat mama api asti saṃmatam yat loke na asti saṃmatam mama api tat na asti saṃmatam iti āgamāt ca na anyayā bhāṣayā mlecchaḥ śakyaḥ grāhayitum yathā na laukika m ṛte lokaḥ śakyaḥ grāhayitum tathā 
[158,i]	iti āditas eva tāvat bhagavatā sva prasiddha padārtha meda sva rūpa vibhāga śravaṇa saṃjāta abhilāṣasya vineya janasya yat etat skandha dhātu āyatana ādikam avidyā taimirikaiḥ satyataḥ parikalpitam upalabdham tat eva tāvat satyam iti upavarṇitam bhagavatā tad darśana apekṣayā ātmani lokasya gaurava utpādana artham vidita niravaśeṣa loka vṛttāntaḥ ayam bhagavān sarvajñaḥ sarva darśī yaḥ evam bhava agra paryantasya vāyu maṇḍala ādeḥ ākāśa dhātu paryavasānasya bhājana lokasya sattva lokasya ca aviparītam sthiti utpāda pralaya ādikam sa ati vicitra prabhedam sa hetukam saphalam sa āsvādam sādīnavam ca upadiṣṭavān iti tat evam bhagavati utpanna sarvajña buddhi vineya janasya uttara kālam tat eva sarvam na vā tathyam iti upadeśitam tatra tathyam nāma yasya anyathātvam na asti vidyate ca pratikṣaṇa vināśi tvāt saṃskārāṇām anyathā bhāvaḥ tasmāt anyathā bhāva sadbhāvāt na vā tathyam vā śabdaḥ cakāra arthaḥ deśanā samuccaye draṣṭavyaḥ sarvam tathyam na ca tathyam iti 
[158,ii_158,iii]	keṣāṃcid sarvam etat tathyam ca atathyam ca iti deśitam tatra bāla jana apekṣayā sarvam etat tathyam ārya jñāna apekṣayā tu sarvam etat mṛṣā taiḥ evam anupalambhāt iti keṣāṃcid tu ati cira abhyasta tattva darśanānām kiṃcid mātrā nutkhāta āvaraṇa tarū mūlānām na eva atathyam na eva tathyaṃtat iti deśitam tasya api kiṃcid mātrasya āvaraṇasya prahāṇa artham vandhyā sutasya avadāta śyāma tā pratiṣedha vat ubhayam etat pratiṣiddham 
[158,iv_158,v]	etat ca buddhānām bhagavatām anuśāsanam unmārgāt apanīya samyak mārga pratiṣṭhāpanam śāsanam evam ānupūrvyā śāsanam anuśāsanam vineya jana nu rūpyeṇa vā śāsanam anuśāsanam sarvāḥ ca etāḥ deśanā buddhānām bhagavatām mahā karuṇa upāya jñānavatām tattva amṛta avatāra upāya tvena vyavasthitāḥ na hi tathāgatāḥ tattva amṛta avatārān upāya bhūta vākyam udāharanti vyādhi anurūpa bhaiṣajya upasaṃhāra vat te vineya jana anujighṛkṣayā yathā anurūpam dharmam deśayanti yathā uktam śatake sat asat sat asat ca iti na ubhayam ca iti kathyate nanu vyādhivaśāt pathyam auṣadham nāma jāyate iti 
[158,vi_158,vii]	kiṃlakṣaṇam punar tat tattvam yasya etāḥ deśanāḥ avatāra artham upadiśante bhagavantaḥ uktam etat asmābhiḥ nivṛttam abhidhātavyam nivṛtte citta gocare iti yadā ca etat evam tadā kim aparam pṛcchayate yadi api evam tathā api vyavahāra satya anurodhena laukika tathya ādi abhyupagama vat tasya api samāropataḥ lakṣaṇam ucyatām iti tat ucyate apara pratyayam śāntam prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam nirvikalpa manāna artham etat tattvasya lakṣaṇam 
[159,i]	tatra na asmin para pratyayaḥ asti iti apara pratyayam para upadeśa agamyam svayam eva adhigantavyam iti arthaḥ yathā hi taimirikāḥ vitatham keśa maśaka makṣikā ādi rūpam paśyantaḥ vitimira upadeśena api na śaknuvanti keśānām yathāvat avasthitam sva rūpam adarśana nyāyena adhigantavyam ataimirikāḥ iva adhigantum kim tarhi ataimirikā upadeśāt mithyā etat iti etāvat mātrakam eva pratipadyante yadā tu timira upaghāti aviparīta śūnyatā darśana añjanān jita buddhi nayanāḥ santaḥ samutpanna tattva jñānāḥ bhavanti tadā tat tattvam anadhigamana yogena svayam adhigacchanti iti evam apara pratyayam bhāvānām yat sva rūpam tat tattvam etat ca śānta svabhāvam ataimirika keśa adarśana vat svabhāva virahitam iti arthaḥ atas eva tat prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam prapañcaḥ hi vāc prapañcayati arthān iti kṛtvā prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam vāgbhiḥ avyāhṛtam iti arthaḥ 
[159,ii_159,iv]	nirvikalpam ca tat vikalpaḥ citta pracāraḥ tad rahita tvāt tat tattvam nirvikalpam yathā uktam sūtre parama artha satyam katamat yatra jñānasya api apracāraḥ kaḥ punar vādaḥ akṣarāṇām iti evam nirvikalpam nānā arthaḥ asya iti nānā artham bhinna artham na nānā arthaḥ anāna artham abhinna artham iti arthaḥ yathā uktam ārya satya dvaya avatāra sūtre 
[159,v]	deva putraḥ āha katamaḥ punar mañjuśrīḥ samyak prayogaḥ mañjuśrīḥ āha yad samā deva putra paramārthataḥ tathatā dharmadhātuḥ atyanta ajātiḥ ca tad samāni paramārthataḥ pañca ānantaryāṇi yad samāni pañca ānantaryāṇi tad samāni dṛṣṭi kṛtāni yad samāni dṛṣṭi kṛtāni tad samāḥ pṛthagjana dharmāḥ yad samāḥ pṛthagjana dharmāḥ tad samāḥ śaikṣa dharmāḥ yad samāḥ śaikṣa dharmāḥ tad samāḥ aśaikṣa dharmāḥ yad samāḥ aśaikṣa dharmāḥ tad samāḥ samyaksaṃbuddha dharmāḥ yad samāḥ samyaksaṃbuddha dharmāḥ tad samam nirvāṇam yad samam nirvāṇam tad samaḥ saṃsāraḥ yad samaḥ saṃsāraḥ tad samaḥ paramārthataḥ saṃkleśaḥ yad samaḥ paramārthataḥ saṃkleśaḥ tad samam paramārthataḥ vyavadānam yad samam paramārthataḥ vyavadānam tad samāḥ paramārthataḥ sarva dharmāḥ evam paramārthataḥ sarva dharma samatā prayuktaḥ deva putra bhikṣuḥ samyak prayuktaḥ iti ucyate 
[159,vi_160,i]	deva putraḥ āha katamayā punar mañjuśrīḥ sama tayā yāvat paramārthataḥ yat samam vyavadānam tad samāḥ sarva dharmāḥ paramārthataḥ iti mañjuśrīḥ āha paramārthataḥ sarva dharma anutpāda sama tayā paramārthataḥ sarva dharma atyantā jāti samatayā paramārthataḥ samāḥ sarva dharmāḥ tat kasmāt hetoḥ paramārthataḥ nirvāṇa ānānā akaraṇāḥ hi deva putra sarva dharmāḥ atyanta nirutpāda tām upādāya tat yathā api nāma deva putra yat ca mṛddhājanasyāmi antaram ākāśam yat ca ratna bhājanasya ākāśam ākāśa dhātuḥ eva eṣaḥ tat paramārthataḥ na kiṃcid nānā karaṇam evam eva deva putra yaḥ saṃkleśaḥ sa paramārthataḥ atyantān utpādatā yat api vyavadānam tat api paramārthataḥ atyantān utpādatā saṃsāraḥ api paramārthataḥ atyantān utpādatā yāvat nirvāṇam api paramārthataḥ atyantān utpādatā na atra kiṃcid paramārthataḥ nānā karaṇam tat kasmāt hetoḥ paramārthataḥ atyanta an utpāda tvāt sarva dharmāṇām iti tat evam anān ārtha tā tattvasya lakṣaṇam veditavyam śūnyatā eka rasa tvāt uttarottara vyākhyānam ca atra veditavyam 
[160,ii_160,iii^1]	evam tāvat āryāṇām jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāra parikṣayāya kṛta kāryāṇām tattva lakṣaṇam laukikam tu tattva lakṣaṇam adhikṛtya ucyate pratītya yat yat bhavati na hi tāvat tat eva tat na ca anyat api tat tasmāt na ucchinnam na api śāśvatam yat kāraṇam pratītya yat kāryam utpadyate tat yathā śāli bījam pratītya pṛthivī ādi sāmagrīm ca śāli aṅkuraḥ upajāyate na hi tāvat tat eva tat iti śakyate vaktum na eva yat eva bījam saḥ eva aṅkuraḥ janya jana kayoḥ ekatva prasaṅgāt tatas ca pitāputrayoḥ api eka tvam syāt ananya tvāt ca aṅkura avasthāyām aṅkura vat bīja grahaṇam api syāt bīja vat ca aṅkurasya api grahaṇam syāt nitya tvam ca evam bījasya syāt avināśa abhyupagamāt tatas ca śāśvata vāda prasaṅgāt mahā doṣa rāśiḥ syāt karma phala ādya bhāva prasaṅgāt evam tāvat yat eva bījam saḥ eva aṅkuraḥ iti na yujyate 
[160,iii^2_160,iv]	na ca anyat api tat tasmāt na api bījāt aṅkurasya anya tvam bījam antareṇa api aṅkura udaya prasaṅgāt yadi anyat anyat anyasmāt anyasmāt api ṛte bhavet iti vacanāt aṅkura avasthāne api bīja anuccheda prasaṅgāt tatas ca satkārya vāda doṣaḥ syāt yatas ca evam yat kāraṇam pratītya yat kāryam utpadyate na eva tat kāraṇam kāryam bhavati na ca tasmāt kāraṇāt tat kāryam anyat tasmāt na kāraṇam ucchinnam na api śāśvatam iti śakyate vyavasthāpayitum yathā uktam ārya deva pādaiḥ yasmāt pravartate bhāvaḥ tena ucchedaḥ na jāyate yasmāt nivartate bhāvaḥ tena nityaḥ na jāyate iti uktam ca ārya lalita vistara sūtre bījasya sataḥ yathā aṅkuraḥ na ca yaḥ bīja sa ca eva aṅkuraḥ na ca anyu tatas na ca eva tat evam anuccheda aśāśvata dharma tā iti 
[160,v_161,i^1]	tat evam yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena aneka artha manāna artham anucchedam aśāśvatam etat tad loka nāthānām buddhānām śāsana amṛtam mahā karuṇa upāya mahā megha paṭala nirantara avacchādita ākāśa dhātu paryanta diś maṇḍalānām rāga ādi kleśa gaṇa samudācāra ati tīkṣṇatara āditya maṇḍala upatāpita jagat jāti jarā maraṇa duḥkha dahana saṃtāpa upaśama tatparāṇām satata avirata yatha anurūpa carita pratipakṣa sat dharma deśana amṛta dhārā pātaiḥ yathā anurūpa vineya jana kuśala mūla śasya oṣadhi phala phulla latā utpanna ati vṛddha yanuji dhṛkṣūṇām saddharma amṛta mahā varṣa varṣiṇām samyaksaṃbuddha mahā nāgānāmatrāṇālaukika trāṇānām anātha nāthānām sakala lokanāthānām etat tad saddharma amṛtam sakala traidhātuka bhava duḥkha kṣaya svabhāvam yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena ekatva anyatva rahitam śāśvata uccheda vāda vigatam ca vijñeyam 
[161,i^2]	etad dharma tattva amṛta pratipannānām śrāvakāṇām śruta cintā bhāvanā kramāt pravartamānānām śīla samādhi prajñā ātmaka skandha traya amṛta rasasya upayogāt niyatam eva jarā maraṇa kṣaya svabhāva nirvāṇa adhigamaḥ bhavati atha api kathaṃcid iha aparipakva kuśala mūla tayā śrutvā api etat saddharma amṛtam dṛṣṭaḥ eva dharme na mokṣam āsādayanti tathā api janma antare api avaśyam eṣām pūrva hetu balāt eva niyatā siddhiḥ saṃpadyate yathā uktam śatake iha yadi api tattva jñaḥ nirvāṇam na adhigacchati prāpnoti ayatnatas avaśyam punar janmani karma vat iti 
[161,ii_161,iii]	atha api kathaṃcid saṃbuddhānām anutpāde śrāvakāṇām punar kṣaye sati ārya mārga upadeśaka kalyāṇa mitra pratyaya vaikalyāt na syāt dharma tattva amṛta adhigamaḥ tathā api pūrva janma antara dharma tattva śravaṇa hetu balāt eva aihalaukikā upadeśa nirapekṣāṇām api praviveka sevā mātra upanata pratyayānām svāyaṃbhuvam jñānam pratyekabuddhānām asaṃsargāt pravartate 
[161,iv]	kāya cetasoḥ pravivekaḥ asaṃsargaḥ kalyāṇa mitra aparyeṣaṇam vā tasmāt asaṃsargāt hetoḥ pratyekabuddhānām asaṃbuddhake api kāle yasmāt bhavati eva dharma tattva adhigamaḥ tasmāt abandhyā siddhiḥ asya saṃbuddha mahā vaidya rāja praṇītasya saddharma tattva amṛta bhaiṣajyasya iti vijñeyam yatas ca etat evam atas arhati prājñaḥ prāṇān api parityajya saddharma tattvam paryeṣitum iti yathā uktam bhagavatā ārya aṣṭa sāhasrikāyām bhagavatyām 
[161,v^1]	katham ca bhagavan sadā praruditena bodhisattvena mahāsattvena iyam prajñāpāramitā paryeṣitā evam uktaḥ bhagavān āyuṣmantam subhūtim sthaviram etat avocat sadā praruditena bodhisattvena mahāsattvena pūrvam prajñāpāramitām paryeṣamāṇena kāye anarthikena jīvita nirapekṣeṇa lābha satkāra ślokeṣu aniśritena paryeṣamāṇena paryeṣitā tena prajñāpāramitām paryeṣamāṇena araṇya gatena antarīkṣāt nirghoṣaḥ śrutaḥ abhūt gaccha kula putra pūrvasyām diśi tatra prajñāpāramitām śroṣyasi tathā ca gaccha yathā na kāya klamatha manasikāram utpādayasi na styānam iddha manasikāram utpādayasi na bhojana manasikāram utpādayasi yāvat mā kvacid cittam praṇidhāḥ adhyātmam vā bahirdhā vā 
[161,v^2]	mā ca kula putra vāmena avalokayan gāḥ mā dakṣiṇena mā pūrveṇa mā paścimena mā uttareṇa mā urdhvam mā adhas mā ca anuvidiśam avalokayan gāḥ tathā ca kula putra gaccha yathā na ātmataḥ na satkāyataḥ calasi na rūpataḥ na vedanā atas na saṃjñātaḥ na saṃskārebhyaḥ na vijñānataḥ calasi yaḥ hi atas calati sa vitiṣṭhate kutas vitiṣṭhate buddha dharmebhyaḥ vitiṣṭhate yaḥ buddha dharmebhyaḥ vitiṣṭhate sa saṃsāre carati yaḥ saṃsāre carati sa prajñāpāramitāyām na carati na ca tām anuprāpnoti iti 
[162,i_162,ii^1]	yāvat māreṇa pāpīyasā udake antar dhāpite atha asya etat abhūt yat nu aham ātmanaḥ kāyam viddhāḥ ime pṛthivī pradeśam rudhireṇa siñcā iyam tat kasya hetoḥ ayam pṛthivī pradeśaḥ uddhata rajaskaḥ mā rajaḥ dhāturitas dharma udgatasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya śarīre nipatet kim aham ātma bhāvena kariṣyāmi avaśyam bhedana dharmiṇā varam khalu punar mama evaṃrūpayā kriyayā ātma bhāvasya vināśaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavet na tu evam niḥsāmarthya kriyayā bahūni ca mama ātma bhāva sahasrāṇi kāma hetoḥ kāmanidānam bhinnāni punar punar saṃsāre saṃsarataḥ na punar evaṃbhūteṣu sthāneṣu atha khalu sadā praruditaḥ bodhisattvaḥ mahāsattvaḥ tīkṣṇam śastram gṛhītvā samantāt ātmānam viddhā samantataḥ tam pṛthivī pradeśam svakena rudhireṇa āsiñcat ityādi atha khalu sadā praruditaḥ bodhisattvaḥ mahāsattvaḥ saha darśanāt eva dharma udgatasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya evaṃrūpam sukham pratyalabhata tat yathā api nāma prathama dhyāna samāpannasya bhikṣoḥ ekāgra manasikārasya bhikṣoḥ 
[162,ii^2]	tatra iyam dharma udgatasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya prajñāpāramitā deśanā yat uta sarva dharma samatayā prajñāpāramitā sama tā sarva dharma vivikta tayā prajñāpāramitā vivikta tā sarva dharma acala tayā prajñāpāramitā acala tā sarva dharma āmanana tayā prajñāpāramitā mananatā sarva dharma astambhita tayā prajñāpāramitā stambhita tā sarva dharma eka rasa tayā prajñāpāramitā eka rasa tā sarva dharma aparyanta tayā prajñāpāramitā paryanta tā sarva dharma anutpāda tayā prajñāpāramitā anutpāda tā sarva dharma anirodha tayā prajñāpāramitā nirodha tā gagana aparyanta tayā prajñāpāramitā paryanta tā yāvat sarva dharma asaṃbhedana tayā prajñāpāramitā saṃbhedana tā sarva dharma anupalabdhi tayā prajñāpāramitā anupalabdhi tā sarva dharma abhibhāvanā samatayā prajñāpāramitā abhibhāvanā sama tā sarva dharma niśceṣṭa tayā prajñāpāramitā niśceṣṭa tā sarva dharma acintya tayā prajñāpāramitā acintya tā veditavyā iti 
[163,i]	atra āha vidyate eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ kāla traya vijñapti hetutvāt iha atīta anāgata pratyutpanna asrayaḥ kālāḥ bhagavatā upadiṣṭāḥ te ca bhāva āśrayāḥ yasmāt utpannaḥ niruddhaḥ hi bhāva svabhāvaḥ atītaḥ iti vyapadiśyate utpannaḥ aniruddhaḥ hi vartamānaḥ alabdha ātma bhāvaḥ anāgataḥ iti evam bhāva svabhāva nibandhana asrayaḥ kālāḥ upadiṣṭāḥ te ca santi tasmāt tad nibandhanaḥ api bhāva svabhāvaḥ asti iti ucyate syāt kāla traya prajñapti hetuḥ bhāva svabhāvaḥ yadi kāla trayam eva bhavat abhimatam bhavet na tu asti yathā ca na asti tathā pratipādayan āha pratyutpannaḥ anāgataḥ ca yadi atītam apekṣya hi pratyutpannaḥ anāgataḥ ca kāle atīte bhaviṣyataḥ 
[163,ii]	iha tāvat yadi vartamāna anāgatau syātām tau apekṣya atītam kālam bhavetām anapekṣya vā tatra yadi atītam apekṣya sidhyete tathā niyatam atīte kāle bhaviṣyataḥ yasmāt yasya hi yatra asattvam tat tena na apekṣyate tat yathā vandhyā srī sva tanayena gagana māla tīla tā sva kusumena sikatā sva tailena avidyamānam api andhakāram pradīpena pradīpaḥ api andhakāreṇa pratidvandvi tvena apekṣyate iti ced na etat evam asya api sādhya sama tvāt tat atra yadi atīte kāle vartamāna anāgatau kālau iṣyete apekṣā siddhayartham evam sati atīte kāle vidyamāna tvāt atīta kāla ātma vat tayoḥ api atīta tvam syāt tatas ca atītaḥ api na syāt yasmāt vartamāna avasthā atikrāntaḥ hi atītaḥ asaṃprāptaḥ anāgataḥ iti syāt yadā tu vartamāna anāgatayoḥ asaṃbhavaḥ eva tadā kutas kasyacid atīta tvam syāt iti atas atītaḥ api na syāt 
[163,iii_163,iv]	atha yathā ukta doṣa parijihīrṣayā pratyutpannaḥ anāgataḥ ca na staḥ tatra punar yadi pratyutpannaḥ anāgataḥ ca syātām kaśram apekṣya tam tatra atīte kāle yadi vartamāna anāgatau kālau na staḥ iti parikalpyate evam api tatra avidyamāna tvāt gagana indīvara vat na asti apekṣā 
[163,v_163,vi]	atha api syāt kāla vādinām vidyate eva kālaḥ tatra kim apekṣayā prayojanam iti ucyate evam api anapekṣya punar siddhiḥ na atītam vidyate tayoḥ pratyutpannaḥ anāgataḥ ca tasmāt kālaḥ na vidyate pratyutpanna anāgatayoḥ asattvam atīta anapekṣa tvāt khara viṣāṇa vat yatas ca evam pratyutpannaḥ anāgataḥ ca tasmāt kālaḥ na vidyate iti vijñeyam 
[164,i]	yadā ca evam atītam apekṣya vā anapekṣya vā pratyutpanna anāgatayoḥ na asti siddhiḥ evam pratyutpanna apekṣayā vā anapekṣayā vai atīta anāgatayoḥ anāgata apekṣayā vā anapekṣayā vā pratyutpannātītayoḥ asiddhau iṣyamāṇāyām tena eva pratyutpanna āgatayoḥ atīta apekṣayā vā anapekṣayā asiddhi krameṇa dūṣaṇa sāmyam atidiśan āha etena eva avaśiṣṭau dvau krameṇa parivartakau uttama adhama madhyādīn eka tva ādīn ca lakṣayet 
[164,ii]	katham kṛtvā yadi atītaḥ anāgataḥ ca pratyutpannam apekṣya hi kālaḥ atītaḥ anāgataḥ ca pratyutpanne bhaviṣyataḥ kālaḥ atītaḥ anāgataḥ ca na staḥ tatra punar yadi kālaḥ atītaḥ anāgataḥ ca syātām katham apekṣya tam anapekṣya punar siddhiḥ na jātam vidyate tayoḥ tena atītaḥ anāgataḥ ca kālaḥ nāma na vidyate 
[164,iii_164,iv]	eṣa tāvat ekaḥ kāla parivartaḥ atītaḥ vartamānaḥ ca yadi ajātam apekṣya hi atītaḥ vartamānaḥ ca kāle ajāte bhaviṣyataḥ atītaḥ vartamānaḥ ca na staḥ tatra punar yadi atītaḥ vartamānaḥ ca syātām katham apekṣya tam anapekṣya punar siddhiḥ na ajātam vidyate tayoḥ atītaḥ vartamānaḥ ca tasmāt kālaḥ na vidyate 
[164,v_164,vii]	eṣa dvitīyaḥ kāla parivartaḥ iti vyākhyāna kārikāḥ iti evaṃdvau kāla parivartau boddhavyau yatas ca evam vicāraṇe kāla trayam na asti tasmāt kālaḥ na vidyate kāla abhāvāt ca bhāva sadbhāvaḥ api na asti iti siddham yathā ca etad kāla trayam vicāritam evam uttama adhama madhyādīn eka tva ādīn ca lakṣayet 
[164,viii]	uttama adhama madhyamān iti ādi śabdena kuśala akuśala avya akṛtāni utpāda sthiti bhaṅgāḥ pūrva anta apara anta madhya antāḥ kāmarūpa ārūpya dhātavaḥ śaikṣā śaikṣana eva śaikṣana eva aśaikṣa ādayaḥ yāvantaḥ padārthāḥ tripadārtha saṃbandha vyavasthitāḥ te sarve gṛhyante eka tva ādīn ca iti anena ādi śabdena dvi tva bahutvayaḥ grahaṇāt te eva uttama ādayaḥ eka tva ādayaḥ ca kāla traya vyākhyānena vyākhyātāḥ veditavyāḥ 
[165,i]	atra āha vidyate eva kālaḥ parimāṇavat tvāt iha yat na asti na tasya parimāṇavat tvam vidyate tat yathā khara viṣāṇasya asti ca kālasya parimāṇavat tvam kṣaṇa lava muhūrta divasa rātrī ahorātra pakṣa māsa saṃvatsara ādi bhedena tasmāt parimāṇa vat tvāt vidyate eva kālaḥ iti ucyate yadi kālaḥ nāma kaścid syāt syāt tasya parimāṇa vat tvam na tu asti yasmāt na āsthitaḥ gṛhyate kālaḥ sthitaḥ kālaḥ na vidyate yaḥ gṛhyeta agṛhītaḥ ca kālaḥ prajñapyate katham 
[165,ii_165,iii]	iha yadi kālaḥ nāma kaścid avasthitaḥ kṣaṇa ādi vyatiriktaḥ syāt sa kṣaṇa ādibhiḥ parimāṇa vat tvāt gṛhyeta na tu avasthitaḥ kūṭasthaḥ kaścid kālaḥ nāma asti yaḥ kṣaṇa ādibhiḥ gṛhyeta tat evam na āsthitaḥ gṛhyate kālaḥ asthita tvāt na gṛhyate iti arthaḥ atha api syāt nityaḥ eva avasthita svabhāvaḥ kālaḥ nāma asti kṣaṇa ādibhiḥ abhivyajyate tathā hi kālaḥ pacati bhūtāni kālaḥ saṃharate prajāḥ kālaḥ supteṣu jāgarti kālaḥ hi duratikramaḥ iti 
[165,iv_165,vi]	yaḥ ca evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ saḥ avasthita svabhāvaḥ asti iti ucyate evam api sthitaḥ kālaḥ na vidyate yaḥ kṣaṇa ādibhiḥ abhivyajyamānaḥ gṛhyeta kasmāt punar sthitaḥ kālaḥ na asti iti ced kṣaṇa ādi vyatirekeṇa āgṛhyamāṇa tvāt api ca ayam kālaḥ saṃskṛta svabhāvaḥ san asti iti asaṃskṛta svabhāvaḥ vā ubhayam ca saṃskṛta parīkṣāyām pratiṣiddham utpāda sthiti bhaṅgānām asiddhau na asti saṃskṛtam saṃskṛtasya api asiddhau ca katham setsyati asaṃskṛtam iti anena tat evam na asti vyavasthitaḥ kālaḥ yaḥ gṛhyeta yaḥ ca idānīm kālaḥ na gṛhyate asthita tvāt avidyamāna svarūpa tvāt saḥ agṛhyamāṇaḥ san katham kṣaṇa ādibhiḥ prajñapayitum bhāvataḥ pāryate iti āha agṛhītaḥ ca kālaḥ prajñapyate katham iti tasmāt na asti eva kālaḥ 
[165,vii_165,viii]	atra āha satyam na asti nityaḥ kālaḥ nāma kaścid rūpa ādi vyatiriktaḥ svabhāva siddhaḥ kim tarhi rūpa ādīn eva sa saṃskārān upādāya prajñaptaḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇa ādi vācyaḥ bhavati tasmāt adoṣaḥ iti ucyate evam api bhāvam pratītya kālaḥ ced kālaḥ bhāvāt ṛte kutas yadi evam bhāvam pratītya kālaḥ bhavati iti bhavatā vyavasthāpyate yadā khalu bhāvaḥ na asti tadā niyatam tad hetukaḥ api kālaḥ na asti iti pratipādayan āha na ca kaścana bhāvaḥ asti
[166,i_166,ii]	iti pūrvam vistareṇa pratipādita tvāt vakṣyamāṇa pratiṣedhāt ca yadā ca evam na kaścid bhāvaḥ asti bhāvataḥ tadā kutas kālaḥ bhaviṣyati kāla abhāvāt ca na santi kṣaṇa lava muhūrta ādayaḥ kāla bhedāḥ tad pariṇāma bhūtāḥ iti atas kutas pariṇāmavat tvena kāla siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati tasmāt na asti eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ iti uktam hi bhagavatā ārya hasti kakṣya sūtre yadi koci dharmāṇa bhavet svabhāvaḥ tatra eva gaccheya jinaḥ sa śrāvakaḥ kūṭastha dharmāṇa siyā na nirvṛtī na niṣprapañcaḥ bhavi jātu paṇḍitaḥ iti 
[166,iii_167,ii]	tathā buddha sahasra śatā yaḥ atītāḥ dharma sahasra śatāni bhaṇitvā na eva ca dharma na ca akṣara kṣīṇāḥ na asti samudbhavu tena akṣīṇā iti tathā utpāda kāle hi tathāgatasya maitreya nāmā tu iha yaḥ bhaviṣyati bhaviṣyati iyam kanaka āvṛtā mahī tasyāḥ idānīm kutas āgamaḥ asau ullāpanāḥ kāma guṇāḥ hi pañca vibhrāmaṇāḥ mohana moṣa dharmiṇaḥ madhyāhna kāle hi yathā eva grīṣme jalam marīcyām hi tathā eva kāmāḥ ekena kalpena bhavet hi lokaḥ ākāśa bhūtaḥ gagana svabhāvaḥ dāham vināśam ca payānti bhīravaḥ kutas āgamaḥ kutra gatiḥ ca teṣām iti tat yathā pañca imāni bhikṣavaḥ saṃjñā mātram pratijñā mātram vyavahāra mātram saṃvṛti mātram yat uta atītaḥ adhvā anāgataḥ adhvā ākāśam nirvāṇam pudgalaḥ ca iti 
[168,i]	atra āha vidyate kālaḥ phala pravṛttau sahakāri kāraṇa bhāvāt yaḥ na asti na asau sahakāri kāraṇa bhāvena pratipadyate vandhyā tanaya vat tasmāt asti kālaḥ sahakāri kāraṇa bhāvāt iha bīja avani salila jvalana pavana gagana abhidhāna hetu pratyaya sāmagrīm pratītya ayam aṅkuraḥ upajāyamānaḥ satyām api bīja ādi pratyaya sāmagryām ṛtu viśeṣa asaṃnidhānāt na upajāyate yathā ca bāhyeṣu evam ādhyātmikeṣu api yathā uktam bhagavatā na praṇaśyanti karmāṇi kalpa koṭi śataiḥ api sāmagrīm prāpya kālam ca phalanti khalu dehinām iti 
[168,ii]	yasmāt ca evam asti kāla apekṣā tasmāt asti asau kālaḥ nāma yaḥ aṅkura ādi pravṛttau sahakāri kāraṇam bhavati iti ucyate syāt sahakārikāraṇa tā kālasya yadi aṅkura ādi phalasya pravṛttiḥ eva syāt na tu asti katham kṛtvā iha bīja ādi hetu pratyaya sāmagrītaḥ aṅkura ādi phala udaye parikalpyamāne vyavasthitasya vā phalasya sāmagryām satyāṃtataḥ utpādaḥ parikalpyeta avyavasthitasya vā kim ca atas yadi tāvat vyavasthitasya parikalpyate tat na yujyate iti pratipādayan āha hetoḥ ca pratyayānām ca sāmagryā jāyate yadi phalam asti ca sāmagryām sāmagryā jāyate katham 
[168,iii]	yadi hetu pratyaya sāmagryām tvad matena phalam asti nanu evam sati yasmāt sāmagryām asti katham tayā tat janyate na hi kuṇḍe dadhi vidyamānam kuṇḍena janyate api ca yat vidyate tad niṣpanna tvāt niṣpanna purovasthita ghaṭa vat na punar janma apekṣate abhivyaktiḥ sthaulyam vā sūkṣma ātmanā vidyamānasya kriyate iti ced tasya api pakṣasya pūrvam eva āgacchati anyatas na agniḥ indhane agniḥ na vidyate iti atra uktam uttaram 
[168,iv_168,v]	atha na asti eva sāmagryām phalam iti parikalpyate etat api na upapadyate iti pratipādayan āha hetoḥ ca pratyayānām ca sāmagryā jāyate yadi phalam na asti ca sāmagryām sāmagryā jāyate katham yadi hetoḥ ca pratyayānām ca sāmagryām na asti tad phalam katham tarhi hetu pratyaya sāmagryā phalam janyate tatra avidyamāna tvāt sikatābhiḥ iva tailam atas eva asaṃbhāvayan āha phalam na asti ca sāmagryām sāmagryā jāyate katham na tad phalam sāmagrītaḥ jāyate iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[168,vi_169,ii]	kim ca anyat hetoḥ ca pratyayānām ca sāmagryām asti ced phalam gṛhyeta nanu sāmagryām sāmagryām ca na gṛhyate yat yatra asti tat tatra gṛhyate tat yathā kuṇḍe dadhi yat ca yatra na asti na tat tatra gṛhyate tat yathā sikatāsu tailam maṇḍūka jaṭāyām śiromaṇiḥ atha syāt vidyamānāḥ api padārthāḥ ati saukṣmyāt ati saṃnikarṣāt ati viprakarṣāt indriya upaghātāt mūrti vat dravya vyavadhānāt mūrti antardhānāt manaḥ navasthānāt paramāṇu vat akṣa stha añjana śalākā vat āditya gati vat taimirika ekaika keśa vat andha badhira ādi rūpa śabda ādi vat kuḍaya ādi vyavahita ghaṭa ādi vat siddha deva piśāca ādi śarīra vat viṣaya antara vyāpṛtasya viṣaya antara vat na gṛhyate iti ced kim khalu eṣā ām agṛhyamāṇānām astitve liṅgam yena eṣām astitve sati anupalabdhiḥ iti syāt anumāna upamāna āgamaiḥ grahaṇāt eṣām astitvam iti ced na tarhi teṣām anupalabdhiḥ iti vaktavyam anumāna ādibhiḥ upalabhyamāna tvāt yat rūpi indriya grāhyam tat ebhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ vidyamānam api sat na gṛhyate iti ced ucyate kim asmābhiḥ evam uktam rūpi indriyaiḥ vidyamānam sat gṛhyeta iti kim tarhi sāmānyena eva yat brūmaḥ gṛhyeta nanu sāmagryām iti 
[169,iii]	atha api manyase yat yatra na asti na tat tasmāt utpadyate sikatābhyaḥ taila vat utpadyate ca sāmagrītaḥ phalam tasmāt anumānataḥ sāmagryām phalasya astitvam iti ucyate yat yatra asti na tat tasmāt utpadyate tat yathā kuṇḍāt dadhi iti asmāt api anumānāt astitvam asya ayuktam iti kṛtvā na asti eva sāmagryām phalam iti kim na gṛhyate 
[169,iv_169,v]	atha api syāt ubhyoḥ api pakṣayoḥ anumāna virodhāt yathā astitvam na yuktam evam na astitvam api iti ucyate na vayam asya asattvam pratipādayāmaḥ kim tarhi para parikalpitam sattvam asya nirākurmaḥ evam na vayam asya sattvam pratipādayāmaḥ kim tarhi para parikalpitam asattvam asya apākurmaḥ anta dvaya parihāreṇa madhyamāyāḥ pratipadaḥ pratipādayitum iṣṭa tvāt iti uktam ca ārya devapādīye śatake stambha ādīnām alaṃkāraḥ gṛhasya arthe nirarthakaḥ satkāryam eva yasya iṣṭam yasya asat kāryam eva ca iti tat evam na sāmagrītaḥ phalam utpadyate vidyamānasya grahaṇa prasaṅgāt iti vyavasthitam 
[169,vi_169,vii]	atha manyase na asti eva sāmagryām phalam iti evam api hetoḥ ca pratyayānām ca sāmagryām na asti ced phalam hetavaḥ pratyayāḥ ca syuḥ ahetu pratyayaiḥ samāḥ yathā hi jvālā aṅgāra ādiṣu aṅkuraḥ na asti iti kṛtvā tasya te hetu pratyayāḥ na bhavanti eva vivakṣitānām api bīja ādīnām hetu pratyaya tā na syāt teṣu aṅkuraḥ na asti iti kṛtvā na ca ahetu pratyayebhyaḥ phala pravṛttiḥ yuktā iti na asti svabhāvataḥ phala pravṛttiḥ 
[170,i]	atra āha na eva hi sāmagryāḥ phala utpādana sāmarthyam asti yatas iyam cintā syāt kim sāmagryām phalam asti uta aho na asti iti kim tarhi hetoḥ phala utpādana sāmarthyam sāmagrī tu hetoḥ anugraha mātram karoti sa hetuḥ phalasya utpatti artham hetum datvā nirudhyate tena ca hetunā anugṛhyamāṇam phalam utpadyate iti ucyate na eva hi ajātasya phalasya hetoḥ anugrahaṇam asti na ca api ajātasya bandhyā tanayasya iva kenacid kiṃcid mātram kartum śakyam iti ayuktā eṣā kalpanā 
[170,ii_170,iii]	api ca hetukam phalasya datvā yadi hetuḥ nirudhyate yat dattam yat niruddham ca hetoḥ ātma dvayam bhavet yadi hetuḥ phalasya utpatti artham hetukam kāraṇam datvā nirudhyate iti parikalpyate evam sati yat dattam yat niruddham ca tad ātma bhāva dvayam hetoḥ syāt na ca etat yuktam ardha śāśvata prasaṅgāt nitya anityayoḥ ca paraspara viruddhayoḥ ekatva abhāvāt 
[170,iv_170,v]	atha hetoḥ ātma bhāva dvaya prasaṅga parihāra artham sarva ātmanā nirodhaḥ iṣyate phalasya utpatti artham kiṃcid api adatvā evam api hetum phalasya ādatvā ca yadi hetuḥ nirudhyate hetau niruddhe jātam tad phalam āhetukam bhavet yadi phalasya kiṃcid api adatvā sarva ātmanā hetuḥ nirudhyate nanu tasmin hetau niruddhe yat phalam utpadyate tat āhetukam syāt na ca āhetukam asti iti ayuktā eṣā kalpanā 
[170,vi_170,vii]	atra āha yadi evam phalasya hetoḥ utpattau doṣaḥ evam sati saha utpannā eva sāmagrī phalasya janikā astu tat yathā pradīpa prabhāyāḥ iti eṣā api kalpanā na upapadyate iti pratipādayan āha phalam saha eva sāmagryāḥ yadi prādurbhavet punar eka kālau prasajyete janakaḥ yaḥ ca janyate na ca eka kālayoḥ savya itara go viṣāṇayoḥ janya janaka tvam dṛṣṭam vāma dakṣiṇa karayoḥ caraṇayoḥ vā iti ayuktā eṣā kalpanā iti ayuktam etat 
[170,viii]	atra āhuḥ eke na eva hi abhūtvā bhāvānām utpattiḥ yuktā ākasmika tva prasaṅgāt tasmāt hetu pratyaya sāmagrītaḥ pūrvam eva tat phalam anāgata avasthāyām vyavasthitam anāgata ātmanā tasya hetu pratyaya sāmagryā vartamāna avasthā janyate dravyam tu vyavasthitam eva iti tān pratyucyate pūrvam eva ca sāmagryāḥ phalam prādurbhavet yadi hetu pratyaya nirmuktam phalam āhetukam bhavet 
[170,ix]	yadi bhavatām abhīpsitam sāmagrītaḥ pūrvam eva phalam svarūpataḥ syāt iti tat hetu pratyaya nirapekṣam syāt tatas ca āhetukam syāt na ca āhetukānām padārthānām astitvam yuktam khara turaga uraga viṣāṇa ādīnām api astitva prasaṅgāt pūrva siddhasya ca punar hetu pratyaya apekṣayā niṣprayojana tva āditi a yuktam etat 
[171,i]	anye punar varṇayanti hetuḥ eva phalam janayati na sāmagrī na ca ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ yasmāt na hi anyohetuḥ anyat phalam yatas kim hetum datvā phalasya hetuḥ nirudhyate uta adatvā eva iti vicāraḥ syāt api tu hetuḥ eva niruddhaḥ phala ātmanā vyavasthitaḥ iti ucyate evam api niruddhe ced phalam hetau hetoḥ saṃkramaṇam bhavet pūrva jātasya hetoḥ ca punarjanma prasajyate 
[171,ii]	yadi niruddhe hetau bhavat matena phalam utpadyate tat ca phalam hetu ātmakam eva bhavati iti parikalpyate evam sati hetoḥ saṃkramaṇam bhavet naṭasya veṣa antara parityāgena veṣa antara saṃcāra vat hetoḥ saṃkramaṇa mātram eva syāt na tu apūrvasya phalasya utpādaḥ tatas ca hetoḥ nityatā eva syāt na ca nityānām astitvam kvacid asti yathā uktam śatake apratītya astitā na asti kadācid kasyacid kvacid na kadācid kvacid kaścid vidyate tena śāśvataḥ iti 
[171,iii_171,iv]	kim ca etasyām kalpanāyām pūrva jātasya ca hetoḥ punarjanma prāpnoti na ca jātasya punar api janma yujyate niṣprayojana tvāt anavasthā prasaṅgāt ca atha manyase yena ātmanā vidyamānaḥ na tena eva ātmanā jāyate yena ca ātmanā avidyamānaḥ tena eva jāyate iti etat api na yuktam aparityakta hetu svabhāvasya hetu svarūpasya phalam iti saṃjñā mātra bhedāt avasthā bhedāt ca dravya abhedasya sādhayitum aśakyatvāt phala avasthāyām ca parityakta hetu svabhāvasya phala śabda vācya tvāt hetuḥ phala ātmanā tiṣṭhati iti yat kiṃcid etat 
[171,v_171,vii]	kim ca anyat yadi hetuḥ phalam janayet niruddhaḥ vā janayet aniruddhaḥ vā phalam api utpannam vā janayet anutpannam vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti pratipādayan āha janayet phalam utpannam niruddhaḥ astaṃgataḥ katham tiṣṭhan api katham hetuḥ phalena janayet hṛtaḥ yadi tāvata niruddhaḥ astaṃgataḥ hetuḥ utpannam sat vidyamānam phalam janayati iti parikalpyate tat na upapadyate kasmāt iti ced katham niruddhaḥ asaṃvidyamānaḥ hetuḥ phalam janayet yadi janayati vandhyā putraḥ api putram janayiṣyati phalam ca sat vidyamānam api janma nirapekṣam api katham hetuḥ janayi ṣyati atha manyase śakti abhāvāt niruddhaḥ na janayati kim tu tiṣṭhan eva hetuḥ phalam janayiṣyati iti ucyate tiṣṭhan api hetuḥ avikṛta rūpaḥ vidyamānena phalena vṛtaḥ saṃbaddhaḥ katham janayet iha hi kāraṇam vikṛtim gacchat jāyate anyasya kāraṇam iti kāraṇa abhāvam pratipadyamānasya hetoḥ avaśyam vikāreṇa bhavitavyam yaḥ tu na vikriyate sa hetu lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ eva na bhavati iti phalena ca saṃbaddhaḥ katham janayet phalasya vidyamāna tvāt 
[172,i_172,ii]	atha manyase vidyamānasya phalasya punar janayitum aśakyatvāt avṛte eva asaṃbaddhaḥ eva hetuḥ phalena phalam janayiṣyati iti etat api ayuktam iti āha atha āvṛtaḥ phalena asau katamat janayet phalam yadi hetuḥ phalena asaṃbaddhaḥ eva iṣyate tadā katamat idānīm phalam janayet sarvam eva vā phalam janayet asaṃbaddha tvāt na vā kiṃcid janayet asaṃbaddha tvāt eva iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[172,iii_172,v]	kim ca anyat yadi hetuḥ phalam janayet sa dṛṣṭvā phalam janayet adṛṣṭvā vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha na hi adṛṣṭvā vā dṛṣṭvā vā hetuḥ janayate phalam tatra yadi hetuḥ dṛṣṭvā janayati iti parikalpyate tat na yujyate yasmāt vidyamānam eva draṣṭum pāryate na avidyamānam vidyamānam ced tat na janyate vidyamāna tvāt iti evam tāvat hetuḥ phalam dṛṣṭvā na janayati adṛṣṭvā api na janayati sarvasya phalasya hetoḥ janakatva prasaṅgāt atha kim idam darśanam kim vā adarśanam iti ucyate prasiddham etat loke upalabdhiḥ darśanam iti 
[172,vi]	nanu etat bīja ādiṣu nirindriyeṣu na saṃbhavati saṃbhavatu mā vā na asmāka mayam paryanuyogaḥ kim tarhi tasya utpāda vādinaḥ tatra yaḥ utpāda vādī brūyāt dṛṣṭvā janayati iti sa vaktavyaḥ na dṛṣṭam etat loke yat bīja ādikam paśyati iti tasmāt ayuktāḥ eṣā kalpanā atha adṛṣṭvā kalpayet evam api yat kiṃcid adṛṣṭam saṃbhavati tat sarvam utpādayet na ca utpādayati tasmāt na adṛṣṭvā api janayati aniṣṭa āpattyā hi vayam para kalpanām vicārayāmaḥ saṃsāra aṭavī kāntāra giridarī prapāta duḥkham ālā samākulāmā tāmi iva buddhi pūrva kartṛkam ca puruṣādi kāraṇinaḥ jagat abhyupagacchantaḥ nirgranthāḥ ca eka indriyam bīja ādikam pratipannāḥ prasaṅgāt na vyativartante iti tasmāt na asti doṣaḥ 
[172,vii]	kim ca anyat yadi yuṣmad abhimatam hetoḥ phalasya ca anyonya ḍhaukana lakṣaṇam saṃgamanam syāt syāt tadānīm tayoḥ janya janaka bhāvaḥ yasmāt na hi paraspara asaṃgatayoḥ āloka andhakārayoḥ saṃsāra nirvāṇa yoḥ janya janaka bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti atas avaśyam hetu phala bhāvayoḥ janya janaka bhāvam icchatā pareṇa saṃgatiḥ abhyupeyā sā ca kāla traye api vicāryamāṇā na saṃbhavati atas hetuḥ phalam na janayati yathā ca saṃgatiḥ na asti tathā pratipādayan āha na atītasya hi atītena phalasya saha hetunā na ajātena na jātena saṃgatiḥ jātu vidyate 
[172,viii]	atītasya tāvat phalasya atītena hetunā saha jātu kadācid api saṃgatiḥ na asti atīta tvena ubhayoḥ api avidyamāna tvāt na api ajātena hetunā atītasya phalasya saṃgatiḥ jātu vidyate naṣṭa ajāta tvena ubhayoḥ api avidyamāna tvāt bhinna kāla tvāt ca na api jātena vartamānena hetunā saha atītasya phalasya saṃgatiḥ saṃbhavati bhinna kāla tvāt naṣṭasya ca phalasya avidyamāna tvāt vandhyā putreṇa iva devadattasya iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[173,i_173,ii]	yathā ca atītasya phalasya atītena anāgata vartamānena hetunā saha na kadācid saṃgatiḥ asti evam vartamānasya api phalasya traikālikena hetunā saha na asti saṃgatiḥ iti tat pratipādayan āha na jātasya hi ajātena phalasya saha hetunā na atītena na jātena saṃgatiḥ jātu vidyate jātasya phalasya bhinna kāla tvāt ajātena ca atītena ca hetunā saha saṃgamanam na asti na api vartamānasya vartamānena hetunā saha saṃgatiḥ asti hetu phalayoḥ yaugapadya abhāvāt tayoḥ ca saṃgatiḥ vaiyarthyāt kim hi vidyamānayoḥ paraspara nirapekṣayoḥ punar saṃgatyā prayojanam iti na asti saṃgatiḥ 
[173,iii_173,iv]	idānīm anāgatasya api phalasya yathā atīta anāgata pratyutpannena hetunā saha saṃgamanam na asti tathā pratipādayan āha na ajātasya hi jātena phalasya saha hetunā na ajātena na naṣṭena saṃgatiḥ jātu vidyate ajātam hi phalam asaṃvidyamānam tasya bhinna kālena vartamānena atītena ca hetunā saha na asti saṃgamanam bhinna kāla tvāt anāgatena api hetunā saha na asti saṃgamanam ubhayoḥ avidyamāna tvāt 
[173,v_173,viii]	yadā ca evam sarvathā hetu phalayoḥ saṃgatiḥ na asti tadā asatyām saṃgatau hetuḥ katham janayate phalam na eva hetuḥ phalam janayati saṃgateḥ avidyamāna tvāt vandhyā putram iva iti abhiprāyaḥ atha api syāt satyām eva saṃgatau hetuḥ phalam janayati iti tat api na yuktam kāla traye api saṃgati anupalabdheḥ atha api kathaṃcid hetu phalayoḥ saṃgatiḥ parikalpyate evam api satyām vā saṃgatau hetuḥ katham janayate phalam saṃnihitasya phalasya punar janma vaiyarthyāt asaṃhitānām ca saṃgateḥ ayukta tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[173,ix_173,x]	kim ca anyat hetuḥ phalena śūnyaḥ ced katham janayate phalam hetuḥ phalena aśūnyaḥ ced katham janayate phalam yaḥ ayam phalasya hetuḥ phalasya janakaḥ iṣyate sa tena śūnyaḥ vā bhavan phalam utpādayet aśūnyaḥ vā tatra hetuḥ śūnyaḥ phalena rahitaḥ phalam na janayati ahetu vat phala śūnya tvāt phalena aśūnyaḥ api hetuḥ phalam na janayati vidyamāna tvāt phalasya vidyamāna putram devadattaḥ iva evam tāvat phala śūnyaḥ vā phala aśūnyaḥ vā hetuḥ phalam na janayati 
[173,xi_174,i]	yat ca api phalam utpadyate tat ca api aśūnyam vā samutpadyate śūnyam vā tatra tāvat phalam na utpatsyate aśūnyam aśūnyam na nirotsyate aniruddham anutpannam aśūnyam tat bhaviṣyati aśūnyam hi phalam apratītya samutpannam svabhāva vyavasthitam tat evaṃvidham phalam na eva utpatsyate svabhāvasya anapāyi tvāt ca na nirotsyate tatas ca aśūnyam tad iṣyamāṇam aniruddham anutpannam ca syāt na ca etat iṣṭam iti atas aśūnyam tad phalam na bhavati utpāda nirodha abhyupagamāt 
[174,ii_174,iii]	idānīm śūnyam api tad phalam na saṃbhavati anudaya avyayavat tva prasaṅgāt iti pratipādayan āha katham utpatsyate śūnyam katham śūnyam nirotsyate śūnyam api aniruddham tat anutpannam prasajyate tatra śūnyam ucyate yat svabhāvena na asti yat ca vastu svabhāvena na asti tat katham utpatsyate katham vā nirotsyate na hi svabhāvena avidyamānasya ākāśa ādeḥ udaya vyayau dṛṣṭau tasmāt śūnyam api tad phalam iṣyamāṇam aniruddham anutpannam ca prasajyate 
[174,iv_174,v]	kim ca anyat yadi hetuḥ phalam janayet sa phalāt avyatiriktaḥ vā janayet vyatiriktaḥ vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha hetoḥ phalasya ca eka tvam na hi jātu upapadyate hetoḥ phalasya ca anya tvam na hi jātu upapadyate tat etat pratijñā mātrakam iti pratipādayan āha eka tve phala hetvoḥ syāt aikyam janaka janyayoḥ pṛthaktve phala hetvoḥ syāt tulyaḥ hetuḥ ahetunā 
[174,vi_174,vii]	yadi hetoḥ phalasya ca eka tvam syāt tadā janya janakayoḥ eka tvam abhyupetam syāt na ca anayoḥ ekatvam pitāputrayoḥ cakṣuḥ cakṣuḥ vijñānayoḥ bīja aṅkurayoḥ ca aikya prasaṅgāt evam tāvat hetoḥ phalasya ca eka tvam na asti idānīm anya tvam api na asti kim kāraṇam yadi hetoḥ phalasya ca bhavat matena abhimatam anya tvam syāt tadā paratra nirapekṣa tvāt hetu nirapekṣam eva phalam syāt na ca etat evam iti atas anya tvam api hetoḥ phalasya ca na saṃbhavati yayoḥ ca evam vicāryamāṇayoḥ tattva anya tve na staḥ tayoḥ na kadācid janya janaka bhāvaḥ iṣyate atas na eva hetuḥ phalam janayati 
[174,viii_174,ix]	kim ca anyat yadi hetuḥ phalam janayet sa tad phalam svabhāvena sadbhūtam vā janayet asat bhūtam vā ubhayathā ca na yujyate iti āha phalam svabhāva sadbhūtam kim hetuḥ janayiṣyati phalam svabhāvāsadbhūtam kim hetuḥ janayiṣyati tatra yat phalam svabhāvena sadbhūtam svabhāvena vidyamānam tat na punar janyate vidyamāna tvāt vidyamāna ghaṭa vat yat api svabhāvena asat bhūtam phalam tat api hetuḥ na janayati svabhāvena asat bhūta tvāt khara viṣāṇa vat 
[175,i_175,ii]	pratibimbena anaikāntika tā iti ced bhavatu anaikāntika tā naiḥsvābhāvyam tu siddham bhāvānām tatas ca sa svabhāva vāda tyāgaḥ syāt asmad vāda anuvarṇanam eva syāt sa svabhāvaḥ ca na kaścid padārthaḥ nāma asti iti pratidvan dvaya bhāvāt niḥsvabhāvaḥ api padārthaḥ na asti iti kutas anaikāntika tā na hi asmākam pratibimbakam sa svabhāvam na api niḥsvabhāvam dharmiṇam antareṇa tad dharmayoḥ api abhāvāt na hi āryāḥ pratibimbakam nāma kiṃcid niḥsvabhāvam sa svabhāvam vā upalabhante iti tatra pūrvam phalam na utpatsyate ityādinā śloka dvayena sākṣāt utpatti kriyā kartṛ tvam phalasya niṣiddham idānīm hetoḥ phala utpatti kriyā prayojaka tvam pratiṣiddham iti ayam asya pūrvakāt viśeṣaḥ iti vijñeyam 
[175,iii_175,iv]	atra āha yadi api hetoḥ phala utpatti kriyā prayojaka tvam niṣiddham tathā api hetuḥ tāvat svabhāvataḥ asti na ca asati phale hetoḥ hetu tvam sidhyati tasmāt phalam api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate syāt hetuḥ yadi ajanayataḥ asya hetu tvam syāt na ca ajanayamānasya hetu tvam upapadyate atha syāt yadi api evam hetoḥ hetu tvam na asti tathā api phalam tāvat asti na ca hetum antareṇa phalam yuktam iti phala sadbhāvāt hetuḥ api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate yadā ajanayamānasya hetoḥ hetu tvam na asti iti uktam tadā hetutva anupapattau ca phalam kasya bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt phalam api na asti iti 
[175,v]	atra āha na eva hi kevalasya hetoḥ phala utpatti kriyāyāḥ prayojaka tvam kim tarhi hetu pratyaya sāmagryā phalam janyate iti ucyate ukta doṣa tvāt na yuktam etat api ca iyam hetu pratyaya sāmagrī yadi phalasya janikā iti kalpyate kim sa asvayam eva tāvat ātmānam janayati uta aho na yadi janayati iti kalpyate tat na yujyate na hi alabdha ātma bhāvasya prayojaka tvam dṛṣṭam iti atas sāmagryāḥ avaśyam labdha ātma bhāvayā bhavitavyam na ca labdha ātma bhāvāyāḥ punar sva ātma utpāde prayojaka tvam yuktam iti atas na sāmagrī sva ātmānam utpādayati yā ca ātmānam na utpādayati sā katham phalam utpādayitum śaknoti iti pratipādayan āha na ca pratyaya hetūnām iyam ātmānam ātmanā yā sāmagrī janayate sā katham janayet phalam 
[175,vi]	pratyayānām hetūnām ca yā iyam sāmagrī sā tāvat ātmanā eva ātmānam na utpādayati sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt satyāḥ punar utpāda vaiyarthyāt ca yā ca evam ātmānam eva tāvat na janayati sā katham phalam janayiṣyati na hi bandhyā duhitā ātmānam janayitum aśaktā satī putram janayiṣyati iti yujyate evam sāmagrī api sva ātmā ajanikā phalam janayati iti na yujyate 
[176,i_176,iii]	tasmāt na sāmagrī kṛtam phalam atha api syāt yadi sāmagrī kṛtam phalam na saṃbhavati evam tarhi asāmagrīkṛtam bhaviṣyati iti ced ucyate na āsāmagrīkṛtam phalam yadā sāmagrī kṛtam phalam na saṃbhavati tadā katham atyanta viruddham asām agrīkṛtam bhaviṣyati asāmagrīkṛtam phalam na saṃbhavati 
[176,iv]	atha syāt yadi api na asti phalam svabhāvataḥ tathā api hetu pratyaya sāmagrī tāvat asti na ca phalam antareṇa hetu pratyaya sāmagrī saṃbhavati iti phalam api saṃbhaviṣyati iti ucyate syāt hetu pratyaya sāmagrī yadi phalam eva bhavet yadā tu yathā uditena nyāyena phalam eva na asti tadā asti pratyaya sāmagrī kutas eva phalam vinā 
[176,v]	phala abhāve sati nirhetukā hetu pratyaya sāmagrī api na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ uktam hi ārya lalita vistara sūtre kaṇṭha uṣṭha pratītya tālukam jihva parivarti ravanti akṣarāḥ na ca kaṇṭha gatā na tāluke akṣara eka ekaśa na upalabhyate sāmagri pratītyatas ca sā vāca mana buddhi vaśena niścarī mana vāca adṛśya rūpiṇī bāhyatas abhyantari na upalabhyate utpāda vyayam vipaśyataḥ vācaruta ghoṣa svarasya paṇḍitaḥ kṣaṇikām vaśikām tadā dṛśī sarva vāca pratiśrutakopamā 
[176,vi]	tathā āryopāli paripṛcchāyām uktam bhagavatā iha śāsani sūramaṇīye pravrajathā gṛhiliṅga jahitvā phalavantu bhaviṣyatha śreṣṭhāḥ eṣu nideśitu kāruṇikena pravrajitva gṛhiliṅga jahitvā sarva phalasya bhaviṣyati prāptiḥ puna dharma sabhāva tulitvā sarva phalāna phalāna ca prāptiḥ alabhanta phalam tatha prāptim āścariyam puna jāyati teṣām aho atikāruṇikaḥ narasiṃhaḥ suṣṭupadeśita yukti jinena iti 
[177,i_177,ii]	tathā ārya prajñāpāramitāyām aṣṭa sāhasrikāyām tena hi kauśika bodhisattvena mahāsattvena mahā saṃnāha saṃnaddhena na rūpe sthātavyam na vedanāyām na saṃjñāyām na saṃskāreṣu na vijñāne sthātavyam na srotaāpatti phale na sakṛdāgāmi phale na anāgāmi phale na arhat tve na pratyekabuddha tve na samyaksaṃbuddha tve sthātavyam iti 
[178,i]	atra āha vidyate eva svabhāvataḥ kālaḥ saṃbhava vibhava nimitta tvāt iha kaṃcid kāla viśeṣam apekṣya aṅkura utpattiḥ bhāvānām utpādaḥ bhavati kaṃcid kāla viśeṣam apekṣya vibhavaḥ vināśaḥ bhavati na sarvadā vidyamānāyām api hetu pratyaya sāmagryām iti atas vidyate eva kālaḥ saṃbhava vibhava nimittattvāt ucyate syāt saṃbhava vibhava nimitta tā kālasya yadi saṃbhava vibhavau eva syātām na tu staḥ yathā ca na staḥ tathā pratipādayan āha vinā vā saha vā na asti vibhavaḥ saṃbhavena vai vinā vā saha vā na asti saṃbhavaḥ vibhavena vai 
[178,ii]	iha yadi saṃbhava vibhavau syātām tau anyonyam saha bhāvena vā syātām vinā abhāvena vā ubhayathā ca vicāryamāṇau na saṃbhavataḥ katham kṛtvā tatra tāvat yathā vinā saṃbhavena utpādena vibhavaḥ vināśaḥ na asti tathā pratipādayan āha bhaviṣyati katham nāma vibhavaḥ saṃbhavam vinā vinā eva janma maraṇam vibhavaḥ na udbhavam vinā 
[178,iii]	saṃbhavam vinā katham nāma vibhavaḥ vināśaḥ bhaviṣyati katham nāma iti anena prasiddham atyanta asaṃbhavam darśayati katham nāma bhaviṣyati na eva etat saṃbhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ yadi punar vinā eva saṃbhavam vibhavaḥ syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ syāt ucyate vinā eva janma maraṇam syāt ajātasya maraṇam syāt na ca ajātasya maraṇam dṛṣṭam iti tasmāt vibhavaḥ na udbhavam vinā bhavitum arhati ādyena atra ślokasya ardhena pratijñā madhyena pādena prasaṅga āpādanam antyena nigamanam iti vijñeyam 
[178,iv_178,v]	evam tāvat vinā saṃbhavena vibhavaḥ na yuktaḥ iti pratipādya idānīm saha saṃbhavena api vibhavaḥ na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha saṃbhavena eva vibhavaḥ katham saha bhaviṣyati na janma maraṇam ca evam tulya kālam hi vidyate yadi hi saṃbhavena saha yugapad tulya kālam vibhavaḥ syāt evam sati janma maraṇe yugapad syātām na ca evam paraspara viruddhe āloka andhakāra vat ekasmin kāle vidyete iti tasmāt saha api saṃbhavena vibhavasya na asti siddhiḥ iti sthitam 
[178,vi_179,i]	yadā ca evam saṃbhavena vinā vā saha vā vibhavasya na asti siddhiḥ evam saṃbhavasya api vinā vā saha vā vibhavena na asti siddhiḥ iti pratipādayan āha bhaviṣyati katham nāma saṃbhavaḥ vibhavam vinā anitya tā hi bhāveṣu na kadācid na vidyate na eva hi saṃbhavaḥ vibhavena vinā yujyate yasmāt anitya tā hi bhāveṣu bhavana dharmakeṣu utpāda dharmakeṣu na kadācid na vidyate kim tarhi sarvadā eva vidyate uktam hi jarā maraṇa dharmeṣu sarva bhāveṣu sarvadā tiṣṭhanti katame bhāvāḥ ye jarā maraṇam vinā iti yadā ca evam nityam anitya tā anugatāḥ sarve bhāvāḥ tadā kutas sā kācid avasthā yā vināśa rahitā syāt iti atas na asti vibhavena vinā utpādaḥ iti evam tāvat vinā vibhavena na asti saṃbhavaḥ śeṣam atra saṃskṛta parīkṣāyām vicāri tattvāt na vicāryate 
[179,ii_179,iii]	yaḥ tu sa hetukaḥ vināśaḥ saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tvāt utpāda vat iti sādhanam utkṣipya antya citta caittakṣaṇaiḥ anaikāntika tām āha sa na yuktam āha tad vināśasya api jāti pratyaya tvena sa hetuka tvāt sādhya sama tvāt ca anaikāntika tā bhāvāt yat api nirdiṣṭam bhāva ātma bhāvaḥ eva abhūtvā bhāvāt utpādaḥ ucyate tasmāt dravya sat utpāda siddheḥ vyavahārataḥ dṛṣṭānta bhāvaḥ iti tat api na yuktam adravyasatām pratibimba ādīnām sa hetuka tva abhyupagamāt yathā uktam ācārya pādaiḥ hetutaḥ saṃbhavaḥ yeṣām tad abhāvāt na santi ye katham nāma na te spaṣṭam pratibimba samāḥ matāḥ iti asmāt āgamāt kutas vyavahārataḥ dṛṣṭānta asiddhiḥ yadi ca bhāvāt yat tattva anya tvena na śakyate vaktum tat saṃvṛtya api na asti iti ucyate nīla ādikam api na asti iti ucyate yathā uktam ratnāvalyām rūpasya abhāva mātra tvāt ākāśam nāma mātrakam bhūtaiḥ vinā kutas rūpam nāma mātrakam api atas iti 
[179,iv]	api ca kutas mādhyamikānām svabhāva rūpam siddha sattākam yasya avasthā viśeṣaḥ utpādaḥ syāt atas ayuktam eva dṛṣṭānta asiddha tā udbhāvanam yat ca uktam na sa hetukaḥ vināśaḥ avināśavat tvāt yathā asaṃskṛtam iti tasya evam bruvataḥ mahāntam virodha mayam hetuḥ ābhavati yathā hi ayam hetuḥ vināśasya nirhetuka tvam sādhayati evam saṃskṛta lakṣaṇa tva abhāvam api sādhayati tathā saṃskāra skandha saṃgraha pratītya samutpāda aṅga saṃgraha ādikam api sarvam virodhayati iti na yuktam etat matam tathā na vijñānam viṣaya svarūpa chedakam avijñānavat tvāt asaṃskṛta vat ityādinā sarva niṣedhāt mahatī aniṣṭāpattiḥ upapadyate asya iti na āstheyam etat 
[179,v_179,vi]	idānīm vibhavena saha yathā saṃbhavasya na asti siddhiḥ tathā pratipādayan āha saṃbhavaḥ vibhavena eva katham saha bhaviṣyati na janma maraṇam ca eva tulya kālam hi vidyate yadi hi saṃbhavaḥ vibhavena eva saha syāt tadā janma maraṇayoḥ tulya kālatā syāt na ca sā saṃbhavati tasmāt sahabhāvena api saṃbhava vibhavayoḥ na asti siddhiḥ 
[180,i_180,ii]	atha syāt yadi api janma maraṇayoḥ ekībhāvena vā nānā bhāvena vā na asti siddhiḥ tathā api vidyete eva saṃbhava vibhavau vācya tvāt vijñāna vat iti ucyate yadi vācya tvena anayoḥ siddhiḥ iṣyate vandhyā putrasya api iṣyatām api ca saha anyonyena vā siddhiḥ vinā anyonyena vā yayoḥ na vidyate tayoḥ siddhiḥ katham nu khalu vidyate 
[180,iii]	sahabhāva asahabhāva rahitam na asti pakṣa antaram yatas saṃbhava vibhavayoḥ siddhiḥ syāt avācya tayā siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced kā iyam avācya tā nāma yadi miśrībhāvaḥ saḥ anupapannaḥ pṛthak pṛthak asiddhayaḥ miśrībhāva abhāvāt anirdhāryamāṇau svarūpa tvāt bandhyā putra śyāma gaura tā ādi vat na staḥ eva saṃbhava vibhavau iti yadā ca evam saṃbhava vibhavau na staḥ tadā tad hetuḥ api kālaḥ na asti iti siddham 
[180,iv_180,v]	kim ca anyat iha imau saṃbhava vibhavau parikalpyamānau kṣaya dharmiṇaḥ vā bhāvasya parikalpyeyātām akṣaya dharmiṇaḥ vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti pratipādayan āha kṣayasya saṃbhavaḥ na asti na akṣayasya api saṃbhavaḥ kṣayasya vibhavaḥ na asti vibhavaḥ na akṣayasya ca tatra kṣayasya kṣaya lakṣaṇasya bhāvasya virodhi dharma sadbhāvāt saṃbhavaḥ na yuktaḥ akṣayasya api bhāva lakṣaṇa viyukta tvāt khara viṣāṇasya iva saṃbhavaḥ na yuktaḥ evam kṣayasya vibhavaḥ na asti kṣaya dharmaḥ hi avidyamānaḥ tasya nirāśrayaḥ vibhavaḥ na yuktaḥ tathā vibhavaḥ na akṣayasya ca akṣaya dharmaḥ hi bhāva abhāva lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇaḥ tasya avidyamānasya kutas vibhavaḥ bhaviṣyati yau ca saṃbhava vibhavau na kṣaya dharmiṇaḥ na akṣaya dharmiṇaḥ bhāvasya saṃbhavataḥ tau na saṃbhavataḥ iti na staḥ saṃbhava vibhavau 
[180,vi]	atra āha vidyete eva bhāvānām saṃbhava vibhavau tad āśrayi dharmi sadbhāvāt iha bhāva āśrayau saṃbhava vibhavau sa ca tāvat bhāvaḥ asti tad sadbhāvāt tad āśritau api dharmau bhaviṣyataḥ iti ucyate syātām bhāva āśritau etau dharmau yadi bhāvaḥ syāt yadā tu bhāvaḥ na asti tadā saṃbhavaḥ vibhavaḥ ca eva vinā bhāvam na vidyate 
[180,vii_180,viii]	kasmāt punarbhāvaḥ na asti iti ced yasmāt saṃbhavam vibhavam ca eva vinā bhāvaḥ na vidyate bhāvasya hi lakṣaṇa bhūtau saṃbhava vibhavau tau ca svarūpataḥ na staḥ iti pratiṣiddhau yadā ca tau bhāvataḥ pratiṣiddhau tadā bhāva lakṣaṇam saṃbhavam vibhavam ca vinā kutas bhāva lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇaḥ bhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati bhāvam ca vinā na staḥ saṃbhava vibhavau 
[180,ix_181,ii]	apare tu pūrva ardham paścimam kṛtvā vyācakṣate staḥ eva saṃbhava vibhavau bhāva dharma tvāt iha yat na asti na tasya asti bhāva dharma tvam tat yathā maṇḍūka jaṭā śiromaṇeḥ bhāva dharmau ca saṃbhava vibhavau tasmāt staḥ eva tau iti yadi kasyacid paramārthataḥ saṃbhava vibhavau syātām sa bhāvaḥ iti yuktam syāt abhidhātum tau ca na staḥ iti saṃbhavam vibhavam ca eva vinā bhāvaḥ na vidyate bhāvasya saṃbhava vibhava sattve vidyamāna tvāt iti bhāvaḥ tat asattve ca hetoḥ asiddhārtha tā tathā saṃbhavaḥ vibhavaḥ ca eva vinā bhāvam na vidyate āśrayasya abhāvāt āśritasya asiddhiḥ iti abhisaṃdhiḥ iti 
[181,iii_181,v]	kim ca anyat iha imau saṃbhava vibhavau parikalpamānau śūnyasya vā bhāvasya parikalpyeyātām aśūnyasya vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti pratipādayan āha saṃbhavaḥ vibhavaḥ ca eva na śūnyasya upapadyate avidyamāna āśraya tvāt ākāśa citra vat iti abhiprāyaḥ tathā saṃbhavaḥ vibhavaḥ ca eva na aśūni asya upapadyate aśūnyasya asattvāt nirāśrayau saṃbhava vibhavau na upapadyataḥ 
[181,vi_181,ix]	kim ca anyat iha yadi saṃbhava vibhavau syātām tau eka tvena vā syātām anya tvena vā ubhayathā ca na upapadyate iti āha saṃbhavaḥ vibhavaḥ ca eva na ekaḥ iti upapadyate paraspara viruddhayoḥ āloka andhakārayoḥ iva ekatva anupapatteḥ saṃbhavaḥ vibhavaḥ ca eva na nānā iti upapadyate ubhayoḥ parasparam avyabhicāri tvāt na hi saṃbhava rahitasya vināśaḥ na vibhava rahitasya saṃbhavaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti evam ubhayoḥ parasparam avyabhicāri tvāt saṃbhavaḥ vibhavaḥ ca eva na nānā iti upapadyate 
[181,x_181,xi]	atha syāt kim anayā sūkṣma īkṣikayā āgopāla aṅganā ādikaḥ hi janaḥ yasmāt saṃbhavam vibhavam ca paśyati tasmāt staḥ saṃbhava vibhavau na hi avidyamānaḥ vandhyā tanayaḥ śakyaḥ draṣṭum iti evam api dṛśyate saṃbhavaḥ ca eva vibhavaḥ ca eva te bhavet ucyate anaikāntikam etat na hi yat yat lokena upalabhyate tasya tasya astitvam tathā hi āgopāla aṅganā ādikaḥ janaḥ gandharvanagara māyāsvapna alāta cakra marīcikā salila ādikam avidyamānam api paśyati indriya upaghātāt evam imau api saṃbhava vibhavau asantau mohāt eva paśyati iti āha dṛśyate saṃbhavaḥ ca eva mohāt vibhavaḥ eva ca 
[181,xii]	atha kasmāt punar etat evam niścīyate avidyamāna svarūpau imau saṃbhava vibhavau mohāt eva vāra lokena dṛśyete iti yuktyā hi etat evam niścīyate kā punar atra yuktiḥ iha yadi kaścid bhāvaḥ nāma bhavet niyatam sa bhāvāt vā jāyeta abhāvāt vā tathā yadi abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid saḥ api bhāvāt vā jāyeta abhāvāt vā ubhayathā ca ubhayoḥ api asaṃbhavaḥ iti āha na bhāvāt jāyate bhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ abhāvāt na jāyate na abhāvāt jāyate abhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ bhāvāt na jāyate 
[182,i]	bhāvāt tāvat saṃbhava ākhyāt bhāvasya saṃbhava ākhyasya utpādaḥ na vidyate kārya kāraṇayoḥ yaugapadya abhāvāt utpādasya ca labdha janmanaḥ punar utpāda vaiyarthyāt abhāvāt api bhāvaḥ na jāyate kim kāraṇam abhāvaḥ hi nāma vibhavaḥ vināśaḥ sa ca bhāva viruddhaḥ tasmāt bhāva viruddhāt katham bhāvaḥ syāt yadi syāt tadā vandhyā duhituḥ api putraḥ syāt na ca etat evam iti tasmāt abhāvāt api bhāvaḥ na bhavati idānīm abhāvaḥ api abhāvāt na bhavati bhāva nivṛtti rūpaḥ hi abhāvaḥ tatas kutas asya kārya karaṇa sāmarthyam yadi syāt nirvāṇasya api kārya karaṇa sāmarthyam syāt yadi ca abhāvāt abhāvaḥ syāt tadā vandhyā duhituḥ api putraḥ syāt na ca etat evam iti tasmāt abhāvāt api abhāvaḥ na bhavati idānīm bhāvāt api abhāvaḥ na bhavati bhāva viruddhaḥ hi abhāvaḥ sa katham bhāvāt bhavet yadi bhavet pradīpāt andhakāraḥ syāt yatas ca evam vicāryamāṇau saṃbhava vibhavau na staḥ tasmāt mohāt eva lokena dṛśyete iti vijñeyam 
[182,ii_182,iii]	athavā ayam anyaḥ pūrva pakṣaḥ iha hi yadi saṃbhava vibhavau syātām tau bhāva āśrayau vā syātām abhāva āśrayau vā tau ca bhāva abhāvau sarvathā vicāryamāṇau na saṃbhavataḥ tatas ca kutas nirāśrayau saṃbhava vibhavau iti atas dṛśyate saṃbhavaḥ ca eva mohāt vibhavaḥ eva ca iti vijñeyam yathā ca bhāva abhāvau na saṃbhavataḥ tathā pratipādayan āha na bhāvāt jāyate bhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ abhāvāt na jāyate na abhāvāt jāyate abhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ bhāvāt na jāyate asya arthaḥ pūrvavat 
[182,iv_182,v]	api ca yadi kaścid bhāvaḥ nāma syāt tasya udayavyayavat tvāt saṃbhava vibhavau syātām na ca kaścid bhāvaḥ svarūpataḥ asti khara viṣāṇa vat svabhāva an utpanna tvāt anutpanna tvam asiddham iti ced tat siddham yasmāt na svatas jāyate bhāvaḥ paratas na eva jāyate na svatas paratas ca eva jāyate jāyate kutas etat ca ādyaḥ eva prakaraṇe vyākhyā tattvāt na punar vyākhyāyate yaḥ ca evam yathā ukta prakāreṇa jāyate saḥ idānīm kutas jāyate na eva kutaścid jāyate iti abhiprāyaḥ avaśyam ca etat evam abhyupeyam sarvathā na asti bhāvasya utpādaḥ iti 
[182,vi_183,i]	bhāva sadbhāvatā abhyupagame ca bhavataḥ śāśvata uccheda darśanam āpadyate bauddha mata anugasya iti āha bhāvam abhyupapannasya śāśvata uccheda darśanam prasajyate yasmāt sa bhāvaḥ hi nityaḥ anityaḥ atha vā bhavet yaḥ hi yathā udita padārtha vyavasthām atikramya bhāva sadbhāva darśanam abhyupaiti tasya avaśyam pravacana atyanta viruddham śāśvata uccheda darśana dvayam āpadyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt sa bhāvaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ nityaḥ vā bhavet anityaḥ vā yadi nityaḥ tadā niyatam śāśvata vādaḥ atha anityaḥ tadā niyatam ucchedaḥ iti 
[183,ii_183,iv]	atra āha bhāvam abhyupapannasya na eva ucchedaḥ na śāśvatam kim kāraṇam yasmāt udaya vyaya saṃtānaḥ phala hetvoḥ bhavaḥ sa hi yaḥ hi hetu phalayoḥ udaya vyaya anuprabandhaḥ sa hi asmākam bhavaḥ saṃsāraḥ tatra yadi hetuḥ nirudhyeta tad hetukam phalam na utpadyeta tadā syāt uccheda vāda doṣaḥ yadi ca hetuḥ na nirudhyeta svarūpeṇa avatiṣṭhet tadā syāt śāśvata vāda darśana doṣaḥ na ca etat evam iti tasmāt bhāva abhyupagame api na asti śāśvata uccheda darśana doṣa dvaya prasaṅgaḥ saḥ eva saṃsāraḥ yaḥ ayam hetu phalā vicchinna krama vartī utpāda vyaya anuprabandhaḥ saṃskārāṇām iti atas na asti asmāka mayam doṣaḥ iti 
[183,v_183,vii]	ucyate udaya vyaya saṃtānaḥ phala hetvoḥ bhavaḥ sa ced nanu evam api vyayasya apunarutpatteḥ hetu ucchedaḥ prasajyate yaḥ hi hetu kṣaṇaḥ phalasya utpattau hetu bhāvam upetya nirudhyate nanu tasya vyayavataḥ hetu kṣaṇasya punar anutpādāt uccheda darśanam āpadyate tava ayam katham na doṣaḥ iti ced bhāvam abhyupapannasya ayam doṣaḥ na ca mayā bhāvaḥ abhyupagataḥ svabhāva anutpanna tvāt sarva dharmāṇām yatra api mayā pratītya yat yat bhavati na hi tāvat tat eva tat na ca anyat api tat tasmāt na ucchedaḥ na api śāśvatam iti uktam tatra api amunā nyāyena naiḥsvābhāvyam eva bhāvānām pratipāditam anyathā hi sati bhāva svarūpe bīja aṅkurayoḥ katham anya tvam na syāt tasmāt na ayam prasaṅgaḥ asmākam bādhakaḥ iti 
[183,viii_184,i]	evam tāvat bhāvam abhyupapannasya hetoḥ punar anutpādāt uccheda darśana prasaṅgam udbhāvyaḥ idānīm śāśvata vāde doṣa prasaṅgam udbhāvayan āha sadbhāvasya svabhāvena na asadbhāvaḥ ca yujyate yadi hi hetoḥ sadbhāvaḥ svabhāvataḥ syāt tasya paścāt asadbhāvaḥ na syāt svabhāvasyāḥ napāyi tvāt tatas ca śāśvata darśana prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva kim ca anyat nirvāṇa kāle ca ucchedaḥ praśamāt bhava saṃtateḥ 
[184,ii]	yadi api hetu phalayoḥ udaya vyaya saṃtāna pravṛttyā śāśvata uccheda darśana prasaṅgaḥ parihriyate tathā api yatra asya saṃtānasya punar api apravṛttiḥ tatra nirvāṇe niyatam uccheda darśanam āpadyate uccheda darśanam ca prahātavyam iti uktam bhagavatā evaṃvidham uccheda darśanam na bhaviṣyati iti ced anyat api kimartham bhavatā bhaviṣyati iti bhāva viccheda ālambana tvāt nirvāṇa kāle bhāva viccheda ālambana vat iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[184,iii_184,iv]	yat ca uktam udaya vyaya saṃtānaḥ phala hetvoḥ bhavaḥ sa hi iti tat api na upapadyate katham kṛtvā iha hi caramaḥ bhavaḥ nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ prathamaḥ gati pratisaṃdhi lakṣaṇaḥ tatra caramaḥ bhavaḥ nirudhyamānaḥ hetu tvena avatiṣṭhate upapatti lakṣaṇaḥ tu prathamaḥ bhavaḥ phala rūpa tvena vyavatiṣṭhate anayoḥ ca bhavayoḥ saṃsāraḥ iti saṃjñā kṛtā 
[184,v]	atra ca idam vicāryate yaḥ eṣa prathamaḥ bhavaḥ phala rūpa tvena vyavasthāpyate sa kim carame bhave niruddhe upajāyate atha aniruddhe uta nirudhyamāne yatas hetu phala anuprabandhāt saṃsāraḥ syāt sarvathā ca vicāryamāṇaḥ na saṃbhavati iti pratipādayan āha carame na niruddhe ca prathamaḥ yujyate bhavaḥ carame na aniruddhe ca prathamaḥ yujyate bhavaḥ 
[184,vi_184,vii]	tatra yadi carame bhave niruddhe prathamaḥ bhavaḥ jāyate iti parikalpyate tadā nirhetuka syāt dahana dagdha bījāt api aṅkura udayaḥ syāt na ca etat iṣṭam tasmāt carame niruddhe prathamaḥ bhavaḥ na yujyate idānīm aniruddhe api carame bhave prathamaḥ bhavaḥ na yujyate yadi syāt nirhetukaḥ syāt dvi rūpa tā ca ekasya sattvasya syāt apūrva sattva prādurbhāvaḥ ca pūrvasya ca nityatā syāt avinaṣṭe ca bīje aṅkura udayaḥ syāt na ca etat evam iṣṭam iti atas carame na aniruddhe ca prathamaḥ yujyate bhavaḥ iti sthitam 
[184,viii_184,ix]	idānīm nirudhyamāne api carame bhave prathamaḥ bhavaḥ yathā na upapadyate tathā pratipādayan āha nirudhyamāne carame prathamaḥ yadi jāyate nirudhyamānaḥ ekaḥ syāt jāyamānaḥ aparaḥ bhavet tatra nirudhyamānaḥ vartamānaḥ vartamāna pratyaya anta vācya tvāt jāyate iti api vartamānaḥ eva ucyate vartamāna śabda vācya tvāt athavā nirudhyamānaḥ nirodha kriyā kārakaḥ yaḥ ca api jāyate asau api jani kriyā kārakaḥ tau ca eka kāla āviṣyamāṇau yaugapadyena eva staḥ tatas ca nirudhyamānaḥ ekaḥ bhavaḥ syāt jāyamānaḥ ca aparaḥ iti yaugapadyena eva dvau bhavau prāpnutaḥ na ca ekasya yugapad dvau bhavau saṃbhavataḥ iti uktam etat 
[185,i_185,ii]	tat evam yathā uktena vicāra kameṇa na ced nirudhyamānaḥ ca jāyamānaḥ ca yujyate sārdham ca mriyate yeṣu teṣu skandheṣu jāyate caśabdaḥ samuccaya arthaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ca iti etat saṃnidhāpayati yadā evam yathā udita nyāyena niruddhe carame prathamaḥ bhavaḥ na saṃbhavati aniruddhe api carame prathamaḥ bhavaḥ na saṃbhavati sārdham ca ekasmiḥ ca kāle caramena bhavena saha prathamaḥ bhavaḥ na saṃbhavati tat kim idānīm yeṣu eva skandheṣu mriyate teṣu eva jāyate iti syāt yeṣu skandheṣu sthitaḥ mriyate teṣu eva jāyate iti atyanta viruddham etat na hi mriyamāṇaḥ jāyate iti dṛṣṭam 
[185,iii_185,vi]	tat evam triṣu api kāleṣu na yuktā bhavat abhimatā bhava saṃtatiḥ carame bhave niruddhe aniruddhe nirudhyamāne yasmāt prathamaḥ bhavaḥ na saṃbhavati tasmāt triṣu api kāleṣu bhavasaṃtirnā asti triṣu kāleṣu yā na asti sā katham bhava saṃtatiḥ yā ca idānīm triṣu kāleṣu na asti kutas sā anyena ātmanā bhaviṣyati iti sarvathā na asti bhavat matā bhava saṃtatiḥ tatas ca yat uktam udaya vyaya saṃtānaḥ phala hetvoḥ bhavaḥ sa hi iti tat na yuktam tatas ca bhāva abhyupagame sati saḥ eva śāśvata uccheda vāda prasaṅgaḥ durnivāraḥ bhavatām iti atas na asti eva bhāvānām svabhāvataḥ utpattiḥ iti siddham yathā uktam ārya samādhi rāja bhaṭṭārake 
[185,vii_186,ii]	tathā bījasya sataḥ yathā aṅkuraḥ na ca yaḥ bīju sa ca eva aṅkuraḥ na ca anyu tatas na ca eva tat evam anuccheda aśāśvata dharma tā mudrāt pratimudra dṛśyate mudra saṃkrānti na ca upalabhyate na ca tatra na ca eva sā anyatas evam saṃskāra anuccheda śāśvatāḥ atas eva uktam ārya nāgārjuna pādaiḥ svādhyāya dīpa mudrā darpaṇa ghoṣa arka kānta bījāmraiḥ skandha pratisaṃdhiḥ asaṃkramaḥ ca vidvadbhiḥ avadhāryau iti tathā bhagavān jāyate cyavate ca api na ca jātiḥ na ca cyutiḥ yasya vijānataḥ eṣa samādhiḥ na asya durlabhaḥ iti 
[186,iii]	tathā sū sukhitā sada te nara loke yehi acintiya jñātibhi dharmāḥ na ca dharmaḥ adharma vikalpaḥ citta papañca vibhāvita sarvi bhāva abhāva vibhāvayi jñānam sarvam acintayi sarvam abhūtam ye puna citta vaśa anuga bālāḥ te dukhitā bhava koṭi śateṣu yaḥ api ca cintayi śūnyaka dharmān saḥ api kumārga papannaku bālaḥ akṣara kīrtita śūnyaka dharmāḥ te ca anakṣara akṣaraḥ uktāḥ śānta paśānta yaḥ cintayi dharmān saḥ api ca cittu na jātu na bhūtaḥ citta vitarkaṇa sarvi papañcāḥ sūkṣma acintiya budhyatha dharmān iti 
[187,i^1]	atra āha vidyate eva bhava saṃtatiḥ tathāgata sadbhāvāt iha hi bhagavatā mahā karuṇa upāya prajñā dvaya dhāriṇā sakala traidhātuka aśeṣa sattva jāti ādi duḥkha vyupaśama eka manasā tribhiḥ kalpa asaṃkhyeyaiḥ saptabhiḥ vā nairantarya krameṇa udyacchatā taiḥ taiḥ niratiśayaiḥ ati vicitraiḥ puṇya kriyā prārambhaiḥ sakala jagat hita udaya eka kriyā lakṣaṇaiḥ priya eka putrāt api adhikatara niravaśeṣa jagat anugraha tatpareṇa mahā karuṇā para vaśena tatra tatra upapatti āyatane kṣiti salila jvalana pavana sādhāraṇa bhaiṣajya mahā mahīruha vat janānām sva icchāte upabhogya tām ātmānam upagamayatā mahākālena sārvajñam sarva ākāra paricchedi padam adhigatam saḥ evam adhigata sarvajña jñānaḥ bhagavān yathā dharmāṇām tattvam vyavasthitam tathā eva aśeṣatas gata tvāt buddha tvāt tathāgataḥ iti ucyate yadi bhava saṃtatiḥ na syāt tadā tathāgataḥ api na syāt na hi ekena janmanā śakyam tathāgata tvam anuprāptum 
[187,i^2]	tasmāt vidyate eva bhava saṃtatiḥ tathāgata sadbhāvāt iti ucyate bhavadīyam eva hi idam ati mahat ajñānam bhava saṃtānasya aviccheda vartitām ca ati dīrgha kālam ca gamayati yasya nāma bhavataḥ ati mahat ajñāna dhana andhakāram eva vicitraiḥ upapatti śarad candra jñāna ālokaiḥ vidhvasyamānam api ati ciratara kāla abhyāsa vāsanā vistara abhivṛddham adya api na vidhvasyate na nivartate yadi hi tathāgataḥ nāma kaścid syāt svabhāvataḥ tadā tasya mahatā kālena abhiniṣpatteḥ bhava saṃtatiḥ syāt na ca tathāgataḥ nāma kaścid bhāva svabhāvataḥ upalabhyate kevalam tu bhavān avidyā timira upahatam ati nayana tayā dvi candra keśa maśaka ādi vat mithyā tathāgatam nāma svabhāvataḥ upalabhate yathā ca tathāgataḥ na asti svabhāvataḥ tathā pratipādayan āha skandhāḥ na na anyaḥ skandhebhyaḥ na asmin skandhāḥ na teṣu saḥ tathāgataḥ skandhavān na katamaḥ atra tathāgataḥ 
[187,ii]	yadi hi tathāgataḥ nāma kaścid padārthaḥ amalaḥ niṣprapañcaḥ syāt sa skandha svabhāvaḥ vā bhavet rūpa vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra vijñāna ākhya skandha pañcaka svabhāvaḥ vā bhavet yadi vā śīla samādhi prajñā vimukti vimukti jñāna darśana ākhya pañca skandha svabhāvaḥ tadvayatiriktaḥ vā bhavet pūrvakāḥ eva pañca skandhāḥ sattva prajñapti nimitta tvāt iha vicāre parigṛhyante na uttare avyāpaka tvāt eṣām pūrvakaiḥ antarbhāvita tvāt iti 
[187,iii]	yadi vā pañca skandha vyatiriktaḥ bhavet tatra tathāgate vā skandhāḥ syuḥ skandheṣu vā sa bhavet tathāgataḥ vā skandhavān bhavet dhanavān iva devadattaḥ sarvathā ca vicāryamāṇaḥ na saṃbhavati katham kṛtvā tatra tāvat skandhāḥ eva na tathāgataḥ kim kāraṇam uktam hi yat indhanam sa ced agniḥ ekatvam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ bhavet iti tat iha api yojyam sa buddhaḥ yaḥ hi upādānam eka tvam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ bhavet iti tathā ātmā skandhā yadi bhavet udayavyaya bhāj bhavet iti uktam tat iha api yojyam buddhaḥ skandhā yadi bhavet udayavyaya bhāj bhavet iti 
[188,i_188,ii]	evam tāvat skandhāḥ na tathāgataḥ idānīm na anyaḥ skandhebhyaḥ tathāgataḥ iti kim kāraṇam uktam hi anyaḥ ced indhanāt agniḥ indhanāt aṣi ṛte bhavet tathā paratra nirapekṣa tvāt apradīpana hetukaḥ punar ārambha vaiyarthyam evam ca akarmakaḥ sati iti tathā iha api yojyam buddhaḥ anyaḥ ced upādānāt upādānam vinā bhavet 
[188,iii_188,vi]	tathā paratra nirapekṣa tvāt anupādāna hetukaḥ punar ārambha vaiyarthyam evam ca akarmakaḥ sati tathā skandhebhyaḥ anyaḥ yadi bhavet bhavet askandha lakṣaṇaḥ iti anya tva abhāvāt ca skandha ādīnām tathāgatasya ca tathāgate skandhāḥ na upapadyante na api skandheṣu tathāgataḥ iti upapadyate uktam ca etad madhyamaka avatāre pakṣa dvaya vyākhyānam skandheṣu ātmā vidyate na eva ca amī santi skandhā ātmani iti iha yasmāt sati anya tve syāt iyam kalpanāḥ vai tat ca anya tvam na asti atas kalpanā eṣā skandhavān api tathāgataḥ yathā na bhavati tathā tatra eva uktam iṣṭaḥ na ātmā rūpavān na asti yasmāt ātmā vattva artha upayogaḥ hi na atas bhede gomān rūpa vān aṣya bhede tattva anya tve arūpataḥ na ātmanaḥ staḥ 
[189,i]	tattva anya tva pakṣe eva tu pañca api pakṣāḥ antargatāḥ vastutas sat kāya dṛṣṭi pravṛtti apekṣayā tu pañca pakṣāḥ samupavarṇyante ācāryeṇa iti vijñeyam yaḥ ca evam skandheṣu pañcadhā vicāryamāṇaḥ na asti tathāgataḥ sa kena anyena ātmanā bhaviṣyati iti sarvathā na saṃbhavati eva tathāgataḥ iti bhāva svabhāvāt apaśyantaḥ ācārya pādāḥ prāhuḥ katamaḥ atra tathāgataḥ iti na asti eva sa kaścid sakala trailokya vastu vipaḥ cit bhāva svabhāvaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tathāgata abhāvāt ca bhava saṃtatiḥ api dravya saṃtatiḥ na asti iti siddham 
[189,ii]	atra eke vadanti na eva hi skandhāḥ tathāgataḥ iti brūmaḥ yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgāt na api skandha vyatiriktaḥ na api tathāgate anāsravān skandhān varṇayāmaḥ himavati parvate iva taru khaṇḍam na api skandheṣu taru khaṇḍe eva siṃham na api skandhavantam varṇayāmaḥ lakṣaṇavantam iva cakravartinam ekatva anyatva anabhyupagamāt eva kim tarhi skandhān amalān upādāya tattva anya tva ādi avācyam tathāgatam vyavasthāpayāmaḥ tasmāt na ayam vidhiḥ asmākam bādhakaḥ iti atra ucyate buddhaḥ skandhān upādāya yadi na asti svabhāvataḥ svabhāvataḥ ca yaḥ na asti kutas sa para bhāvataḥ 
[189,iii]	yadi hi buddhaḥ bhagavān amalān skandhān upādāya tattva anya tvena avaktavyaḥ prajñapyate na tarhi svabhāvataḥ saḥ asti iti vyaktam āpadyate pratibimba vat upādāya prajñapyamāna tvāt yaḥ ca idānīm svabhāvataḥ na asti ātmīyena svarūpeṇa sa katham avidyamānaḥ svabhāvataḥ skandhān upādāya para bhāvataḥ bhaviṣyati iti na hi avidyamānaḥ vandhyā tanayaḥ para bhāvam apekṣya bhavati iti yujyate 
[189,iv]	atha syāt yathā eva hi pratibimbakam svabhāvataḥ asaṃvidyamānam api para bhāvam mukha ādarśa ādikam apekṣya bhavati evam ca tathāgataḥ api svabhāvataḥ asaṃvidyamānaḥ anāsravān pañca skandhān upādāya para bhāvataḥ bhaviṣyati iti evam api pratītya para bhāvam yaḥ saḥ anātmā iti upapadyate yaḥ ca anātmā sa ca katham bhaviṣyati tathāgataḥ 
[189,v]	yadi pratibimba vat para bhāvam pratītya tathāgataḥ iṣyate evam sati pratibimba vat eva sa tathāgataḥ anātmā iti upapadyate na tu svabhāvataḥ iti yujyate ātma śabdaḥ ayam svabhāva śabda paryāyaḥ yaḥ ca anātmā niḥsvabhāvaḥ pratibimba vat eva sa katham tathāgataḥ svabhāva rūpataḥ bhaviṣyati aviparīta mārga gataḥ na bhaviṣyati iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[189,vi_190,ii]	kim ca anyat iha yadi tathāgatasya kaścid svabhāvaḥ syāt tadā tad svabhāva apekṣayā skandha svabhāvaḥ para bhāvaḥ iti syāt tam ca para bhāvam pratītya tathāgataḥ syāt yadā tu tathāgatasya svabhāvaḥ eva na asti tadā kutas skandhānām paratvam syāt iti pratipādayan āha yadi na asti svabhāvaḥ ca para bhāvaḥ katham bhavet yadā ca evam svabhāva para bhāvau na staḥ tadā svabhāva para bhāvābhyām ṛte kaḥ sa tathāgataḥ padārthaḥ hi bhavan svabhāvaḥ bhavet para bhāvaḥ vā tābhyām tu vinā kaḥ asau aparaḥ padārthaḥ asti yaḥ tathāgataḥ iti vyavasthāpyate tasmāt na asti svabhāvataḥ tathāgataḥ iti 
[190,iii_190,iv]	kim ca anyat skandhān yadi anupādāya bhavet kaścid tathāgataḥ saḥ idānīṃm upādadyāt upādāya tatas bhavet yadi manyase skandhebhyaḥ tattva anya tvena avaktavyaḥ tathāgataḥ skandhān upādāya prajñapyate iti tat kadā yujyate yadi skandhān anupādāya agṛhītvā pūrvam kaścid tathāgataḥ nāma bhavet sa skandha anupādadyāt vyatiriktaḥ eva hi pūrva siddhaḥ dhanāt devadattaḥ dhanasya upādānam kurute tadvat etān skandhān anupādāya yadi kaścid tathāgataḥ syāt saḥ idānīm skandha anupādadyāt tatas ca tān skandhān upādāya tatas bhavet 
[190,v_190,vii]	vicāryamāṇaḥ tu sarvathā skandhān ca api anupādāya na asti kaścid tathāgataḥ nirhetuka tva prasaṅgāt yaḥ ca na asti anupādāya saḥ upādāsyate katham avidyamāna tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ yadā ca evam na kiṃcid api upādatte tadā skandhān upādāya tathāgataḥ nāma bhaviṣyati iti na upapadyate 
[190,viii_190,ix]	yadā ca evam tathāgataḥ upādānāt pūrvam avidyamāna tvāt na kiṃcid upādatte tadā tad upādānasya api kenacid api anupādīyamānasya upādāna tvam na saṃbhavati eva iti pratipādayan āha na bhavati anupādattam upādānam ca kiṃcana yadā ca evam upādānam kenacid api anupādīyamāna tvāt upādānam na bhavati iti tadā upādāna abhāvāt upādātā api kaścid na asti iti pratipādayan āha na ca asti nirupādānaḥ kathaṃcana tathāgataḥ iti 
[190,x_190,xi]	tat evam yathā upapādita nyāyena tattva anya tvena yaḥ na asti mṛgyamāṇaḥ ca pañcadhā upādānena sa katham prajñapyeta tathāgataḥ yaḥ hi tathāgataḥ vicāryamāṇaḥ mṛgyamāṇaḥ tattvena skandhebhyaḥ ekatvena na asti anya tvena skandhebhyaḥ pṛthaktvena ca yaḥ na asti evam tattva anyatva asa tvāt ādhāra ādheya tadvat pakṣa pañca prakāraiḥ mṛgyamāṇaḥ yaḥ na asti sa katham atyantaḥ asaṃvidyamānaḥ tathāgataḥ upādānena śakyaḥ prajñapayitum iti atas api na asti tathāgataḥ nāma svabhāvataḥ 
[191,i_191,iii]	na kevalam anena vicāreṇa tathāgataḥ eva na asti yat api idam upādānam tad svabhāva tvāt na vidyate yat api idam upādānam rūpa vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra vijñāna ākhyam skandha pañcakam tat api svabhāvena na vidyate pratītyasamutpanna tvāt skandha parīkṣāyām ca vistareṇa pratiṣiddha tvāt atha api syāt yadi api svabhāvataḥ upādānam na asti tathā api hetu pratyaya ātmakāt para bhāvā dbhaviṣyati iti tadā api na upapadyate iti pratipādayan āha svabhāvataḥ ca yat na asti kutas tad para bhāvataḥ 
[191,iv_191,vii]	na hi bandhyā sūnuḥ svabhāvataḥ asaṃvidyamānaḥ śakyaḥ para bhāvena prajñapayitum iti atas upādānam api na asti athavā yat api idam upādānam tad svabhāvāt na vidyate upādātṛ sāpekṣa tvāt upādātṛ nirapekṣasya ca upādāna tva abhāvāt na asti svabhāva siddham upādānam atha yadi api upādātṛ nirapekṣam upādānam svabhāva siddham na saṃbhavati evam tad upādātṛ apekṣam eva bhavatu iti ucyate evam api svabhāvataḥ ca yat na asti kutas tad para bhāvataḥ svabhāvataḥ yat upādānam na siddham tad avidyamāna svabhāvam katham upādātuḥ para bhāvataḥ bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt upādānam api na asti iti 
[191,viii_191,x]	idānīm yathāprasādhitam eva artham upadarśayan āha evam śūnyam upādānam upādātā ca sarvaśas sarveṇa prakāreṇa vicāryamāṇam śūnyam upādānam niḥsvabhāvam upādātā ca śūnyaḥ svabhāva rahitaḥ tena idānīm upādānena prajñapyate ca śūnyena katham śūnyaḥ tathāgataḥ na eva tad saṃbhavati yat avidyamānena avidyamānasya tathāgatasya prajñaptiḥ syāt iti tasmāt skandhān upādāya tathāgataḥ prajñapyate iti na upapadyate 
[191,xi^1]	atra āhuḥ aho vata hatā pratyāśā asmākam ye hi nāma vayam sva vikalpa vikalpita ati kaṭhina kudarśana mālu tāla tā jāla avabaddheṣu nirvāṇa pura gāmi aviparīta mārga gamana paribhraṣṭeṣu anatikrānta saṃsāra aṭavī kāntāra durgeṣu kaṇa bhakṣa akṣa pāda digambara jaimi ninaiyāyika prabhṛtiṣu tīrthakareṣu aviparīta svarga apavarga mārga upadeśa abhimāniṣu spṛhām parityajya niravaśeṣa anya tīrthya mata andhakāra upaghātakam svarga apavarga anugāmya viparīta mārga saṃprakāśakam sat dharma deśanā ati paṭutara kiraṇa vyāpta aśeṣa āśā mukham vividha vineya janam ati kamala kuṅmala vibodhana tat param
[191,xi^2]	yathāvat avasthita padārtha tattva artha bhājanānām amala eka cakṣuḥ bhūtam sakala jagat śaraṇya bhūtam advitīyam daśa bala vaiśāradyā veṇika buddha dharma amala maṇḍalam mahāyāna mahānaya sārathi varam sapta bodhi aṅga uttuṅga turaṃga padāti yojitam sakala tribhuvana jana jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāra kāntāra sarit ucchoṣaṇa tad param catura sama mārāra ati samara śara saṃpāta vijayinam sakala jagat asat grāha rāhu graha vigraha udgraha nirāsinam tathāgata savitāram ajñāna dhana gahana andhakāra nirākaraṇāya mokṣa arthinaḥ atuttara samyaksaṃbodhi arthinaḥ śaraṇam pratipannāḥ tasya ca tvayā evam śūnyam upādānam upādātā ca sarvaśas 
[191,xi^3]	prajñapyate ca śūnyena katham śūnyaḥ tathāgataḥ ityādinā svabhāvataḥ asattvam vruvatā bhavatā hatā asmākam mokṣa pratyāśā anuttara samyaksaṃbodhya āgama abhilāṣaḥ iti tat alam bhavatā tathāgata mahā āditya pracchādakena ākālika dhana dhana āvalī visaraṇena jagat andhakāra upamena iti ucyate asmākam eva hatā pratyāśāḥ bhavadvidheṣu abudha janeṣu ye hi nāma bhavantaḥ mokṣa kāma tayā anya tīrthya matāni parityajya bhagavantam tathāgatam api aviparītam parama śāstāram pratipadya parama gambhīram anuttaram sarva tīrthya vāda asā dhāraṇam nairātmya siṃhanādam asahamānāḥ kuraṅgamāḥ iva su ādhi mukti daridra tayā vividha kudṛṣṭi vyāla mālā ākulam viparyasta jana anuyātam tam eva mahā ghora saṃsāra aṭavī kāntāra cāraka anuga mārgam avagāhante na hi tathāgatāḥ kadācid api ātmanaḥ skandhānām vā astitvam prajñapayanti yathā uktam bhagavatyām 
[192,i_192,iii]	buddhaḥ api āyuṣman subhūte māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ buddha dharmāḥ api āyuṣman subhūte māyā upamāḥ svapna upamāḥ iti tathā dharma svabhāvatu śūnya viviktaḥ bodhi svabhāvatu śūnya viviktā yaḥ hi caret sa pi śūnya svabhāvaḥ jñānavataḥ na tu bāla janasya iti na ca vayam sarvathā eva niṣprapañcānām tathāgatānām nāstitvam brūmaḥ yat asmākam tad apavāda kṛtaḥ doṣaḥ syāt 
[192,iv_192,v]	api ca niḥsvabhāvam hi tathāgatam vyācakṣāṇena aviparīta artha abhidhitsunā yoginām satā sarvathā śūnyam iti na vaktavyam aśūnyam iti vā bhavet ubhayam na ubhayam ca iti sarvam etat na vaktavyam asmābhiḥ kim tu anukte yathāvat avasthitam svabhāvam pratipattā pratipattum na samarthaḥ iti atas vayam api āropataḥ vyavahāra satye eva sthitvā vyavahāra artham vineya jana anurodhena śūnyam iti api brūmaḥ aśūnyam iti api śūnyāśūnyam iti api na eva śūnyam na aśūnyam iti api brūmaḥ atas eva āha prajñapti artham tu kathyate iti yathā uktam bhagavatā 
[193,i_193,iii]	śūnyāḥ sarva dharmāḥ niḥsvabhāva yogena nirnimittāḥ sarva dharmāḥ nirnimitta tām upādāya apraṇihitāḥ sarva dharmāḥ apraṇidhāna yogena prakṛti prabhāsvarāḥ sarva dharmāḥ prajñāpāramitā pariśuddhayā iti anyatra aśūnyam uktam atītam ced bhikṣavaḥ rūpam na abhaviṣyan na śrutavān ārya śrāvakaḥ atītam rūpam abhyanandiṣyat yasmāt tarhi bhikṣavaḥ asti atītam rūpam tasmāt ārya śrāvakaḥ śrutavān atītam rūpam abhinandati iti anāgatam ced bhikṣavaḥ ityādi evam yāvat atītam ced bhikṣavaḥ vijñānam na abhaviṣyat ityādi pūrvavat 
[193,iv_193,vi]	tathā sautra antika mate atīta anāgatam śūnyam anyat aśūnyam viprayuktā vijñaptiḥ śūnyā vijñāna vāde api kalpita svabhāvasya śūnya tvam apratītya samutpanna tvāt taimirika dvi candra ādi darśana vat na śūnyam na api ca aśūnyam tasmāt sarvam vidhīyate tathā sattvāt asattvāt ca madhyamā pratipad ca sā iti yena tu abhiprāyeṇa śūnya tva ādikam upadiśyate saḥ ātma parīkṣātaḥ boddhavyaḥ 
[193,vii]	yathā uktam sūtre māyā upamam jagat idam bhavatā naṭa raṅga svapna sadṛśam vihitam na ātmā na sattva na ca jīva gatī dharmāḥ marīci daka candra samāḥ śūnyam ca śāntam anupāda mayam avijānadeva jagat udbhramatī teṣām upāya naya yukti śataiḥ avatārayasi api kṛpālu tayā rāga ādibhiḥ ca bahu roga śataiḥ saṃtrāsitam sakalam īkṣi jagat vaidya upamaḥ vicarase apratimaḥ parimocayam sugata sattva śatān ratha cakra vat bhramati sarva jagat tiryakṣu preta nirayeṣu gatāḥ mūḍhāḥ adeśika anātha gatāḥ teṣām pradarśayasi mārga varam iti sarvāḥ tu etāḥ kalpanā niṣprapañce tathāgate na saṃbhavanti 
[194,i_194,ii]	na ca kevalam śūnya tva ādikam eva catuṣṭayam tathāgate na saṃbhavati api ca śāśvata aśāśvata ādyā kutas śānte catuṣṭayam anta ananta ādi ca api atra kuntaḥ śānte catuṣṭayam iha caturdaśa avyākṛta vastūni bhagavatā nirdiṣṭāni tat yathā śāśvataḥ lokaḥ aśāśvataḥ lokaḥ śāśvataḥ ca aśāśvataḥ ca lokaḥ na eva śāśvataḥ na aśāśvataḥ ca lokaḥ iti catuṣṭayam antavān lokaḥ anantavān lokaḥ antavān ca anantavān ca lokaḥ na eva antavān na anantavān ca lokaḥ iti dvitīyam bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt na bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt bhavati ca na bhavati ca tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt na eva bhavati na na bhavati ca tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt iti tṛtīyam sa jīvaḥ tat śarīram anyaḥ jīvaḥ anyat śarīram iti tāni etāni caturdaśa vastūni avyākṛta tvāt avyākṛta vastūni iti ucyante tatra yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena yathā śūnya tva ādikam catuṣṭayam prakṛtyā śānte niḥsvabhāve tathāgate na saṃbhavati evam śāśvata aśāśvata ādikam api catuṣṭayam atra na saṃbhavati asaṃbhavāt eva ca catuṣṭayam vandhyā putrasya śyāma gaura tva ādi vat na vyākṛtam bhagavatā lokasya yathā ca etat catuṣṭayam tathāgate na saṃbhavati evam anta ananta ādikam api śānte tathāgate na saṃbhavati 
[194,iii_194,iv]	idānīm bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt iti ādikasya api kalpanā catuṣṭayasya pravṛtti asaṃbhava mudbhau ayan āha yena grāhaḥ gṛhītaḥ tu ghanaḥ asti iti tathāgataḥ na asti iti sa vikalpayat nirvṛtasya api kalpayet yena hi ghanataraḥ mahatā abhiniveśena asti tathāgataḥ iti grāhaḥ gṛhītaḥ parikalpaḥ utpāditaḥ saḥ niyatam parinirvṛte tathāgate na bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt maraṇāt uttara kālam na bhavati ucchinnaḥ tathāgataḥ na saṃvidyate iti parikalpayet tasya evam vikalpayataḥ syāt dṛṣṭi kṛtam 
[194,v_194,vi]	yasya tu na kasyāṃcid api avasthāyām svabhāva śūnya tvāt tathāgatasya astitva nāstitvam tasya pakṣe svabhāvataḥ ca śūnye asmin cintā na eva upapadyate param nirodhāt bhavati buddhaḥ na bhavati iti vā ākāśe citra rūpa kalpanāvat eṣā kalpanā na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[195,i_195,ii]	tat evam prakṛti śānte niḥsvabhāve tathāgate sarva prapañca atīte manda buddhi tayā śāśvatā śāśvata ādikayā nitya anityāsti nāsti śūnyā śūnya sarvajñā sarva jña ādikayā kalpanayā prapañcayanti ye buddham prapañca atītam avyayam te prapañca hatāḥ sarve na paśyanti tathāgatam vastu nibandhanāḥ hi prapañcāḥ syuḥ avastukaḥ ca tathāgataḥ kutas prapañcānām pravṛtti saṃbhavaḥ iti atas prapañca atītaḥ tathāgataḥ anutpāda svabhāva avāt ca svabhāva antarāgamanāt avyayaḥ tam itthaṃvidham tathāgatam sva utprekṣita mithyā parikalpa mala malina mānasatayā vividhaiḥ abhūtaiḥ parikalpa viśeṣaiḥ ye buddham bhagavantam prapañcayanti te svakaiḥ eva prapañcaiḥ hatāḥ santaḥ tathāgata guṇa samṛddheḥ atyanta parokṣa vartinaḥ bhavanti tatas ca śava bhūtāḥ etasmin pravacane na paśyanti tathāgatam jāti andhāḥ iva ādityam atas eva āha bhagavān ye mām rūpeṇa adrākṣuḥ ye mām ghoṣeṇa anvayuḥ mithyā prahāṇa prasṛtāḥ na mām drakṣyanti te janāḥ dharmataḥ buddhāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ dharma kāyāḥ hi nāyakāḥ dharmatā ca api avijñeyā na sā śakyāḥ vijānitum iti 
[195,iii_195,iv]	tat atra tathāgata parīkṣāyām sattva lokaḥ sakalaḥ sa sura asura narādiḥ parīkṣitaḥ yathā ca ayam sattva lokaḥ niḥsvabhāvaḥ tathā bhājana lokasya api vāyu maṇḍala āderakaniṣṭha vitāna bhavana paryantasya naiḥsvābhāvyam udbhāvayan āha tathāgataḥ yat svabhāvaḥ tad svabhāvam idam jagat idam jagat iti ayam bhājana loke iti arthaḥ kiṃsvabhāvaḥ tathāgataḥ punar iti āha tathāgataḥ niḥsvabhāvaḥ niḥsvabhāvam idam jagat 
[195,v_196,i]	iti yathā ca jagataḥ naiḥsvābhāvyam tathā pratyaya parīkṣā ādibhiḥ pratipāditam atas eva uktam sūtre anupāda dharmaḥ satatam tathāgataḥ sarve ca dharmāḥ sugatena sādṛśāḥ nimitta grāheṇa tu bāla buddhayaḥ asatsu dharmeṣu caranti loke tathāgataḥ hi pratibimba bhūtaḥ kuśalasya dharmasya anāsravasya na eva atra tathatā na tathāgataḥ asti bimbam ca saṃdṛśyati sarve loke iti uktam ca bhagavatyām prajñāpāramitāyām
