[196,ii]	atha khalu te deva putrāḥ āyuṣmantam subhūtim sthaviram etat avocan kim punar ārya subhūte māyā upamāḥ te sattvāḥ na te māyā evam ukte āyuṣmān subhūtiḥ tān deva putrān etat avocat māyā upamāḥ te deva putrāḥ sattvāḥ svapna upamāḥ te deva putrāḥ sattvāḥ iti hi māyā ca sattvāḥ ca advayam eta dadvaidhīkāram iti hi svapnaḥ ca sattvāḥ ca advayam etat ad vaidhīkāram sarva dharmāḥ api deva putrāḥ māyā upamāḥ svapna upamāḥ strotaāpannaḥ api māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ strotaāpatti phalam api māyā upamam svapna upamam evam sakṛdāgāmi api sakṛdāgāmi phalam api anāgāmi api anāgāmi phalam api arhan api māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ arhat tva phalam api māyā upamam svapna upamam pratyekabuddhaḥ api māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ pratyekabuddha tvam api māyā upamam svapna upamam samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ api māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ iti samyaksaṃbuddha tvam api māyā upamam svapna upamam iti vadāmi 
[196,iii]	atha khalu deva putrāḥ āyuṣmantam subhūtim etat avocan samyaksaṃbuddhaḥ api māyā upamaḥ svapna upamaḥ iti samyaksaṃbuddha tvam api māyā upamam svapna upamam iti ārya subhūte vadasi subhūtiḥ āha nirvāṇam api deva putrāḥ māyā upamam svapna upamam iti vadāmi kim punar anyam dharmam deva putrāḥ āhuḥ nirvāṇam api ārya subhūte māyā upamam svapna upamam iti vadasi subhūtiḥ āha yadi api deva putrāḥ nirvāṇāt api anyaḥ kaścid dharmaḥ viśiṣṭataraḥ syāt tam api aham māyā upamam svapna upamam iti vadeyam iti hi māyā ca nirvāṇam ca advayam etat ad vaidhīkāram iti 
[197,i]	atra āha vidyate eva bhava saṃtatiḥ tad kāraṇa sadbhāvāt iha hi kleśebhyaḥ karma pravartate karma kleśa hetukā janma maraṇa paraṃparā upajāyate sā ca bhava saṃtatiḥ vyapadiśyate tasyāḥ ca pradhānam kāraṇam kleśāḥ prahīṇa kleśānām bhava saṃtateḥ abhāvāt te ca rāga ādayaḥ kleśāḥ santi tasmāt kārya bhūtā api janma maraṇa paraṃparā aviccheda prabandhena bhava saṃtatiḥ api bhaviṣyati iti ucyate syāt bhava saṃtatiḥ yadi tad hetu bhūtāḥ kleśāḥ syuḥ na tu santi katham kṛtvā iha bhagavadbhiḥ buddhaiḥ sakala tribhuvana jana saṃkleśa śatru vidhvaṃsibhiḥ catur māra arāti samara parājayaiḥ saṃkalpa prabhavaḥ rāgaḥ dveṣaḥ mohaḥ ca kathyate śubha aśubha viparyāsān saṃbhavanti pratītya hi 
[197,ii_197,v]	saṃkalpaḥ vitarkaḥ saṃkalpāt prabhavati iti saṃkalpa prabhavaḥ kāma jānāmi te mūlam saṃkalpāt kila jāyase na tvām saṃkalpayiṣyāmi tatas me na bhaviṣyasi iti gāthā abhidhānāt saṃkalpa prabhavaḥ rāgaḥ dveṣaḥ mohaḥ ca kathyate etat mūlaka tvāt anyeṣām kleśānām mukhya tvāt eṣām eva upādānam trayāṇām ete ca trayaḥ kleśāḥ śubha aśubha viparyāsān saṃbhavanti pratītya hi 
[197,vi_197,vii]	tatra hi śubham ākāram pratītya rāgaḥ utpadyate aśubham pratītya dveṣaḥ viparyāsān pratītya mohaḥ utpadyate saṃkalpaḥ tu eṣām trayāṇām api sādhāraṇa kāraṇam utpattau katham punar mohaḥ saṃkalpa prabhavaḥ ucyate uktam hi pratītyasamutpāde bhagavatā avidyā api bhikṣavaḥ sa hetukā sa pratyayā sa nidānā kaḥ ca bhikṣavaḥ avidyāyāḥ hetuḥ ayoniśaḥ bhikṣavaḥ manaskāraḥ avidyāyāḥ hetuḥ āvilaḥ moha jaḥ manaskāraḥ bhikṣavaḥ avidyāyāḥ hetuḥ iti atas avidyā saṃkalpa prabhavā bhavati 
[197,viii_197,ix]	tatas ca śubha aśubha viparyāsān saṃbhavanti pratītya ye te svabhāvāt na vidyante tasmāt kleśāḥ na tattvataḥ iti yadi rāga ādayaḥ svabhāva siddhāḥ syuḥ na eva te śubha aśubha viparyāsān pratītya saṃbhaveyuḥ svabhāvasya akṛtrima tvāt para nirapekṣa tvāt ca bhavanti ca śubha aśubha viparyāsān pratītya tasmāt niḥsvabhāvāḥ eva te tattvataḥ na vidyante paramārthataḥ svabhāvataḥ na vidyante iti arthaḥ 
[198,i_198,ii]	api ca ātmanaḥ astitva nāstitvena kathaṃcid ca sidhyataḥ tam vinā asti tvana astitve kleśānām sidhyataḥ katham ātmanaḥ yathā astitvanā astitve na staḥ tathā uktam vistareṇa tatas ca tad āśritasya dharmasya kutas astitvana astitve bhaviṣyataḥ 
[198,iii_198,iv]	atha syāt yadi astitvanā astitve ātmanaḥ na staḥ tadā kim atra kleśānām āyātam yatas teṣām api astitvanā astitve na staḥ iti ucyate kasyacid hi bhavanti ime kleśāḥ sa ca na sidhyati kaścid āhaḥ vinā kaṃcid santi kleśāḥ na kasyacid iha amī rāga ādayaḥ kuḍayam citra vat phalam pakva tā ādi vat ca utpattau āśrayam apekṣante tatas ca kasyacid ete bhavanti na vinā kaṃcid āśrayam sa ca āśrayaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ ātmā vā cittam vā bhavet sa ca eṣām āśrayaḥ pūrvam eva pratiṣiddha tvāt na asti tam ca kaṃcid āśrayam vinā kasya kleśāḥ bhavantu na eva kasyacid bhavanti tasya avidyamāna tvāt āho vinā kaṃcid santi kleśāḥ na kasyacid 
[198,v]	atra āha na eva hi kleśānām kaścid āśrayaḥ pūrvam siddhaḥ abhyupagamyate na ca ātmā nāma kaścid asti yaḥ āśraya tvena vyavasthāpyeta nirhetuka tvāt vyoma cūta taru vat kim tarhi kliṣṭam cittam pratītya kleśāḥ upajāyante tat ca cittam saha eva kleśaiḥ upajāyate iti etat api na yuktam iti āha sva kāya dṛṣṭi vat kleśāḥ kliṣṭe santi na pañcadhā sva kāya dṛṣṭi vat kliṣṭam kleśeṣu api na pañcadhā 
[198,vi^1]	sva kāyaḥ hi nāma rūpa ādi lakṣaṇa saṃhatiḥ sva kāya dṛṣṭiḥ sva kāye ātma dṛṣṭiḥ ātmīya ākāra grahaṇa pravṛttā yathā iyam pañcadhā vicāryamāṇā sva kāye na saṃbhavati skandhāḥ na na anyaḥ skandhebhyaḥ na asmin skandhāḥ na teṣu saḥ tathāgataḥ skandhavān na katamaḥ atra tathāgataḥ iti anena evam kliṣṭe api kleśāḥ vicāryamāṇāḥ pañcadhā na saṃbhavanti tatra kliśyanti iti kleśā kliśyate iti kliṣṭam tatra yat eva kliṣṭam tat eva kleśāḥ iti na yujyate dagdhṛ dāhyayoḥ api ekatva prasaṅgāt anyat kliṣṭam anye kleśāḥ iti na yujyate paratra nirapekṣa tvāt akliṣṭa hetuka kleśa prasaṅgāt 
[198,vi^2]	atas eva ca ekatva anyatva abhāvāt ādhāra ādheya tadvat pakṣāṇām ca abhāvāt na kleśeṣu kliṣṭam na kliṣṭe kleśāḥ na api kleśa vat kliṣṭam iti evam kliṣṭe pañcadhā vicāryamāṇāḥ kleśāḥ na saṃbhavanti yathā ca kliṣṭa hetukāḥ kleśāḥ na saṃbhavanti evam kleśa hetukam api kliṣṭam kleśeṣu vicāryamāṇam pañcadhā na saṃbhavati na hi kleśāḥ eva kliṣṭam kartṛ karmaṇoḥ ekatva prasaṅgāt na anye kleśāḥ anyat kliṣṭam nirapekṣa tva prasaṅgāt na ca kliṣṭe kleśāḥ na ca kleśeṣu kliṣṭam na kliṣṭavantaḥ kleśāḥ iti evam sva kāya dṛṣṭi vat eva kliṣṭam kleśeṣu api pañcadhā na asti yatas ca evam atas paraspara apekṣayā api kleśa akliṣṭayoḥ na asti siddhiḥ 
[199,i_199,iii]	atra āha yadi api tvayā kleśāḥ pratiṣiddhāḥ tathā api kleśa hetavaḥ śubha aśubha viparyāsāḥ tāvat santi tad sadbhāvāt ca kleśāḥ santi iti ucyate syuḥ kleśāḥ yadi śubha aśubha viparyāsāḥ eva syuḥ yāvatā ete api pratītya sa sutpanna tvāt vakṣyamāṇa pratiṣedhāt ca yadā ca te na santi svabhāvataḥ tadā svabhāvataḥ na vidyante śubha aśubha viparyayāḥ pratītyasamutpanna tvāt vakṣyamāṇa pratiṣedhāt ca yadā ca te na santi svabhāvataḥ tadā pratītya katamān kleśāḥ śubha aśubha viparyayān na eva santi kleśāḥ tad hetu śubha aśubha viparyaya abhāvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[199,iv]	atra āha vidyante eva kleśāḥ tad ālambana sadbhāvāt iha hi yat na asti na tasya ālambana masti tat yathā vandhyā sūnoḥ asti ca rūpa śabda gandha rasa spraṣṭavya dharma ākhyam ṣaḍvidham ālambanam tasmāt ālambana sadbhāvāt vidyante eva kleśāḥ iti ucyate asti etat yat bhavadbhiḥ rūpa śabda rasa sparśāḥ gandhāḥ dharmāḥ ca ṣaḍvidham vastu rāgasya dveṣasya mohasya ca vikalpyate 
[199,v^1]	tatra vastu ālambanam vasati iti vai asmin rāga ādikam tad utpatteḥ iti kṛtvā tat ca tad ālambanam ṣoḍhā bhavati indriyāṇām ṣaṇṇām pariccheda karāṇām anyonya bhedāt rūpam śabdāḥ gandhāḥ rasāḥ spraṣṭavyāni dharmāḥ ca iti tatra idam iha amutra iti nirūpaṇāt rūpaṇāt ca rūpam tena śabdena śabdyante prakāśyante padārthāḥ iti śabdaḥ gandhyante hiṃsyante yatra prāptāḥ tatas anyatra āgamanāt gandhāḥ rasyate āsvādyate iti rasaḥ spṛśyate iti sparśaḥ sva lakṣaṇa asā dhāraṇāt nirvāṇa agra dharma ādhāraṇāt dharmāḥ 
[199,v^2]	tat etat ṣaḍvidham vastu bhavati kasya rāgasya dveṣasya mohasya tatra rañjanam rāgaḥ raktiḥ adhyavasānam rajyate vā anena cittam iti rāgaḥ dūṣaṇam doṣaḥ āghātaḥ sattva viṣayaḥ asattva viṣayaḥ vā dūṣyate vā anena citam iti doṣaḥ mohanam mohaḥ saṃmohaḥ padārtha svarūpa aparijñānam muhyate vā anena cittam iti mohaḥ tat eṣām kleśānām rūpa ādikam ṣaḍvidham vastu ālambanam bhavati tatra śubha ākāra adhyāropeṇa yathā rūpa ādibhyaḥ rāgaḥ upajāyate aśubha ākāra adhyāropeṇa dveṣaḥ nitya ātma ādi adhyāropeṇa mohaḥ saṃbhavati iti 
[199,vi_200,i]	satyam vikalpyate etat bāla janaiḥ ṣaḍvidham vastu kim tu avidyamāna svabhāva sattākam etat rāga ādīnām ālambana tvena parikalpyate bhavatā taimirikaiḥ iva asat keśa maśaka makṣikāt vi candra ādikam iti pratipādayan āha rūpa śabda rasa sparśāḥ gandhāḥ dharmāḥ ca kevalāḥ kevalāḥ iti parikalpita mātrāḥ niḥsvabhāvāḥ iti arthaḥ yadi niḥsvabhāvāḥ katham tarhi upalabhyante iti ucyate gandharvanagara ākārāḥ marīci svapna saṃnibhāḥ iti ete upalabhyante 
[200,ii_200,iii]	yathā gandharvanagara ādi prakhyāḥ ete kevalam viparyāsāt upalabhyante tadā aśubham vā śubham vā api kutas teṣu bhaviṣyati māyā puruṣa kalpeṣu pratibimba sameṣu ca tat anena mithyā āśraya samutpanna tvāt śubha aśubhayoḥ api nimittayoḥ mṛṣā tvam eva bhavati yathā uktam ahaṃkāra udbhavāḥ skandhāḥ saḥ ahaṃkāraḥ anṛtaḥ arthataḥ bījam yasya anṛtam tasya prarohaḥ satyataḥ kutas skandhān asatyān dṛṣṭvā evam ahaṃkāraḥ prahīyate ahaṃkāra prahāṇāt ca na punar skandha saṃbhavaḥ iti 
[200,iv_200,v]	na ca kevalam āśraya mithyā tve śubha aśubhayoḥ nimittayoḥ mithyātvam api ca anayā api upapattyā anayoḥ mithyātvam iti pratipādayan āha anapekṣya śubham na asti aśubham prajñapayemahi yat pratītya śubham tasmāt śubham na eva upapadyate iha yadi śubham nāma kiṃcid syāt niyatam tat aśubham apekṣya bhavet pārāvāra vat bīja aṅkura vat hrasva dīrgha vat vā śubhasya saṃbandhi antara padārtha sāpekṣa tvāt tat ca api apekṣaṇīyam aśubham śubhena vinā na asti anapekṣya śubham na asti aśubham śubham nirapekṣya aśubham na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ yat aśubham pratītya yat aśubham apekṣya śubham prajñapayemahi vyavasthāpayemahi yat śabdena anantarasya aśubhasya parāmarśaḥ prajñapayemahi iti anena uttarasya śubhasya saṃbandhaḥ yatas ca evam śubhasya prajñaptau saṃbandhi antaram apekṣaṇīyam aśubha ākhyam padārtha antaram na asti tasmāt śubham na eva upapadyate hrasva asaṃbhavāt iva dīrgham pāra asaṃbhavāt iva avāram iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[200,vi_200,vii]	idānīm aśubham api yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha anapekṣya aśubham na asti śubham prajñapayemahi yat pratītya aśubham tasmāt aśubham na eva vidyate yadi hi aśubham nāma kiṃcid syāt niyatam eva tat śubham apekṣya bhavet pārāvāra vat hrasva dīrgha vat vā aśubhasya saṃbandhi antara padārtha sāpekṣa tvāt tat ca api apekṣaṇīyam śubham aśubhena vinā na asti anapekṣya aśubham na asti śubham aśubham nirapekṣya śubham na saṃbhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ yat śubham pratītya yat śubham apekṣya aśubham prajñapayemahi aśubham vyavasthāpayemahi atra api yat śabdena anantarasya śubhasya parāmarśaḥ prajñapayemahi iti anena ca uttarasya aśubhasya saṃbandhaḥ yatas ca evam aśubhasya prajñaptau saṃbandhi antaram apekṣaṇīyam śubha ākhyam padārtha antaram na asti tasmāt aśubham na eva vidyate 
[201,i_201,ii]	yatas ca evam śubha aśubhayoḥ asaṃbhavaḥ atas avidyamāne ca śubhe kutas rāgaḥ bhaviṣyati aśubhe avidyamāne ca kutas dveṣaḥ bhaviṣyati śubha aśubha nimittakayoḥ rāga dveṣayoḥ śubha aśubha nimitta abhāve sati nirhetuka tvāt na asti saṃbhavaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[201,iii_201,iv]	tat evam śubha aśubha nimitta abhāvena rāga dveṣayoḥ abhāvam upapādya viparyāsa svabhāva abhāva pratipādanena mohasya api adhunā svabhāva abhāvam pratipādayan āha anitye nityam iti evam yadi grāhaḥ viparyayaḥ na anityam vidyate śūnye kutas grāhaḥ viparyayaḥ iha catvāraḥ viparyāsāḥ ucyante tat yathā anitye pratikṣaṇa vināśini skandha pañcake yaḥ nityam iti grāhaḥ sa viparyāsaḥ tathā anityasya dhruvā pīḍā pīḍā yasya na tad sukham tasmāt anityam yat sarvam duḥkham tat iti jāyate iti amunā nyāyena yat anityam tad duḥkham sarva saṃskārāḥ ca anityāḥ tasmāt duḥkha ātmake skandha pañcake yaḥ sukham iti viparītaḥ grāhaḥ saḥ aparaḥ viparyāsaḥ tathā śukra śoṇita saṃparka bījam viṣ mūtra vardhitam amedhya rūpam ājānan rajyase atra kaya icchayā amedhya puñja pracchanne tad kleda ārdreṇa carmaṇā yaḥ śayīta sa nārīṇām śayīta jaghana udare ityādi 
[201,v_201,vi]	evam idam śarīram sarva ātmanā satatam aśuci svabhāvam tatra yaḥ mohāt śuci tvena grāhaḥ abhiniveśaḥ sa viparyāsaḥ tathā pañca skandhakam ātma lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇam asthira tvāt udaya vyaya dharmi tvāt ca nirātmakam ātma svabhāva śūnyam tasmin yaḥ ātma grāhaḥ abhiniveśaḥ anātmani ātma abhiniveśaḥ sa viparyāsaḥ iti ete catvāraḥ viparyāsāḥ saṃmohasya hetu bhūtāḥ atra idānīm vicāryate yadi nitya tvam nitya darśanam svabhāva śūnyeṣu nitya grāhaḥ viparyāsaḥ iti evam vyavasthāpyate nanu ca svabhāva śūnyeṣu skandheṣu anitya tvam api na asti iti na anityam vidyate śūnye kutas grāhaḥ viparyayaḥ 
[201,vii_202,ii]	anitya tvam hi viparītam apekṣya nitya tvam viparyāsaḥ iti vyavasthāpyate na ca anitya tvam vidyate śūnye yadā anitya tvasya abhāvaḥ tadā kutas tat virodhi nitya tvam nitya darśana viparyāsaḥ bhaviṣyati iti bhāvaḥ tasmāt na asti viparyāsaḥ yathā ca anitya tvam śūnye na saṃbhavati bhāva svabhāva rahite sa svabhāvena anutpanne evam duḥkha tvam api na saṃbhavati aśuci tvam api na asti anātmaka tvam api na asti yadā ca svabhāva śūnya tvāt duḥkha tva ādikam na asti tadā kutas tad vipakṣa bhūtāḥ nitya sukha śucī ātma viparyāsāḥ bhaviṣyanti tasmāt santi viparyāsāḥ svarūpataḥ tad abhāve kutas bhaviṣyati avidyā hetu abhāvāt yathā uktam bhagavatā avidyayā na eva kadāci vidyate avidyata pratyaya saṃbhavaḥ ca avidyamānā iyam avidya loke tasmāt mayā uktaḥ avidyaḥ eṣā tathā katham bhagavat mohaḥ dhāraṇī padam bhagavān āha atyanta muktaḥ hi mañjuśrīḥ mohaḥ tena ucyate mohaḥ ityādinā viparyayaḥ iti vyavasthāpyate 
[202,iii_202,iv]	nanu evam sati svabhāvena avidyamāne padārthe anityam iti api grāhaḥ na saṃbhavati iti asau api kasmāt na viparyāsaḥ iti vyavasthāpyate iti pratipādayan āha anitye nityam iti evam yadi grāhaḥ viparyayaḥ anityam iti api grāhaḥ śūnye kim na viparyayaḥ yadā ca ubhayasya api vaiparītyam nityasya anityasya ca tadā tadvayatiriktam tṛtīyam aparam na asti yat na viparyayaḥ syāt yadā ca aviparyāsaḥ na asti tadā kim apekṣaḥ viparyāsaḥ syāt iti tasmāt amunā api nyāyena na asti viparyayaḥ tasya abhāvāt ca na asti avidyā svarūpataḥ yathā ca anitye nityam iti evam grāhaḥ viparyāsaḥ na saṃbhavati evam śeṣa viparyāsa asaṃbhave api yojyam atas eva uktam bhagavatā ārya dṛḍha āśaya paripṛcchāyām 
[202,v]	bhagavān āha kim etat kula putra tasya bhavati yaḥ mārgeṇa niḥsaraṇam paryeṣate na kula putra tathāgatena rañjanīyān dharmān parivarjya rāga prahāṇam prajñaptam evam na doṣaṇīyān mohanīyāna dharmān parivarjya tathāgatena doṣa moha prahāṇam prajñaptam tat kasmāt hetoḥ na kula putra tathāgatāḥ kasyacid dharmasya utsargāya vā pratilambhāya vā dharmam deśayanti na parijñāyai na prahāṇāya na sākṣāt kriyāyai nābhi samayāya na saṃsāra caraṇa tāyai na nirvāṇa gamana tāyai na utkṣepāya na prabhedāya na hi kula putra dvaya prabhāvitā tathāgata dharma tā tatra ye dvaye caranti na te samyak prayuktāḥ mithyā prayuktāḥ te vaktavyāḥ katamat ca kula putra dvayam aham rāgam prahāsyāmi iti dvayam etat aham dveṣam prahāsyāmi iti dvayam etat aham moham prahāsyāmi iti dvayam etat ye evaṃprayuktāḥ na te samyak prayuktā mithyā prayuktāḥ te veditavyāḥ 
[203,i]	tat yathā api nāma kula putra kaścid eva puruṣaḥ māyā ākāra nāṭake pratyupasthite māyā kāra nirmitām striyam dṛṣṭvā rāga cittam utpādayet sa rāga parīta cittaḥ parṣad śāradya bhayena utthāya āsanāt apakramet saḥ apakramya tām eva striyam aśubhataḥ manasi kuryāt anityatas duḥkhataḥ śūnyataḥ anātmataḥ manasi kuryāt bhagavān āha evam eva kula putraḥ iha eke bhikṣu bhikṣuṇī upāsa ka upāsikāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ ye anutpannān dharmān ajātān aśubhataḥ manasi kurvanti anityataḥ duḥkhataḥ anātmataḥ manasi kurvanti na aham teṣām moha puruṣāṇām mārga bhāvanām vadāmi mithyā prayuktāḥ te veditavyāḥ 
[203,ii]	tat yathā api nāma kula putra kaścid eva puruṣaḥ suptaḥ svapna antare sva gṛhe rāja bhāryām paśyet sa tayā sārdham śayyām kalpayet smṛti saṃmoṣāt ca evam kalpayet viruddhaḥ asmi iti sa bhīta srastaḥ palāyet mā mām rājā vidhyet sa mā mām jīvitāt vyavaropayet tat kim manyase kula putra api nu sa puruṣaḥ bhīta srastaḥ palāyamānaḥ tatas rāja bhāryā nidāna bhayāt parimucyeta āha naḥ bhagavan tat kasya hetoḥ tathā hi bhagavan tena puruṣeṇa astriyām strī saṃjñā utpāditā abhūtam ca parikalpitam bhagavān āha evam eva kula putraḥ iha eke bhikṣu bhikṣuṇī upāsa ka upāsikāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ ye arāge rāga saṃjñām utpādya rāga bhaya bhītāḥ rāga niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante evam adoṣe doṣa saṃjñām utpādya doṣa bhaya bhītāḥ doṣa niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante amohe moha saṃjñām utpādya moha bhaya bhītāḥ moha niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante na aham teṣām moha puruṣāṇām mārga bhāvanām vadāmi mithyā prayuktāḥ te veditavyāḥ 
[203,iii]	tat yathā api nāma kula putra sa puruṣaḥ abhaye bhaya saṃjñām utpādayet asat samāropeṇa evam eva kula putra sarva bāla pṛthagjanāḥ rāga koṭim virāga koṭim aprajā anantaḥ rāga koṭi bhaya bhītāḥ virāga koṭim niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante doṣa koṭim akiṃcana koṭim aprajānantaḥ doṣa koṭi bhaya bhītāḥ akiṃcana koṭim niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante moha koṭim śūnyatā koṭim aprajānantaḥ moha koṭi bhaya bhītāḥ śūnyatā koṭim niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante na aham teṣām kula putra moha puruṣāṇām mārga bhāvanām vadāmi mithyā prayuktāḥ te veditavyāḥ iti vistaraḥ 
[203,iv]	atra āha yadi api anitye nityam iti evam grāhaḥ viparyayaḥ na saṃbhavati tathā api eṣa tāvat grāhaḥ asti grāhaḥ ca nāma saṃgrahaṇam bhāva rūpaḥ tasya ca avaśyam sādhanena karaṇena bhavitavyam sādhakatamena nitya tva ādinā kartrā ca bhavitavyam svatantreṇa nitya ātmanā cittena vā karmaṇā ca kartuḥ īpsitatamena viṣayeṇa rūpa ādinā satyām ca bhāva karaṇa kartṛ karmaṇām siddhau sarva siddheḥ iṣṭa siddhiḥ syāt asmākam iti ucyate alīkā iyam pratyāśā nanu ca yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena yena gṛhṇāti yogrāhaḥ grahītā yat ca gṛhyate upaśāntāni sarvāṇi tasmāt grāhaḥ na vidyate 
[203,v_204,i]	iha hi kaścid grahītā yena viśeṣeṇa nitya tva ādinā karaṇa bhūtena kiṃcid karma bhūtam rūpa śabda ādikam vastu gṛhṇāti tat yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pūrvam pratipāditam katham kṛtvā anitye nityam iti evam yadi grāhaḥ viparyayaḥ ityādinā yathā nitya tva ādikam karaṇam na saṃbhavati tathā pratipāditam grahītā api yathā na asti tathā ātmanaḥ astitvana astitve na kathaṃcid ca sidhyataḥ iti anena pratipāditam yat ca gṛhyate tat api na asti tathā rūpa śabda rasa sparśāḥ gandhāḥ dharmāḥ ca kevalāḥ iti anena pratipāditam yadā ca evam kartṛ karaṇa karmāṇi na siddhāni tadā kutas nirhetukaḥ grāhaḥ bhaviṣyati tatas ca yena gṛhṇāti yaḥ grāhaḥ grahītā yat ca gṛhyate upaśāntāni sarvāṇi svabhāvena anutpanna tva anirvṛtāni sarvāṇi iti arthaḥ yatas ca evam evam tasmāt grāhaḥ na vidyate athavā pratyaya parīkṣā ādibhiḥ prakaraṇaiḥ yasmāt sarveṣām eva karaṇa kartṛ karmaṇām sarvathā anutpādaḥ pratipāditaḥ tasmāt sarvāṇi etāni bhāva svarūpa virahāt upaśāntāni atas ca grāhaḥ na vidyate 
[204,ii_204,iii]	atra āha vidyante eva viparyayāḥ viparīta sadbhāvāt iha hi viparyāsa anugataḥ devadattaḥ nāma vidyate na ca vinā viparyāsaiḥ sa viparyāsa anugataḥ saṃbhavati tasmāt santi viparyāsāḥ viparyasta sadbhāvāt iti ucyate iha asmābhiḥ karaṇa kartṛ karmaṇām abhāvāt sarvathā grāhaḥ eva na asti iti pratipāditam tatas ca avidyamāne grāhe ca mithyā vā samyak eva vā bhavet viparyayaḥ kasya bhavet kasya aviparyayaḥ samyak vā mithyā vā kasyacid kiṃcid api agṛhṇataḥ kutas viparīta tvam aviparīta tvam vā iti tasmāt na santi viparyayāḥ 
[204,iv]	api ca ime viparyayāḥ kasyacid iṣyamāṇāḥ viparītasya parikalpyeran aviparītasya vā viparyasyamānasya vā sarvathā ca na upapadyante iti pratipādayan āha na ca api viparītasya saṃbhavanti viparyayāḥ na ca api aviparītasya saṃbhavanti viparyayāḥ na viparyasyamānasya saṃbhavanti viparyayāḥ vimṛśasva svayam kasya saṃbhavanti viparyayāḥ 
[204,v]	tatra tāvat viparītasya viparyayāḥ na saṃbhavanti kim kāraṇam yasmāt yaḥ hi viparīta sa viparītaḥ eva kim tasya punar api viparyaya saṃbandhaḥ kuryāt niṣprayojana tvāt aviparītasya api viparyayāḥ na yujyante vibuddha buddhi nayanānām api ajñāna nidrā timira upaśamāt buddhānām viparyaya prasaṅgāt tathā viparyasyamānasya api na santi viparyayāḥ viparyasyamānasya bhāvasya abhāvāt kaḥ hi nāma asau aparaḥ padārthaḥ yaḥ viparīta aviparīta vinirmuktaḥ viparyasyamānaḥ nāma bhaviṣyati ardha viparītaḥ viparyasyamānaḥ iti ced ardha viparītaḥ hi nāma yasya kiṃcid viparītam kiṃcid aviparītam tatra yat asya kiṃcid viparītam tad viparyāsaḥ na viparyāsayati viparyasta tvāt yat api asya aviparītam tat api viparyāsaḥ na viparyāsayati aviparyasta tvāt tasmāt viparyasyamānasya api kasyacid viparyāsāḥ na saṃbhavanti yadā ca evam viparīta aviparīta viparyasyamānāḥ na saṃbhavanti bhavān idānīm vimṛśatu svayam prajñayā madhyasthaḥ san kasya saṃbhavanti viparyāsāḥ iti tat evam āśrayasya abhāvāt na santi viparyayāḥ 
[205,i_205,iii]	kim ca anyat anutpannāḥ katham nāma bhaviṣyanti viparyayāḥ viparyayeṣu ajāteṣu viparyaya gataḥ kutas tatra na svatas jāyate bhāvaḥ paratas na eva jāyate na svatas paratas ca iti viparyaya gataḥ kutas kutas viparītaḥ iti arthaḥ tatas ca yat uktam santi viparyayāḥ viparyaya gata sadbhāvāt iti tat na yuktam 
[205,iv_205,v]	yasya api kathaṃcid viparyāsa catuṣṭayam asti eva iti abhyupagamyate tathā api tasya viparīta tvam aśakyam āsthātum kim kāraṇam yasmāt ātmā ca śuci nityaṃ na sukham ca yadi vidyate ātmā ca śuci nityam ca sukham ca na viparyayaḥ yadi etāni ātma śuci niti asukhāni viparyāsāḥ iti vyavasthāpyante kim etāni santi atha na santi yadi vidyante na tarhi viparyāsāḥ vidyamāna tvāt anātma ādi vat 
[205,vi_205,vii]	atha na vidyante tadā eṣām avidyamāna tvāt na kevalam na asti viparyāsa tvam viparyāsa pratibandhya bhāvāt anātma ādīnām api aviparyāsa ādīnām na asti sadbhāvaḥ iti pratipādayan āha na ātmā ca śuci nityam ca sukham ca yadi vidyate anātma aśuci anityam ca na eva duḥkham ca vidyate yadi ātmā ca śuci nityam ca na vidyate iti manyase viparyāsa asaṃbhavāt evam sati ātma ādīnām api abhāvāt yadi etat anātma ādikamaviparyāsa tvena gṛhītam tat api tarhi tyajyatām pratiṣedhya abhāve pratiṣedhasya abhāvāt yadā ca evam anātma ādikam na saṃbhavati tadā tat api svarūpataḥ avidyamāna tvāt ātma ādi vat katham na viparyāsaḥ syāt tasmāt jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāra cāraka āgāra bandhanāt mumukṣubhiḥ aṣṭau api ete viparyāsāḥ tyājyāḥ 
[205,viii_206,i]	asya ca yathā upavarṇita viparyāsa vicārasya avidyā ādi prahāṇa hetu tvena mahārtha tām pratipādayan āha evam nirudhyate avidyā viparyaya nirodhanāt avidyāyām niruddhāyām saṃskāra ādyam nirudhyate yadā ayam yogī yathā uditena nyāyena viparyāsāt na upalabhate tadā evam viparyāsān upalambhanena tad hetukāḥ avidyā nirudhyate tad nirodhāt ca saṃskāra ādayaḥ avidyā hetukāḥ jarā maraṇa śoka parideva duḥkha daurmanasya upāyāsa paryantāḥ dharmāḥ nirudhyante 
[206,ii]	avidyā hi sakalasya eva saṃkleśa gaṇasya jāti ādi duḥkhasya ca hetu bhūtā yathā hi kāya indriya hetukāni sarvāṇi rūpi indriyāṇi kāya indriye nirudhyamāne nirudhyante evam avidyā hetukāni saṃskāra ādīni bhava aṅgāni pravartamānāni niyatam avidyāyām niruddhāyām nirudhyante iti pratipādayan āha avidyāyām niruddhāyām saṃskāra ādyam nirudhyate iti 
[206,iii]	atra āha yadi viparyāsa nirodhāt avidyā nirudhyate asti tarhi avidyā yasyāḥ evam viparyāsa nirodhāt nirodhaḥ bhavati na tarhi avidyamānāyāḥ gagana cūta latāyāḥ prahāṇa upāya anveṣam asti tasmāt vidyate eva avidyā tad nirodha upāya anveṣaṇa sadbhāvāt tatas ca santi tad hetukāḥ rāga ādayaḥ kleśāḥ kleśa asadbhāvāt ca asti eva saṃsāre bhava saṃtatiḥ ucyate atra hi nāma ati mahat anartha pāṇḍityam parasya yaḥ hi nāma sarva ātmanā atyanta duḥkha āyāsa kleśa asamañjase saṃsāre nirantara phulla phala prada saṃkleśa viṣa vṛkṣe parārtha udaya saṃbaddha kakṣaiḥ sādhubhiḥ prajñā upāya mahā anila balaiḥ niḥśeṣam tad unmūlyamānaiḥ na kevalam na sāhāyyena avatiṣṭhante api khalu tad unmūla kānām ati mahā anila balānām iva bhāva sadbhāva vāda mahā śailāyamānaḥ iva ati virodhi tayā avasthitaḥ bhavān āhopuruṣikayā tasya eva kleśa viṣa vṛkṣasya jāti jarā maraṇa śoka āyāsa visara duḥkha eka phalasya sutarām bhāva abhiniveśa toya āsravaiḥ āropaṇam ādriyate 
[206,iv]	api ca yadi avidyā ādīnām saṃkleśānām prahāṇam saṃbhavet syāt tad prahāṇa upāya anveṣaṇam na ca teṣām prahāṇam saṃbhavati yadi syāt tadā tattva rūpataḥ vidyamānānām vā syāt avidyamānānām vā kim ca atas tatra yadi svarūpataḥ sat bhatānām kleśānām prahāṇam iṣyate tat na upapadyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt yadi bhūtāḥ svabhāvena kleśāḥ kecid hi kasyacid katham nāma prahīyeran kaḥ svabhāvam prahāsyati 
[206,v]	svabhāvataḥ vidyamānānām bhāvānām na śakyaḥ svabhāvaḥ vinivartayitum na hi kṣiti ādīnām kaṭhina tva ādi svabhāvaḥ nivartate evam yadi ime kleśāḥ svabhāvataḥ sadbhūtāḥ syuḥ kecid iti avidyā ādayaḥ kasyacid iti pudgalasya katham nāma prahīyeran na eva te kasyacid kathaṃcid nāma prahīyeran kasmāt punar na te prahīyante iti āha kaḥ svabhāvam prahāsyati iti svabhāvasya vinivartayitum aśakyatvāt ākāśānāvaraṇa vinivartana asaṃbhava vat iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[206,vi_207,i]	atha svabhāvena asat bhūtāḥ iti vikalpyate evam api prahāṇa asaṃbhavaḥ eva iti āha yadi abhūtāḥ svabhāvena kleśāḥ kecid hi kasyacid katham nāma prahīyeran kaḥ asadbhāvam prahāsyati abhūtāḥ api kleśāḥ svabhāvena avidyamānāḥ aśakyāḥ eva prahātum na hi agneḥ śaityam asaṃvidyamānam śakyam apākartum evam ime api kleśāḥ kecid yadi kasyacid svabhāvataḥ na vidyante kaḥ tān prahāsyati na eva kaścid prahāsyati tat evam ubhaya pakṣe api prahāṇa asaṃbhavāt na asti prahāṇam kleśānām prahāṇa abhāvāt ca kutas kleśa prahāṇa upāya anveṣaṇam iti atas yat uktam vidyante eva avidyā ādayaḥ kleśāḥ tad prahāṇa upāya anveṣaṇāt iti tat ayuktam iti yathā uktam ārya samādhi rāje 
[207,ii_207,iii]	yaḥ rajyeta yatra vā rajyeta yena vā rajyeta yaḥ duṣyeta yatra vā duṣyeta yena vā duṣyeta yaḥ muhyeta yatra vā muhyeta yena vā muhyeta sa tam dharma na samanupaśyati tam dharmam na upalabhate sa tam dharmam asam anupaśyan anupalabhamānaḥ araktaḥ aduṣṭaḥ amūḍhaḥ aviparyasta cittaḥ samāhitaḥ iti ucyate tīrṇaḥ pāragaḥ iti ucyate kṣema prāptaḥ iti ucyate iti vistaraḥ tathā ādarśa pṛṣṭhe tatha taila pātre nirīkṣate nārimukham su alaṃkṛtam saḥ tatra rāgam janayitva bālaḥ pradhāvitaḥ kāmi gaveṣamāṇaḥ mukhasya saṃkrānti yadā na vidyate bimbe mukham na eva kadāci labhyate mūḍhaḥ yathā saḥ janayeta rāgam tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān ityādi 
[207,iv_208,ii]	tathā rūpeṇa darśitā bodhī bodhaye rūpa darśitam viṣa bhāgena śabdena uttaraḥ dharmu deśitaḥ śabdena uttaram rūpam gambhīram ca svabhāvataḥ samam rūpam ca bodhiḥ ca nānātvam na sa labhyate yathā nirvāṇu gambhīram śabdena saṃprakāśitam labhyate na ca nirvāṇam sa ca śabdaḥ na labhyate śabdaḥ ca api nirvāṇam ca ubhayam tat na labhyate evam śūnyeṣu dharmeṣu nirvāṇam saṃprakāśitam nirvāṇam nivṛttiḥ eva nirvāṇam ca na labhyate apravṛttiḥ hi dharmāṇām yathā paścāt tathā purā sarva dharmāḥ svabhāvena nirvāṇa sama sādṛśāḥ jñātā naiṣkramya sāre hi ye yuktāḥ buddha bodhaye tathā jñānena jānāmi ahu skandha śūnyatām jñātvā ca kleśa ihi na saṃvasāmi vyāhāra mātreṇa hi vyāharāmi parinirvṛtaḥ lokam imam carāmi tathā parinirvṛta loki te śūrāḥ yehi svabhāvata jñātibhi dharmāḥ kāma guṇaiḥ hi caranti asaṅgāḥ saṅgu vivarjiya sattva vinenti iti 
[209,i_209,ii^1]	atra āha yadi śūnyam idam sarvam udayaḥ na asti na vyayaḥ caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvaḥ te prasajyate yadi yuktyā na upapadyate iti kṛtvā sarvam idam bāhyam ādhyātmikam bhāva jātam śūnyam iti pratipāditam nanu ca evam sati bahavaḥ ca mahāntaḥ ca doṣāḥ bhavataḥ āpadyante katham kṛtvā yadi sarvam idam śūnyam syāt tadā yat śūnyam tat na asti yat ca na asti tad avidyamāna tvāt vandhyā putra vat na eva utpadyate na ca api nirudhyate iti na kasyacid padārthasya udayaḥ vyayaḥ ca tad abhāvāt ca caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvaḥ te śūnya vādinaḥ prasajyate katham kṛtvā iha hi pūrva hetu janitāḥ pratītya samutpannāḥ pañca upādāna skandhāḥ duḥkha duḥkha tayā vipariṇāma duḥkha tayā saṃskāra duḥkha tayā ca pratikūla varti tvāt ca pīḍā ātmaka tvena duḥkham iti ucyate etat ca duḥkham āryāḥ eva viparyāsa prahāṇe sati duḥkham iti saṃjānate na anāryāḥ viparyāsa anugata tvāt yathādarśanam ca padārtha svabhāva vyavasthānāt 
[209,ii^2]	yathā hi viparyasta indriyāṇām madhura svabhāvam api guḍa śarkarā ādikam tikta tayā upalabhamānānām jvara ādi roga āturāṇām tikta tā eva satyam tad jñāna apekṣayā mādhuryam tena ātmanā tasya vastunaḥ anupalabhyamāna tvāt evam iha api yadi api pañca upādāna skandhāḥ duḥkha svabhāvāḥ bhavanti tathā api ye etān duḥkha ātmakān paśyanti teṣām eva duḥkham vyavasthāpyate na viparyāsa anugamāt anyathā upalabhamānānām iti atas āryāṇām eva duḥkha ātma tā satyam iti kṛtvā duḥkham ārya satyam iti ucyate nanu ca anāryaiḥ duḥkhāḥ vedanā duḥkham iti paricchidyate iti evam tat katham duḥkham āryāṇām eva satyam 
[209,ii^3]	satyam na hi duḥkhā eva vedanā kevalam duḥkha satyam kim tarhi pañca api upādāna skandhāḥ iti atas āryāṇām eva tat satyam iti kṛtvā ārya satyam iti vyavasthāpyate yathā uktam ūrṇā pakṣma yathā eva hi kara tala saṃstham na vedyate puṃbhiḥ akṣi gatam tu tat eva hi janayati aratim ca pīḍām ca kara tala sadṛśaḥ bālaḥ na vetti saṃskāra duḥkha tā pakṣma akṣi sadṛśaḥ tu vidvān tena eva udvejate gāḍham iti tasmāt āryāṇām eva tad duḥkha satyam iti duḥkham ārya satyam iti vyavasthāpyate 
[209,iii_209,iv]	kadā ca tad duḥkham ārya satyam yujyate yadā saṃskārāṇām udaya vyayau saṃbhavataḥ yadā tu śūnya tvāt na kiṃcid utpadyate na api kiṃcid nirudhyate tadā na asti duḥkham asati ca duḥkhe kutas samudaya satyam yatas hi hetoḥ duḥkham samudeti samutpadyate sa hetuḥ tṛṣṇā karma kleśa lakṣaṇaḥ samudayaḥ iti ucyate yadā tu phala bhūtam duḥkha satyam na asti tadā phala rahitasya hetukatva anupapatteḥ samudayaḥ api na asti 
[210,i]	duḥkhasya ca vigamaḥ apunarutpādaḥ nirodhaḥ iti ucyate yadā tu duḥkham eva na asti tadā kasya nirodhaḥ syāt iti atas duḥkha nirodhaḥ api na saṃbhavati asati hi duḥkhe nirodha satyasya api abhāvaḥ asati ca duḥkha nirodhe kutas duḥkha nirodha gāminī ārya aṣṭa aṅga mārga anugā pratipad bhaviṣyati iti mārga satyam api na asti iti tat evam śūnya tvam bhāvānām bruvataḥ caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvaḥ prasajyate 
[210,ii_210,iii]	tatas ca kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ucyate parijñā ca prahāṇam ca bhāvanā sākṣi karma ca caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvāt na upapadyate caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāva prasaṅge sati yat etat anitya ādibhiḥ ākāraiḥ duḥkha satya parijñānam duḥkha samudayasya ca prahāṇam duḥkha nirodha gāminyāḥ ca pratipadaḥ bhāvanā duḥkha nirodhasya ca sākṣi karma sākṣātkaraṇam tat na upapadyate 
[210,iv]	yadi duḥkha ādīnām ārya satyānām abhāve sati parijñāna ādikam na asti tadā kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ucyate tad abhāvāt na vidyante catvāri ārya phalāni ca phala abhāve phala sthāḥ naḥ na santi pratipannakāḥ saṃghaḥ na asti na ced santi te aṣṭau puruṣa pudgalāḥ abhāvāt ca ārya satyānām saddharmaḥ api na vidyate dharme ca asati saṃghe ca katham buddhaḥ bhaviṣyati 
[210,v^1]	yadā ca evam duḥkha parijñāna ādikam na asti tadā asmin asati srotaāpatti sakṛdāgāmi anāgāmī arhatphala ākhyam phala catuṣṭayam na upapadyate katham kṛtvā iha kleśānām prahāṇam saṃpiṇḍitam phala ākhyam pratilabhate tat yathā saṃyojana traya prahāṇe sati ṣoḍaśe mārge anvayajña āna kṣaṇe yat kleśa prahāṇam tat srotaāpatti phalam kāma avacarāṇām bhāvanā prahātavyānām kleśānām adhimātra madhya mṛdūnām prakārāṇām punar adhimātra madhya mṛdu prakāra bhedena pratyekam bhidyamānānām nava prakārāḥ bhavanti tatra kāma avacara ṣaṣṭha kleśa prakāra parikṣaye vimukti mārge yat prahāṇam tat sakṛdāgāmi phalam teṣām eva kāma avacarāṇām navama prakāra kleśa parikṣaye vimukti mārge yat kleśa prahāṇam tad anāgāmi phalam 
[210,v^2]	rūpārūpya avacarāṇām kleśānām bhāvanā prahātavyānām bhūmau bhūmau nava prakāra bheda bhinnānām yāvat na eva saṃjñāna asaṃjñā yatana bhūmikanavam akleśa prakāra parikṣaye vimukti mārge yat prahāṇam tad arhat phalam iti etāni catvāri phalāni tāni etāni katham yujyante yadi duḥkhasya parijñānam saṃbhavati samudayasya prahāṇam nirodhasya sākṣātkaraṇam ārya mārgasya ca bhāvanā bhavati yadā tu duḥkha ādīnām ārya satyānām abhāve sati duḥkha parijñāna ādikam na asti tadā na santi tāni catvāri phalāni caturṇā ca phalānām abhāve sati ye teṣu vyavasthitāḥ phala sthāḥ catvāraḥ ārya pudgalāḥ te na santi atas eva ca pratipannakāḥ api catvāraḥ ārya pudgalāḥ na saṃvidyante 
[211,i]	iha hi ṣoḍaśāt mārge anvaya jñāna kṣaṇāt pūrve ye pañcadaśa kṣānti jñā na kṣaṇāḥ tat yathā traidhātuka duḥkha abhisamaye duḥkha satya ālambanāḥ catvāraḥ kṣānti jñā na kṣaṇāḥ tatra katame traidhātuka duḥkha abhisamaye catvāraḥ kṣānti jñā na kṣaṇāḥ tat yathā k ā m ā v a c a r a d u ḥ k h a d a rśana prahātavyasat kāya anta grāha mithyā dṛṣṭi dṛṣṭi parāmarśa śīla vrata parāmarśa vicikitsā rāga pratighamāna avidyā ākhya daśa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ anitya duḥkha śūnya an ātma ākāra utpannaḥ kāma avacara duḥkha satya ālambanaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ duḥkhe dharma jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ tad ālambana ākāraḥ eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ duḥkhe dharma jñāna kṣaṇaḥ dvitīyaḥ evam rūpa ārūpya avacara duḥkha satya ālambanaḥ pratigha varjita anantara ukta aṣṭādaśa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ duḥkha ādi ākāra utpannaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ duḥkhe anvayajñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tad ālambana ākāraḥ eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ duḥkhe anvayajñānakṣaṇaḥ caturthaḥ 
[211,ii]	yathā ca ete traidhātuka avacara duḥkha satya abhisamaye kṣānti jñā na kṣaṇāḥ catvāraḥ evam kāma avacara sam udaya darśana prahāta vyamithyā dṛṣṭi dṛṣṭi parāmarśa vicikitsā rāga pratighamāna avidyā ākhya sapta anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ hetu samudaya prabhava pratyaya ākāra utpannaḥ kāma avacara sam udaya sati ālambanaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ samudaye dharma jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ tad ālambana ākāraḥ eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ samudaye dharma jñāna kṣayaḥ dvitīyaḥ evam rūpa ārūpya avacara samudaya sati ālambanaḥ pratigha varjita anantara ukta dvādaśa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ samudaya sati ākāra utpannaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ samudaye anvayajñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tad ālambana ākāraḥ eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ samudaye anvayajñānakṣaṇaḥ caturthaḥ iti ete traidhātuka avacara duḥkha samudaya satya abhisamaye catvāraḥ kṣaṇāḥ 
[211,iii]	yathā ca ete catvāraḥ kṣaṇāḥ traidhātuka duḥkha samudaya satya abhisamaye evam kāma avacara duḥkha nirodha darśana prahātavya sam udaya ukta sapta anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ nirodha śānta praṇīta niḥsaraṇa ākāra utpannaḥ kāma avacara duḥkha nirodha satya ālambanaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ nirodhe dharma jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ tad ālambana ākāraḥ eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ nirodhe dharma jñāna kṣaṇaḥ dvitīyaḥ etaiḥ eva ākāraiḥ rūpa ārūpya avacara duḥkha nirodha satya ālambanaḥ pratigha varjita dvādaśa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ nirodhe anvayajñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tad ālambana ākāraḥ eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ nirodhe anvayajñānakṣaṇaḥ caturthaḥ iti ete traidhātuka avacara duḥkha nirodha satya abhisamaye catvāraḥ kṣaṇāḥ 
[211,iv_211,v]	evam kāma avacara duḥkha nirodha gāmi mārga darśana prahāta vya nirodha ukta anuśayeṣu śīla vrata parāmarśam aṣṭamam prakṣipya aṣṭa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ mārga nyāya pratipad naiḥ yāṇika ākāra utpannaḥ kāma avacara duḥkha nirodha gāmi mārga ālambanaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ mārge dharma jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ tad ālambana ākāraḥ eva ca vimukti mārga lakṣaṇaḥ mārge dharma jñāna kṣaṇaḥ dvitīyaḥ etaiḥ eva ākāraiḥ rūpa ārūpya avacara duḥkha nirodha gāmi mārga ālambanaḥ pratigha varjita caturdaśa anuśaya pratipakṣaḥ ānantarya mārga lakṣaṇaḥ mārge anvaya jñāna kṣānti kṣaṇaḥ tṛtīyaḥ iti ete pañcadaśa kṣaṇāḥ darśana mārga abhidhānāḥ evam vyavasthitaḥ āryaḥ srotaāpatti phala sākṣāt kriyāyai pratipannakaḥ iti ucyate ṣoḍaśe tu mārge anvaya jñāna sthitaḥ sa srotaāpannaḥ iti ucyate 
[212,i]	te ete aṣṭāśītiḥ anuśayāḥ satyānām darśana mātreṇa bhāvanām anapekṣya eva prahīyante iti kṛtvā darśana prahātavyāḥ iti ucyante yathā dṛṣṭa satya ākāra bhāvanayā tu ye paścāt prahīyante te bhāvanā prahātavyāḥ te ca daśa anuśayāḥ bhavanti kāmāvacarāḥ rāga pratighamāna avidyāḥ rūpāvacarāḥ eva pratigha varjita asrayaḥ ārūpya avacarāḥ ca trayaḥ ete eva iti daśa bhavanti ete ca yathā uktena nyāyena bhūmau bhūmau navadhāḥ bhidyante kāmadhātau caturṣu dhyāneṣu caturṣu ārūpyeṣu ekaikasya ca kleśa prakārasya prahāṇa artham ānantarya vimukti mārga bhedena dvau dvau jñāna kṣaṇau vyavasthā apyete kleśa kṣaṇa viparyayeṇa adhimātra adhimātraḥ hi kleśa prakāraḥ mṛdu mṛdubhyām ānantarya vimukti mārgābhyām prahīyate yāvat mṛdu mṛdu kleśa prakāraḥ adhimātra adhimātrābhyām jñāna kṣaṇābhyām prahīyate sthūlam hi malam alpa prayatna sādhyam sūkṣmam tu mahā yatna sādhyam rajaka vastra dhāvana sādharmyeṇa iti vijñeyam 
[212,ii]	tatra darśana mārgāt ūrdhvam kāma avacara bhāvanā prahātavya ṣaṣṭha kleśa prakāra pratipakṣa vimukti mārga ākhya jñā nakṣaṇāt arvāk jñāna kṣaṇa avasthitaḥ āryaḥ sakṛdāgāmi phala pratipannakaḥ iti ucyate sakṛt imam lokam āgatya parinirvāṇāt sakṛdāgāmi iti ucyate tad phala arthaṃpratipannakaḥ prayoga sthaḥ sakṛdāgāmi phala pratipannakaḥ iti ucyate ṣaṣṭhe tu kṣaṇe sakṛdāgāmi iti ucyate 
[212,iii]	ṣaṣṭhāt kṣaṇāt ūrdhva navama kleśa prakāra prahāṇa vimukti mārga kṣaṇāt arvāk jñā na kṣaṇeṣu vartamānaḥ āryaḥ anāgāmi phalapratipannakaḥ iti ucyate anāgatya imam lokam tatra eva parinirvāṇāt anāgāmī iti ucyate tad phala artham pratipannakaḥ prayoga sthaḥ anāgāmi phalapratipannakaḥ iti ucyate navame tu kṣaṇe anāgāmī iti ucyate 
[212,iv]	kāma avacara navamavimukti mārga kṣaṇāt ūrdhvam na eva saṃjñāna asaṃjñā tayana bhūmi kanavam akleśa prakāra prahāṇa vimukti mārga kṣaṇāt arvāk jñā na kṣaṇeṣu vartamānaḥ āryaḥ arhat phala pratipannakaḥ iti ucyate sa deva mānuṣa asurāt lokāt pūjā arha tvāt arhan iti ucyate tad phala artham pratipannakaḥ prayoga sthaḥ arhat phala pratipannakaḥ iti ucyate bhava agrika navam akleśa prakāra prahāṇāt tu navama vimukti mārge vyavasthitaḥ arhan bhavati 
[212,v]	te ete catvāraḥ pratipannakāḥ pudgalāḥ catvāraḥ ca phala sthāḥ iti ete aṣṭau mahāpuruṣa pudgalāḥ bhavanti parama dakṣiṇārhā uktā bhagavatā yathā uktam sūtre pṛṣṭaḥ sa devarājena śakreṇa vaśavartinā kṛṣatām yajamānānām prāṇinām puṇya kāṅkṣiṇām kurvatām śraddhat dadhānānām puṇyam aupadhikam sadā sukṣetram te pravakṣyāmi yatra dattam mahat phalam pratipannakāḥ catvāraḥ catvāraḥ ca phala sthitāḥ eṣa saṃghaḥ dakṣiṇīyaḥ vidyā caraṇa saṃpadā iti 
[212,vi]	yadi catvāri ārya satyāni na santi teṣām ca parijñānāni tadā satya darśana bhāvanā labhyānām phalānām abhāvāt pratipannaka phala stha pudgalānām abhāvaḥ eva atas ca saṃghaḥ na asti tatra adhigama dharmeṇa pratyakṣa dharma tayā sarva māraiḥ api buddhe bhagavati abhedya tvāt avetya prasāda lābhena saṃghaḥ sa na syāt na ced santi te aṣṭau puruṣa pudgalāḥ 
[213,i_213,ii]	ārya satyānām ca abhāvāt saddharmaḥ api na saṃbhavati satām āryāṇām dharmaḥ saddharmaḥ tatra nirodha satyam phala dharmaḥ mārga satyam tu phala avatāra dharmaḥ eṣa tāvat adhigama dharmaḥ tad saṃprakāśikāḥ deśanā āgama dharmaḥ sarvaḥ eṣaḥ ārya satyānām abhāve sati na asti iti abhāvāt ca ārya satyānām saddharmaḥ api na vidyate dharme ca asati saṃghe ca katham buddhaḥ bhaviṣyati yadi hi yathā uktaḥ dharmaḥ syāt tadā tad dharma pratipattyā sarva ākāra sarva dharma abhisaṃbodhāt buddhaḥ bhavati iti yuktam syāt yadi ca saṃghaḥ syāt tadā tad upadeśaiḥ upacīyamāna jñāna saṃbhāraḥ tad dāna māna śaraṇa gamana ādibhiḥ ca upacīyamāna puṇya saṃbhāraḥ kramāt buddhaḥ bhavet 
[213,iii]	athavā asati saṃghe srotaāpatti phala pratipannaka ādīnām abhāvaḥ syāt na ca pratipannaka ādi tvam aprāpya buddha tvam āpyate avaśyam hi pūrvam bhagavatā kasmiṃścid phale vyavasthātavyam tatra ca phale vyavasthitaḥ saṃgha antaḥ pātyā iva bhagavān bhavati saṃghe ca asati niyatam na asti bhagavān buddhaḥ atha bhagavān api aśaikṣa antarbhāvāt saṃgha antargataḥ eva tathā ca buddha pramukhaḥ bhikṣu saṃghaḥ iti abhidhānāt saṃgha antargataḥ eva bhagavān iti kecid varṇayanti teṣām matena spaṣṭam eva etat dharme ca asati saṃghe ca katham buddhaḥ bhaviṣyati iti 
[213,iv_213,v]	madhya uddeśikāḥ ca mahā vastu upadiṣṭa bhūmi vyavasthayā prathama bhūmi sthitam bodhisattvam utpanna darśana mārgam vyācakṣāṇāḥ saṃgha antaḥpātinam vyācakṣate tadā saṃghe ca asati bodhisattvaḥ api na asti iti katham buddhaḥ bhaviṣyati iti spaṣṭam eva etat tat evam trīṇi api ratnāni bruvāṇaḥ pratibādhase śūnyatām iti evam vadan buddha dharma saṃgha ākhyāni trīṇi api durlabha tvāt kadācid eva utpattitaḥ alpa puṇyānām ca tad aprāpteḥ mahārgha mūlya tvāt ratnāni pratibādhase 
[213,vi_213,vii]	kim ca anyat śūnyatām phala sadbhāvam adharmam dharmam eva ca sarva saṃvyavahārān ca laukikān pratibādhase śūnyatām bruvāṇaḥ iti anena saṃbandhaḥ yadi sarvam idam śūnyam yadā sarvam eva na asti tadā sarva antaḥ pāti tvāt dharma adharmau saha tad hetukena iṣṭa aniṣṭa phalena na saṃbhavataḥ sarve eva ca amī laukikāḥ vyavahārāḥ kuru paca khāda tiṣṭha gaccha āgacchaḥ iti evamādayaḥ api sarva antargata tvāt sarva dharmāṇām ca śūnya tvāt na eva yujyante iti atas na ayam yathā upavarṇitaḥ nyāyaḥ jyāyān iti 
[213,viii_214,i]	atra brūmaḥ śūnyatāyām na tvam vetsi prayojanam śūnyatām śūnyatā artham ca tatas evam vihanyase sa bhavān sva vikalpanayā eva nāstitvam śūnyatā arthaḥ iti evam viparītam adhyāropya yadi sarvam idam śūnyam udayaḥ na asti na vyayaḥ ityādinā upālambham bruvāṇaḥ asmāsu mahāntam khedam āpannaḥ atīva vihanyate vividhaiḥ bhūtaiḥ parikalpaiḥ hanyate iti arthaḥ na tu ayam asmābhiḥ atra śāstre śūnyatā artham upavarṇitaḥ yaḥ tvayā parigṛhītaḥ śūnyatā artham ca ajānānaḥ śūnyatām api na jānāsi na ca api śūnyatāyāḥ yat prayojanam tat vijānāsi tatas ca yathā avasthita vastu svarūpa aparijñānena etat tvayā bahu ca ayuktam asmad vaya ākhyāna asaṃbaddham eva upavarṇitam 
[214,ii_214,v]	atha kim punar śūnyatāyām prayojanam uktam eva tad ātma parīkṣāyām karma kleśa kṣayāt mokṣaḥ karma kleśāḥ vikalpataḥ te prapañcāt prapañcaḥ tu śūnyatāyām nirudhyate iti atas niravaśeṣa prapañca upaśama artham śūnyatā upadiśyate tasmāt sarva prapañca upaśamaḥ śūnyatāyām prayojanam bhavān tu nāstitvam śūnyatā artham parikalpayan prapañca jālam eva saṃvardhayamānaḥ na śūnyatāyām prayojanam vetti atha kā punar śūnyatā sā api tatra eva uktā apara pratyayam śāntam prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam nirvikalpa manāna artham etat tatvasya lakṣaṇam iti 
[214,vi]	atas prapañca nivṛtti svabhāvāyām śūnyatāyām kutas nāstitvam iti śūnyatām apina jānāti bhavān yam ca artham upādāya śūnyatā śabdaḥ pravartate tam api iha eva pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ yaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ śūnyatām tām pracakṣmahe sā prajñaptiḥ upādāya pratipatsā eva madhyamā iti yaḥ pratyayaiḥ jāyati sa hi ajātaḥ na tasya utpādu svabhāvataḥ asti yaḥ pratyaya adhīnu sa śūnyu uktaḥ yaḥ śūnyatām jānati saḥ apramattaḥ 
[214,vii]	iti bhagavataḥ gāthā vacanāt evam pratītyasamutpāda śabdasya yaḥ arthaḥ saḥ eva śūnyatā śabdasya arthaḥ na punar abhāva śabdasya yaḥ arthaḥ sa śūnyatā śabdasya arthaḥ abhāva śabda artham ca śūnyatā artham iti adhyāropya bhavān asmān upālabhate tasmāt śūnyatā śabda artham api na jānāti ajānānaḥ ca tvam evam upālambham kurvan niyatam vihanyase 
[214,viii_215,i]	kaḥ ca asmākam yathoktam upālambham karoti yaḥ bhagavat pravacana upadiṣṭa aviparīta satya dvaya vibhāgam na jānāti kevalam grantha mātra adhyayana paraḥ eva iti atas ācāryaḥ karuṇayā parasya mithyā pravacana artha avabodha nirāsa artham bhagavat pravacana upadiṣṭa aviparīta satya dvaya vyavasthām eva tāvat adhikṛtya āha dve satye samupāśritya buddhānām dharma deśanā loka saṃvṛti satyam ca satyam ca paramārthataḥ iha hi bhagavatām buddhānām satya dvayam āśritya dharma deśanā pravartate katamat satya dvayam loka saṃvṛti satyam ca parama artha satyam ca tatra skandha ātmā lokaḥ ākhyātaḥ tatra lokaḥ hi niśritaḥ 
[215,ii]	iti vacanāt pañca skandhān upādāya prajñapyamānaḥ pudgalaḥ lokaḥ iti ucyate samantāt varaṇam saṃvṛtiḥ ajñānam hi samantāt sarva padārtha tattva avacchādanāt saṃvṛtiḥ iti ucyate paraspara saṃbhavanam vā saṃvṛtiḥ anyonya samāśrayeṇa iti arthaḥ athavā saṃvṛtiḥ saṃketaḥ loka vyavahāraḥ iti arthaḥ sa ca abhidhāna abhidheya jñāna jñeya ādi lakṣaṇaḥ loke saṃvṛtiḥ loka saṃvṛtiḥ kim punar aloka saṃvṛtiḥ api asti yatas evam viśiṣyate loka saṃvṛtiḥ iti yathā avasthita padārtha anuvādaḥ eṣaḥ na atra eṣā cintā avatarati athavā timira kāmalā ādi upahata indriya viparīta darśana avasthānāḥ te alokāḥ teṣām yā saṃvṛti rasa avaloka saṃvṛtiḥ atas viśiṣyate loka saṃvṛtiḥ iti etat ca madhyamaka avatāre vistareṇa uktam tatas veditavyam loka saṃvṛtyā satyam loka saṃvṛti satyam sarve eva ayam abhidhāna abhidheya jñāna jñeya ādi vyavahāraḥ aśeṣaḥ loka saṃvṛti satyam iti ucyate na hi paramārthataḥ ete vyavahārāḥ saṃbhavanti tatra hi nivṛttam abhidhātavyam nivṛtte citta gocare anutpanna aniruddhā hi nirvāṇam iva dharma tā 
[215,iii]	iti kṛtvā kutas tatra parama arthe vācām pravṛttiḥ kutas vā jñānasya sa hi parama arthaḥ apara pratyayaḥ śāntaḥ pratyātma vedyaḥ āryāṇām sarva prapañca atītaḥ sa na upadiśyate na ca api jñāyate uktam hi pūrvam apara pratyayam śāntam prapañcaiḥ aprapañcitam nirvikalpa manāna artham etat tattvasya lakṣaṇam iti 
[215,iv]	paramaḥ ca āsau arthaḥ ca iti parama arthaḥ tat eva satyam parama artha satyam anayoḥ ca satyayoḥ vibhāgaḥ vistareṇa madhyamaka avatārāt avaseyaḥ tat etat satya dvayam āśritya buddhānām bhagavatām dharma deśanā pravartate evam vyavasthite deśanā krame ye anayoḥ na vijānanti vibhāgam satyayoḥ dvayoḥ te tattvam na vijānanti gambhīram buddha śāsane 
[215,v_216,i]	atra āha yadi tarhi parama arthaḥ niṣprapañca svabhāvaḥ saḥ eva astu tat kim anayā aparayā skandha dhātu āyata nāri asatya pratītyasamutpāda ādi deśanayā prayojanam aparama arthayā ata tvam hi parityājyam yat ca parityājyam kim tena upadiṣṭena ucyate satyam etat evam kim tu laukikam vyavahāram anabhyupagamya abhidhāna abhidheya jñāna jñeya ādi lakṣaṇam aśakyaḥ eva parama arthaḥ deśayitum adeśitaḥ ca na śakyaḥ adhigantum anadhigamya ca parama artham na śakyam nirvāṇam adhigantum iti pratipādayan āha vyavahāram anāśritya parama arthaḥ na deśyate paramārtham anāgamya nirvāṇam na adhigamyate tasmāt nirvāṇa adhigama upāya tvāt avaśyam eva yathā avasthitā saṃvṛtiḥ ādau eva abhyupeyāḥ bhājanam iva salila arthinā iti 
[216,ii_216,iii]	tat evam yaḥ saṃvṛti parama artha lakṣaṇa satya dvayasya vyavasthām apākṛtya śūnyatām varṇayati tam tathāvidham pudgalam vināśayati durdṛṣṭā śūnyatā manda medhasam sarpaḥ yathā durgṛhītaḥ vidyā vā duṣprasādhitā saṃvṛti satyam hi ajñāna mātra samutthāpitam niḥsvabhāvam buddhā tasya parama artha lakṣaṇām śūnyatām pratipadyamānaḥ yogī na anta dvaye patati kim tadā āsīt yat idānīm na asti iti evam pūrvam bhāva svabhāva anupalambhāt paścāt api na astitām na pratipadyate pratibimba ākārāyāḥ ca loka saṃvṛteḥ abādhanāt karma karma phala dharma adharma ādikam api na bādhate na ca api parama artham bhāva svabhāva tvena samāropayati niḥsvabhāvānām eva padārthānām karma phala ādi darśanāt sa svabhāvanām ca adarśanāt 
[216,iv]	yaḥ tu evam satya dvaya vibhāgam apaśyan śūnyatām saṃskārāṇām paśyati sa śūnyatām paśyan mumukṣuḥ na astitām vā saṃskārāṇām parikalpayet yadi vā śūnyatām kāṃcid bhāvataḥ satīm tasyāḥ ca āśraya artham bhāva svabhāvam api parikalpayet ubhayathā ca asya durdṛṣṭā śūnyatā niyatam vināśayet katham kṛtvā yadi tāvat sarvam idam śūnyam sarvam na asti iti parikalpayet tadā asya mithyādṛṣṭiḥ āpadyate yathā uktam vināśayati durdṛṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ ayam avipaścitam na astita adṛṣṭi samale yasmāt asmin nimajjati 
[216,v_216,vi]	atha sarva apavādam kartum na icchati tadā niyatam asya śūnyatāyāḥ pratikṣepaḥ āpadyate katham hi nāma amī bhāvāḥ sakala sura asura nara lokaiḥ upalabhyamānāḥ api śūnyāḥ bhaviṣyanti tasmāt na niḥsvabhāva arthaḥ śūnyatā arthaḥ iti evam pratikṣipya sat dharma vyasana saṃvartanīyena pāpakena karmaṇā niyatam apāya anvayāt yathā uktam ārya ratna āvalyām aparaḥ api asya durjñānāt mūrkhaḥ paṇḍita mānikaḥ pratikṣepa vinaṣṭa ātmā yāti avīcim adhomukhaḥ iti evam tāvat abhāvena gṛhyamāṇā śūnyatā grahītāram vināśayati atha ayam bhāvena śūnyatām parikalpayet tad āśrayāṇām ca saṃskārāṇām astitvam evam api nirvāṇa gāmini mārge vipratipanna tvāt śūnyatā upadeśa vihvalaḥ jāyeta tat evam bhāva rūpeṇa api śūnyatā gṛhyamāṇā grahītāram vināśayati 
[216,vii]	nanu ca yat upakārakam tat anyathā kriyamāṇam akāla uptam iva bījam na phalāya kalpate kāloptam ca mahate phala lābhāya jāyate evam eva maṇi mantra auṣadha ādibhiḥ gṛhyamāṇaḥ sarpaḥ mahāntam dhana skandham āvahati śiromaṇi grahaṇāt tena ca vyāla grāhakāṇām jīvikā kalpanāt yathā uddeśa tiraskāreṇa tu gṛhyamāṇaḥ grahītāram eva vināśayati yathā ca yathopadeśam prasādhitā vidyā sādhakam anugṛhṇāti upadeśa paribhraṣṭā tu sādhyamānā sādhakam eva vināśayati evam iha api yathopadeśam śūnyatā mahatī vidyā sādhyamānā gṛhyamāṇā bhāva abhāva ādi grāha tiraskāreṇa madhyamayā pratipadā grahītāram parameṇa jāti jarā maraṇa ādi duḥkha hutāśana śamana eka rasena nirupadhi śeṣa nirvāṇa jala dhara dhārā varṣa mukhena yojayati yathā upadeśa viśeṣa vigamena tu gṛhyamāṇā niyatam yathā uditena nyāyena grahītāram eva vināśayati 
[217,i_217,ii]	yatas ca evam śūnyatā durgṛhītā grahītāram vināśayati manda prajñaiḥ ca aśakyā samyak grahītum atas ca pratyudāvṛttam cittam deśayitum muneḥ dharmam matvā asya dharmasya mandaiḥ duravagāha tām yasmāt ayam śūnyatā lakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ manda medha samalpa prajñam sattvam viparyāsa grahaṇāt vināśayati atas eva asya dharmasya mandaiḥ duravagāha tām matvā anuttarām samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbudhya sarva sattva dhātum ca avalokya dharmasya ca atigāmbhīryam saddharmam deśayitum cittam pratinivṛttam muneḥ buddhasya bhagavataḥ mahā upāya jñāna viśeṣa śālinaḥ yathā uktam sūtre 
[217,iii]	atha bhagavataḥ acira abhisaṃbuddhasya etat abhavat adhigataḥ mayā dharmaḥ gambhīraḥ gambhīra avabhāsaḥ atarkaḥ atarka avacaraḥ sūkṣmaḥ paṇḍita vijña vedanīyaḥ saced tam aham pareṣām ārocayeyam pare ca me na vibhāvayeyuḥ sa mama vighātaḥ syāt klamathaḥ syāt cetasaḥ anudayaḥ syāt yat nu aham ekāki araṇye pravivikte dṛṣṭa dharma sukha vihāram anuprāptaḥ vihareyam iti vistaraḥ 
[217,iv_217,v]	tat evam satya dvaya aviparīta vyavasthām avijñāya śūnyatāyām adhilayam yam punar kurute bhavān doṣa prasaṅgaḥ na asmākam sa śūnye na upapadyate yaḥ ayam bhavatā mahān doṣa prasaṅgaḥ asmāsu prakṣiptaḥ yadi śūnyam idam sarvam udayaḥ na asti na vyayaḥ ityādinā sa yasmāt satya dvaya vyavasthā anabhijñena satā śūnyatām śūnyatā artham śūnyatā prayojanam ca yathāvat abuddhāḥ upakṣiptaḥ saḥ asmākam śūnye śūnyatā vāde na upapadyate yatas ca na upapadyate atas yam bhavān doṣa prasaṅgam śūnyatāyām udbhāvayan śūnyatāyām adhilayam adhikṣepam nirākaraṇam pratikṣepam karoti saḥ adhilayaḥ asmākam na upapadyate abhāva artham hi śūnyatā artham adhyāropya prasaṅgaḥ udbhāvitaḥ bhavatā na ca vayam abhāva artham śūnyatā artham vyācakṣmahe kim tarhi pratītyasamutpāda artham iti atas na yuktam etat śūnyatā darśana dūṣaṇam 
[217,vi_218,i]	na ca kevalam yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ asmad pakṣe na avatarati api khalu sarvam eva satya ādi vyavasthānam sutarām upapadyate iti pratipādayan āha sarvam ca yujyate tasya śūnyatā yasya yujyate sarvaṃna yujyate tasya śūnyam yasya na yujyate yasya hi sarva bhāva svabhāva śūnyatā iyam yujyate tasya sarvam etat yathā upavarṇitam yujyate katham kṛtvā yasmāt pratītyasamutpādam hi vayam śūnyatā iti vyācakṣmahe yaḥ pratyayaiḥ jāyati sa hi ajātaḥ na tasya utpādu svabhāvataḥ asti yaḥ pratyaya adhīnu sa śūnye uktaḥ yaḥ śūnyatām jānati saḥ apramattaḥ iti gāthā vacanāt śūnyāḥ sarva dharmāḥ niḥsvabhāva yogena iti prajñāpāramitā abhidhānāt 
[218,ii^1]	tasmāt yasya iyam śūnyatā yujyate rocate kṣamate tasya pratītyasamutpādaḥ yujyate yasya pratītyasamutpādaḥ yujyate tasya catvāri ārya satyāni yujyante katham kṛtvā yasmāt pratītyasamutpannam hi duḥkham bhavati na apratītya samutpannam tat ca niḥsvabhāva tvāt śūnyam sati ca duḥkhe duḥkha samudayaḥ duḥkha nirodhaḥ duḥkha nirodha gāminī ca pratipad yujyate tatas ca duḥkha parijñānam samudaya prahāṇam nirodha sākṣāt karaṇam mārga bhāvanā ca yujyate sati ca duḥkha ādi satya parijñāna ādike phalāni yujyante satsu ca phaleṣu phala sthāḥ yujyante satsu ca phala stheṣu pratipannakāḥ yujyante satsu ca pratipannaka phala stheṣu saṃghaḥ yujyate 
[218,ii^2]	ārya satyānām ca sadbhāve sati saddharmaḥ api yujyate sati ca saddharme saṃghe ca buddhaḥ api yujyate tatas ca trīṇi api ratnāni yujyante laukika lokottarāḥ ca padārthāḥ sarve viśeṣa adhigamāḥ yujyante dharma adharmam tad phalam sugati durgatiḥ laukikāḥ ca sarva saṃvyavahārāḥ yujyante tat evam sarvam ca yujyate tasya śūnyatā yasya yujyate yasya sarva bhāva svabhāva śūnyatā yujyate tasya sarvam etat yathā uditam yujyate saṃpadyate iti arthaḥ yasya tu śūnyatā yathā uditā na yujyate tasya pratītyasamutpāda abhāvāt sarvam na yujyate yathā ca na yujyate tathā vistareṇa pratipādayiṣyati 
[218,iii_219,i]	tat evam āsmākīne su pariśuddhatare sarva vyavasthāsu aviruddhe vyavasthite atisthūle ati āsanne tad viruddhe ca svakīye pakṣe doṣavati atimoghaḥ yathāvat avasthitau guṇa doṣau apaśyan sa tvam doṣān ātmanīnān asmāsu paripātayan aśvam eva abhiruḍhaḥ san aśvam eva asi vismṛtaḥ yathā hi kaścid yam eva aśvam ārūḍhaḥ tam eva vismṛtaḥ san tad apahāra doṣeṇa parān upālabhate evam eva bhavān pratītyasamutpāda lakṣaṇa śūnyatā darśana aśvam ārūḍhaḥ eva atyanta vikṣepāt tam anupalambhamānaḥ asmān parivadati 
[219,ii_219,iii]	ke punar te parasya doṣāḥ yān anupalabhamānaḥ śūnyatā vādinam eva upālabhate iti tān pratipādayan āha svabhāvāt yadi bhāvānām sadbhāvam anupaśyasi ahetu pratyayān bhāvān tvam evam sati paśyasi yadi tvam svabhāvena vidyamānān bhāvān paśyasi tadā svabhāvasya hetu pratyaya nirapekṣa tvāt ahetu pratyayān avidyamāna hetu pratyayān padārthān bāhya ādhyātmika bheda bhinnāt nirhetukān tvam evam sati paśyasi 
[219,iv_219,v]	sati ca ahetuka tva abhyupagame kāryam ca kāraṇam ca eva kartāram karaṇam kriyām utpādam ca nirodham ca phalam ca pratibādhase katham kṛtvā yadi iha ghaṭaḥ svabhāvataḥ asti iti parikalpayasi tadā asya svabhāvataḥ vidyamānasya kim mṛd ādibhiḥ hetu pratyayaiḥ prayojanam iti teṣām abhāvaḥ syāt nirhetukam ca kāryam ghaṭa ākhyam na upapadyate asati ca asmin cakra ādikasya karaṇasya kartuḥ kumbhakārasya ghaṭa karaṇa kriyāyāḥ ca abhāvāḥ dutpāda nirodhayoḥ abhāvaḥ asatoḥ ca utpāda nirodhayoḥ kutas phalam iti sa svabhāva abhyupagame sati sarvam etat kārya ādikam pratibādhase tat evam bhavataḥ sa svabhāva abhyupagame sati sarvam eva na yujyate 
[219,vi_219,ix]	asmākam tu bhāva svabhāva śūnyatāvādinām sarvam etat upapadyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt vayam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ śūnyatām tām pracakṣmahe sā prajñaptiḥ upādāya pratipatsā eva madhyamā yaḥ ayam pratītyasamutpādaḥ hetu pratyayān apekṣya aṅkura vijñāna ādīnām prādurbhāvaḥ sa svabhāve na anutpādaḥ yaḥ ca svabhāvena anutpādaḥ bhāvānām sā śūnyatā yathā bhagavatā uktam yaḥ pratyatyaiḥ jāyati sa hi ajātaḥ na tasya utpādu svabhāvataḥ asti yaḥ pratyaya adhīnu sa śūnye uktaḥ yaḥ śūnyatām jānati saḥ apramattaḥ iti tathā ārya laṅka avatāre svabhāva anutpattim saṃdhāya mahāmate sarva dharmāḥ śūnyāḥ iti mayā deśitāḥ iti vistareṇa uktam dvayardha śatikāyām śūnyāḥ sarva dharmāḥ niḥsvabhāva yogena iti 
[219,x]	yā ca iyam svabhāva śūnyatā sā prajñaptiḥ upādāya sā eva śūnyatā upādāya prajñaptiḥ iti vyavasthāpyate cakra ādīni upādāya rathāṅgāni rathaḥ prajñapyate tasya yā sva aṅgāni upādāya prajñaptiḥ sā svabhāvena anutpattiḥ yā ca svabhāvena anutpattiḥ sā śūnyatā sā eva svabhāva anutpatti lakṣaṇā śūnyatā madhyamā pratipad iti vyavasthāpyate yasya hi svabhāvena anutpattiḥ tasya astitva abhāvaḥ svabhāvena ca anutpannasya vigama abhāvāt na astitva abhāvaḥ iti atas bhāva abhāva anta dvaya rahita tvāt sarva svabhāva anutpatti lakṣaṇā śūnyatā madhyamā pratipad madhyamaḥ mārgaḥ iti ucyate tat evam pratītyasamutpādasya eva etāḥ viśeṣa saṃjñāḥ śūnyatā upādāya prajñaptiḥ madhyamā pratipad iti 
[220,i_220,ii]	vicāryamāṇaḥ ca sarvathā apratītya samutpannaḥ dharmaḥ kaścid na vidyate yasmāt tasmāt aśūnyaḥ hi dharmaḥ kaścid na vidyate yaḥ hi apratītya samutpannaḥ dharmaḥ sa na saṃvidyate yathā uktam śatake apratītya astitā na asti kadācid kasyacid kvacid na kadācid kvacid kaścid vidyate tena śāśvataḥ ākāśa ādīni kalpyante nityāni iti pṛthagjanaiḥ laukikena api teṣu arthān na paśyanti vicakṣaṇāḥ iti 
[220,iii_220,iv]	uktam ca bhagavatā pratītya dharmān adhigacchate vidū na ca anta dṛṣṭīya karoti niśrayam sa hetu sa pratyaya dharma jānati ahetu apratyaya na asti dharma tā evam apratītya samutpannaḥ dharmaḥ kaścid na vidyate apratīsam utpannaḥ ca śūnyaḥ tasmāt aśūnyaḥ dharmaḥ na asti yatas etat evam atas asmākam sarva dharmāḥ ca śūnyāḥ na ca para ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ 
[220,v_220,vi]	bhavataḥ tu sa svabhāva vādinaḥ yadi aśūnyam idam sarvam udayaḥ na asti na vyayaḥ tadā niyatam udaya vyayayoḥ abhāve sati caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvaḥ te prasajyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt apratītya samutpannam kutas duḥkham bhaviṣyati anityam uktam duḥkham hi tat svābhāvye na vidyate 
[220,vii]	yat hi sa svabhāvam na tat pratītya utpadyate yat ca apratītya samutpannam na tat anityam bhavati na hi gaganakusumam avidyamānam anityam anityam ca duḥkhamuktam bhava gatā yat anityam tat duḥkham iti tathā ca śataka śāstre anityasya dhruvā pīḍā pīḍā yasya na tad sukham tasmāt anityam yat sarvam duḥkham tat iti jāyate iti yat ca anityam svābhāvye sa svabhāva tve abhyupagamyamāne bhāvānām tat na vidyate iti 
[221,i_221,ii]	evam tāvat sa svabhāva tve sati bhāvānām duḥkham na yujyate na ca kevalam duḥkham eva na yujyate sati sa svabhāva abhyupagame samudayaḥ api na yujyate iti pratipādayan āha svabhāvataḥ vidyamānam kim punar samudeṣyate tasmāt samudayaḥ na asti śūnyatām pratibādhataḥ iha samudeti asmāt duḥkham iti duḥkhasya hetutaḥ samudayaḥ iti ucyate tat asya duḥkhasya śūnyatām pratibādhamānasya sa svabhāvam duḥkham abhyupagacchataḥ tasya punar utpāda vaiyarthyāt tad hetu kalpanā vaii arthyam eva iti evam śūnyatām pratibādhamānasya samudayaḥ api bhavataḥ na yujyate 
[221,iii_221,iv]	svābhāvikam eva duḥkham abhyupagacchataḥ duḥkha nirodhaḥ api na yujyate iti pratipādayan āha na nirodhaḥ svabhāvena sataḥ duḥkhasya vidyate svabhāva paryavasthānāt nirodham pratibādhase yadi hi svabhāvataḥ duḥkham syāt tadā svabhāvasya anapāyi tvāt kutas asya nirodha tvam iti evam svabhāva paryavasthānāt svabhāvam gṛhītvā pratyavatiṣṭhamānaḥ duḥkha nirodham api pratibādhase 
[221,v_221,vii]	idānīm ārya mārgaḥ api sa svabhāva vādinaḥ yathā na upapadyate tathā pratipādayan āha svābhāvye sati mārgasya bhāvanā na upapadyate atha asau bhāvyate mārgaḥ svābhāvyam te na vidyate yadi hi sa svabhāvāḥ bhāvāḥ bhaveyuḥ tadā mārgaḥ api sa svabhāvaḥ eva iti kṛtvā abhāvitaḥ eva asau asti tasya kim punar bhāvanayā iti evam svābhāvye sati mārgasya bhāvanā na upapadyate atha asya mārgasya bhāvanā abhyupagamyate bhavatā evam tarhi svabhāvatā ārya mārgasya na syāt kāryatvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[221,viii_221,ix]	api ca duḥkhasya nirodha prāpti artham samudayasya ca prahāṇa artham bhāvanā mārgasya iṣyate pūrva uktena tu nyāyena sa svabhāva vādinaḥ bhavataḥ yadā duḥkham samudayaḥ nirodhaḥ ca na vidyate mārgaḥ duḥkha nirodha tvāt katamaḥ prāpayiṣyati na asti eva asau duḥkha nirodhaḥ yat nirodhāt mārgaḥ bhāvitaḥ san prāpayiṣyati tasmāt ārya mārgaḥ api evam na upapadyate iti evam sa svabhāva vādinaḥ caturṇām ārya satyānām abhāvaḥ prāpnoti 
[221,x_222,i]	idānīm duḥkha ādi parijñāna ādikam api yathā parasya na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha svabhāvena aparijñānam yadi tasya punar katham parijñānam nanu kila svabhāvaḥ samavasthitaḥ yadi pūrvam duḥkham aparijñāta svabhāvam tat paścāt parijñāyate iti kalpyate tat ayuktam kim kāraṇam yasmāt nanu kila svabhāvaḥ samavasthitaḥ yaḥ hi svabhāvaḥ sa kila loke samavasthitaḥ na eva anyathātvam āpadyate vahneḥ auṣṇya vat yadā ca svabhāvasya anyathātvam na asti tadā pūrvam aparijñāta svabhāvasya duḥkhasya paścāt api parijñānam na upapadyate iti atas duḥkha parijñānam api na saṃbhavati 
[222,ii_222,iv]	yadā ca etad duḥkha parijñānam api na saṃbhavati tadā prahāṇa sākṣāt karaṇe bhāvanā ca evam eva te parijñāvan na yujyante catvāri api phalāni ca yat etat samudayasya prahāṇam nirodhasya ca sākṣātkaraṇam te ete dve prahāṇa sākṣāt karaṇe yā ca mārgasya bhāvanā eṣā api evam eva te duḥkha parijñāna asaṃbhavān na yujyante samudayasya svabhāvena aprahīṇasya svabhāvasya anapāyi tvāt paścāt api prahāṇam na upapadyate evam bhāvanā sā akṣātkaraṇe api yojyam na ca kevalam parijñāna ādikam eva na saṃbhavati sa svabhāva vāde api ca parijñāvan na yujyante catvāri api phalāni ca yathā svabhāvena aparijñātasya duḥkhasya parijñānam na yuktam evam svabhāvena avidyamānasya pūrvam srotaāpatti phalasya paścāt astitvam na saṃbhavati yathā srotaāpatti phalasya evam sakṛdāgāmi anāgāmi arhat phalānām abhāvaḥ veditavyaḥ 
[222,v_222,vi]	na ca kevalam etāni phalāni parijñāvan na yujyante kim tarhi adhigamaḥ api eṣām na yujyate iti pratipādayan āha svabhāvena anadhigatam yat phalam tat punar katham śakyam samadhigantum syāt svabhāvam parigṛhṇataḥ svabhāvasya avijahana prakṛtika tvāt bhāva svabhāva vādam abhyupagacchataḥ pūrvam anadhigata svabhāvānām paścāt api adhigamaḥ na upapadyate 
[222,vii]	tatas ca phala abhāve phala sthāḥ naḥ na santi pratipannakāḥ saṃghaḥ na asti na ced santi te aṣṭau puruṣa pudgalāḥ abhāvāt ca ārya satyānām saddharmaḥ api na vidyate dharme ca asati saṃghe ca katham buddhaḥ bhaviṣyati anayoḥ ca ślokayoḥ pūrvavat eva arthaḥ veditavyaḥ 
[222,viii_223,i]	api ca sa svabhāva abhyupagame sati apratītya api bodhim ca tava buddhaḥ prasajyate apratītya api buddham ca tava bodhiḥ prasajyate yadi hi svabhāvataḥ buddhaḥ nāma kaścid bhāvaḥ syāt sa bodhim sarvajña jñānam apratītya api anapekṣya api syāt akṛtrimaḥ svabhāvaḥ hi nirapekṣaḥ paratra ca iti vacanāt tathā vinā api buddhena bodhiḥ syāt anapekṣya api buddham nirāśrayā bodhiḥ syāt 
[223,ii_223,iii]	kim ca anyat yaḥ ca abuddhaḥ svabhāvena sa bodhāya ghaṭan api na bodhisattva caryāyām bodhim te adhigamiṣyati iha hi buddha tvāt pūrvam abuddha svabhāvasya sataḥ pudgalasya satyām api bodhisattva caryāyām bodhi artham ghaṭamānasya api na eva bodhiḥ syāt abuddha svabhāvasya vyāvartayitum aśakyatvāt 
[223,iv_223,v]	kim ca anyat na ca dharmam adharmam vā kaścid jātu kariṣyati kim aśūnyasya kartavyam svabhāvaḥ kriyate na hi sati hi svabhāva vāda abhyupagame dharma adharmayoḥ karaṇam na upapadyate kim hi aśūnyasya kartavyam na hi svabhāvasya aśūnyasya kāraṇam upapadyate vidyamāna tvāt 
[223,vi_223,vii]	kim ca anyat vinā dharmam adharmam ca phalam hi tava vidyate dharma adharma nimittam ca phalam tava na vidyate yat etad dharma adharma nimittakam iṣṭa aniṣṭa phalam yadi tat svabhāvataḥ asti tat vinā api dharma adharmābhyām syāt yadā ca vinā dharma adharmam phalam tava asti tadā dharma adharma jam phalam tava na saṃbhavati dharma adharma upārjana vaiyarthyam syāt dharma adharma nimittam ca phalam tava na vidyate iti 
[223,viii_223,ix]	atha dharma adharma nimittakam phalam bhavati iti parikalpyate na tarhi tad phalam aśūnyam iti pratipādayan āha dharma adharma nimittam vā yadi te vidyate phalam dharma adharma samutpannam aśūnyam te katham phalam śūnyam eva etat pratītyasamutpanna tvāt pratibimba vat iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[223,x_224,i]	api ca sarve eva hi ete gaccha kuru paca paṭha tiṣṭha iti evamādayaḥ laukikāḥ vyavahārāḥ pratītya samutpannāḥ tān yadi sa svabhāvān icchati bhavān tadā bhavatā pratītyasamutpādaḥ bādhitaḥ bhavati tad bādhanāt ca sarve eva laukikāḥ vyavahārāḥ bādhitāḥ bhavanti iti pratipādayan āha sarva saṃvyavahārān ca laukikān pratibādhase yat pratītyasamutpāda śūnyatām pratibādhase yat śabdaḥ kriyā viśeṣaṇam yat bādhase iti anena saṃbadhyate 
[224,ii_224,iii]	kim ca anyat na kartavyam bhavet kiṃcid anārabdhā bhavet kriyā kārakaḥ syāt akurvāṇaḥ śūnyatām pratibādhataḥ yadi hi sva rūpa śūnyāḥ padārthāḥ na bhaveyuḥ sa svabhāvāḥ eva bhaveyuḥ tadā svabhāvasya vidyamāna tvāt na kenacid kasyacid kiṃcid kartavyam syāt na hi nabhasaḥ anāvaraṇa tvam kenacid kriyate akriyamāṇā ca kriyā syāt kriyām ca akurvāṇasya kāraka tvam syāt na ca etat evam iti tasmāt na aśūnyāḥ padārthāḥ 
[224,iv_224,vii]	kim ca anyat ajātam aniruddham ca kūṭastham ca bhaviṣyati vicitrābhiḥ avasthābhiḥ svabhāve rahitam jagat vicitrābhiḥ avasthāmiḥ svabhāva racitam svabhāvena eva racitam apratītya samutpannam jagat svabhāva śūnya vādinām svabhāvena eva yadi bhāvāḥ sa svabhāvāḥ syuḥ tadā svabhāvasya akṛtrima tvāt avyāvartana tvāt ca sarvam idam jagat ajātam aniruddham ca syāt ajāta aniruddha tvāt jagat kūṭastham syāt hetu pratyaya anapekṣam vicitrābhiḥ avasthābhiḥ rahitam apratītya samutpannam jagat aśūn yavādinām syāt yathā uktam pitāputra samāgame syāt yadi kiṃcid aśūnyam na vadet jinu tasya vyākaraṇam tathā hi sthitam tat svake svake bhāve kūṭastham avikāram na tasya vṛddhiḥ na parihāṇiḥ iti tathā ārya hasti kakṣya sūtre yadi koci dharmāṇa bhavet svabhāvaḥ tatra eva gaccheya jinaḥ sa śrāvakaḥ kūṭastha dharmāṇa siyā na nirvṛtī na niṣprapañcaḥ bhavi jātu paṇḍitaḥ iti 
[224,viii_225,i]	na ca kevalam sa svabhāva vāda abhyupagame laukikāḥ eva vyavahārāḥ na upapadyante api ca loka uttarāḥ eva api na upapadyante iti pratipādayan āha asaṃprāptasya ca prāptiḥ duḥkha paryanta karma ca sarva kleśa prahāṇam ca yadi aśūnyam na vidyate yadi hi aśūnyam sa svabhāvam sarvam etat syāt tadā yat asaṃprāptam tat asaṃprāptam eva iti asaṃprāptasya ca phalasya prāptiḥ na syāt tadā duḥkha paryanta kāraṇam ca pūrvam na abhūt iti sāṃpratam api na syāt sarveṣām ca kleśānām pūrvam prahāṇam na abhūt iti paścāt api prahāṇam na syāt 
[225,ii_225,iii]	tat evam yasmāt sa svabhāva vāda abhyupagame sati sarvam etat na yujyate atas yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam paśyati idam sa paśyati duḥkham samudayam ca eva nirodham mārgam eva ca yaḥ hi sarva dharma pratītyasamutpāda lakṣaṇām svabhāva śūnyatām samyak paśyati sa catvāri ārya satyāni paśyati yathābhūtāni tattvataḥ 
[225,iv_225,vi]	yathā uktam ārya mañjuśrī paripṛcchāyām yena mañju śrīḥ anutpādaḥ sarva dharmāṇām dṛṣṭaḥ tena duḥkham parijñātam yena na astitā sarva dharmāṇām dṛṣṭā tasya samudayaḥ prahīṇaḥ yena atyanta parinirvṛtāḥ sarva dharmāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tena nirodhaḥ sākṣātkṛtaḥ yena mañju śrīra bhāvaḥ sarva dharmāṇām dṛṣṭaḥ tena mārgaḥ bhāvitaḥ iti vistaraḥ uktam ca ārya dhyāyita muṣṭi sūtre 
[225,vii^1]	atha khalu bhagavān mañju śriyam kumāra bhūtam etat avocat caturṇā mañjuśrīḥ ārya satyānām yathābhūta adarśanāt caturbhiḥ viparyāsaiḥ viparyasta cittāḥ sattvāḥ evabhimama bhūtam saṃsāram na atikrāmanti evam ukte mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ bhagavantam etat avocat deśayatu bhagavān kasya upalambhataḥ sattvāḥ saṃsāram na atikrāmanti bhagavān āha ātma ātmīya upalambhataḥ mañjuśrīḥ sattvāḥ saṃsāram na atikrāmanti tat kasya hetoḥ yaḥ hi mañjuśrīḥ ātmānam param ca samanupaśyati tasya karma abhisaṃskārāḥ bhavanti bālaḥ mañju śrīraśrutavān pṛthagjanaḥ atyanta parinirvṛtān sarva dharmānaprajānānaḥ ātmānam param ca upalabhate upalabhya abhiniviśate abhiniviṣṭaḥ san rajyate duṣyate muhyate 
[225,vii^2]	sa raktaḥ duṣṭaḥ mūḍhaḥ san trividham karma abhisaṃskaroti kāyena vācā manasā saḥ asat samāropeṇa vikalpayati aham raktaḥ aham duṣṭaḥ aham mūḍhaḥ iti tasya tathāgata śāsane pravrajitasya evam bhavati aham śīlavān aham brahmacārī saṃsāram samatikrāmiṣyāmi aham nirvāṇam anuprāpsyāmi aham duḥkhebhyaḥ mokṣyāmi sa kalpayati ime dharmāḥ kuśalāḥ ime dharmāḥ akuśalāḥ iti ime dharmāḥ prahātavyāḥ ime dharmāḥ sākṣāt kartavyāḥ duḥkham parijñātavyam samudayaḥ prahātavyaḥ nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ mārgaḥ bhāvayitavyaḥ sa kalpayati anityāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ ādīptāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ yat nu aham sarva saṃskārebhyaḥ palāyeyam 
[225,vii^3]	tasya eva mavekṣamāṇasya utpadyate nirvitsaha gataḥ manasikāraḥ animitta purogataḥ tasya evam bhavati eṣā sā duḥkha parijñā yā iyam eṣām dharmāṇām parijñā tasya evam bhavati yat nu aham samudayam prajaheyam sa sarva dharmebhyaḥ artīyate jehrīyate vitarati vijugupsate uttrasyati saṃtrasyati saṃtrāsam āpadyate tasya evam bhavati iyam eṣām dharmāṇām sākṣātkriyā idam samudaya prahāṇam yadidam ebhyaḥ dharmebhyaḥ artīyanā tasya evam bhavati nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ samudayam kalpayitvā nirodham saṃjānāti tasya evam bhavati eṣā sā nirodha sākṣāt kriyā tasya evam bhavati yat nūnam aham mārgam bhāvayeyam 
[225,vii^4]	saḥ ekaḥ rahaḥ gataḥ tān dharmān manasi kurvan śamatham pratilabhate tasya tena nirvitsaha gatena manasikāreṇa śamathe utpadyate tasya sarva dharmeṣu cittam na pralīyate prativahati pratyudāvartate tebhyaḥ ca ārtīyate jehrīyate anabhinandana acittam samutpadyate tasya evam bhavati muktaḥ asmi sarva duḥkhebhyaḥ na mama bhūyas uttarim kiṃcitkaraṇīyam arhan asmi iti ātmānam saṃjānāti sa maraṇa kāla samaye utpattim ātmanaḥ deveṣu paśyati tasya kāṅkṣā vicikitsā ca bhavati buddha bodhau sa vicikitsām āpatitaḥ kālagataḥ mahānirayeṣu prapatati tat kasya hetoḥ yathā api idam anutpannān sarva dharmān vikalpayitvā tathāgate vicikitsām vimatim utpādayati 
[226,i^1]	atha khalu mañjuśrīḥ kumāra bhūtaḥ bhagavantam etat avocat katham punar bhagavan catvāri ārya satyāni draṣṭavyāni bhagavān āha yena mañju śrīḥ anutpannāḥ sarva dharmāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tena duḥkham parijñātam yena asamutthitāḥ sarva dharmāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tasya samudayaḥ prahīṇaḥ yena atyanta parinirvṛtāḥ sarva dharmāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tena nirodhaḥ sākṣātkṛtaḥ yena atyanta śūnyāḥ sarva dharmāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tena mārgaḥ bhāvitaḥ yena mañjuśrīḥ evam catvāri ārya satyāni dṛṣṭāni sa na kalpayati ime dharmāḥ kuśalāḥ ime dharmāḥ akuśalāḥ ime dharmāḥ prahātavyāḥ ime dharmāḥ sākṣāt kartavyāḥ duḥkham parijñātavyam samudayaḥ prahātavyaḥ nirodhaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ mārgaḥ bhāvayitavyaḥ iti tat kasya hetoḥ tathā hi sa tam dharmam na samanupaśyati na upalabhate yam parikalpayet 
[226,i^2]	bāla pṛthagjanāḥ tu etān dharmān kalpayantaḥ rajyanti ca dviṣyanti ca muhyanti ca sa na kaṃcid dharmam āvyūhati nirvyūhati tasya evamanāvyūhataḥ anirvyūhataḥ traidhātuke cittam na sajjati ajātam sarva tra edhātukam samanupaśyati māyā upamam svapna upamam pratiśrutka upamam evaṃsvabhāvān sarva dharmān paśyan anunaya pratidhāpa gataḥ bhavati sarva sattveṣu tat kasya hetoḥ tathā hi sa tān dharmān na upalabhate yatra anunīyeta vā pratihanyeta vā saḥ ākāśa samena cittena buddham api na samanupaśyati dharmam api na samanupaśyati saṃdham api na samanupaśyati sarva dharmān śūnyān iti samanupaśyat na kvacid dharme vicikitsām utpādayati avicikitsan nirupādānaḥ bhavati nirupādānaḥ anupādāya parinirvāti iti vistaraḥ 
[227,i_227,ii]	atra āha yadi śūnyam idam sarvam udayaḥ na asti na vyayaḥ prahāṇāt vā nirodhāt vā kasya nirvāṇam iṣyate iha hi bhagavatā uṣita brahmacaryāṇām tathāgata śāsana pratipanna annām dharma anudharma pratipatti yuktānām pudgalānām dvividham nirvāṇam upavarṇitam sa upadhi śeṣam nirupadhi śeṣam ca tatra niravaśeṣasya avidyā rāga ādikasya kleśa gaṇasya prahāṇāt sa upadhi śeṣam nirvāṇam iṣyate tatra upadhīyate asmin ātma snehaḥ iti upadhiḥ upadhi śabdena ātma prajñapti nimittāḥ pañca upādāna skandhāḥ ucyante śiṣyate iti śeṣaḥ upadhiḥ eva śeṣaḥ upadhi śeṣaḥ saha upadhi śeṣeṇa vartate iti sa upadhi śeṣam kim tat nirvāṇam tat ca skandha mātrakam eva kevalam sat kāya dṛṣṭayā ādi kleśa taskara rahitam avaśiṣyate nihata aśeṣa caura gaṇa grāma mātra avasthāna sādharmyeṇa tat sa upadhi śeṣam nirvāṇam yatra tu nirvāṇe skandha pañcakam api na asti tad nirupadhi śeṣam nirvāṇam nirgataḥ upadhi śeṣaḥ asmin iti kṛtvā nihata aśeṣa caura gaṇasya grāma mātrasya api vināśa sādharmyeṇa tat eva ca adhikṛtya ucyate abhedi kāyaḥ nirodhi saññā vedanā pi ti dahaṃsu sabbā vūpa samiṃsu saṃkhārā viññāṇam attham agamā ti 
[227,iii_227,iv]	tathā asaṃlīnena kāyena vedanām adhya vāsayat pradyotasya iva nirvāṇam vimokṣaḥ tasya cetasaḥ iti tat evam nirupadhi śeṣam nirvāṇam skandhānām nirodhāt labhyate etat ca dvividham nirvāṇam katham yujyate yadi kleśānām skandhānām ca nirodhaḥ bhavati yadā tu sarvam idam śūnyam na eva kiṃcid utpadyate na api kiṃcid nirudhyate tadā kutas kleśāḥ kutas vā skandhāḥ yeṣām nirodhe nirvāṇam syāt iti tasmāt vidyate eva bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ iti 
[227,v_228,i]	atra ucyate nanu evam api sa svabhāva abhyupagame yadi aśūnyam idam sarvam udayaḥ na asti na vyayaḥ prahāṇāt vā nirodhāt vā kasya nirvāṇam iṣyate svabhāvena hi vyavasthitānām kleśānām skandhānām ca svabhāvasya anapāyi tvāt kutas nivṛttiḥ yatas tad nivṛttyā nirvāṇam syāt iti tasmāt svabhāva vādinām na eva nirvāṇam upapadyate na ca śūnyatā vādinaḥ skandha nivṛtti lakṣaṇam kleśa nivṛtti lakṣaṇam vā nirvāṇam icchanti yatas teṣām ayam doṣaḥ syāt iti atas anupālambhaḥ eva ayam śūnya vādinām 
[228,ii_228,iii]	yadi khalu śūnyatā vādinaḥ kleśānām skandhānām vā nivṛtti lakṣaṇam nirvāṇam na icchanti kiṃlakṣaṇam tarhi icchanti ucyate aprahīṇam asaṃprāptam anucchinnam aśāśvatam aniruddham anutpannam etat nirvāṇam ucyate yat hi na eva prahīyate rāga ādi vat na api prāpyate śrāmaṇya phala vat na api ucchidyate skandha ādi vat yat ca api na nityam aśūn yavat tat svabhāvataḥ aniruddham anutpannam ca sarva prapañca upaśama lakṣaṇam nirvāṇam uktam tat kutas tasmin itthaṃvidhe niṣprapañce kleśa kalpanā yeṣām kleśānām prahāṇān nirvāṇam bhavet kutas vā skandha kalpanā tatra yeṣām skandhānām nirodhāt tat bhavet yāvat hi etāḥ kalpanāḥ pravartante tāvat na asti nirvāṇa adhigamaḥ sarva prapañca parikṣayāt eva tad adhigamāt 
[228,iv_228,v]	atha syāt yadi api nirvāṇe na santi kleśāḥ na ca api skandhāḥ tathā api nirvāṇāt arvāk vidyante tatas teṣām parikṣayāt nirvāṇam bhaviṣyati iti ucyate tyajyatām ayam grāhaḥ yasmāt nirvāṇāt arvāk svabhāvataḥ vidyamānānām na punar abhāvaḥ śakyate kartum tasmāt nirvāṇa abhilāṣiṇā tyājyā eṣā kalpanā vakṣyati hi nivāṇasya ca yā koṭiḥ koṭiḥ saṃsaraṇasya ca na tayoḥ antaram kiṃcid su sūkṣmam api vidyate iti tat evam nirvāṇe na kasyacid prahāṇam na api kasyacid nirodhaḥ iti vijñeyam tatas ca niravaśeṣa kalpanā kṣaya rūpam eva nirvāṇam uktam ca bhagavatā nirvṛtti dharmāṇa ca asti dharmāḥ ye na iha astī na te jātu asti asti iti na asti iti ca kalpanāvatām evam carantāna na duḥkha śāmyati iti 
[228,vi^1]	asyāḥ gāthāyāḥ ayam arthaḥ nivṛtau nirupadhi śeṣe nirvāṇa dhātau dharmāṇām kleśa karma janma lakṣaṇānām skandhānām vā sarvathā astaṃgamāt astitvam na asti evam ca sarva vādinām abhimatam ye tarhi dharmāḥ iha nirvṛtau na santi pradīpa udayāt andhakāra upalabdha rajju sarpa bhaya ādi vat na te jātu asti na te dharmāḥ kleśa karma janma ādi lakṣaṇāḥ kasmiṃścid kāle saṃsāra avasthāyām api tattvataḥ vidyante na hi rajjuḥ andhakāra avasthāyām svarūpataḥ sarpaḥ asti sadbhūta sarpa vat andhakāre api āloke api kāya cakṣuḥ bhyām agrahaṇāt katham tarhi saṃsāraḥ iti ced ucyate ātma ātmīya asat graha grastānām bāla pṛthagjanānām asat svarūpāḥ api bhāvāḥ satyataḥ pratibhāsante taimirikāṇām iva asat keśa maśaka ādayaḥ iva iti āha asti iti na asti iti ca kalpanāvatām evam carantāna na duḥkha śāmyati iti 
[228,vi^2]	asti iti bhāva sadbhāva kalpanāvatām jaiminīya kāṇādakāpila ādīnām vaibhāṣika paryantānām na asti iti ca kalpanāvatām nāstikānām apāya gati niṣṭhānām tad anyeṣām ca atīta anāgata saṃsthānām vijñapti viprayukta saṃskārāṇām nāstivādinām tad anyat asti vādinām parikalpita svabhāvasya na astivādinām paratantra pariniṣpanna svabhāvayoḥ asti vādinām evam asti nāstivādinām evam caratām na duḥkham saṃsāraḥ śāmyati iti tathā yatha śaṅkitena viṣa saṃjña abhyupeti no ca api koṣṭha gantu āviṣṭa papadyate evam eva bālu apagataḥ jāyi mriyate sadā abhūtaḥ iti tat evam na kasyacid nirvāṇe prahāṇam na api kasyacid nirodhaḥ iti vijñeyam tatas ca sarva kalpanā kṣaya rūpam eva nirvāṇam yathā uktam ārya ratna āvalyām na ca abhāvaḥ api nirvāṇam kutas eva asya bhāvanā bhāva abhāva parāmarśa kṣayaḥ nirvāṇam ucyate iti 
[229,i_229,ii]	ye tu sarva kalpanā upaśama rūpam nirvāṇam apratipadyamānāḥ bhāva abhāva tad ubhaya anubhaya rūpam nirvāṇam parikalpayanti tān prati ucyate bhāvaḥ tāvat na nirvāṇam jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇam prasajyeta asti bhāvaḥ hi na jarā maraṇam vinā tatra eke bhāvataḥ nirvāṇam abhiniviṣṭāḥ evam ācakṣate iha kleśa karma janma saṃtāna pravṛtti niyata rodha bhūtaḥ jala pravāha rodha bhūta setu sthānīyaḥ nirodha ātmakaḥ padārthaḥ tad nirvāṇam na ca avidyamāna svabhāvaḥ dharmaḥ evam kārya kārī dṛśyate nanu ca yaḥ asyāḥ nandī rāga sahagatāyāḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ kṣayaḥ virāgaḥ nirodhaḥ nirvāṇam iti uktam na ca kṣaya mātram bhāvaḥ bhavitum arhati tathā pradyotasya iva nirvāṇam vimokṣaḥ tasya cetasaḥ iti uktam na ca pradyotasya nivṛttiḥ bhāvaḥ iti upapadyate ucyate na etat evam vijñeyam tṛṣṇāyāḥ kṣayaḥ tṛṣṇā kṣayaḥ iti kim tarhi tṛṣṇāyāḥ kṣayaḥ asmin iti nirvāṇa ākhye dharme sati bhavati sa tṛṣṇā kṣayaḥ iti vaktavyam pradīpaḥ ca dṛṣṭānta mātram tatra api yasmin sati cetasaḥ vimokṣaḥ bhavati iti veditavyam iti 
[230,i_230,ii]	evam bhāve nirvāṇa vyavasthāpite ācāryaḥ nirūpayati bhāvaḥ tāvat na nirvāṇam kim kāraṇam yasmāt jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇam prasajyeta bhāvasya jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇa avyabhicāri tvāt tatas ca nirvāṇam eva tat na syāt jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇa tvāt vijñāna vat iti abhiprāyaḥ tām eva ca jarā maraṇa lakṣaṇa vyabhicāritām spaṣṭayan āha asti bhāvaḥ hi na jarā maraṇam vinā iti yaḥ hi jarā maraṇa rahitaḥ sa bhāvaḥ eva na saṃbhavati kha puṣpa vat jarā maraṇa rahita tvāt 
[230,iii_230,v]	kim ca anyat bhāvaḥ ca yadi nirvāṇam nirvāṇam saṃskṛtam bhavet na asaṃskṛtaḥ hi vidyate bhāvaḥ kvacana kaścana yadi nirvāṇam bhāvaḥ syāt tadā tat nirvāṇam saṃskṛtam bhavet vijñāna ādi vat bhāva tvāt yaḥ tu asaṃskṛtaḥ na asau bhāvaḥ tat yathā khara viṣāṇa vat iti vyatirekam upadarśayan āha na asaṃskṛtaḥ hi vidyate bhāvaḥ kvacana kaścana kvacana iti adhikaraṇe deśe kāle siddhānte vā kaścana iti ādheye ādhyātmikaḥ bāhya ātmikaḥ vā iti arthaḥ 
[230,vi_230,vii]	kim ca anyat bhāvaḥ ca yadi nirvāṇam anupādāya tat katham nirvāṇam na anupādāya kaścid bhāvaḥ hi vidyate yadi bhavat matena nirvāṇam bhāvaḥ syāt tad upādāya bhavet sva kāraṇa sāmagrīm āśritya bhavet iti arthaḥ na ca evam upādāya nirvāṇam iṣyate kim tarhi anupādāya tat yadi bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam anupādāya tat katham nirvāṇam syāt na eva anupādāya syāt bhāva tvāt vijñāna ādi vat vyatireka kāraṇam āha na anupādāya kaścid bhāvaḥ hi vidyate iti 
[230,viii_230,ix]	atra āha yadi bhāvaḥ hi na nirvāṇam yathā udita doṣa prasaṅgāt kim tarhi abhāvaḥ eva nirvāṇam kleśa janma nivṛtti mātra tvāt iti ucyate etat api ayuktam yasmāt yadi bhāvaḥ na nirvāṇam abhāvaḥ kim bhaviṣyati nirvāṇam yatra bhāvaḥ na na abhāvaḥ tatra vidyate yadi bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam na iṣyate yadi nirvāṇam bhāvaḥ iti na iṣyate tadā kim abhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati nirvāṇam abhāvaḥ api na bhaviṣyati iti arthaḥ kleśa janmanoḥ abhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti ced evam tarhi kleśa janmanoḥ anitya tā nirvāṇam iti syāt anitya tā eva hi kleśa janmanoḥ abhāvaḥ na anyat iti atas anitya tā eva nirvāṇam syāt na ca etat iṣṭam ayatnena eva mokṣa prasaṅgāt iti uktam eva etat 
[231,i_231,ii]	kim ca anyat yadi abhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam anupādāya tat katham nirvāṇam na hi abhāvaḥ asti yaḥ anupādāya vidyate tatra abhāvaḥ anitya tā vā bhāvam upādāya prajñapyate khara viṣāṇa ādīnām anitya tā anupalambhāt lakṣaṇam āśritya lakṣyam prajñapyate lakṣyam āśritya ca lakṣaṇam atas paraspara apekṣikyām lakṣya lakṣaṇa pravṛttau kutas lakṣyam bhāvam apekṣya anitya tā bhaviṣyati tasmāt abhāvaḥ api upādāya prajñapyate tatas yadi abhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam tat katham anupādāya nirvāṇam bhavet upādāya eva tat bhavet abhāva tvāt vināśa vat etat eva spaṣṭayan āha na hi abhāvaḥ asti yaḥ anupādāya vidyate iti 
[231,iii_231,iv]	yadi tarhi abhāvaḥ anupādāya na asti kim idānīm upādāya bandhyā putra ādayaḥ abhāvāḥ bhaviṣyanti kena etat uktam vandhyā putra ādayaḥ abhāvāḥ iti uktam hi pūrvam bhāvasya ced aprasiddhiḥ abhāvaḥ na eva sidhyati bhāvasya hi anyathābhāvam abhāvam bruvate janāḥ iti tasmāt na bandhyā putra ādīnām abhāva tvam yat ca api ucyate ākāśam śaśa śṛṅgam ca vandhyāyāḥ putraḥ eva ca asantaḥ ca abhilapyante tathā bhāveṣu kalpanā iti 
[231,v]	tatra api bhāva kalpanā pratiṣedha mātram na abhāva kalpanā bhāva tva asiddheḥ eva iti vijñeyam vandhyā putraḥ iti śabda mātram eva etat na asya arthaḥ upalabhyate yasya arthasya bhāva tvam abhāva tvam vā syāt iti kutas anupalabhyamāna svabhāvasya bhāva abhāva kalpanā yokṣyate tasmāt na bandhyā putraḥ abhāvaḥ iti vijñeyam tatas ca sthitam eva na hi abhāvaḥ asti yaḥ anupādāya vidyate iti 
[231,vi_231,vii]	atra āha yadi bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam na bhavati abhāvaḥ api kim tarhi nirvāṇam iti ucyate iha hi bhagavadbhiḥ tathāgataiḥ yaḥ ājavaṃjavībhāvaḥ upādāya pratītya vā saḥ apratītya anupādāya nirvāṇam upadiśyate tatra ājavaṃjavībhāvaḥ āgamana gamana bhāva janma maraṇa paraṃparā iti arthaḥ sa ca ayam āja vaṃjavībhāvaḥ kadācid hetu pratyaya sāmagrīm āśritya asti iti prajñapyate dīrgha hrasva vat kadācid utpadyate iti prajñapyate pradīpa prabhāvat bīja aṅkura vat sarvathā yadi ayam upādāya prajñapyate yadi vā pratītya jāyate iti vyavasthāpyate sarvathā asya janma maraṇa paraṃpara aprabandhasya apratītya vā anupādāya vā apravṛttiḥ tat nirvāṇam iti vyavasthāpyate na ca apravṛtti mātram bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā iti parikalpitu pāryate iti evam na bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ nirvāṇam
