[232,i]	athavā yeṣām saṃskārāḥ saṃsaranti iti pakṣaḥ teṣām pratītya pratītya yaḥ utpādaḥ ca vināśaḥ ca saḥ apratītya apravartamānaḥ nirvāṇam iti kathyate yeṣām tu pudgalaḥ saṃsarati teṣām tasya nitya anitya tvena avācyasya tat tad upādānam āśritya yaḥ ājavaṃjavībhāvaḥ saḥ upādāya pravartate saḥ eva upādāya upādāya pravartayamānaḥ san idānīm anupādāya apravartayamānaḥ nirvāṇam iti vyapadiśyate na ca saṃskārāṇām pudgalasya vā apravṛtti mātrakam bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā iti śakyam parikalpayitum iti atas api na bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti yujyate 
[232,ii_232,iii]	kim ca anyat prahāṇam ca abravīt śāstā bhavasya vibhavasya ca tasmāt na bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti yujyate tatra sūtraḥ uktam ye kecid bhikṣavaḥ bhavena bhavasya niḥsaraṇam paryeṣante vibhavena vā aparijñātam tat teṣām iti ubhayam hi etat parityājyam bhave tṛṣṇā vibhave tṛṣṇā ca na ca etat nirvāṇam prahātavyam uktam bhagavatā kim tarhi aprahātavyam tat yadi nirvāṇam bhāva rūpam syāt abhāva rūpam vā tat api prahātavyam bhavet na ca prahātavyam 
[232,iv_232,vi]	tasmāt na bhāvaḥ na abhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti yujyate yeṣām api kleśa janmanoḥ tatra abhāvāt abhāva rūpam nirvāṇam svayam ca bhāva rūpa tvāt bhāva rūpam iti ubhaya rūpam teṣām ubhaya rūpam iti nirvāṇam na upapadyate iti pratipādayan āha bhavet abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam ubhayam yadi bhavet abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ ca mokṣaḥ tat ca na yujyate yadi bhāva abhāva ubhaya rūpam nirvāṇam syāt tadā bhāvaḥ ca abhāvaḥ ca mokṣaḥ iti syāt tatas ca yaḥ saṃskārāṇām ātma lābhaḥ tasya ca vigamaḥ saḥ eva mokṣaḥ syāt na ca saṃskārāḥ eva mokṣaḥ iti yujyate atas eva āha tat ca na yujyate iti 
[232,vii_232,viii]	kim ca anyat bhavet abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam ubhayam yadi na anupādāya nirvāṇam upādāya ubhayam hi tat yadi bhāva abhāva rūpam nirvāṇam syāt tadā hetu pratyaya sāmagrīm upādāya āśritya bhavet na anupādāya kim kāraṇam yasmāt upādāya ubhayam hi tat bhāvam upādāya abhāvaḥ abhāvam ca upādāya bhāvaḥ iti kṛtvā ubhayam etat bhāvam ca abhāvam ca upādāya eva bhavati na anupādāya evam nirvāṇam bhavet bhāva abhāva rūpam na ca etat evam iti na yuktam etat 
[233,i_233,ii]	kim ca anyat bhavet abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇam ubhayam katham asaṃskṛtam ca nirvāṇam bhāva abhāvau ca saṃskṛtau bhāvaḥ hi sva hetu pratyaya sāmagrī saṃbhūta tvāt saṃskṛtaḥ abhāvaḥ api bhāvam pratītya saṃbhūta tvāt jāti pratyaya jarā maraṇa vacanāt ca saṃskṛtaḥ tat yadi bhāva abhāva svabhāvam nirvāṇam syāt tadā na asaṃskṛtam kim tu saṃskṛtam eva yasmāt na ca saṃskṛtam iṣyate tasmāt na bhāva abhāva svarūpam nirvāṇam yujyate 
[233,iii_233,iv]	atha api syāt na eva hi nirvāṇam bhāva abhāva svarūpam kim tarhi nirvāṇe bhāva abhāvau iti evam api na yuktam kutas yasmāt bhavet abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇe ubhayam katham tayoḥ ekatra na astitvam āloka tamasoḥ yathā bhāva abhāvayoḥ api paraspara viruddhayoḥ ekatra nirvāṇe na asti saṃbhavaḥ iti atas bhavet abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ ca nirvāṇe ubhayam katham na eva bhavet iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[233,v_233,vi]	idānīm yathā na eva bhāvaḥ na eva abhāvaḥ nirvāṇam yujyate tathā pratipādayan āha na eva abhāvaḥ na eva bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti yā añjanā abhāve ca eva bhāve ca sā siddhe sati sidhyati yadi hi bhāvaḥ nāma kaścid syāt tadā tad pratiṣedhena na eva bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti eṣā kalpanā yadi kaścid abhāvaḥ syāt tadā tad pratiṣedhena na eva abhāvaḥ nirvāṇam syāt yadā ca bhāva abhāvau eva na staḥ tadā tad pratiṣedhaḥ api na asti iti tasmāt na eva bhāvaḥ na eva abhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti yā kalpanā sā api na upapadyate eva iti na yuktam etat 
[233,vii_233,viii^1]	kim ca anyat na eva abhāvaḥ na eva bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam yadi vidyate na eva abhāvaḥ na eva bhāvaḥ iti kena tat ajyate yadi etat nirvāṇam na eva abhāva rūpam na eva bhāva rūpam asti iti kalpyate kena tadānīm tat itthaṃvidham na ubhaya rūpam nirvāṇam asti iti ajyate gṛhyate prakāśate vā kim tatra nirvāṇe kaścid evaṃvidhaḥ pratipattā asti atha na asti yadi asti evam sati nirvāṇe api tava ātmā syāt na ca iṣṭam nirupādānasya ātmanaḥ astitva abhāvāt atha na asti kena etat itthaṃvidham nirvāṇam asti iti paricchidyate saṃsāra avasthitaḥ paricchinatti iti ced yadi saṃsāra avasthitaḥ paricchinatti sa kim vijñānena paricchinatti utta jñānena 
[233,viii^2]	yadi vijñānena iti parikalpyate tat na yujyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt nimitta ālambanam vijñānam na ca nirvāṇe kiṃcid nimittam asti tasmāt na tad tāvat vijñānena ālambyate jñānena api na jñāyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt jñānena hi śūnyatā ālambanena bhavitavyam tat ca anutpāda rūpam eva iti katham tena avidyamāna svarūpeṇa na eva abhāvaḥ na eva bhāvaḥ nirvāṇam iti gṛhyate sarva prapañca atīta rūpa tvāt jñānasya iti tasmāt na kenacid nirvāṇam na eva abhāvaḥ na eva bhāvaḥ iti ajyate anajyamānam aprakāśyamānam agṛhyamāṇam tat evam asti iti na yujyate 
[234,i_234,iii]	sarvathā yathā ca nirvāṇe etāḥ catasraḥ kalpanāḥ na saṃbhavanti evam nirvāṇa adhigantari api tathāgate etāḥ kalpanāḥ na eva saṃbhavanti iti pratipādayan āha param nirodhāt bhagavān bhavati iti eva na uhyate na bhavati ubhayam ca iti na ubhayam ca iti na uhyate uktam hi pūrvam ghana grāha gṛhītaḥ tu yena asti iti tathāgataḥ na asti iti vā kalpayan sa nirvṛtasya vikalpayet evam tāvat param nirodhāt bhavati tathāgataḥ na bhavati ca iti na uhyate etat dvayasya abhāvāt ubhayam iti api na uhyate ubhayasya abhāvāt eva na ubhayam iti na uhyate na gṛhyate 
[234,iv_234,v]	na ca kevalam param nirodhāt caturbhiḥ prakāraiḥ bhagavān na uhyate api ca tiṣṭhamānaḥ api bhagavān bhavati iti eva na uhyate na bhavati ubhayaṃca iti na ubhayam ca iti na uhyate yathā na ājyam na cohyam tathā tathāgata parīkṣāyām pratipāditam 
[234,vi_234,vii]	atas eva na saṃsārasya nirvāṇāt kiṃcid asti viśeṣaṇam na nirvāṇasya saṃsārāt kiṃcid asti viśeṣaṇam yasmāt tiṣṭhan api bhagavān bhavati iti evamādinā na uhyate parinirvṛtaḥ api na uhyate bhavati iti evamādinā atas eva saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ parasparataḥ na asti kaścid viśeṣaḥ vicāryamāṇayoḥ tulya rūpa tvāt yat ca api idam uktam bhagavatā anavara agraḥ hi bhikṣavaḥ jāti jarā maraṇa saṃsāraḥ iti tat api atas eva upapannam saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ viśeṣasya abhāvāt 
[235,i_235,ii]	tathā hi nirvāṇasya ca yā koṭiḥ koṭiḥ saṃsaraṇasya ca na tayoḥ antaram kiṃcid su sūkṣmam api vidyate na ca kevalam saṃsārasya nirvāṇena aviśiṣṭa tvāt pūrva apara koṭi kalpanā na saṃbhavati yāḥ api etāḥ param nirodhāt anta ādyāḥ śāśvata ādyāḥ ca dṛṣṭayaḥ nirvāṇam apara antam ca pūrva antam ca samāśritāḥ tāḥ api atas eva na upapadyante saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ ubhayoḥ api prakṛti śānta tvena eka rasa tvāt 
[235,iii]	tatra param nirodhāt itya nena upalakṣaṇena catasraḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ parigṛhyante tat yathā bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt na bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāta bhavati ca na bhavati ca tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt na eva bhavati na na bhavati tathāgataḥ param maraṇāt iti etāḥ catasraḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ nirvāṇa parāmarśena pravṛttāḥ 
[235,iv^1]	anta ādyāḥ api dṛṣṭayaḥ tat yathā antavān lokaḥ anantavān ca antavān ca ānantavān ca na eva antavān na anantavān lokaḥ iti etāḥ catasraḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ apara antam samāśritya pravṛttāḥ tatra ātmanaḥ lokasya vā anāgatam utpādam apaśyan antavān lokaḥ iti evam kalpayan apara antam ālambya pravartate evam anāgatam utpādam paśyan anantavān lokaḥ iti pravartate paśyan ca apaśyan ca ubhayathā prātipadyate dvaya pratiṣedhena na eva antavān na anantavān iti pratipadyate śāśvataḥ lokaḥ aśāśvataḥ lokaḥ śāśvataḥ ca aśāśvataḥ ca na eva śāśvataḥ na eva aśāśvātaḥ lokaḥ iti etāḥ catasraḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ pūrva antam samāśritya pravartante 
[235,iv^2_235,v]	tatra ātmanaḥ lokasya vai atītam utpādam paśyan śāśvataḥ lokaḥ iti pratipadyate apaśyan aśāśvate iti pratipadyate paśyan ca apaśyan ca śāśvataḥ ca aśāśvataḥ ca iti pratipadyate na eva paśyat aiva apaśyat na eva śāśvataḥ na aśāśvataḥ ca iti pratipadyate pūrva antam āśritya tāḥ ca etāḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ katham yujyante yadi kasyacid padārthasya kaścid svabhāvaḥ bhavet tasya bhāva abhāva kalpanāt syuḥ etāḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ yadā tu saṃsāra nirvāṇayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ pratipāditaḥ tadā śūnyeṣu sarva dharmeṣu kim anantam kim anta vat kim anantam antavat ca na anantam na antavat ca kim kim tat eva kim anyat kim śāśvatam kim aśāśvatam aśāśvatam śāśvatam ca kim vā na ubhayam api atas caturdaśa api etāni avyākṛta vastūni asati bhāva svarūpe na eva yujyante yaḥ tu bhāva svarūpam adhyāropya tad vigama avigamataḥ etāḥ dṛṣṭīḥ utpādya abhiniviśate tasya ayam abhiniveśaḥ nirvāṇa pura gāminam panthānam niruṇaddhi sāṃsārikeṣu ca duḥkheṣu niyojayati iti vijñeyam 
[235,vi]	atra āha yadi evam bhavatā nirvāṇam api pratiṣiddham nanu ca yaḥ eṣa bhava gatāḥ ananta carita sattva rāśi anuvartakena vidita aviparīta sakala jagat āśaya svabhāvena mahā karūṇa aparatantreṇa priya eka putra kaprema anugata aśeṣa tribhuvana janena carita pratipakṣa anurūpaḥ dharmaḥ deśitaḥ lokasya nirvāṇa adhigama artham saḥ evam sati vyarthaḥ eva jāyate ucyate yadi kaścid dharmaḥ nāma svabhāva rūpataḥ syāt kecid ca sattvāḥ tasya dharmasya śrotāraḥ syuḥ kaścid vā deśitāḥ buddhaḥ bhagavān nāma bhāva svabhāvaḥ syāt syāt etat evam yadā tu sarva upalambha upaśamaḥ prapañca upaśamaḥ śivaḥ na kvacid kasyacid kaścid dharmaḥ buddhena deśitaḥ 
[236,i^1]	tadā kutas asmākam yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iha hi sarveṣām prapañcānām nimittānām yaḥ upaśamaḥ apravṛttiḥ tad nirvāṇam saḥ eva ca upaśamaḥ prakṛtyā eva upaśānta tvāt śivaḥ vācām apravṛtteḥ vā prapañca upaśamaḥ cittasya apravṛtteḥ śivaḥ kleśānām apravṛttyā vā janmanaḥ apravṛttyā śivaḥ kleśa prahāṇena vā prapañca upaśamaḥ niravaśeṣa vāsanā prahāṇe śivaḥ jñeya anupalabdhyā vā prapañca upaśamaḥ jñāna anupalabdhyā śivaḥ yadā ca evam buddhāḥ bhagavantaḥ sarva prapañca upaśa anta rūpe nirvāṇe śive asthāna yogena nabhasi iva haṃsa rājāḥ sthitāḥ sva puṇya jñāna saṃbhāra pakṣa pāta vāte vāta gagane vā gaganasya akiṃcana tvāt tadā sarva nimittān upalambhāt na kvacid deveṣu vā manuṣyeṣu vā na kasyacid devasya vā manuṣyasya vā na kaścid dharmaḥ sāṃkleśikaḥ vā vaiyavadānikaḥ vā deśitaḥ iti vijñeyam 
[236,i^2]	yathā uktam ārya tathāgata guhya sūtre yām ca rātrim śānta mate tathāgataḥ anuttarām samyaksaṃbodhim abhisaṃbuddhaḥ yām ca rātrim anupādāya parinirvāsyati atra antare tathāgatena ekam api akṣaram na udāhṛtam na vyāhṛtam na api pravyāharati na api pravyāhariṣyati atha ca yathā adhimuktāḥ sarva sattvāḥ nānā dhātvāśayāḥ tām tām vividhām tathāgata vācam niścarantīm saṃjānanti teṣām evam pṛthak pṛthak bhavati ayam bhagavān asmabhyam imam dharmam deśayati vayam ca tathāgatasya dharma deśanām śṛṇumaḥ tatra tathāgataḥ na kalpayati na vikalpayati sarva kalpa vikalpa jāla vāsanā prapañca vigataḥ hi śānta mate tathāgataḥ iti vistaraḥ 
[236,ii_236,iii]	tathā avāca anakṣarāḥ sarva śūnyāḥ śānta ādi nirmalāḥ yaḥ evam jānati dharmān kumāraḥ buddha sā ucyate yadi tarhi evam na kvacid kasyacid kaścid dharmaḥ buddhena deśitaḥ tat katham ime ete vicitrāḥ pravacana vyavahārāḥ prajñāyante ucyate avidyā nidrā anugatānām dehinām svapnāyamānānām iva sva vikalpa abhyudayaḥ eṣaḥ ayam bhagavān sakala tribhuvana sura asura nara nāthaḥ imam dharmam asmabhyam deśayati iti yathā uktam bhagavatā tathāgataḥ hi pratibimba bhūtaḥ kuśalasya dharmasya anāsravasya na eva atra tathatā na tathāgataḥ asti bimbam ca saṃdṛśyati sarva loke iti 
[237,i]	etat ca tathāgata vāc guhya parivarte vistareṇa vyākhyātam tatas ca nirvāṇa artham dharma deśanāyāḥ abhāvāt kutas dharma deśanāyāḥ sadbhāvena nirvāṇasya astitvam bhaviṣyati tasmāt nirvāṇam api na asti iti siddham uktam ca bhagavatā anirvāṇam hi nirvāṇam lokanāthena deśitam ākāśena kṛtaḥ granthiḥ ākāśena eva mocitaḥ iti 
[237,ii]	tathā na teṣām bhagavan saṃsāra samatikramaḥ ye nirvāṇam bhāvataḥ paryeṣante tat kasya hetoḥ nirvāṇam iti bhagavan yaḥ praśamaḥ sarva nimittānām uparatiḥ sarva in jita samiñjitānām tat ime bhagavat moha puruṣāḥ ye su ākhyāte dharma vinaye pravrajya tīrthika dṛṣṭau nipatitā nirvāṇam bhāvataḥ paryeṣante tat yathā tilebhyaḥ tailam kṣīrāt sarpiḥ atyanta parinirvṛteṣu bhagavan sarva dharmeṣu ye nirvāṇam mārganti tān aham ābhimānikān tīrthikān iti vadāmi na bhagavan yoga ācāraḥ samyak pratipannaḥ kasyacid dharmasya utpādam vā nirodham vā karoti na api kasyacid dharmasya prāptim icchati nābhi samayam iti vistaraḥ 
[238,i_238,ii]	atra āha yat uktam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ śūnyatām tām pracakṣmahe sā prajñaptiḥ upādāya pratipatsā eva madhyamā iti kaḥ punar asau pratītyasamutpādaḥ yaḥ śūnyatā iti ucyate athavā yat etat uktam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam paśyati idam sa paśyati duḥkham samudayam ca eva nirodham mārgam eva ca iti tat katamaḥ asau pratītyasamutpādaḥ iti atas tad aṅga prabheda vivakṣayā it amucyate punarbhavāya saṃskārānavidyā nivṛtaḥ tridhā abhisaṃskurute yān taiḥ gatim gacchati karmabhiḥ 
[238,iii]	tatra avidyā ajñānam tamaḥ yathābhūta artha pracchādakam stimita tā avidyayā nivṛtaḥ chāditaḥ pudgalaḥ punarbhavāya punarbhava artham punarbhava utpatti artham abhisaṃskaroti utpādayati yān kuśala ādi cetanā viśeṣān te punarbhava abhisaṃskārāt saṃskārāḥ te ca trividhāḥ kuśalāḥ akuśalāḥ ānejyāḥ ca yadi vā kāyikāḥ vācikāḥ mānasāḥ ca iti tān trividhān karma lakṣaṇān saṃskārān avidyā nivṛtaḥ pudgalaḥ karoti taiḥ ca saṃskāraiḥ abhisaṃskṛtaiḥ karmabhiḥ karma saṃjñitaiḥ tad hetukām gatim gacchati 
[238,iv_238,vi]	tatas asya vijñānam saṃniviśate saṃskāra pratyayam gatau kṛta upacita saṃskārasya asya pudgalasya saṃskāra anurūpāyām gatau deva ādikāyām saṃskāra hetukam vijñānam saṃniviśate praviśati upapadyate saṃsāra anartha bīja bhūtam tatas uttara kālam saṃniviṣṭe atha vijñāne nāma rūpam niṣicyate tatra karma kleśa āviddham tasmin tasmin upapatti āyatane nāmayati iti nāma saṃjñā vaśena vā artheṣu nāmayati iti nāma catvāraḥ arūpiṇaḥ skandhā nāma iti vyapadiśyate 
[238,vii_239,ii]	rūpyate iti rūpam bādhyate iti arthaḥ idam ca rūpam pūrvakam ca nāma ubhayam etat abhisaṃkṣipya nāma rūpam iti vyavasthāpyate tatra bimba pratibimba nyāyena svādhyāya dīpa mudrā pratimudrā ādi nyāyena vā māraṇa antikeṣu skandheṣu nirudhyamāneṣu ekasmin eva kṣaṇe tulā daṇḍa nāma unnāma nyāyena eva aupapattyā aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ yathā karma ākṣepataḥ upajāyante evam ca bimba pratibimba mudrā pratimudrā nyāyena pratītyasamutpādaḥ sidhyati tulā daṇḍa nāma unnāma nyāyena tu yat vijñānam saṃniviśate iti uktam tat bāla loka bodha anurodhena samāna kāle eva bhava pratisaṃdhiḥ iti tathā samānena samāna kālam lokasya duḥkham ca sukha udayam ca hartum ca kartum ca sadā astu śaktiḥ tamaḥ prakāśam ca yathā eva bhānoḥ iti na tu punar pratītyasamutpāda svarūpa vicakṣaṇānām evam vaktum yujyate sāhacarya ādi tvam eka kṣaṇe tulā daṇḍa nāmā unnāma dṛṣṭāntena iti 
[239,iii_239,iv]	janma unmukham na sat idam yadi jāyamānaṃnāśa unmukham sat api nāma nirudhyamānam iṣṭam tadā katham idam tulayā samānam kartrā vinā janiḥ iyam na ca yukta rūpā ityādi vacanāt yathā bimba pratibimba mudrā pratimudrā ādi nyāyena kṣaṇika tvam na iṣyate bhavadbhiḥ tathā anyasya api bhāvasya utpāda samanantara dhvaṃsinaḥ kṣaṇika tvam na yuktam yatas jāti jarā sthiti anitya tā ākhyāni catvāri saṃskṛta lakṣaṇāni utpadyamānasya bhāvasya bāhyasya ādhyātmikasya vai ekasmin eva kṣaṇe bhavanti iti abhidharma pāṭhaḥ tatra jāti jarayoḥ paraspara virodhāt sthiti anitya tayoḥ ca ekasmin eva bhāve na yugapad saṃbhavaḥ iṣyate sadbhiḥ kṣaṇike sarvathā abhāvāt kutas kācid purāṇa tā sthairyāt akṣaṇike ca api kutas kācid purāṇa tā yathā antaḥ asti kṣaṇasya evamādi madhyam ca kalpyatām antaka tvāt kṣaṇasya evam na lokasya kṣaṇa sthitiḥ ādi madhya avasānāni cintyāni kṣaṇa vat punar ādi madhya avasāna tvam na svatas paratas api vā 
[239,v^1]	iti madhyamaka siddhānta pāṭhāt kṣaṇika padārtha asiddheḥ asiddhiḥ avaseyā na ca jāti maraṇayoḥ paraspara bhinna lakṣaṇayoḥ ekasmin kṣaṇe saṃbhavaḥ bhavet saṃśaya niścaya jñānayoḥ āloka andhakārayoḥ jñāna ajñānayoḥ bīja aṅkurayoḥ maraṇa bhava upapatti bhavayoḥ bhinna lakṣaṇayoḥ iti ādi vat paraspara nirapekṣayoḥ eva sva hetu pratyaya siddhayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ yujyate savya itara go viṣāṇayoḥ yuvati stanayoḥ nara karṇayoḥ iti ādi vat na tu punar kadācid api paraspara viruddhayoḥ vināśa utpādayoḥ yathā uktam rāga rakta parīkṣāyām saha eva punar udbhūtiḥ na yuktā rāga raktayoḥ bhavetām rāga raktau hi nirapekṣau parasparam na ekatve sahabhāvaḥ asti na tena eva hi tat saha 
[239,v^2]	pṛthaktve sahabhāvaḥ atha kutas eva bhaviṣyati evam raktena rāgasya siddhiḥ na saha na asaha rāga vat sarva dharmāṇām siddhiḥ na saha na asaha iti pratiṣedhāt kutas samāna kālatā bhāvānām maraṇa bhava upapatti bhavayoḥ iti atas sahabhāvaḥ vineya jana bodha anurodha pravṛttaḥ eva iti lakṣyate tena na ekasmin eva kṣaṇe nāma unnāmau tulāyāḥ saṃbhavataḥ nāma unnāmayoḥ kāla bhedāt balavat puruṣāt chaṭā mātreṇa pañca ṣaṣṭiḥ kṣaṇāḥ atikrāmanti iti pāṭhāt utpala patra śata sahasra vedha vat sūcī agreṇa iti tathā api atra utpala patra śata sahasra vedhaḥ sūcī agreṇa kramaśas vedhaḥ avaseyaḥ kṣaṇānām ati sūkṣma tvāt eka kṣaṇena śloka akṣara pada udāharaṇa vat 
[240,i]	kim ca anirodham anutpādam anucchedam aśāśvatam aneka artha manāna artham anāgamam anirgamam yaḥ pratītyasamutpādam prapañca upaśamam śivam iti pāṭhāt utpāda nirodhayoḥ asaṃbhavaḥ eva pratipāditaḥ śāstre madhyamake āgama sūtreṣu avināśam anutpannam dharmadhātu samam jagat sattva dhātum ca deśa iti eṣā loka anuvartanā trīṣu adhvasu sattvānām prakṛtim na upalambhati sattva dhātum ca deśa iti eṣā loka anuvartanā ityādi 
[240,ii]	tathā phena piṇḍa upamam rūpam vedanā budbuda upamā marīci sadṛśī saṃjñā saṃskārāḥ kadalī nibhāḥ māyā upamam ca vijñānam uktam āditya bandhunā evam dharmān vīkṣamāṇaḥ bhikṣuḥ ārabdha vīryavān divā vā yadi vā rātrau saṃprajānan pratismṛtaḥ pratividhyet padam śāntam saṃskāra upaśamam śivam iti 
[240,iii^1]	etāḥ ca gāthāḥ sarva nikāya śāstra sūtreṣu paṭhayante atas phena piṇḍa ādīnām hetu pratyaya sāmagrīm prāpya pratītya samutpannānām sāra vastu vigatānām kutas kṣaṇikā kṣaṇika cintā iti mahāyāna sūtreṣu ca su pinā upamā bhava gatī sakalā na hi kaści jāyati na caḥ mriyate na ca karma naśyati kadāci kṛtam phalu deti kṛṣṇa śubha saṃsarataḥ na ca śāśvatam na ca uccheda punaḥ na ca karma saṃcayu na ca api sthitiḥ na ca saḥ api kṛtva punar āspṛśatī na ca anyu kṛtva puna vedayate yathā kumārī supina antarasmim sva putra jātam ca mṛtaṃca paśyati jāte ati tuṣṭā mṛti daurmanasyitā tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān 
[240,iii^2]	yathā eva grāma antari lekha darśanāt kriyāḥ pravartanti pṛthak śubha aśubhāḥ na lekha saṃkrānti girāya vidyate tathā upamān jānatha sarva dharmān mudrāt pratimudra dṛśyate mudra saṃkrānti na ca upalabhyate na ca tatra na ca eva sā anyatas evam saṃskāra anuccheda śāśvatāḥ bījasya sataḥ yathā aṅkuraḥ na ca yaḥ bīju sa ca eva aṅkuraḥ na ca anyu tatas na ca eva tat evam anuccheda aśāśvata dharma tā yatha muñja pratītya balbajam rajju vyāyāma balena vartitā ghaṭiyantra sa cakra vartate teṣu ekaikasu na asti vartanā tatha sarva bhava aṅga vartinī anyam anya upacayena niśritā ekaikeṣu teṣu vartanī pūrvam aparāntatu na upalabhyate 
[242,i_242,ii]	atas eva uktam ācārya nāgārjuna pādaiḥ svādhyāya dīpa mudrā darpaṇa ghoṣa arka kānta bīja amlaiḥ skandha pratisaṃdhiḥ asaṃkramaḥ ca vidvadbhiḥ upadhāryau iti śatakaśāstre ca ārya deva pādaiḥ mahā bodhi caryā sthira prasthāna sthitaiḥ alāta cakra nirmāṇa svapna māyā ambu candrakaiḥ dhūmikā antar pratiśrutkā marī ci abhraiḥ samaḥ bhavaḥ iti 
[242,iii_242,iv]	tat evam bimba pratibimba ādi nyāyena mātuḥ kukṣau vijñāne saṃmūrcchite vijñāna pratyayam nāma rūpam niṣicyate kṣarati prādurbhavati iti arthaḥ yadi iha gatau vijñānam na saṃmūrchitam syāt tadā nāma rūpa prādurbhāvaḥ na syāt saced ānanda vijñānam mātuḥ kukṣim na avakrāmeta na tat kalalam kalala tvāya saṃvarteta iti vacanāt 
[242,v_242,vii]	tat evam niṣikte nāma rūpe tu ṣaṣ āyatana saṃbhavaḥ duḥkha utpattyā āya dvāra bhāvena darśana śravaṇa ghrāṇa rasa sparśa manaa ākhyam ṣaṣ āyatanam nāma rūpa hetukam upajāyate sa cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭvā saumanasya sthānīyāni abhiniviśate abhiniviṣṭaḥ san rāga jam dveva jam moha jam karma karoti ityādinā duḥkha utpatta āvāya dvāra tvam ṣaṇṇām āyatanānām tat evam saṃbhūte ṣaṣ āyatane uttara kālam ṣaṣ āyatanam āgamya saṃsparśaḥ saṃpravartate kaḥ punar ayam saṃsparśaḥ katham vā saṃpravartate iti pratipādayan āha cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpam ca samanvāhāram eva ca nāma rūpam pratītya evam vijñānam saṃpravartate saṃnipāta srayāṇām yaḥ rūpa vijñāna cakṣuṣām sparśaḥ saḥ
[242,viii_242,ix]	cakṣuḥ indriyam pratītya rūpāṇi ca samanvāhāram ca pratītya manaskāram viṣaya ādi vilakṣaṇam samanantara pratyayam vijñāna bīja bhūtam cakṣuḥ vijñānam utpadyate tatra cakṣuḥ ca rūpa āyatanam ca rūpam samanvāhāraḥ catuḥskandha lakṣaṇam nāma tat etat trayam pratītya utpadyamānam cakṣuḥ vijñānam nāma rūpam pratītya utpadyate tat evam eṣām indriya viṣaya vijñānānām trayāṇām yaḥ saṃnipātaḥ saha utpādaḥ anyonya upakāreṇa tulyam yā pravṛttiḥ sa spṛṣṭi lakṣaṇaḥ sparśaḥ tatas uttara kālam tasmāt sparśāt ca vedanā saṃpravartate iṣṭa aniṣṭa ubhaya viparīta viṣaya anubhūtiḥ viṣaya anubhavaḥ vedanam vittiḥ vedanā iti ucyate duḥkhā sukhā aduḥkha asukhā ca trividhā yathā ca eṣām rūpa vijñāna cakṣuṣām trayāṇām saṃnipāta lakṣaṇam sparśam āgamya vedanā uktā evam śeṣa indriya viṣaya vijñāna traya saṃnipāta lakṣaṇa sparśa hetukā vedanā vyākhyeyā 
[243,i_243,iii]	tatas uttara kālam vedanā pratyayā tṛṣṇā saṃpravartate iti vartate vedanā pratyayaḥ yasyāḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ sā vedanā pratyayā kiṃviṣayā punar sā tṛṣṇā vedanā viṣayā eva kim kāraṇam yasmāt asau tṛṣṇāluḥ vedanā artham hi tṛṣyate vedanā nimittam eva abhilāṣam karoti iti arthaḥ katham kṛtvā yadi tāvat sukhā vedanā asya upajāyate sa tasyāḥ punar punar saṃyoga artham paritṛṣyate atha duḥkhā tadā tasyāḥ visaṃyoga artham paritṛṣyate atha aduḥkha asukhā tasyāḥ api nityam aparibhraṃśa artham paritṛṣyate saḥ evam tṛṣyamāṇaḥ upādānam upādatte caturvidham saḥ evam vedanāsu abhiniviṣṭaḥ saktaḥ tṛṣṇā pratyayam kāma dṛṣṭi śīla vrata ātma vāda upādāna ākhyam caturvidham karma ākṣepa kāraṇam parigṛhṇāti tat evam asya tṛṣṇā pratyayam upādānam bhavati 
[243,iv_243,v]	tatas uttara kālam upādāne sati bhavaḥ upādātuḥ pravartate syāt hi yadi anupādānaḥ mucyeta na bhavet bhavaḥ pañca skandhāḥ sa ca bhavaḥ caturvidhasya yathā uktasya upādānasya upādātā grahītā utpādayitā tasya upādātuḥ upādānapratyayaḥ bhavaḥ upajāyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt yaḥ hi anutpādita vedanā tṛṣṇaḥ pratisaṃkhyāna balena tṛṣṇām asvīkurvan caturvidham upādānam pravihāya upādātā amalā dvaya jñāna saṃmukhībhāvāt syāt hi yadi anupādānaḥ mucyeta saḥ tadānīm tasya na bhavet bhavaḥ 
[243,vi_243,vii]	kaḥ punar ayam bhavaḥ pañca skandhāḥ sa ca bhavaḥ yaḥ upādānāt pravartate sa pañca skandha svabhāvaḥ veditavyaḥ trividham api kāyikam vācikam mānasikam ca karma bhavati asmāt anāgatam skandha pañcakam bhavaḥ iti vyapadiśyate tatra kāyikam vācikam karma rūpa skandha svabhāvam karma vijñapti tvāt mānasam tu catur skandha svabhāvam iti evam sa bhavaḥ pañca skandhāḥ iti vijñeyam tasmāt bhavāt jātiḥ pravartate anāgata skandha utpādaḥ jātiḥ sā ca bhavāt pravartate tatas uttara kālam jarā maraṇa duḥkha ādi śokāḥ sa paridevanāḥ daurmanasyam upāyāsāḥ jāteḥ etat pravartate 
[243,viii_244,i]	jāti hetukāḥ ete jarā maraṇa ādayaḥ pravartante eṣām ca yathāsūtram eva vyākhyānam veditavyam tatra skandha paripākaḥ jarā jīrṇasya skandha bhedaḥ maraṇam mriyamāṇasya vigacchataḥ saṃmūḍhasya sāmiṣaṅgaḥ hṛdaya saṃtāpaḥ śokaḥ śoka samutthitaḥ vāc pralāpaḥ paridevaḥ pañca indriya asāta nipātaḥ duḥkham manaḥ niṣṭa nipātaḥ daurmanasyam duḥkha daurmanasya bahu tva saṃbhūtāḥ upāyāsāḥ iti tat evam yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena kevalasya evam etasya duḥkha skandhasya saṃbhavaḥ kevalasya iti ātma ātmīya svabhāva vigatasya bāla pṛthagjana parikalpita mātrasya duḥkha ātmakasya sukha avyāmiśrasya eva iti arthaḥ evam iti hetu pratyaya mātra balena eva iti arthaḥ duḥkha skandhasya iti duḥkha samudāyasya duḥkha samūhasya duḥkha rāśeḥ iti arthaḥ 
[244,ii_244,iii]	yatas ca evam yathā upavarṇitāt avidyā ādikāt eva bhava aṅgānām pravṛttiḥ atas saṃsāra mūlān saṃskārān avidvān saṃskaroti atas avidvān kārakaḥ tasmāt na vidvān tattva darśanāt tatra saṃsārasya vijñāna ādi pravṛtti lakṣaṇasya mūlam pradhānam kāraṇam saṃskārāḥ tatas ca saṃsāra mūlān saṃskārān avidvān saṃskaroti 
[244,iv]	avidyā anugataḥ yaḥ pudgalaḥ bhikṣavaḥ puṇyān api saṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti apuṇyān api saṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti āneñjyān api saṃskārān abhisaṃskaroti iti bhagavat vacanāt yatas ca evam avidvān kārakaḥ tasmāt avidvān eva pudgalaḥ kārakaḥ bhavati saṃskārāṇām na vidvān tattva darśī prahīṇa avidyaḥ kim kāraṇam tattva darśanāt tattva darśane hi sarva padārthanām eva anupalambhāt na asti kiṃcid yat ā ālambya karma kuryāt iti 
[244,v_244,vi]	yatas ca evam avidyāyām eva satyām saṃskārāḥ pravartante asatyām na pravartante atas avidyāyām niruddhāyām saṃskārāṇām asaṃbhavaḥ hetu vaiyarthyāt tasyāḥ punar avidyāyāḥ kutas nirodhaḥ iti āha avidyāyāḥ nirodhaḥ tu jñānena asya eva bhāvanāt asya eva pratītyasamutpādasya yathāvat aviparīta bhāvanātaḥ avidyā prahīyate yaḥ hi pratītyasamutpādam samyak paśyati sa sūkṣmasya api bhāvasya na svarūpam upalabhate pratibimba sva prālāta cakra mudga āt i vat tu svabhāva śūnyatām sarveṣām bhāvānām avatarati saḥ eva svabhāva śūnyatām sarveṣām bhāvānām avatīrṇaḥ na kiṃcid vastu upalabhate bāhyam ādhyātmikam vā saḥ anupalabhamānaḥ na kvacid dharme muhyati amūḍhaḥ ca karma na karoti iti evam pratītyasamutpāda bhāvanayā tattvam avatarati tattva darśinaḥ yoginaḥ niyatam eva avidyā prahīyate prahīṇa avidyasya saṃskārāḥ nirudhyante 
[244,vii_245,i]	yathā ca evam avidyā nirodhāt saṃskārāḥ nirudhyante evam tasya tasya nirodhena tat tat na abhipravartate duḥkha skandhaḥ kevalaḥ ayam evam samyak nirudhyate pūrvasya pūrvasya aṅgasya nirodhena utarasya uttarasya aṅgasya nirodhaḥ bhavati iti vijñeyam anayā ca ānupūrvyā ayam yogī ātma ātmīya ādya darśana āyāsa nirastaḥ kāraka vedaka vi rahitam bhāva svabhāva śūnyam duḥkha rāśim punar anutpattyā samyak nirodhayati yathā uktam ārya śāli stamba sūtre 
[245,ii^1]	evam ādhyātmikaḥ api pratītyasamutpādaḥ dvābhyām eva kāraṇābhyām utpadyate katamābhyām dvābhyām hetu upanibandhataḥ pratyaya upanibandhataḥ ca tatra ādhyātmikasya pratītyasamutpādasya hetu upanibandhaḥ katamaḥ yat idam avidyā pratyayāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃskāra pratyayam vijñānam vijñāna pratyayam nāma rūpam nāma rūpa pratyayam ṣaṣ āyatanam ṣaṣ āyatana pratyayaḥ sparśaḥ sparśa pratyayā vedanā vedanā pratyayā tṛṣṇā tṛṣṇā pratyayam upādānam upādāna pratyayaḥ bhavaḥ bhava pratyayā jātiḥ jāti pratyayāḥ jarā maraṇa śoka parideva duḥkha daurmanasya upāyāsāḥ saṃbhavanti evam asya kevalasya mahataḥ duḥkha skandhasya samudayaḥ bhavati avidyā ced na abhaviṣyat na eva saṃskārāḥ prajñāsyante 
[245,ii^2]	evam yāvat jātiḥ ced na abhaviṣyat jarā maraṇam na prajñāsyate athavā satyām avidyāyām saṃskārāṇām abhinirvṛttiḥ bhavati evam yāvat jātyām satyām jarā maraṇasya abhinirvṛttiḥ bhavati atra avidyāyāḥ na evam bhavati aham saṃskārān abhinirvartayāmi iti saṃskārāṇām api na evam bhavati vayam avidyayā abhinirvartitāḥ iti evam yāvat jāteḥ api na evam bhavati aham jarā maraṇam abhinirvartayāmi iti jarā maraṇasya api na evam bhavati aham jātyā abhinirvartitam iti atha ca satyām avidyāyām saṃskārāṇa abhinirvṛtti rbhavati prādurbhāvaḥ evam yāvat jātyām satyām jarā maraṇasya abhinirvṛttiḥ bhavati prādurbhāvaḥ evam ādhyātmikasya pratītyasamutpādasya hetu upanibandhaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ 
[245,iii^1]	katham ādhyātmikasya pratītyasamutpādasya pratyaya upanibandhaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ iti ṣaṇṇām dhātūnām samavāyāt katameṣām ṣaṇṇām dhātūnām samavāyāt yat idam pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśa vijñāna dhātūnām samavāyāt ādhyātmikasya pratītyasamutpādasya pratyaya upanibandhaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ tatra ādhyātmikasya pratītyasamutpādasya pṛthivī dhātuḥ katamaḥ yaḥ kāyasya saṃśleṣāt kaṭhina bhāvam abhinirvartayati ayam ucyate pṛthivī dhātuḥ yaḥ kāyasya anuparigraha kṛtyam karoti ayam ucyate abdhātuḥ yaḥ kāyasya aśita bhakṣitam paripācayati ayam ucyate tejaḥ dhātuḥ yaḥ kāyasya āśvāsa praśvāsa kṛtyam karoti ayam ucyate vāyudhātuḥ yaḥ kāyasya antar śauṣīryam abhinirvartayati ayam ucyate ākāśa dhātuḥ yaḥ nāma rūpam abhinirvartayati naḍa kalāpa yogena pañca vijñāna kāya saṃyuktam sa āsravam ca manaḥ vijñānam ayam ucyate bhikṣavaḥ vijñāna dhātuḥ tatra asatām eṣām pratyayānām kāyasya utpattiḥ na bhavati yadā tu ādhyātmikaḥ pṛthivī dhātuḥ avikalaḥ bhavati evam ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśa vijñāna dhātavaḥ ca avikalāḥ bhavanti tatas sarveṣām samavāyāt kāyasya utpattiḥ bhavati 
[245,iii^2]	tatra pṛthivī dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya kaṭhina bhāvam abhinirvartayāmi iti ap dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya anuparigraha kṛtyam karomi iti tejaḥ dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya aśita pīta khāditam paripācayāmi iti vāyu dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya āśvāsa praśvāsa kṛtyam karomi iti ākāśa dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya antar śauṣīryam abhinirvartayāmi iti vijñāna dhātoḥ na evam bhavati aham kāyasya nāma rūpam abhinirvartayāmi iti kāyasya api na evam bhavati aham emiḥ pratyayaiḥ janitaḥ iti atha ca punar satām eṣām pratyayānām samavāyāt kāyasya utpatti rbhavati tatra pṛthivī dhātuḥ na ātmā na sattvaḥ na jīvaḥ na jantuḥ na manujaḥ na mānavaḥ na strī na pumān na napuṃsakam na ca aham na mama na ca anyasya kasyacid evam ap dhātuḥ tejaḥ dhātuḥ vāyudhātuḥ a ākāśa dhātuḥ vijñāna dhātuḥ na ātmā na sattvaḥ na jīvaḥ na jantuḥ na manujaḥ na mānavaḥ na strī na pumān na napuṃsakam na ca aham na mama na ca anyasya kasyacid 
[246,i^1]	tatra avidyā katamā yāḥ eṣām evam ṣaṇṇām dhātūnāyamaiksaṃjñā piṇḍa saṃjñā nitya saṃjñā dhruva saṃjñā śāśvata saṃjñā sukha saṃjñā ātma saṃjñā sattva saṃjñā jīva pudgala m anuja mānava saṃjñā ahaṃkāra saṃjñā mamakāra saṃjñā evamādi vividham ajñānam iyam ucyate avidyā iti evam avidyāyām satyām viṣayeṣu rāga dveṣa mohāḥ pravartante tatra ye rāga dveṣa mohāḥ viṣayeṣu amī saṃskārāḥ iti ucyante vastu prativijñaptiḥ vijñānam vijñāna sahabhuvaḥ catvāraḥ skandhāḥ arūpiṇaḥ upādāna ākhyāḥ tad nāma rūpam catvāri mahābhūtāni tāni ca upādāya rūpam tat ca nāma rūpam aikadhyam abhisaṃkṣipya tad nāma rūpam 
[246,i^2]	nāma rūpa saṃniśritāni indriyāṇi ṣaṣ āyatanam trayāṇām dharmāṇām saṃnipātaḥ sparśaḥ sparśa anubhavaḥ vedanā vedanā adhyavasānam tṛṣṇā tṛṣṇā vaipulyam upādānam upādāna nirjātam punarbhava janakam karma bhavaḥ bhava hetukaḥ skandha prādurbhāvaḥ jātiḥ jātasya skandhasya paripākaḥ jarā jīrṇasya skandhasya vināśaḥ maraṇam mriyamāṇasya saṃmūḍhasya sa abhiṣvaṅgasya antardāhaḥ śokaḥ śoka uttham ālapanam paridevaḥ pañca vijñāna kāya saṃyuktam asātam anubhavanam duḥkham manasā saṃyuktam mānasam duḥkham dārmanasyam ye ca api anye evamādayaḥ upakleśāḥ te upāyāsāḥ iti 
[246,ii]	tatra moha andhakāra arthena avidyā abhisaṃskāra arthena saṃskārāḥ vijñāpana arthena vijñānam anyonya upastambha na arthena nāma rūpam āya dvāra arthena ṣaṣ āyatanam sparśana arthena sparśaḥ anubhavana arthena vedanā paritarṣaṇa arthena tṛṣṇā upādāna arthena upādānam punarbhava arthena bhavaḥ janma arthena jātiḥ paripāka arthena jarā vināśa arthena maraṇam śocana arthena śokaḥ paridevana arthena paridevaḥ kāya paripīḍana arthena duḥkham citta saṃpīḍana arthena daurmanasyam upakleśa arthena upāyāsāḥ 
[246,iii^1]	athavā tattve apratipattiḥ mithyāpratipattiḥ ajñānam avidyā evam avidyāyām satyām trividhāḥ saṃskārāḥ abhinirvartante puṇya upagāḥ apuṇya upagāḥ ānen jya upagāḥ tatra puṇya upagānām saṃskārāṇām puṇya upagamā iva vijñānam bhavati apuṇya upagānām saṃskārāṇām apuṇya upagamā iva vijñānam bhavati āneñjya upagānām saṃskārāṇāmāneñjya upagam eva vijñānam bhavati idam ucyate vijñānam vijñāna pratyayam nāma rūpam iti vedanā ādayaḥ arūpiṇaḥ catvāraḥ skandhāḥ tatra tatra bhave nāmayanti iti nāma saha rūpa skandhena ca nāma rūpam ca iti nāma rūpam ucyate nāma rūpa vivṛddhayā ṣaḍbhiḥ āyatana dvāraiḥ kṛtya kriyāḥ pravartante prajñāyante tad nāma rūpa pratyayam ṣaṣ āyatanam iti ucyate ṣaḍbhyaḥ ca āyatanebhyaḥ ṣaṭ sparśakāyāḥ pravartante ayam ṣaṣ āyatana pratyayaḥ sparśaḥ iti ucyate 
[246,iii^2]	yat jātīyaḥ sparśaḥ bhavati tad jātīyā vedanā pravartate iyam ucyate bhikṣavaḥ sparśa pratyayāḥ vedanā iti yaḥ tām vedanām viśeṣeṇa āsvādayati abhinandati adhyavasyati adhyavasāya tiṣṭhati sā vedanā pratyayā tṛṣṇā iti ucyate āsvādana abhinandana adhyavasāna sthānāt ātma priya rūpa sāta rūpaiḥ viyogaḥ mā bhūt nityam aparityāgaḥ bhavet iti yā evam prārthanā idam ucyate bhikṣavaḥ tṛṣṇā pratyayam upādānam yatra vastuni sa tṛṣṇaḥ tasya vastunaḥ arjanāya viṭhapanāya upādānam upādatte tatra tatra prārthayate evam prārthayamānaḥ punarbhava janakam karma samutthāpayati kāyena vācā manasā ca saḥ upādānapratyayaḥ bhavaḥ iti ucyate tad karma nirjātānām skandhānām abhinirvṛtiḥ yā sā bhava pratyayā jātiḥ iti ucyate jātyā abhinirvṛttānām skandhānām upacayana paripākāt vināśaḥ bhavati tat idam jāti pratyayam jarā maraṇam iti ucyate 
[247,i]	evam ayam dvādaśa aṅgaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ anyonya hetukaḥ anyonya pratyayaḥ na eva anityaḥ na eva nityaḥ na saṃskṛtaḥ na asaṃskṛtaḥ na ahetukaḥ na apratyayaḥ na vedayitā na avedayitā na pratītyasamutpannaḥ na apratītya samutpannaḥ na kṣaya dharmaḥ na akṣaya dharmaḥ na vināśa dharmaḥ na avināśa dharmaḥ na nirodha dharmaḥ na anirodha dharmaḥ anādi kāla pravṛttaḥ anucchinnaḥ anupravartate nadī srota vat 
[247,ii]	yadi api ayam dvādaśa aṅgaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ anucchinnaḥ anupravartate nadī srota vat atha ca imāni asya dvādaśa aṅgasya pratītyasamutpādasya catvāri aṅgāni saṃghāta kriyāyai hetu tvena pravartante katamāni catvāri yat uta avidyā tṛṣṇā karma vijñānam ca tatra vijñānam bīja svabhāva tvena hetuḥ karma kṣetra svabhāva tvena hetuḥ avidyā tṛṣṇā ca kleśa svabhāva tvena hetuḥ karma kleśāḥ vijñāna bījam janayanti tatra karma vijñāna bījasya kṣetra kāryam karoti tṛṣṇā vijñāna bījam snehayati avidyā vijñāna bījam avakirati asatām teṣām pratyayānām vijñāna bījasi abhinirvṛttiḥ na bhavati tatra karmaṇaḥ na evam bhavati aham vijñāna bījasya kṣetra kāryam karomi iti tṛṣṇāyāḥ api na evam bhavati aham vijñānasya sneha kāryam karom iti avidyāyāḥ api na evam bhavati aham vijñāna bījam avakirāmi iti vijñāna bījasya api na evam bhavati aham ebhiḥ pratyayaiḥ janitam iti 
[247,iii]	atha ca vijñāna bījam karma kṣetra pratiṣṭhitam tṛṣṇā sneha abhiṣyanditam avidyayā su avakīrṇam vibhajyamānam virohati tatra tatra upapattyāṃyatana pratisaṃdhau mātuḥ kukṣau nāma rūpa aṅkuram abhinirvartayati sa ca nāma rūpa aṅkuraḥ na svayaṃkṛtaḥ na para kṛtaḥ na ubhaya kṛtaḥ na īśvara kṛtaḥ na kāla pariṇāmitaḥ na prakṛti saṃbhūtaḥ na ca eka kāraṇa adhīnaḥ na api ahetu samutpannaḥ atha ca mātā pitṛ saṃyogāt ṛtu samavāyāt anyeṣām pratyayānām samavāyāt āsvāda anuviddham vijñāna bījam mātuḥ kukṣau nāma rūpa aṅkuram abhinirvartayati asvāmikeṣu dharmeṣu aparigraheṣu amameṣu ākāśa sameṣu māyā lakṣaṇa svabhāveṣu hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt 
[247,iv^1]	tat yathā pañcabhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ cakṣuḥ vijñānam utpadyate katamaiḥ pañcabhiḥ yat uta cakṣuḥ pratītya rūpam ca ālokam ca ākāśam ca tad jamana sikāram ca pratītya utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam tatra cakṣuḥ vijñānasya cakṣuḥ āśraya kṛtyam karoti rūpam ālambana kṛtyam karoti ālokaḥ avabhāsa kṛtyam karoti ākāśam anāvaraṇa kṛtyam karoti tad ja manasikāraḥ samanvāharaṇa kṛtyam karoti asatām eṣām pratyayānām cakṣuḥ vijñānam na utpadyate yadā tu cakṣuḥ ādhyātmikam āyatanam avikalam bhavati evam rūpa āloka ākāśa tajja manasikārāḥ ca avikalāḥ bhavanti tatas sarveṣām samavāyāt cakṣuḥ vijñānam utpadyate 
[247,iv^2]	tatra cakṣuṣaḥ na evam bhavati aham cakṣuḥ vijñānasya āśraya kṛtyam karomi iti ālokasya api na evam bhavati aham cakṣuḥ vijñānasya avabhāsa kṛtyam karomi iti ākāśasya api na evam bhavati aham cakṣuḥ vijñānasya anāvaraṇa kṛtyam karom iti tad ja mana sikārasya api na evam bhavati aham cakṣuḥ vijñānasya samanvāharaṇa kṛtyam karomi iti cakṣuḥ vijñānasya api na evam bhavati aham ebhiḥ pratyayaiḥ janitam iti atha ca satām eṣām pratyayānām samavāyāt cakṣuḥ vijñānasya utpattiḥ bhavati evam śeṣāṇām indriyāṇām yathāyogam karaṇīyam 
[248,i]	tatra na kaścid dharmaḥ asmāt lokāt para lokam saṃkrāmati asti ca karma phala prativijñaptiḥ hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt tat yathā bhikṣavaḥ su pariśuddhe ādarśa maṇḍale mukha pratibimbakam dṛśyate na ca tatra ādarśa maṇḍale mukham saṃkrāmati asti ca mukha prativijñaptiḥ hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt evam asmāt lokāt na kaścid cyutaḥ na api anyatra upapannaḥ asti ca karma phala prativijñaptiḥ hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt tat yathā bhikṣavaḥ candra maṇḍalam catvāriṃśat yojana śatam ūrdhvam vrajati atha ca punar parītte api udaka bhājane candrasya pratibimbam dṛśyate na ca tasmāt sthānāt ūrdhvam nabhasaḥ cyutam parītte udakasya bhājane saṃkrāntam bhavati asti ca candra maṇḍala prativijñaptiḥ hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt evam asmāt lokāt na kaścid cyutaḥ na anyatra upapannaḥ asti ca karma phala prativijñaptiḥ hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt 
[248,ii]	tat yathā agniḥ upādāna pratyaye sati jvalati upādāna vaikalyāt na jvalati evam eva bhikṣavaḥ karma kleśa janitam vijñāna bījam tatra tatra upapatti āyatana pratisaṃdhau mātuḥ kukṣau nāma rūpa aṅkuram abhinirvartayati asvāmikeṣu dharmeṣu aparigraheṣu māyā lakṣaṇa svabhāveṣu amameṣu kṛtrimeṣu hetu pratyayānām avaikalyāt 
[248,iii^1]	tatra ādhyātmikaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ pañcabhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ draṣṭavyaḥ katamaiḥ pañcabhiḥ na śāśvatataḥ na ucchedataḥ na saṃkrāntitaḥ parītta hetu vipula phala abhinirvṛttitaḥ tad sadṛśa anuprabandhataḥ ca iti katham na śāśvatataḥ yasmāt anye māraṇa antikāḥ skandhāḥ anye aupapatti aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ na tu yaḥ eva māraṇa antikāḥ skandhāḥ te eva aupapatti aṃśikāḥ api tu māraṇa antikāḥ skandhāḥ nirudhyante tasmin eva ca samaye aupapatti aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ prādurbhavanti atas na śāśvatataḥ katham na ucchedataḥ na ca pūrva niruddheṣu māraṇa antikeṣu skandheṣu aupapatti aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ prādurbhavanti na api aniruddheṣu 
[248,iii^2]	api tu māraṇa antikāḥ skandhāḥ nirudhyante tasmin eva ca samaye aupapatti aṃśikāḥ skandhāḥ prādurbhavanti tulā daṇḍa unnābha avanāma vat candra bimba pratibimba vat atas na ucchedataḥ katham na saṃkrāntitaḥ visadṛśāḥ sattva nikāyāḥ sabhāgāyām jātyām jātim abhinirvartayanti atas na saṃkrāntitaḥ katham parītta hetutaḥ vipula phala abhinirvṛttitaḥ parīttam karma kriyate vipulaḥ phala vipākaḥ anubhūyate atas parītta hetutaḥ vipula phala abhinirvṛttitaḥ katham tad sadṛśa anuprabandhataḥ yathāvedanīyam karma kriyate tathā vedanīyaḥ vipākaḥ anubhūyate atas tad sadṛśa anuprabandhataḥ ca iti vistaraḥ 
[249,i]	yaḥ ca evam pratītyasamutpādam yathābhūtam samyak paśyati sa na pūrva antam pratisarati na apara antam pratisarati ityādi sūtre paṭhayate tatra katamaḥ pūrva antaḥ katamaḥ apara antaḥ katham na pratisarati iti tat vayutpati artham idam ārabhyate tatra vartamānam ātma bhāvam apekṣya atītāḥ ātma bhāvāḥ pūrva antaḥ iti ucyate pūrvaḥ hi janma paraṃpara aṃśaḥ pūrva antaḥ tam na pratisarati dṛṣṭi prakāraiḥ na ālambate pratītyasamutpādasya yathāvat avasthita tattva darśanāt na anyathā avasthitam vastu anyathā abhiniviśate tatra aṣṭau dṛṣṭayaḥ pūrva antam ālambya anyathā pravṛttāḥ tat yathā abhūmatītam adhvānam nābhūm iti ca dṛṣṭayaḥ yāḥ tāḥ śāśvata loka ādyāḥ pūrva antam samupāśritāḥ 
[249,ii]	tatra iti śabdaḥ ādi arthaḥ athavā dṛṣṭi dvaya upādānam upalakṣaṇa artham catastraḥ tu etāḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ tat yathā kim nu aham abhūvam atītam adhvānam na abhūvam atītam adhvānam abhūvam ca na abhūvam ca na eva abhūvam na na abhūvam iti etāḥ catasraḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ pūrva antam samāśritāḥ aparāḥ api catasraḥ iti āha yāḥ tāḥ śāśvata loka ādyāḥ pūrvam prasaṅgena upavarṇitāḥ tāḥ api pūrva antam samupāśritāḥ 
[249,iii]	tatra yadi api pūrva antāt dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayāt uttaram dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayam na atibhidyate tathā api tāvat mātra viśeṣam āśritya pṛthak upādīyate tat ca uttaratra vyākhyāsyāmaḥ tatra śāśvataḥ lokaḥ iti etat abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti etasmāt na atibhidyate athavā ayam viśeṣaḥ yat śāśvataḥ lokaḥ iti eṣām dṛṣṭiḥ sāmānyena pūrva antam āśritā abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti eṣā tu ātmanaḥ eva pūrva anta parāmarśena pravṛttā na sāmānyena iti evam anyāsu api dṛṣṭiṣu viśeṣaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti evam tāvat aṣṭau etāḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ pūrva antam samupāśritāḥ 
[249,iv]	uktaḥ pūrva antar tad ālambikābhiḥ dṛṣṭibhiḥ sārdham idānīm aparāntaḥ ucyate tatra vartamānam ātma bhāvam apekṣya bhāvinaḥ ātma bhāvāḥ aparāntaḥ iti ucyate aparaḥ hi janma paraṃpara aṃśaḥ apara antaḥ tam na pratisarati dṛṣṭi prakāraiḥ na ālambate pratītyasamutpādasya yathāvat avasthita tattva darśanāt na anyathā avasthitam vastu anyathā abhiniviśate tatra aṣṭau dṛṣṭayaḥ apara antam ālambya anyathā pravṛttāḥ tat yathā dṛṣṭayaḥ na bhaviṣyāmi kim anyaḥ anāgate adhvani bhaviṣyāmi iti ca antādyāḥ apara antam samāśritāḥ 
[249,v]	iha api dṛṣṭi dvaya upādānam upalakṣaṇa artham catastraḥ tu etāḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ tat yathā kim nu bhaviṣyāmi anāgatam adhvānam na bhaviṣyāmi bhaviṣyāmi ca na bhaviṣyāmi ca na eva bhaviṣyāmi na ca na bhaviṣyāmi anāgatam adhvānam iti etāḥ catasraḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ apara antam samāśritāḥ kim etāḥ eva catasraḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ apara antam samāśritāḥ na iti āha kim tarhi aparāḥ api catasraḥ vidyante anta ādyāḥ apara antam samāśritāḥ tatra anta ādyāḥ catasraḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ sāmānyena apara antam āśritya pravṛttāḥ kim tu bhaviṣyāmi anāgatam adhvānam iti etāḥ tu ātmanaḥ eva apara antam āśritya pravṛttāḥ iti evam dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayasya viśeṣaḥ iti boddhavyam 
[250,i_250,ii]	tatra ādyasya tāvat pūrva anta ālambikasya dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayasya yathā na saṃbhavaḥ tathā pratipādayan āha abhūmatītam adhvānam iti etat na upapadyate yaḥ hi janmasu pūrveṣu saḥ eva na bhavati ayam tatra yaḥ eva atīteṣu janmasu babhūva yadi saḥ eva ayam adhunā syāt tadā yuktam asya grahītum abhūvam aham atītam adhvānam iti na ca etat evam saṃbhavati nitya tva prasaṅgāt nityasya ca saṃsaraṇa anupapatteḥ eka gati sthasya api nānā gati saṃgṛhīta tva prasaṅgāt iha hi pūrvam yadi naraka ādi gatikaḥ bhūtvā idānīm karma vaicitryāt manuṣyeṣu upapannaḥ evaṃkalpayet aham eva asau nārakaḥ āsam iti tat asya na yuktam katham hi nāma manuṣyaḥ san nāraka ādikaḥ syāt 
[250,iii]	yat tarhi idam paṭhayate sūtre aham eva sa tena kālena tena samayena māndhātā nāma rājā cakravartī abhūvam iti tat katham veditavyam iti anyatva pratiṣedha param tat vacanam na ekatva pratipādakam iti vijñeyam atas eva hi na anyaḥ sa tena kālena tena samayena iti paṭhayate yadi punar saḥ eva ayam iti pūrvakasya ca adhunātanasya ca eka tvam syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ syāt uktaḥ tāvat atra doṣaḥ nitya tvam syāt iti 
[250,iv_250,vi]	tathā api bhūyaḥ ucyate saḥ eva ātmā iti tu bhavet upādānam viśiṣyate yadi saḥ eva pūrvakaḥ ātmā ayam idānīm syāt tadā upādānasya pañca skandha lakṣaṇasya viśeṣaḥ na syāt upādātura viśeṣāt pūrva avasthāyām iva na ca evam upādāna aviśeṣaḥ asya ātmanaḥ kim tarhi viśiṣyate eva upādānam upādātuḥ karma bhedāt kāraka bhedāt ca tatas ca upādāna viśeṣāt saḥ eva ayam ātmā iti na yujyate atha manyase viśiṣyatām upādānam ātmā tu ekaḥ eva iti atas ātmanaḥ aviśiṣṭa tvāt abhūmatītam adhvānam iti etat bhaviṣyati eva ucyate upādāna vinirmuktaḥ ātmā te katamaḥ punar 
[250,vii]	yadi hi anyat upādānam anyaḥ ca ātmā syāt tadā upādāna viśeṣe api ātmanaḥ aviśeṣāt syāt etat evam na ca etat bhedena darśayitum śakyam ayam asau ātmā idam asya upādānam iti upādāna viśiṣṭa svabhāva tvāt ātmanaḥ ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt pṛthak grahaṇa prasaṅgāt ca yadā ca evam upādāna vinirmuktaḥ ātmā darśayitum na śakyate tadā upādāna viśeṣe api ātmā viśeṣaḥ iti na śakyate kalpayitum 
[251,i_251,ii]	atha api kaścid parikalpayet satyam upādāna vinirmuktaḥ iti evam na saṃbhavati kim upādānam eva ātma tvena parikalpyate iti etat api na yuktam iti pratipādayan āha upādāna vinirmuktaḥ na asti ātmā iti kṛte sati syāt upādānam eva ātmā na asti ca ātmā iti vaḥ punar yathā tāvat upādānam eva ātmā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha na ca upādānam eva ātmā vyeti tat samudeti ca katham hi nāma upādānam upādātā bhaviṣyati 
[251,iii]	tatra yat etat pañca upādāna skandha ākhyam upādānam tat pratikṣaṇam utpadyate ca vinaśyati ca na ca evam ātmā pratikṣaṇam utpadyate ca vinaśyati ca ātmā skandhebhyaḥ tattva anyatva ādinā ca nitya anitya tvena api aśakyaḥ eva vaktum aneka doṣa prasaṅgāt nitya tve hi ātmanaḥ śāśvata vādaḥ syāt anitya tve ca uccheda vāda prasaṅgaḥ tatas ca tat ubhayam śāśvata uccheda ākhyam mahā nartha karam iti na upagantavyam atas upādānam eva ātmā iti tāvat na yujyate 
[251,iv_251,v]	api ca katham hi nāma upādānam upādātā bhaviṣyati iha upādīyate iti upādānam karma tasya ca avaśyam upādātrāḥ upārjakena bhavitavyam tasya ca upādānasya yadi ātma tvam iṣyate tatra upādānam eva upādātā iti api vidyate tatas ca kartṛ karmaṇoḥ aikye sati chetṛ chettavya ghaṭa kumbhakāra agni indhana ādīnām api aikyam syāt na ca etat dṛṣṭam yuktam vā iti pratipādayan āha katham hi nāma upādānam upādātā bhaviṣyati iti api tu atyanta asaṃbhavaḥ eva asya pakṣasya iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[251,vi_251,vii]	atra āha satyam upādāna mātram ātmā na yujyate kim tarhi upādāna vyatiriktaḥ eva ātmā bhaviṣyati etat api na yuktam kim kāraṇam yasmāt anyaḥ punar upādānāt ātmā na eva upapadyate gṛhyate hi anupādānaḥ yadi anyaḥ na ca gṛhyate yadi upādānāt ātmā vyatiriktaḥ syāt gṛhyeta saḥ upādāna vyatiriktaḥ ghaṭāt iva paṭaḥ na ca evam gṛhyate tasmāt upādāna vyatiriktaḥ api na asti anupādānaḥ upādāna vyatirekeṇa agṛhyamāṇa tvāt kha puṣpa vat iti abhiprāyaḥ 
[252,i_252,ii]	idānīm yathā upapāditam artham nigamayan āha evam na anyaḥ upādānāt na ca upādānam eva saḥ ātmā na asti anupādānaḥ atha syāt yadi ātmā upādāna svarūpaḥ na bhavati upādāna upādātroḥ eka tva prasaṅgāt udaya vyaya prasaṅgāt ca sa hi anyaḥ api na bhavati upādānam anapekṣya bhedena grahaṇa prasaṅgāt na ca api anupādānaḥ upādāna nirapekṣasya grahaṇa prasaṅgāt evam tarhi na asti ātmā iti astu ucyate na api na asti eṣa niścayaḥ 
[252,iii]	yaḥ hi nāma skandhān upādāya prajñapyate sa katham na asti iti syāt na hi avidyamānaḥ vandhyā tanayaḥ skandhān upādāya prajñapyate katham sati upādāne upādātā na asti iti yujyate tasmāt na astitvam api asya na yujyate tasmāt na asti ātmā iti niścayaḥ api eṣa na upapadyate asya tu ātmanaḥ vyavasthānam vistareṇa madhyamaka avatārāt avaseyam iha api ca pūrvam eva sthāna sthāneṣu kṛtā vyavasthā iti na punar iha tadvayava sthāne yatnaḥ āsthīyate 
[252,iv_252,v]	evam tāvat abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti eṣā kalpanā na upapadyate idānīm na abhūvam atītam adhvānam ityet api yathā na upapadyate tathā pratipādayan āha na abhūm atītam adhvānam iti etat na upapadyate yaḥ hi janmasu pūrveṣu tatas anyaḥ na bhavati ayam yadi pūrvakāt ātmanaḥ asya adhunātanasya ātmanaḥ anya tvam syāt tadānīm na abhūm atītam adhvānam iti syāt na ca etat evam saṃbhavati tasmāt na abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti etat na upapadyate 
[252,vi_252,vii]	yadi punar pūrvakāt ātmanaḥ asya anya tvam syāt kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ucyate yadi hi ayam bhavet anyaḥ pratyākhyāya api tam bhavet tathā eva ca sa saṃtiṣṭhet tatra jāyeta vā amṛtaḥ yadi hi ayam adhunātanaḥ ātmā pūrvakāt ātmanaḥ anyaḥ syāt tadā tam pūrvakam ātmānam pratyākhyāya parityajya tad nirapekṣaḥ atad dhetukaḥ eva syāt kim ca anyat tathā eva ca sa saṃtiṣṭhet tatra yadi pūrvakāt ātmanaḥ asya anya tvam syāt tadā anya tvāt ghaṭa utpāde paṭa avināśa vat pūrvasya ātmanā uttarasmin api ātmani samutpadyamāne api anirodhaḥ syāt aniruddha tvāt ca yatra pūrvam deva manuṣya ādi janmasu upapannaḥ yena varṇa saṃsthāna ādinā pūrvam upalabhyamānaḥ tena eva prakāreṇa tathā eva sa tatra avatiṣṭheta tathā eva avatiṣṭheta iti tasmāt na abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti etat na upapadyate 
[252,viii]	atra āha tatra yat uktam yadi hi ayam bhavet anyaḥ pratyākhyāya api tam bhavet iti yadi puna pūrvakam ātmānam pratyākhyāya ayam iha bhavet kaḥ doṣaḥ syāt tatra doṣāḥ bahavaḥ syuḥ katham iti ced yasmāt evam sati ucchedaḥ karmaṇām nāśaḥ tathā anya kṛta karmaṇām anyena paribhogaḥ syāt evamādi prasajyate 
[253,i]	yadi pūrvakam ātmānam pratyākhyāya ayam ātmā bhavet tadā pūrvakasya ātmanaḥ tatra naṣṭa tvāt iha ca anyasya eva ca utpādanāt pūrvakasya ātmanaḥ ucchedaḥ syāt tasmin ca ātmani ucchinne karmaṇā ām adatta phalānām eva āśraya vicchedena vicchedāt bhoktaḥ ca abhāvāt nāśaḥ eva syāt atha pūrvakena ātmanā kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ uttareṇa ātmanā phala paribhogaḥ parikalpyate tathā api anyena kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phalasya anyena upabhogaḥ syāt tatas ca akṛta abhyāgam abhayam syāt karma akṛtakam yadi iti evamādi aniṣṭam āpadyate 
[253,ii]	api ca yadi ayam ātmā pūrvakāt ātmanaḥ anyaḥ eva atra upapannaḥ syāt tadā pūrvam abhūtvā paścāt utpannaḥ iti syāt na ca etat yuktam iti pratipādayan āha na api abhūtvā samudbhūtaḥ doṣaḥ hi atra prasajyate kṛtakaḥ vā bhavet ātmā saṃbhūtaḥ vā api ahetukaḥ iti yadi hi ātmā pūrvam abhūtvā paścāt utpannaḥ syāt tadā kṛtakaḥ eva ātmā syāt na ca kṛtakaḥ ātmā iṣyate anitya tva prasaṅgāt vyatiriktasya ca tat niṣpādakasya kartuḥ abhāvāt kutas kṛtaka tvam ātmanaḥ yojyeta kṛtake ca ātmani parikalpyamāne ādimān saṃsāraḥ syāt eva apūrva sattvasya prādurbhāvaḥ ca na ca etat evam tasmāt na kṛtakaḥ ātmā api ca saṃbhūtaḥ vā api ahetukaḥ abhūtvā prāc ātmā samutpadyamānaḥ nirhetukaḥ eva upapadyate pūrvam hi ātmā na asti iti akṛtakaḥ nirhetukaḥ syāt vā śabdaḥ vikalpe kṛtakaḥ vā bhavet ātmā yadi vā na abhūvam atītam adhvānam iti etat na abhyupeyam saṃbhūtaḥ vā api ahetukaḥ yadi vā na abhūm atītam adhvānam iti etat na upapadyate iti abhyupagamyatām 
[253,iii_253,iv]	idānīm yathā upavarṇitam eva artham nigamayan āha evam dṛṣṭiḥ atīte yā na abhūm aham abhūmaham ubhayam na ubhayam ca iti na eṣā samupapadyate evam yathā upavarṇitena nyāyena abhūmatītam adhvānam iti yā dṛṣṭiḥ eṣā api na eva upapadyate etat dvayasya abhāvāt ca ubhayam api na upapadyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt dvayam hi etat samāhatam ubhayam iti kalpyate ekaikasya ca pṛthak pṛthak abhāvāt kutas tad samāhāraḥ iti ubhayam api na saṃbhavati ubhayasya abhāvāt kutas tad pratiṣedhena na ubhayam bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt na eva abhūvam na na abhūvam iti etat api na upapadyate 
[254,i_254,iii]	tat evam pūrva antam samāśritasya dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayasya asaṃbhavam udbhāvyaḥ idānīm aparānta samāśritasya pratiṣedham āha adhvani anāgate kim nu bhaviṣyāmi iti darśanam na bhaviṣyāmi ca iti etat atītena adhvanā samam yathā eva hi atīte adhvani dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayam niṣiddham evam anāgate api adhvani dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayam niṣedhanīya m ukta pāṭha parivartanena tat yathā adhvani anāgate kim nu bhaviṣyāmi iti asaṃgatam aiṣya janmani yaḥ bhāvaḥ saḥ eva na bhavati ayam iti evamādinā sarvam samam yojyam eka tva pratiṣedhe evam anyatva pratiṣedhe api samam yojyam na syām anāgate kāle iti etat na upapadyate aiṣya janmani yaḥ bhāvaḥ tatas anyaḥ na bhavati ayam iti evamādinā pūrva śloka pāṭha parivartanena 
[254,iv_254,v]	idānīm pūrva antam samāśritasya śāśvata ādi dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayasya pratiṣedha artham āha sa devaḥ sa manuṣyaḥ ced evam bhavati śāśvatam anutpannaḥ ca devaḥ syāt jāyate na hi śāśvatam iha hi kaścid manuṣya gati sthaḥ kuśalam karma kṛtvā deva gatim gacchati tatra yadi saḥ eva devaḥ saḥ eva manuṣyaḥ iti evam ubhayoḥ aikyam syāt tadā śāśvatam syāt na ca etat evam yat eva eva manuṣyaḥ bhavet iti atas na asti kiṃcid śāśvatam api ca śāśvata vāde sati asamutpannaḥ ca devaḥ syāt kim kāraṇam yasmāt jāyate na hi śāśvatam yat hi vastu śāśvatam tat vidyamāna tvāt na eva jāyate tatas ca anutpannaḥ devaḥ syāt anutpannaḥ devaḥ na yujyate iti evam tāvat śāśvatam na yujyate 
[254,vi_254,vii]	idānīm aśāśvatam api yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha devāt anyaḥ manuṣyaḥ ced aśāśvatam ataḥ bhavet devāt anyaḥ manuṣyaḥ ced saṃtatiḥ na upapadyate yadi hi anyaḥ devaḥ anyaḥ ca manuṣyaḥ syāt tadā pūrvakasya manuṣya ātmanaḥ tatra naṣṭa tvāt iha ca anyasya eva utpādāt sa pūrvakaḥ manuṣya ātmā tatra vinaṣṭaḥ iti aśāśvatam syāt tad saṃtāna anuvṛttyā na aśāśvatam iti ced ucyate devāt anyaḥ manuṣyaḥ ced saṃtatiḥ na upapadyate 
[254,viii]	yadi devāt anyaḥ manuṣyaḥ bhavet tadā yathā nimbasya naḥ āmra taru saṃtānaḥ bhavati evam manuṣyasya devaḥ eka saṃtāna patitaḥ na syāt tatas ca pūrvakasya vināśāt aśāśvatam eva bhavet athavā yadi devāt anyaḥ manuṣyaḥ bhavet tadā saṃtāna anuvṛttiḥ na syāt asti ca iyam saṃtāna anuvṛttiḥ devasya manuṣyaḥ eka saṃtāna patitaḥ iti tasmāt saṃtāna abhāva prasaṅgāt devāt anyaḥ manuṣyaḥ na bhavati yatas ca evam atas aśāśvatam api na asti 
[255,i_255,ii]	idānīm śāśvata aśāśvata pratiṣedha artham āha divyaḥ yadi eka deśaḥ syāt eka deśaḥ ca mānuṣaḥ aśāśvatam śāśvatam ca bhavet tat ca na yujyate yadi ayam manuṣyaḥ aṃśena manuṣya tām vijahyāt aṃśena vihāya manuṣya tām deva ātma bhāvam upādadyāt tadā eka deśasya nāśādaśāśvatam syāt eka deśasya ca avasthānāt śāśvatam syāt etat ca ayuktam yat ekasya divya gati saṃgṛhītaḥ eka deśaḥ syāt eka deśaḥ ca manuṣyaḥ syāt tasmāt śāśvatam ca aśāśvatam ca etat ubhayam na upapadyate 
[255,iii_255,iv]	idānīm naśāśvatana eva aśāśvata dṛṣṭi pratiṣedha artham āha aśāśvatam śāśvatam ca prasiddham ubhayam yadi siddhe na śāśvatam kāmam na eva aśāśvatam iti api yadi śāśvatam kiṃcid vastu syāt tadā paścāt aśāśvata darśanāt na eva śāśvatam iti syāt evam yadi kiṃcid aśāśvatam syāt tadā tasya paścāt śāśvata upapattitaḥ na aśāśvatam iti syāt yadā tu śāśvata aśāśvatam eva aprasiddham tadā kutas tad pratiṣedhena na eva śāśvatam na aśāśvatam syāt iti tasmāt etat api ayuktam 
[255,v]	atha syāt anādi janma maraṇa paraṃpara apravṛttam avicchinna kamam saṃsāra prabandham upalabhya śāśvata mā ātmānam parikalpayāmaḥ asti asau śāśvataḥ kaścid padārthaḥ yaḥ hi nāma evam anādimati saṃsāre paribhraman adya api upalabhyate iti ucyate etat api na upapadyate kim kāraṇam yaḥ hi nāma kutaścid āgataḥ kaścid kiṃcid gacchet punar kvacid yadi tasmāt anādiḥ tu saṃsāraḥ syāt na ca asti saḥ 
[255,vi]	yadi hi saṃskārāṇām ātmanaḥ va kutaścid gati antarāt gamanam gati antaram āgamanam syāt tatas ca ganti antarāt punar kvacid gamanam syāt tadānīm ana ādiḥ saṃsāraḥ syāt na ca kutaścid kasyacid āgamanam saṃbhavati nityasya vā anityasya vā āgamana anupapatteḥ na ca api itas punar kasyacid kvacid gamanam saṃbhavati nityasya vā anityasya gamana anupapatteḥ yadā ca evam na saṃbhavati tadā kutas janma maraṇa paraṃparāyāḥ ati dīrgha tvena ādi anupalambhāt anādimān saṃsāraḥ syāt saṃsartuḥ abhāvāt kutas anādimat tvam ādima tvam vā saṃsārasya saṃbhavet yadā ca na saṃbhavati tadā yat uktam asti asau śāśvataḥ kaścid padārthaḥ yaḥ hi nāma evam anādimati saṃsāre paribhraman adya api upalabhyate iti tat na yuktam 
[256,i_256,ii]	atas ca evam yathā udita nyāyena na asti ced śāśvataḥ kaścid kaḥ bhaviṣyati aśāśvataḥ śāśvataḥ aśāśvataḥ ca api dvābhyāmābhyām tiraskṛtaḥ yadā ca evam śāśvataḥ eva padārthaḥ na saṃbhavati tadā kasya vigama nāt aśāśvataḥ syāt śāśvata aśāśvata anupalambhāt ca kutas ubhayam kutas na ubhayam iti tasmāt evam śāśvata ādi dṛṣṭi catuṣṭayam pūrva ante saṃsārasya na saṃbhavati 
[256,iii_256,iv]	idānīm anta ananta ādi catuṣṭayam apara ante yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha antavān yadi lokaḥ syāt para lokaḥ katham bhavet atha api anantavān lokaḥ para lokaḥ katham bhavet yadi hi antavān vināśāt ūrdhvam pūrva lokaḥ na syāt tadā para lokaḥ na syāt asti ca para lokaḥ iti antavān lokaḥ iti na upapadyate atha api anantavān lokaḥ syāt tadānīm api para lokaḥ katham bhavet na eva para lokaḥ syāt iti abhiprāyaḥ na ca para lokaḥ na asti atas para loka sadbhāvādantavān api lokaḥ na bhavati 
[256,v_256,vi]	idānīm antavat tvam anantava tvam ca ubhayam etat lokasya yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha skandhānām eṣa saṃtānaḥ yasmāt dīpa arciṣām iva pravartate tasmāt na anta anantavat tvam ca yujyate pūrva uttara hetu phala bhāva saṃbandha nairantarya avicchinnakama vartī yasmāt ayam pradīpa vat pratikṣaṇa vināśī skandha saṃtānaḥ pravartate tasmāt hetu phala pravṛtti darśanāt na antavat tvam na anantavat tvam ca yujyate 
[256,vii_256,viii]	katham kṛtvā pūrve yadi ca bhajyeran utpadyeran na ca api amī skandhāḥ skandhān pratītya imān atha lokaḥ antavān bhavet yadi pūrve manuṣya skandhāḥ naśyeyuḥ tān ca pratītya uttare deva gati upapatti saṃgṛhītāḥ na upapadyeran tadā antavān lokaḥ bhavet taila varti kṣaya niruddha pradīpa vat uttara ātma bhāva utpādāt na asti antavat tvam 
[256,ix_256,x]	pūrve yadi na bhajyeran utpadyeran na ca api amī skandhāḥ skandhān pratītya imān lokaḥ anantaḥ bhavet atha atha yadi pūrvakāḥ skandhāḥ na naśyeṣuḥ tān pratītya uttare phala bhūtāḥ skandhāḥ na utpadyeran tadā anantaḥ avināśī lokaḥ syāt sva rūpāt apracyuta tvāt yadā tu pūrvakāḥ skandhāḥ nirudhyante tad hetukāḥ ca apare skandhāḥ uttarakālam jāyante tadā pūrvakānām anavasthānāt kutas anantavat tvam saṃsārasya syāt 
[256,xi_257,i]	idānīm tṛtīyam ubhaya pakṣa bhāvam pratipādayan āha antavān eka deśaḥ ced eka deśaḥ tu anantavān syāt antavān anantaḥ ca lokaḥ tat ca na yujyate yadi hi kasyacid eka deśasya vināśaḥ syāt eka deśasya ca gati antara gamanam syāt yāt tadānīmantavān ca lokaḥ anantavān ca na ca etat evam saṃbhavati yat eka deśaḥ naśyati eka deśaḥ na naśyati iti atas antavān ca anantavān ca lokaḥ iti na yujyate 
[257,ii_257,iii]	kasmāt punar eka deśasya vināśaḥ eka deśasya ca avasthānam na yujyate iti pratipādayan āha katham tāvat upādātuḥ eka deśaḥ vinaṅkṣyate na naṅkṣyate ca eka deśaḥ evam ca etat na yujyate iha eka deśasya vināśe eka deśasya ca avasthāne parikalpyamāne yadi vā upādātuḥ eka deśasya vināśaḥ avasthānam vā parikalpyeta yadi vā upādānasya tatra yadi tāvat upādātuḥ eka deśasya vināśaḥ eka deśasya ca avasthānam parikalpyate tat na yujyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt katham tāvat upādātuḥ eka deśaḥ vinaṅkṣyate na naṅkṣyate ca eka deśaḥ
[257,iv_257,v]	na eva hi atra kācid upapattiḥ asti yayā eka deśasya vināśam eka deśasya ca avināśam parikalpayiṣyāmaḥ atas eva upapattim apaśyan ācāryaḥ āha evam ca etat na yujyate iti athavā upādātā hi nāma ātmā sa ca skandheṣu pañcadhā mṛgyamāṇaḥ na saṃbhavati yaḥ ca na saṃbhavati tasya katham eka deśaḥ vinaṅkṣyate eka deśaḥ ca na naṅkṣyate atas eva āha evam ca etat na yujyate iti athavā yadi upādātuḥ eka deśaḥ naśyet eka deśaḥ ca na naśyet tadā ekasya eva upādātuḥ deva tvam aṃśena anyena manuṣya tvam syāt na ca etat iṣyate iti āha evam ca etat na yujyate iti evam tāvat upādāturantavat tvam anantavat tvam ca na yuktam iti 
[257,vi_257,vii]	idānīm upādānasya api yathā na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha upādāna eka deśaḥ ca katham nāma vinaṅkṣyate na naṅkṣyate ca eka deśaḥ na etat api upapadyate upādātṛ vat etat api vyākhyeyam 
[257,viii_257,ix]	tat evam ubhaya darśana asaṃbhavam pratipādya idānīm yathā na ubhayam api na saṃbhavati tathā pratipādayan āha antavat ca api anantam ca prasiddham ubhayam yadi siddhe na eva anta vat kāmam na eva ananta vat iti api pratiṣedhyasya vastunaḥ asaṃbhavāt pratiṣedhasya api asaṃbhavaḥ iti atas antavat tve ca anantavat tve ca ubhayasmin apratīte kasya pratiṣedhena na eva antavān na anantavān lokaḥ iti dṛṣṭi saṃbhavaḥ syāt iti 
[257,x]	evam tāvat sāṃvṛtam pratibimba ākāram upādātāram upādānam ca abhyupetya api śāśvata ādi dṛṣṭayasaṃbhavam pratipādya idānīm sarvathā bhāva svabhāva anupalambhena bandhyā putra śyāma gaura ta ādi vat śāśvata ādi dṛṣṭīnām a saṃbhavam pratipipādayiṣuḥ āha athavā sarva bhāvānām śūnya tvāt śāśvata ādayaḥ kva kasya katamāḥ kasmāt saṃbhaviṣyanti dṛṣṭayaḥ 
[258,i_258,ii]	iha sarva bhāvānām pratītyasamutpanna tvāt śūnya tvam sakalena śāstreṇa pratipāditam tatas ca sarva bhāvānām śūnya tvāt katamāḥ tāḥ sarva bhāva bāhyāḥ śāśvata ādyāḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ bhaviṣyanti yāḥ kaścid grahīṣyati yatas tad nirākaraṇam ārapsyāmahe tathā kim vā ālambanam yat sarva bhāva anantargatam yatra etāḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ utpatsyante yatra etāḥ dṛṣṭīḥ nivārayiṣyāmaḥ katamaḥ ca asau bhāvaḥ pudgalaḥ vā sarva bhāva bāhyāḥ yasya etāḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ utpatsyante yam dṛṣṭibhyaḥ nivārayiṣyāmaḥ kim vā dṛṣṭīnām utpatti kāraṇam ālambana nimittam sarva bhāva bāhyam yasmāt nimittāt utpadyamānāḥ śāśvata ādikāḥ dṛṣṭīḥ vārayiṣyāmaḥ sarveṣām eva hi padārthānām sarva bhāva antargata tvāt śūnya tvam śūnya tvāt ca sarve eva hi te padārthāḥ na upalabhyante iti kva kasya katamāḥ kasmāt saṃbhaviṣyanti dṛṣṭayaḥ na eva kāścid na eva kvacid na eva kasyacid na api kenacid ākāreṇa saṃbhaviṣyanti iti abhiprāyaḥ asaṃbhave ca sati āsām parikalpanā eva na utpadyate iti ayuktāḥ eva etāḥ dṛṣṭayaḥ 
[258,iii_258,iv]	tat evam sarva dṛṣṭi prahāṇāya yaḥ saddharmam adeśayat anukampām upādāya tam namasyāmi gautamam tatra saṃsāra nirvāṇa prahāṇa adhigama upalambha prapāta patana saṃdhāraṇāt dharmaḥ satām āryāṇām kṛta kāryāṇām dharmaḥ saddharmaḥ yadi vā śobhanaḥ dharmaḥ saddharmaḥ sakala saṃsāra duḥkha kṣaya kara tvena praśaṃsanīya tvāt yaḥ saddharmam anirodham anutpādam anucchedam aśāśvatam aneka artha manāna artham anāgamam anirgamam prapañca upaśamam śivam pratītyasamutpāda saṃjñayā hi deśitavān sarva dṛṣṭi prahāṇa artham jagatām anukampām upādāya mahā karuṇām eva āśritya priya eka putra adhikatara prema pātra sakala tribhuvana janaḥ na lābha satkāra pratyupakāra ādi lipsayā tam namasyāmi niruttaram advitīyam śāstāram kiṃnāmadheyam gautamam parama ṛṣi gotra saṃbhūtam iti arthaḥ 
[258,v_258,vi^1]	yathā uktam ārya śāli stamba sūtre āryam aitreyeṇa mahā bodhisattvena yaḥ imam pratītyasamutpādam evam yathābhūtam samyak prajñayā satata samitam ajīvam nirjīvam yathāvat aviparītam ajātam abhūtam akṛtam asaṃskṛtam apratigham anāvaraṇam śivam abhayam anāhāryam avyayam avyupaśama svabhāvam paśyati asataḥ tucchataḥ riktataḥ asārataḥ rogataḥ gaṇḍataḥ śalyataḥ aghataḥ anityataḥ duḥkhataḥ śūnyataḥ anātmataḥ na sa pūrva antam pratisarati kim nu aham abhūvam atīte adhvani āhosvit na abhūvam atīte adhvani kaḥ nu aham abhūvam atīte adhvani katham nu aham abhūvam atīte adhvani 
[258,vi^2_259,i]	apara antam vā punar na pratisarati kim nu aham bhaviṣyāmi anāgate adhvani āhosvit na bhaviṣyāmi anāgate adhvani kaḥ nu bhaviṣyāmi anāgate adhvani katham nu bhaviṣyāmi anāgate adhvani pratyutpannam vā punar na pratisarati kim nu idam katham nu idam ke santaḥ ke bhaviṣyāmaḥ ayam sattvaḥ kutam āgataḥ saḥ itas cyutaḥ kutra gamiṣyati iti yāni ekeṣām śramaṇa brāhmaṇānām pṛthak loke dṛṣṭi gatāni bhaviṣyanti tat yathā ātma vāda pratisaṃyuktāni jīva vāda pratisaṃyuktāni kautuka maṅgala pratisaṃyuktāni tāni asya tasmin samaye prahīṇāni bhavanti parijñātāni samucchinna mūlāni tāla mastaka vadana ābhāsa gatāni āyatyām anutpāda ani rodha dharmāṇi atha khalu āyuṣmān śāriputraḥ maitreyasya bodhisattvasya mahāsattvasya bhāṣitam abhinandya anupramodya utthāya āsanāt prakrāntaḥ prakrāntāḥ te ca bhikṣavaḥ iti
